is our feet-wash, here are our tuber fruits, here are the juicy fruits of ours... " [1-10-17]_END

B_1_C_11_7
BEGIN_
तं च राजा दशरथो यष्टुकामः कृतांजलिः |
ऋष्यशृङ्गं द्विजश्रेष्ठं वरयिष्यति धर्मवित् || १-११-८
यज्ञार्थं प्रसवार्थं च स्वर्गार्थं च नरेश्वरः |
लभते च स तं कामं द्विजमुख्याद्विशांपतिः || १-११-९_END
BEGIN_
"That king, the desirer of performing vedic ritual, the knower of virtue and the lord of people, namely Dasharatha 
will be requesting that best Brahman Rishyasringa with his palms adjoined in supplication 
for the conduct of ritual, for progeny and even for his heavenly abodes, and that king of 
all the quarters of earth will accomplish those desires from that eminent Brahman Rishyasringa. 
[1-11-8,9]_END

B_1_C_12_0
BEGIN_
ततः काले बहुतिथे कस्मिंश्चित्सुमनोहरे |वसन्ते समनुप्राप्ते राज्ञो यष्टुं मनोऽभवत् ||१-१२-१_END
BEGIN_
After a lapse some time when spring season has come the king Dasharatha desired to perform the Vedic 
ritual. [1-12-1]_END

B_1_C_1_82
BEGIN_
राजवंशान् शतगुणान् स्थापयिष्यति राघवः |चातुर्वर्ण्यं च लोकेऽस्मिन् स्वे स्वे धर्मे नियोक्ष्यति 
|| १-१-९६_END
BEGIN_
"In this world Raghava will establish kingly dynasties in hundredfold and he will be maintaining the 
four-caste system positing each in his own duty, may it be caste-bound or provincial-kingdom-bound 
duty, in order to achieve a perfect social harmony... [1-1-96]_END

B_1_C_10_16
BEGIN_
प्रतिगृह्य तु तां पूजां सर्वा एव समुत्सुकाः |
ऋषेर्भीताश्च शीघ्रं तु गमनाय मतिं दधुः || १-१०-१८_END
BEGIN_
"All of them have received that kind of worship much enthusiastically, but dread at the arrival 
of the sage Vibhandaka, they quickly made-up their mind to make away from there. [1-10-18]_END

B_1_C_11_8
BEGIN_
पुत्राश्चास्य भविष्यन्ति चत्वारोऽमितविक्रमाः |
वंशप्रतिष्ठानकराः सर्वभूतेषु विश्रुताः || १-११-१०_END
BEGIN_
"There will be four sons to king Dasharatha that abound with valour, enrich dynasty's reputation 
and they will be renowned among all beings." Thus said Sage Sanat Kumara to other sages. [1-11-10]_END

B_1_C_12_1
BEGIN_
ततः प्रसाद्य शिरसा तं विप्रं देववर्णिनम् |यज्ञाय वरयामास संतानार्थं कुलस्य च || १-१२-२_END
BEGIN_
Then bowing his head before that Brahmana sage Rishyasringa whose is glow is like that of a deity, King 
Dasharatha verily beseeched that sage to conduct Vedic ritual on his behalf as he wished to beget progeny 
to maintaining his family line. [1-12-2]_END

B_1_C_1_83
BEGIN_
दशवर्षसहस्राणि दशवर्षशतानि च |रामो राज्यमुपासित्वा ब्रह्मलोकं गमिष्यति || १-१-९७_END
BEGIN_
"Having served the kingdom for ten thousand years and another one thousand years, i.e. for a total 
of eleven thousand years, Rama will go to the abode of Brahma... [1-1-97]_END

B_1_C_10_17
BEGIN_
अस्माकमपि मुख्यानि फलानीमानि वै द्विज |
गृहाण विप्र भद्रं ते भक्षयस्व च मा चिरम् || १-१०-१९_END
BEGIN_
" 'Take these important fruits of ours, oh, Brahman, you be safe, oh, holy one... eat them 
before long....' Said courtesans to Rishyasringa.] [1-10-19]_END

B_1_C_11_9
BEGIN_
एवं स देवप्रवरः पूर्वं कथितवान्कथाम् |
सनत्कुमारो भगवान्पुरा देवयुगे प्रभुः || १-११-११_END
BEGIN_
"This way he that ancient and godly Sage Sanatkumaara, who is also Brahma's brain-child like 
Narada, said this legend in earlier Divine Era, called krita yuga..." thus Sumantra continued 
his narration to Dasharatha. [1-11-11]_END

B_1_C_12_2
BEGIN_
तथेति च स राजानमुवाच च सुसत्कृतः |
संभाराः संभ्रियन्तां ते तुरगश्च विमुच्यताम् || १-१२-३
सरव्याश्चोत्तरे तीरे यज्ञभूमिर्विधीयताम् |_END
BEGIN_
Sage Rishyasringa who by now is well-honoured by the king said to the king, "So it shall be, let the 
paraphernalia for ritual be garnered and let your ritual horse be released as a prerogative and 
let the ritual place be decided on the northern banks of Sarayu River...." [1-12-3]_END

B_1_C_1_84
BEGIN_
इदं पवित्रं पापघ्नं पुण्यं वेदैश्च सम्मितम् |यः पठेद्रामचरितं सर्वपापैः प्रमुच्यते || १-१-९८_END
BEGIN_
"This Ramayana is holy, sin-eradicating, merit-endowing, and conformable with the teachings of Vedas.
Whoever reads this Legend of Rama, will be verily liberated of all sins... [1-1-98]_END

B_1_C_10_18
BEGIN_
ततस्तास्तं समालिंग्य सर्वा हर्षसमन्विताः |
मोदकान्प्रददुस्तस्मै भक्ष्यांश्च विविधान् शुभान् || १-१०-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Then all of the courtesans have embraced him and all of them with a kind of mirthfulness 
in the offing, presented sweet-balls and other varieties of best sweetmeats to him. [1-10-20]_END

B_1_C_11_10
BEGIN_
स त्वं पुरुषशार्दूल तमानय सुसत्कृतम् |
स्वयमेव महाराज गत्वा सबलवाहनः || १-११-१२_END
BEGIN_
" Oh, great king the tigerly-man, he that Sage Rishyasringa be led here on your proceeding 
in person with staff and transport and on adoring him well personally." Thus Sumantra concluded 
his narration. [1-11-12]_END

B_1_C_12_3
BEGIN_

ततो नृपोऽब्रवीद्वाक्यं सुमन्त्रं मन्त्रिसत्तमम् || १-१२-४सुमंत्रावाहय क्षिप्रमृत्विजो ब्रह्मवादिनः |
सुयज्ञं वामदेवं च जाबालिमथ काश्यपम् || १-१२-५पुरोहितं वसिष्ठं च ये चान्ये द्विजसत्तमाः |_END
BEGIN_
Then King Dasharatha said to his best minister Sumantra, "Let the Vedic scholars and ritual conductors 
like Sages Suyajna, Vaamadeva, Jaabaali, and Kaashyapa, along with the family priest Vashishta, as well 
as other Vedic Brahmans that are there, they all be invited swiftly..." [1-12-4, 5, 6a]_END

B_1_C_1_85
BEGIN_
एतदाख्यानमायुष्यं पठन् रामायणं नरः |सपुत्रपौत्रः सगणः प्रेत्य स्वर्गे महीयते || १-१-९९_END
BEGIN_
"This Ramayana is long-life giving. A narrative by reading which a human will be blessed with sons and grandsons, and after enjoying worldly
comforts with attendants, will be adored in heaven after demise... 
[1-1-99]_END

B_1_C_10_19
BEGIN_
तानि चास्वाद्य तेजस्वी फलानीति स्म मन्यते |
अनास्वादितपूर्वाणि वने नित्यनिवासिनाम् || १-१०-२१_END
BEGIN_
"Having relished the sweets, that resplendent sage supposed them to be fruits only, for he 
did not taste sweets earlier, as he is always forest-bound. [1-10-21]_END

B_1_C_11_11
BEGIN_
सुमंत्रस्य वचः श्रुत्वा हृष्टो दशरथोऽभवत् |
अनुमान्य वसिष्ठं च सूतवाक्यं निशम्य च || १-११-१३
सान्तःपुरः सहामात्यः प्रययौ यत्र स द्विजः |_END


B_1_C_12_4
BEGIN_
ततः सुमंत्रस्त्वरितं गत्वा त्वरितविक्रमः || १-१२-६समानयत्स तान्सर्वान् समस्तान्वेदपारगान् 
|तान् पूजयित्वा धर्मात्मा राजा दशरथस्तदा || १-१२-७धर्मार्थसहितं युक्तं श्लक्ष्णं वचनमब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
Then Sumantra being a quickest person went quickly and fetched all those Vedic scholars and clergymen. 
Then the virtuous king Dasharatha having offered due worships to all the sages and saints brought in 
by Sumantra, uttered these words which are with virtue and meaning, in an impressible manner. [1-12-6, 
7, 8a]_END

B_1_C_1_86
BEGIN_
पठन् द्विजो वागृषभत्वमीयात् |स्यात् क्षत्रियो भूमिपतित्वमीयात् ||वणिग्जनः पण्यफलत्वमीयात् |जनश्च शूद्रोऽपि महत्त्वमीयात् || १-१-१००_END
BEGIN_
"By reading this Ramayana, that person if a Brahmana obtains excellency in speech, if a Kshatriya obtains land-lordship, if Vaisya
attains profit in trade and even if a Sudra attains excellence." Thus Sage Narada gave a gist of Ramayana 
to Sage-poet Valmiki. [1-1-100]_END

B_1_C_10_20
BEGIN_
आपृच्छ्य च तदा विप्रं व्रतचर्यां निवेद्य च |
गच्छन्ति स्मापदेशात्ताः भीतास्तस्य पितुः स्त्रियः || १-१०-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Taking leave of the Sage Rishyasringa on pretence that they also have to perform devotional 
duties, they the courtesans departed from there on the pretext of their daily worship, while 
they actually feared for the arrival of Rishyasringa's father who may hurl curses on his arrival... 
[1-10-22]_END

B_1_C_11_12
BEGIN_
वनानि सरितश्चैव व्यतिक्रम्य शनैः शनैः || १-११-१४
अभिचक्राम तं देशं यत्र वै मुनिपुंगवः |_END
BEGIN_
On crossing over the rivers and forests slowly and steadily Dasharatha entered that kingdom 
where that eminent Brahman is there. [1-11-14b, 15a]_END

B_1_C_12_5
BEGIN_
मम लालप्यमानस्य पुत्रार्थं नास्ति वै सुखम् || १-१२-८तदर्थं हयमेधेन यक्ष्यामीति मतिर्मम |
तदहं यष्टुमिच्छामि शास्त्रदृष्टेन कर्मणा || १-१२-९ऋषिपुत्रप्रभावेण कामान्प्राप्स्यामि चाप्यहम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
"My mind is tumultuous without quietude for I have no sons... hence I am thinking of performing the 
Vedic Horse Ritual for progeny... I wish to perform the ritual as enshrined in the scriptures and by 
strict observances... I wish to get my desires fulfilled through the divine influence of the Sage's 
son, Rishyasringa... [1-12-8, 9, 10a]_END

B_1_C_10_21
BEGIN_
गतासु तासु सर्वासु काश्यपस्यात्मजो द्विजः |
अस्वस्थहृदयश्चासीद् दुःखाच्च परिवर्तते || १-१०-२३_END
BEGIN_
"After the departure of all them the courtesans, that Brahman Rishyasringa, the grandson of 
Sage Kaashyapa, is disturbed at heart and even behaved sadly... [1-10-23]_END

B_1_C_12_6
BEGIN_
ततः साध्विति तद्वाक्यं ब्राह्मणाः प्रत्यपूजयन् || १-१२-१०वसिष्ठप्रमुखाः सर्वे पार्थिवस्य मुखाच्च्युतम् |
ऋष्यशृङ्गपुरोगाश्च प्रत्यूचुर्नृपतिं तदा || १-१२-११_END
BEGIN_
Then "Splendid, splendid is this idea," said the Brahmana scholars blessing the king. Then Sage Vashishta 
along with all other important personalities have applauded the idea that has come out of the king's 
voice, and all those Vedic scholars and clerj~nmen keeping Rishyasringa at helm of affairs said this 
to the king, in appreciation of that idea. [1-12-10b, 11]_END

B_1_C_11_13
BEGIN_
आसाद्य तं द्विजश्रेष्ठं रोमपादसमीपगम् || १-११-१५
ऋषिपुत्रं ददर्शाथो दीप्यमानमिवानलम् |_END
BEGIN_
Then Dasharatha saw that best Brahman who he is nearby king Romapada, and who is resplendent 
like ritual fire. [1-11-15b, 16a]_END

B_1_C_10_22
BEGIN_
ततोऽपरेद्युस्तं देशमाजगाम स वीर्यवान् |
विभाण्डकसुतः श्रीमान्मनसा चिन्तयन्मुहुः || १-१०-२४
मनोज्ञा यत्र ता दृष्टा वारमुख्याः स्वलंकृताः |_END
BEGIN_
"Then on the next day Rishyasringa, son of Vibhandaka and the prosperous sage with ascetic 
power has arrived at that place where he saw well-decorated and delightful courtesans recollecting 
in mind repetitively about them alone. [1-10-24, 25a]_END

B_1_C_11_14
BEGIN_
ततो राजा यथायोग्यं पूजां चक्रे विशेषतः || १-११-१६
सखित्वात्तस्य वै राज्ञः प्रहृष्टेनान्तरात्मना |_END
BEGIN_
Then king Romapada gladdened at heart of hearts paid excellent respects to king Dasharatha 
procedurally and in view of their friendship.[1-11-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_12_7
BEGIN_
संभाराः संभ्रियन्तां ते तुरगश्च विमुच्यताम् |सरव्याश्चोत्तरे तीरे यज्ञभूमिर्विधीयताम् || १-१२-१२
सर्वथा प्राप्यसे पुत्रांश्चतुरोऽमितविक्रमान् |यस्य ते धार्मिकी बुद्धिरियं पुत्रार्थमागता || 
१-१२-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Because a virtuous thinking of begetting sons through Vedic ritual has come to you, you will by all 
means get four sons with boundless valour... let ritual paraphernalia be garnered and let your ritual-horse 
be released and let the ritual place be decided on the northern banks of Sarayu River...." 
The Vedic seers thus blessed Dasharatha. [1-12-12, 13]_END

B_1_C_10_23
BEGIN_
दृष्टैव च ततो विप्रमायान्तं हृष्टमानसाः || १-१०-२५
उपसृत्य ततः सर्वास्तास्तमूचुरिदं वचः |
एह्याश्रमपदं सौम्य ह्यस्माकमिति चाब्रुवन् || १-१०-२६_END
BEGIN_
" Then on seeing the arrival of that Brahman, the courtesans felt happy at heart, and all 
of those courtesans on surrounding him said, "oh, gentle one, welcome to the threshold of 
our hermitage... [1-10-25b, 26]_END

B_1_C_11_15
BEGIN_
रोमपादेन चाख्यातमृषिपुत्राय धीमते || १-११-१७
सख्यं संबन्धकं चैव तदा तं प्रत्यपूजयत् |_END
BEGIN_
Then Romapada informed the wise sage Rishyasringa about the friendship and relation with Dasharatha, 
and then that sage worshipped king Dasharatha in his return. [1-11-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_12_8
BEGIN_
ततः प्रीतोऽभवद्राजा श्रुत्वा तत् द्विजभाषितम् |अमात्यांश्चाब्रवीद्राजा हर्षेणेदं शुभाक्षरम् 
|| १-१२-१४_END
BEGIN_
Then the king is gladdened to hear the blessing advises of the Vedic scholars, and he spoke to the other 
ministers of his court, with happiness derived from those good words. [1-12-14]_END

B_1_C_10_24
BEGIN_
चित्राण्यत्र बहूनि स्युर्मूलानि च फलनि च |
तत्राप्येष विशेषेण विधिर्हि भविता ध्रुवम् || १-१०-२७_END
BEGIN_
"There are excellent tuber fruits and fruits and there will be a very distinctive hospitality... 
definitely indeed..." So said the courtesans.[1-10-27]_END

B_1_C_11_16
BEGIN_
एवं सुसत्कृतस्तेन सहोषित्वा नरर्षभः || १-११-१८
सप्ताष्टदिवसान् राजा राजानमिदमब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
Thus well received by king Romapada, king Dasharatha spent seven to eight days with him, and 
then spoke this to king Romapada. [1-11-18b, 19a]_END

B_1_C_12_9
BEGIN_
गुरूणां वचनाच्छीघ्रं संभाराः संभ्रियन्तु मे |समर्थाधिष्ठितश्चाश्वः सोपाध्यायो विमुच्यताम् 
|| १-१२-१५सरयव्याश्चोत्तरे तीरे यज्ञभूमिर्विधीयताम् |शांतयश्चाभिवर्धन्तां यथाकल्पं यथाविधि || १-१२-१६
शक्यः कर्तुमयं यज्ञः सर्वेणापि महीक्षिता | नापराधो भवेत्कष्टो यद्यस्मिन् 
क्रतुसत्तमे || १-१२-१७छिद्रं हि मृगयन्तेऽत्र विद्वांसो ब्रह्मराक्षसाः | विघ्नितस्य हि यज्ञस्य 
सद्यः कर्ता विनश्यति || १-१२-१८तद्यथा विधिपूर्वं मे क्रतुरेष समाप्यते |तथा विधानं क्रियतां 
समर्थाः करणेष्विह || १-१२-१९_END
BEGIN_
The king said to his executives, "As advised by my Vedic teachers, let the paraphernalia for my ritual 
be procured... let the ritual-horse be released, guarded well by gallant men in its journey... and let 
religious teachers follow that horse as per tradition... let the ritual place be decided on the northern 
banks of Sarayu River... let the peace invocations be prevailing and prospering throughout as ordained 
in the scriptures and tradition... all the kings on this earth would have performed this Horse Ritual, 
if only they can perform this without a mistake... thus, this is a great and difficult ritual... the 
Brahma-demons will be hunting for the faults performed in the rituals whereat they can inteject themselves 
in to the proceedings of the ritual in order to ruin it... further, the performer of the ritual also 
gets ruined if there were be to be faults... that is why this ritual shall be conducted faultlessly 
till its conclusion, and with absolute adherence to the scriptures... since all of you assembled here 
are efficient ones in conducting such rituals without faults, I hope you all will organise carefully.... 
[1-12-15,16,17,18, 19]_END

B_1_C_10_25
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा तु वचनं तासां सर्वासां हृदयङ्गमम् |
गमनाय मतिं चक्रे तं च निन्युस्तदा स्त्रियः || १-१०-२८_END
BEGIN_
"On hearing the heart-pleasing words of all those courtesans, Rishyasringa made up his mind 
to go over there, and then those women took him away [to their place in Anga Kingdom.] [1-10-28]_END

B_1_C_11_17
BEGIN_
शांता तव सुता राजन् सह भर्त्रा विशांपते || १-११-१९
मदीयं नगरं यातु कार्यं हि महदुद्यतम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lord of subjects, your daughter Princess Shanta may go over my city Ayodhya along with 
her husband Rishyasringa, as oh, king, I am contemplating to perform a great Vedic ritual, 
indeed." So said Dasharatha to Romapada. [1-11-19b, 20a]_END

B_1_C_12_10
BEGIN_
तथेति च ततः सर्वे मंत्रिणः प्रत्यपूजयन् |पार्थिवेन्द्रस्य तद्वाक्यं यथाज्ञप्तमकुर्वत 
|| १-१२-२०_END
BEGIN_
In appreciation of his orders all the ministers replied the king saying "it will be done accordingly..." 
and indeed they have faultlessly carried out works as ordered. [1-12-20]_END

B_1_C_10_26
BEGIN_
तत्र चानीयमाने तु विप्रे तस्मिन्महात्मनि |
ववर्ष सहसा देवो जगत्प्रह्लादयंस्तदा || १-१०-२९_END
BEGIN_
"While that great soul ad Brahman Rishyasringa while being brought into Anga Kingdom, then 
the Rain-god quickly showered rain in Anga kingdom to the delight of the world. [1-10-29]_END

B_1_C_12_11
BEGIN_
ततो द्विजास्ते धर्मज्ञमस्तुवन्पार्थिवर्षभम् |अनुज्ञातास्ततः सर्वे पुनर्जग्मुर्यथागतम् || १-१२-२१_END
BEGIN_
Then all the Brahmans applauded the virtuous king and who is like a Sacred Bull among the kings for 
his virtuous endeavour of undertaking the Vedic ritual, and with his permission all of them returned 
from there as they have come. [1-12-21]_END

B_1_C_11_18
BEGIN_
तथेति राजा संश्रुत्य गमनं तस्य धीमतः || १-११-२०
उवाच वचनं विप्रं गच्छ त्वं सह भार्यया |_END
BEGIN_
"So it shall be" said king Romapada agreeing to their travel with king Dasharatha, and addressed 
these words to that Brahman sage and his son-in-law, Sage Rishyasringa "You may proceed along 
with your wife." [1-11-20b, 21a]_END

B_1_C_10_27
BEGIN_
वर्षेणैवागतं विप्रं विषयं स्वं नराधिपः |
प्रत्युद्गम्य मुनिं प्रह्वः शिरसा च महीं गतः || १-१०-३०
अर्घ्यं च प्रददौ तस्मै न्यायतः सुसमाहितः |
वव्रे प्रसादं विप्रेन्द्रान्मा विप्रं मन्युराविशेत् || १-१०-३१_END
BEGIN_
"The king Romapada personally proceeded towards that Brahman Rishyasring who is now 
entering Anga kingdom along with rains, made prostratiion before him, offered water 
customarily with dedication, and then the king Romapada besought beneficence 
of the best sage Rishyasringa to save him and his kingdom from the fury of his father Sage Vibhandaka, 
if sage Vibhandaka were to know about this pursuit of bringing Rishyasringa to Anga 
country, at a later time ... [1-10-30, 31]_END

B_1_C_11_19
BEGIN_
ऋषिपुत्रः प्रतिश्रुत्य तथेत्याह नृपं तदा || १-११-२१
स नृपेणाभ्यनुज्ञातः प्रययौ सह भार्यया |_END
BEGIN_
Then Rishyasringa agreed and replied to the king Romapada "So it will be done" and then having 
been permitted by the king he set forth along with his wife. [1-11-21b, 22a]_END

B_1_C_12_12
BEGIN_
गतेष्वथ द्विजाग्र्येषु मंत्रिणस्तान्नराधिपः |विसर्जयित्वा स्वं वेश्म प्रविवेश महाद्युतिः ||१-१२-२२_END
BEGIN_
On the departure of the prominent Brahmans, King Dasharatha sent off those ministers who are still available 
there for further orders from the king, and then he the great resplendent king has entered his own palace. 
[1-12-22]_END

B_1_C_10_28
BEGIN_
अन्तःपुरं प्रविश्यास्मै कन्यां दत्त्वा यथाविधि |
शांतां शान्तेन मनसा राजा हर्षमवाप सः || १-१०-३२_END
BEGIN_
"On entering the palace princess Shanta is given to Rishyasringa in customary marriage, and 
then that King Romapada obtained rejoice with a peaceful mind. [1-10-32]_END

B_1_C_11_20
BEGIN_
तावन्योन्यांजलिं कृत्वा स्नेहात्संश्लिष्य चोरसा || १-११-२२
ननंदतुर्दशरथो रोमपादश्च वीर्यवान् |_END
BEGIN_
Those valiant kings greeted each other with thanksgiving palm-fold, and in friendship they 
embraced each other and gladdened. [1-11-22b, 23a]_END

B_1_C_10_29
BEGIN_
एवं स न्यवसत्तत्र सर्वकामैः सुपूजितः |
ऋष्यशृङ्गो महातेजाः शन्तया सह भार्यया || १-१०-३३_END
BEGIN_
" Thus that great fulgent Rishyasringa lived in Anga kingdom along with his wife Shanta, and 
with all his desires fulfilled and also well worshipped" [Thus Sumantra said the legend of 
Rishyasringa to King Dasharatha.] [1-10-33]_END

B_1_C_11_21
BEGIN_
ततः सुहृदमापृच्छ्य प्रस्थितो रघुनन्दनः || १-११-२३
पौरेभ्यः प्रेषयामास दूतान्वै शीघ्रगामिनः |_END
BEGIN_
Then king Dasharatha who set forth to Ayodhya bade farewell to his friend king Romapada, and 
he firstly sent quick-footed messengers to Ayodhya to inform his citizens about his arrival 
along with Sage Rishyasringa. [1-11-23b, 24a]_END

B_1_C_11_22
BEGIN_
क्रियतां नगरं सर्वं क्षिप्रमेव स्वलंकृतम् || १-११-२४
धूपितं सिक्तसम्मृष्टं पताकाभिरलंकृतम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Let the entire city of Ayodhya be well decorated very quickly, let her streets be sprinkled 
with water and then swept, let the flags of welcome be hoisted.." Thus, king Dasharatha ordered 
messengers that are sent beforehand. [1-11-24b, 25a]_END

B_1_C_11_23
BEGIN_
ततः प्रहृष्टाः पौरास्ते श्रुत्वा राजानमागतम् || १-११-२५
तथा प्रचक्रुस्तत्सर्वं राज्ञा यत्प्रेषितं तदा |_END
BEGIN_
Then on hearing the arrival of their king all the citizens felt very happy and readily performed 
all those works exactly as ordered by their king. [1-11-25b, 26a]_END

B_1_C_11_24
BEGIN_
ततः स्वलंकृतं राजा नगरं प्रविवेश ह || १-११-२६
शङ्खदुन्दुभिनिर्घोषैः पुरस्कृत्य द्विजर्षभम् |_END
BEGIN_
Then king Dasharatha keeping Rishyasringa before him entered the well-decorated city Ayodhya 
amidst the full sounding of conch shells and drumbeats. [1-11-26b, 27a]_END

B_1_C_11_25
BEGIN_
ततः प्रमुदिताः सर्वे दृष्ट्वा तं नागरा द्विजम् || १-११-२७
प्रवेश्यमानं सत्कृत्य नरेन्द्रेणेन्द्रकर्मणा |
यथा दिवि सुरेन्द्रेण सहस्राक्षेण काश्यपम् || १-११-२८_END
BEGIN_
Then all the citizens are very happy on seeing that Brahman, Sage Rishyasringa, who is well 
honoured and being entered into the city by their king Dasharatha, as has been done once by 
Indra when he entered sage Kashyapa's son Vamana, the dwarfish boy and the incarnation of 
Vishnu, into heavens, and thus those citizens felt that their human lord Dasharatha vies with 
divine lord Indra. [1-11-27b, 28]_END

B_1_C_11_26
BEGIN_
अन्तःपुरं प्रवेश्यैनं पूजां कृत्वा च शास्त्रतः |
कृतकृत्यं तदात्मानं मेने तस्योपवाहनात् || १-११-२९_END
BEGIN_
Dasharatha entered the sage into the palace chambers and worshipped him there as ordained 
in the scriptures, and in bringing the Sage here into his country, king Dasharatha believed 
that his desired is fulfilled. [1-11-28]_END

B_1_C_11_27
BEGIN_
अन्तःपुरस्त्रियः सर्वाः शांतां दृष्ट्वा तथागताम् |
सह भर्त्रा विशालाक्षीं प्रीत्यानंदमुपागमन् || १-११-३०_END
BEGIN_
On seeing her, the broad-eyed Shanta, who came there along with her husband all the ladies 
of palace derived happiness for the homecoming of their own daughter, as it were. [1-11-29]_END

B_1_C_11_28
BEGIN_
पूज्यमाना तु ताभिः सा राज्ञा चैव विशेषतः |
उवास तत्र सुखिता कञ्चित्कालं सहर्त्विजा || १-११-३१_END
BEGIN_
Shanta thus being admired by all of them, and in an exceptional manner by Dasharatha, comfortably 
resided there along with her husband, the Vedic scholar Rishyasringa. [1-11-31]_END

B_1_C_13_0
BEGIN_
पुनः प्राप्ते वसन्ते तु पूर्णः संवत्सरोऽभवत् |
प्रसवार्थं गतो यष्टुं हयमेधेन वीर्यवान् || १-१३-१_END
BEGIN_
On completion of one full year another springtime arrived, and then Dasharatha a determined 
one to beget progeny by performing Horse Ritual entered the ritual hall. [1-13-1]_END

B_1_C_13_1
BEGIN_
अभिवाद्य वसिष्ठं च न्यायतः प्रतिपूज्य च |
अब्रवीत्प्रश्रितं वाक्यं प्रसवार्थं द्विजोत्तमम् || १-१३-२_END
BEGIN_
Greeting and even adoring the Sage Vashishta customarily Dasharatha said these very humble 
words to him. [1-13-2]_END

B_1_C_13_2
BEGIN_
यज्ञो मे क्रियतां ब्रह्मन् यथोक्तं मुनिपुङ्गव |
यथा न विघ्नः क्रियते यज्ञांगेषु विधीयताम् || १-१३-३_END
BEGIN_
"Let my ritual be performed scripturally, oh eminent Brahman, let it be conducted in such 
a way that no obstacle occurs even in its ancillary functions. [1-13-3]_END

B_1_C_13_3
BEGIN_
भवान्स्निग्धः सुहृन्मह्यं गुरुश्च परमो महान् |
वोढव्यो भवता चैव भारो यज्ञस्य चोद्यतः || १-१३-४_END
BEGIN_
"You being my very reverent royal priest are friendly and kind-hearted to me, and you alone 
shall shoulder the burden of the commenced ritual in all good faith and credence. [1-13-4]_END

B_1_C_13_4
BEGIN_
तथेति च स राजानमब्रवीत् द्विजसत्तमः |
करिष्ये सर्वमेवैतद्भवता यत्समर्थितम् ||१-१३-५_END
BEGIN_
Then that reverent Brahman Vashishta said to king, "Whatever that is requested or decided 
by you, I will see that all of them are materialised accordingly. [1-13-5]_END

B_1_C_13_5
BEGIN_
ततोऽब्रवीत् द्विजान्वृद्धान् यज्ञकर्मसु निष्ठितान् |
स्थापत्ये निष्ठितांश्चैव वृद्धान्परमधार्मिकान् || १-१३-६
कर्मान्तिकान् शिल्पकरान् वर्धकीन् खनकानपि |
गणकान् शिल्पिनश्चैव तथैव नटनर्तकान् || १-१३-७
तथा शुचीन् शास्त्रविदः पुरुषान्सुबहुश्रुतान् |
यज्ञकर्म समीहन्तां भवन्तो राजशासनात् || १-१३-८
इष्टका बहुसाहस्री शीघ्रमानीयतामिति |
औपकार्याः क्रियन्तां च राज्ञो बहुगुणान्विताः || १-१३-९_END
BEGIN_
Then Sage Vashishta then summoned and spoke to elderly Brahman scholars, and elderly architects 
who are all proficient and elderly experts in conducting the construction of the ritual hall 
etc. Then summoned are the construction supervisors, brick-makers, carpenters, earth-diggers, 
accountants, and sculptors. So also the actors and dancers are summoned. Thus flawless scholars 
in scriptures and those men who are well read in Veda-s, are called and he addressed them 
saying, "Performance of the ritual be organised by the order of the king. Bricks in many thousands 
be brought quickly and royal palaces as temporary guesthouses be built for the kingly guests, 
with very many facilities included in them. [1-13-6,7,8,9]_END

B_1_C_13_6
BEGIN_
ब्राह्मणावसथाश्चैव कर्तव्याः शतशः शुभाः |
भक्ष्यान्नपानैर्बहुभिः समुपेताः सुनिष्ठिताः ||१-१३-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Like that, for accommodating Brahmans hundreds of sanctified houses be built, well endowed 
and well established with very many eatables, foods, and potables. [1-13-10]_END

B_1_C_13_7
BEGIN_
तथा पौरजनस्यापि कर्तव्याश्च सुविस्तराः |
आगतानां सुदूराच्च पार्थिवानां पृथक् पृथक् || १-१३-११_END
BEGIN_
"So also, accommodation is to be given for city dwellers too, in very spacious housing, and 
severally for the kings arriving from distant places.[1-13-11]_END

B_1_C_13_8
BEGIN_
वाजिवारणशलाश्च तथा शय्यागृहाणि च |
भटानां महदावास वैदेशिकनिवासिनाम् || १-१३-१२_END
BEGIN_
"For horses stables, reposing stalls for elephants, like that great billets for soldiers may 
be built for those foreign-country dwellers arriving in here on their horses and elephants 
along with their soldiers. [1-13-12]_END

B_1_C_13_9
BEGIN_
आवासा बहुभक्ष्या वै सर्वकामैरुपस्थिताः |
तथा पौरजनस्यापि जनस्य बहुशोभनम् || १-१३-१३_END
BEGIN_
"These lodgings are to be arranged with many foods and utilities for the people of this city 
and for others coming from distant countries, and a very grand food be given in all of them. 
[1-13-13]_END

B_1_C_13_10
BEGIN_
दातव्यमन्नं विधिवत्सत्कृत्य न तु लीलया |
सर्वे वर्णा यथा पूजां प्राप्नुवन्ति सुसत्कृताः || १-१३-१४
न चावज्ञा प्रयोक्तव्या कामक्रोधवशादपि |_END
BEGIN_
"Food is to be given dutifully treating all of them well but not just illusively, and the 
people of all the castes shall be well honoured as they would get their due respect, and no 
disrespect be shown, even when overcome by passion or anger at anyone. [1-13-14, 15a]_END

B_1_C_14_0
BEGIN_
अथ संवत्सरे पूर्णे तस्मिन् प्राप्ते तुरंगमे |
सरय्वाश्चोत्तरे तीरे राज्ञो यज्ञोऽभ्यवर्तत || १-१४-१_END
BEGIN_
Then after completion of one year and on regaining the ritual horse, the Emperor Dasharatha 
commenced his Vedic Ritual on the northern banks of River Sarayu. [1-14-1]_END

B_1_C_14_1
BEGIN_
ऋष्यशृङ्गं पुरस्कृत्य कर्म चक्रुर्द्विजर्षभाः |
अश्वमेधे महायज्ञे राज्ञोऽस्य सुमहात्मनः || १-१४-२_END
BEGIN_
Keeping Rishyasringa at the helm of affairs those eminent Brahmans commenced, ashva-medha 
, the Horse-ritual of that noble-souled Dasharatha. [1-14-2]_END

B_1_C_13_11
BEGIN_
यज्ञकर्मसु ये व्यग्राः पुरुषाः शिल्पिनस्तथा || १-१३-१५
तेषामपि विशेषेण पूजा कार्या यथाक्रमम् |
ये स्युः संपूजिता सर्वे वसुभिर्भोजनेन च || १-१३-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Exceptionally respectable are those men and architects that are preoccupied in the works 
of the ritual as they deserve, and those men involved in these works shall be well-treated 
with funds and food. [1-13-15b, 16]_END

B_1_C_14_2
BEGIN_
कर्म कुर्वन्ति विधिवद्याजका वेदपारगाः |
यथाविधि यथान्यायं परिक्रामन्ति शास्त्रतः || १-१४-३_END
BEGIN_
Those well-versed conductors of Vedic rituals called ritviks , have started to perform 
works relating to ritual as per canon and rules, and conducted them scripturally and customarily. 
[1-14-3]_END

B_1_C_13_12
BEGIN_
यथा सर्वं सुविहितं न किंचित्परिहीयते |
तथा भवन्तः कुर्वन्तु प्रीतियुक्तेन चेतसा || १-१३-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Thus, as to how all this be well organised without least negligence, thus you all shall administer 
in all your cooperation and good spirit." Thus Sage Vashishta spoke to the organisers. [1-13-17]_END

B_1_C_14_3
BEGIN_
प्रवर्ग्यं शास्त्रतः कृत्वा तथैवोपसदं द्विजाः |
चक्रुश्च विधिवत्सर्वमधिकं कर्म शास्त्रतः || १-१४-४_END
BEGIN_
On performing pravargya ritual as per scriptures, like that upasada ritual 
too, those Brahmans have customarily performed all of those other rituals incidental to the 
main one scripturally. [1-14-4]_END

B_1_C_13_13
BEGIN_
ततः सर्वे समागम्य वसिष्ठमिदमब्रुवन् |
यथेष्टं तत्सुविहितं न किंचित्परिहीयते || १-१३-१८
यथोक्तं तत्करिष्यामो न किंचित्परिहास्यते |_END
BEGIN_
Then all of them collectively replied to Sage Vashishta "As desired, all the well ordered 
works will not be neglected in the least, and they will be done as ordered, and not the least 
of them will be slighted." So said the artisans to Sage Vashishta. [1-13-18, 19a]_END

B_1_C_14_4
BEGIN_
अभिपूज्य तदा हृष्टाः सर्वे चक्रुर्यथाविधि |
प्रातःसवनपूर्वाणि कर्माणि मुनिपुंगवाः || १-१४-५_END
BEGIN_
Then all of those distinguished sages are contended with what they have performed by worshipping 
gods already summoned, they also conducted early morning savana ritual and its ancillaries 
as enjoined. [1-14-5]_END

B_1_C_13_14
BEGIN_
ततः सुमंत्रमाहूय वसिष्ठो वाक्यमब्रवीत् || १-१३-१९
निमंत्रयस्व नृपतीन्पृथिव्यां ये च धार्मिकाः |
ब्राह्मणान् क्षत्रियान् वैश्यान् शूद्रांश्चैव सहस्रशः || १-१३-२०
समानयस्व सत्कृत्य सर्वदेशेषु मानवान् |_END
BEGIN_
"Then on calling for Sumantra, Sage Vashishta said these words to him, "Let all those kings 
of the earth that are righteous be invited, and let all the people from all the kingdoms, 
say Brahmans, Kshatriya-s, Vaisya-s, Shudra-s be invited in scores duly honouring them." So 
said Vashishta to Sumantra. [1-13-19b, 20, 21a]_END

B_1_C_14_5
BEGIN_
ऐन्द्रश्च विधिवद्दत्तो राजा चाभिषुतोऽनघः | 
माध्यंदिनं च सवनं प्रावर्तत यथाक्रमम् || १-१४-६_END
BEGIN_
The oblations addressed to Indra are well given as ordained, and the flawless king Dasharatha 
also crushed the Soma creeper to squeeze Soma juice, and thus the mid-day savana 
ritual has come to pass according to sequence. [1-14-6]_END

B_1_C_13_15
BEGIN_
मिथिलाधिपतिं शूरं जनकं सत्यवादिनम् || १-१३-२१
तमानय महाभागं स्वयमेव सुसत्कृतम् |
पूर्वसंबन्धिनं ज्ञात्वा ततः पूर्वं ब्रवीमि ते || १-१३-२२_END
BEGIN_
"You personally invite Janaka the king of Mithila, a valiant one and an advocate of truth, 
honouring his well and duly bearing in mind that he is a long-time associate of our King Dasharatha, 
hence I am telling you in the first instance. [1-13-21b,22]_END

B_1_C_15_0
BEGIN_
मेधावी तु ततो ध्यात्वा स किञ्चिदिदमुत्तरम् |
लब्धसंज्ञः ततस्तं तु वेदज्ञो नृपमब्रवीत् || १-१५-१_END
BEGIN_
That intellectual sage and one proficient in Veda-s Rishyasringa contemplated for a while, 
and gaining indications as to which ritual is to be performed, then said the king. [1-15-1]_END

B_1_C_13_16
BEGIN_
तथा काशीपतिं स्निग्धं सततं प्रियवादिनम् |
सद् वृत्तं देवसंकाशं स्वयमेवानयस्व ह || १-१३-२३_END
BEGIN_
"Thus that King of Kaashi who is always a friendly, affectionate and a cordial one, indeed 
he shall be invited by you personally. [1-13-23]_END

B_1_C_14_6
BEGIN_
तृतीयसवनं चैव राज्ञोऽस्य सुमहात्मनः |
चक्रुस्ते शास्त्रतो दृष्ट्वा तथा ब्राह्मणपुंगवाः || १-१४-७_END
BEGIN_
Like that those proficient Brahmans have also performed the third savana , ritual 
of that great-exalted soul Dasharatha according to the viewpoint of scriptures. [1-14-7]_END

B_1_C_15_1
BEGIN_
इष्टिं तेऽहं करिष्यामि पुत्रीयां पुत्रकारणात् |
अथर्वशिरसि प्रोक्तैर्मन्त्रैः सिद्धां विधानतः || १-१५-२_END
BEGIN_
"I will procedurally conduct the ritual contained in the preamble of atharva-veda 
with procedural hymns, called <<em>>putra kaameSTi i.e., the ritual that bestows sons, for 
your benefit." [1-15-2]_END

B_1_C_13_17
BEGIN_
तथा केकयराजानं वृद्धं परमधार्मिकम् |
श्वशुरं राजसिंहस्य सपुत्रं त्वमिहानय || १-१३-२४_END
BEGIN_
"Likewise, King of Kekaya, an elderly, very virtuous, and also the father-in-law of our Lion-King 
Dasharatha, you personally invite him along with his sons. [1-13-24]_END

B_1_C_14_7
BEGIN_
आह्वयांचक्रिरे तत्र शक्रादीन् विबुधोत्तमान् |
ऋष्यशृङ्गादयो मन्त्रैः शिक्षाक्षरसमन्वितैः || १-१४-८_END
BEGIN_
Rishyasringa and other best scholars with their well lettered and intonated Vedic hymns have 
invoked Indra and other gods to that place. [1-14-8]_END

B_1_C_15_2
BEGIN_
ततः प्राक्रमदिष्टिं तां पुत्रीयां पुत्रकारणात् |
जुहाव चाग्नौ तेजस्वी मन्त्रदृष्टेन कर्मणा || १-१५-३_END
BEGIN_
Then that resplendent Sage Rishyasringa commenced that putrakaameSTi ritual, offering 
oblations into sacred fire with ritual acts meticulously contained in hymns. [1-15-3]_END

B_1_C_13_18
BEGIN_
अङ्गेश्वरं महेष्वासं रोमपादं सुसत्कृतम् |
वयस्यं राजसिंहस्य समानय यशस्विनम् || १-१३-२५_END
BEGIN_
"Romapada, the lord of Anga kingdom and the user of great bow, let that illustrious one be 
invited well honoured, for he is the friend of our lion-king Dasharatha. [1-13-25]_END

B_1_C_14_8
BEGIN_
गीतिभिर्मधुरैः स्निग्धैर्मन्त्राह्वानैर्यथार्हतः |
होतारो ददुरावाह्य हविर्भागान् दिवौकसाम् || १-१४-९_END
BEGIN_
The hotaa -s, invocators, have welcomed the celestials for partaking oblations by 
singing saama Veda hymns sweetly and harmoniously, and on inviting them with Vedic 
hymns they have offered oblations to them. [1-14-9]_END

B_1_C_15_3
BEGIN_
ततो देवाः सगन्धर्वाः सिद्धाश्च परमर्षयः |
भागप्रतिग्रहार्थं वै समवेता यथाविधि || १-१५-४_END
BEGIN_
Then the deities along with celestial beings, siddha-s, i.e., the souls that obtained salvation, 
and also other esteemed sages who by now are the residents of Heavens have duteously assembled 
in the firmament to receive their part of the oblations. [1-15-4]_END

B_1_C_13_19
BEGIN_
तथा कोसलराजानं भानुमंतं सुसत्कृतम् |
मगधाधिपतिं शूरं सर्वशास्त्रविशारदम् || १-१३-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Like that King of Kosala namely Bhanumanta, and the King of Magadha, a brave one and a profound 
one in all scriptural knowledge, let them be honoured well and be invited. [1-13-26]_END

B_1_C_14_9
BEGIN_
न चाहुतमभूत्तत्र स्खलितं वा न किंचन |
दृश्यते ब्रह्मवत्सर्वं क्षेमयुक्तं हि चक्रिरे || १-१४-१०_END
BEGIN_
There is no unburnt oblation resulted in that fire-ritual nor even a small mishap slipped 
in the performance of ritual. Everything appeared canonically correct and hymn oriented. Indeed 
the ritual is performed in a secure way. [1-14-10]_END

B_1_C_15_4
BEGIN_
ताः समेत्य यथान्यायं तस्मिन् सदसि देवताः |
अब्रुवन् लोककर्तारं ब्रह्माणं वचनं ततः || १-१५-५_END
BEGIN_
Those deities who procedurally assembled there in that congregation then spoke to Brahma, 
the creator of worlds. [1-15-5]_END

B_1_C_13_20
BEGIN_
प्राप्तिज्ञं परमोदारं सत्कृतं पुरुषर्षभम् |
राज्ञः शासनमादाय चोदयस्व नृपर्षभान् |
प्राचीनान् सिन्धुसौवीरान् सौराष्ट्रेयांश्च पार्थिवान् || १-१३-२७_END
BEGIN_
"And Praaptijna, the king of Magadha, the kind-hearted and best one among kings, be well honoured 
and invited. Further, taking the orders of King Dasharatha and motivated by those orders, 
the kings of Sindhu, Sauviira and Sauraastra kingdoms may also be invited. [1-13-27]_END

B_1_C_14_10
BEGIN_
न तेष्वहःसु श्रान्तो वा क्षुधितो वापि दृश्यते |
नाविद्वान् ब्राह्मणस्तत्र नाशतानुचरस्तथा || १-१४-११_END
BEGIN_
In these days of ritual none found there to be weary or hungry, and there is no single unscholarly 
person, nor any Brahman without at least a hundred apprentices. [1-14-11]_END

B_1_C_15_5
BEGIN_
भगवंस्त्वत्प्रसादेन रावणो नाम राक्षसः |
सर्वान्नो बाधते वीर्याच्छासितुं तं न शक्नुमः || १-१५-६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh! God, the demon named Ravana is torturing all of us with his intrepidity, as you have 
blessed him, and we are unable to control him. [1-15-6]_END

B_1_C_13_21
BEGIN_
दाक्षिणात्यान्नरेन्द्रांश्च समस्तानानयस्व ह |
सन्ति स्निग्धाश्च ये चान्ये राजानः पृथिवीतले || १-१३-२८
तानानय यथा क्षिप्रं सानुगान् सहबान्धवान् |
एतान् दूतैर्महाभागैरानयस्व नृपाज्ञया || १-१३-२९_END
BEGIN_
"All of the kings of southern kingdoms be invited, and should there be any other friends and 
other friendly kings on the surface of the earth, they too shall be invited as early as possible 
with all their followers, relatives through highly illustrious envoys, of course with the 
orders of our king." Thus Sage Vashishta said to minister Sumantra. [1-13-28, 29]_END

B_1_C_14_11
BEGIN_
ब्राह्मणा भुञ्जते नित्यं नाथवन्तश्च भुञ्जते |
तापसा भुञ्जते चापि श्रमणाश्चैव भुञ्जते || १-१४-१२_END
BEGIN_
Given anytime the Brahmans, servants, sages, and pilgrims are fed with food for their arrival 
at the place of boarding is unpredictable, and that arrival is dependent on their duties for 
Brahmans, and by their masters for servants, and for pilgrims that do not have a particular 
time of arrival or departure. [1-14-12]_END

B_1_C_15_6
BEGIN_
त्वया तस्मै वरो दत्तः प्रीतेन भगवान् तदा |
मानयन्तश्च तं नित्यं सर्वं तस्य क्षमामहे || १-१५-७_END
BEGIN_
"You have given boon to him appreciating his ascesis and oh, god, with high regard to that 
boon of yours we are tolerating all the cruel acts of Ravana from then onwards [1-15-7]_END

B_1_C_16_0
BEGIN_
ततो नारायणो विष्णुः नियुक्तः सुरसत्तमैः |
जानन्नपि सुरानेवं श्लक्ष्णं वचनमब्रवीत् || १-१६-१_END
BEGIN_
Later when the Omnipresent Narayana is thus nominated by best gods, and though he knows the 
outcome, he gently spoke these words to gods in this way. [1-16-1]_END

B_1_C_13_22
BEGIN_
वसिष्ठवाक्यं तच्छ्रुत्वा सुमंत्रस्त्वरितस्तदा |
व्यादिशत्पुरुषांस्तत्र राज्ञामानयने शुभान् || १-१३-३०_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that word of Vashishta, Sumantra expeditiously ordered devout envoys to invite 
all those kings to their kingdom. [1-13-30]_END

B_1_C_14_12
BEGIN_
वृद्धाश्च व्याधिताश्चैव स्त्रियो बालास्तथैव च |
अनिशं भुञ्जमानानां न तृप्तिरुपलभ्यते || १-१४-१३_END
BEGIN_
Elderly people, sick ones, women and children though dining on always thus, no satisfaction 
to complete the meal is attained for themselves, as the food served is that pleasant._END

B_1_C_15_7
BEGIN_
उद्वेजयति लोकांस्त्रीनुच्छ्रितान् द्वेष्टि दुर्मतिः |
शक्रं त्रिदशराजानं प्रधर्षयितुमिच्छति || १-१५-८_END
BEGIN_
"That malevolent Ravana is tormenting all the three worlds, hating the functionary deities 
of cosmos, and always desires to assail Indra, the king of all the functionary deities of 
universe. [1-15-8]_END

B_1_C_16_1
BEGIN_
उपायः को वधे तस्य राक्षसाधिपतेः सुराः |
यमहं तं समास्थाय निहन्यामृषिकण्टकम् || १-१६-२_END
BEGIN_
"What is the idea to eliminate that demon's chief Ravana, oh, gods, adopting which strategy 
I will have to eliminate that thorn in the side of sages?" Thus Vishnu asked the gods. [1-16-2]_END

B_1_C_13_23
BEGIN_
स्वयमेव हि धर्मात्मा प्रयातो मुनिशासनात् |
सुमंत्रस्त्वरितो भूत्वा समानेतुं महीक्षितः || १-१३-३१_END
BEGIN_
That virtuous Sumantra became brisk upon sage's words and personally journeyed to fetch all 
the rulers on the earth. [1-13-31]_END

B_1_C_14_13
BEGIN_
दीयतां दीयतामन्नं वासांसि विविधानि च |
इति संचोदितास्तत्र तथा चक्रुरनेकशः || १-१४-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Food be given abundantly, clothing be given variously" are the directives, accordingly the 
king's men have distributed numerously there at the ritual place. [1-14-14]_END

B_1_C_15_8
BEGIN_
ऋषीन् यक्षान् सगन्धर्वानसुरान् ब्राह्मणांस्तथा |
अतिक्रामति दुर्धर्षो वरदानेन मोहितः || १-१५-९_END
BEGIN_
"That invincible one is further self-conceited by the boons you have accorded, and he is overbearingly 
torturing the sages, celestial beings like yaksha-s, gandharva-s, asura-s, and like that even 
the Brahmans. [1-15-9]_END

B_1_C_16_2
BEGIN_
एवमुक्ताः सुराः सर्वे प्रत्यूचुर्विष्णुमव्ययम् |
मानुषं रूपमास्थाय रावणं जहि संयुगे || १-१६-३_END
BEGIN_
Asked thus all the gods said to that sempiternal Vishnu, "on assuming a human form, eliminate 
Ravana in a war." [1-16-3]_END

B_1_C_13_24
BEGIN_
ते च कर्मान्तिकाः सर्वे वसिष्ठाय महर्षये |
सर्वं निवेदयन्ति स्म यज्ञे यदुपकल्पितम् || १-१३-३२_END
BEGIN_
All those artisans engaged in ritual works have reported Vashishta, the details of all those 
ritual works that are accomplished. [1-13-32]_END

B_1_C_14_14
BEGIN_
अन्नकूटाश्च दृश्यन्ते बहवो पर्वतोपमाः |
दिवसे दिवसे तत्र सिद्धस्य विधिवत्तदा || १-१४-१५_END
BEGIN_
Heaps of foodstuffs are also appearing there, many of them and mountain similar, which is 
made available customarily, day after day. [1-14-15]_END

B_1_C_15_9
BEGIN_
नैनं सूर्यः प्रतपति पार्श्वे वाति न मारुतः |
चलोर्मिमाली तं दृष्ट्वा समुद्रोऽपि न कंपते || १-१५-१०_END
BEGIN_
"The Sun-god will not verily parch Ravana, the Air-god will not puff at his sides, and on 
seeing Ravana, the lord of the undulating waves, namely the ocean will not pulsate either. 
[1-15-10]_END

B_1_C_16_3
BEGIN_
स हि तेपे तपस्तीव्रं दीर्घकालमरिंदम |
येन तुष्टोऽभवद्ब्रह्मा लोककृल्लोकपूर्वजः || १-१६-४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, destroyer of enemies, he that Ravana undertook a vehement ascesis for a long period, 
thereby the creator of worlds and the first born one Brahma, felt gladsome of his ascesis. 
[1-16-4]_END

B_1_C_13_25
BEGIN_
ततः प्रीतो द्विजश्रेष्ठस्तान्सर्वान्मुनिरब्रवीत् |
अवज्ञया न दातव्यं कस्यचिल्लीलयापि वा || १-१३-३३
अवज्ञया कृतं हन्याद्दातारं नात्र संशयः |_END
BEGIN_
Then, that satisfied saint and eminent Brahman Vashishta, spoke this way to all of them, "nothing 
is to be endowed to anyone either with disrespect or deceptively, the deeds done with disrespect 
will kill the donor and there is no doubt about it." [1-13-33, 34a]_END

B_1_C_14_15
BEGIN_
नानादेशादनुप्राप्ताः पुरुषाः स्त्रीगणास्तथा |
अन्नपानैः सुविहितास्तस्मिन्यज्ञे महात्मनः || १-१४-१६_END
BEGIN_
To that ritual of that great-souled Dasharatha masses of men and women have arrived from different 
countries, and they are all well-pleased with the sumptuous food and drink supplied. [1-14-16]_END

B_1_C_15_10
BEGIN_
तन्महन्नो भयं तस्माद्राक्षसाद्घोरदर्शनात् |
वधार्थं तस्य भगवन्नुपायं कर्तुमर्हसि || १-१५-११_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, there is a great panic for all of us from that demon with an awesome look, hence 
oh, god, it will be apt of you to give a thought for his elimination. [1-15-11]_END

B_1_C_16_4
BEGIN_
सन्तुष्टः प्रददौ तस्मै राक्षसाय वरं प्रभुः |
नानाविधेभ्यो भूतेभ्यो भयं नान्यत्र मानुषात् || १-१६-५
अवज्ञाताः पुरा तेन वरदाने हि मानवाः |_END
BEGIN_
"Satisfied with his ascesis Brahma gave boon to that demon that he shall have no fear for 
his life from many kinds of beings, excepting humans, because that demon indeed slighted humans 
earlier at the time of bestowing boon. [1-16-5, 6a]_END

B_1_C_13_26
BEGIN_
ततः कैश्चिदहोरात्रैरुपयाता महीक्षितः || १-१३-३४
बहूनि रत्नान्यादाय राज्ञो दशरथस्य ह |_END
BEGIN_
Then in some days and nights many kings have arrived taking precious gems with them as gifts 
for Dasharatha. [1-13-34b, 35a]_END

B_1_C_14_16
BEGIN_
अन्नं हि विधिवत्स्वादु प्रशंसन्ति द्विजर्षभाः |
अहो तृप्ताः स्म भद्रं त इति शुश्राव राघवः || १-१४-१७_END
BEGIN_
"The eminent Brahmans have appreciated the food that is prepared by perfect cooking to be 
relishable, and it is heard as they said, "oh, Raghava, blessed are you for we are satisfied..." 
[1-14-17]_END

B_1_C_15_11
BEGIN_
एवमुक्तः सुरैः सर्वैः चिन्तयित्वा ततोऽब्रवीत् |
हन्तायं विदितस्तस्य वधोपायो दुरात्मनः || १-१५-१२_END
BEGIN_
When all the deities spoke to Brahma thus, he thought for a while and then said "Aha! The 
idea to kill that evil-minded Ravana is discerned. [1-15-12]_END

B_1_C_13_27
BEGIN_
ततो वसिष्ठः सुप्रीतो राजानमिदमब्रवीत् || १-१३-३५
उपयाता नरव्याघ्र राजानस्तव शासनात् |
मयापि सत्कृताः सर्वे यथार्हं राजसत्तमाः || १-१३-३६_END
BEGIN_
Then the well pleased Sage Vashishta said this to King Dasharatha "the kings from distant 
kingdoms have arrived at your behest, oh, tigerly-man, and these best kings are well honoured 
by me also as per their status. [1-13-35b, 36]_END

B_1_C_14_17
BEGIN_
स्वलंकृताश्च पुरुषा ब्राह्मणान्पर्यवेषयन् |
उपासते च तानन्ये सुमृष्टमणिकुण्डलाः || १-१४-१८_END
BEGIN_
Well-decorated men have served food to Brahmans, while others who wore gem-studded and lustrous 
earrings have helped them. [1-14-18]_END

B_1_C_16_5
BEGIN_
एवं पितामहात्तस्माद्वरदानेन गर्वितः || १-१६-६
उत्सादयति लोकांस्त्रीन् स्त्रियश्चाप्यपकर्षति |
तस्मात्तस्य वधो दृष्टो मानुषेभ्यः परन्तप || १-१६-७_END
BEGIN_
"Thus, on getting boon from the Forefather Brahma he has become arrogant and torturing the 
three worlds, and he is even abducting women. As such, oh, enemy destroyer Vishnu, his elimination 
is envisaged through humans alone." So said gods to Vishnu. [1-16-6b, 7]_END

B_1_C_15_12
BEGIN_
तेन गन्धर्वयक्षाणां देवतानां च रक्षसाम् |
अवध्योऽस्मीति वागुक्ता तथेक्तं च तन्मया || १-१५-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Ravana said while seeking boon that, 'I shall not be killed by gandharva-s, yaksha-s, or 
by gods, or by other demons...' and I also said 'so be it..." [1-15-13]_END

B_1_C_13_28
BEGIN_
यज्ञीयं च कृतं सर्वं पुरुषैः सुसमाहितैः |
निर्यातु च भवान्यष्टुं यज्ञायतनमन्तिकात् || १-१३-३७_END
BEGIN_
"All the ritual works are also completed by the well coalescent men, thus you may start towards 
the ritual place that is nearby, to perform your ritual." Said Sage Vashishta to King Dasharatha. 
[1-13-37]_END

B_1_C_14_18
BEGIN_
कर्मान्तरे तदा विप्रा हेतुवादान्बहूनपि |
प्राहुः स्म वाग्मिनो धीराः परस्परजिगीषया || १-१४-१९_END
BEGIN_
Those eminent Brahmans that are good debaters have debated many intellectual debates to defeat 
each other, during the gap-periods of ritual works. [1-14-19]_END

B_1_C_16_6
BEGIN_
इत्येतद्वचनं श्रुत्वा सुराणां विष्णुरात्मवान् |
पितरं रोचयामास तदा दशरथं नृपम् || १-१६-८_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that speech of gods said that way, he that kind-hearted Vishnu then chose Dasharatha 
as his father in human world. [1-16-8]_END

B_1_C_15_13
BEGIN_
नाकीर्तयदवज्ञानात्तद्रक्षो मानुषांस्तदा |
तस्मात् स मानुषाद्वध्यो मृत्युर्नान्योऽस्य विद्यते || १-१५-१४_END
BEGIN_
"That demon did not express about humans then with his disrespect to them, and evidently his 
death does not occur otherwise." So said Brahma to gods. [1-15-14]_END

B_1_C_13_29
BEGIN_
सर्वकामैरुपहृतैरुपेतं वै समन्ततः |
द्रष्टुमर्हसि राजेन्द्र मनसेव विनिर्मितम् || १-१३-३८_END
BEGIN_
"All the desirable paraphernalia is arranged and made available everywhere, and it is apt 
of you see ritual hall that is as though built by your mere wish. [1-13-38]_END

B_1_C_14_19
BEGIN_
दिवसे दिवसे तत्र संस्तरे कुशला द्विजाः |
सर्वकर्माणि चक्रुस्ते यथाशास्त्रं प्रचोदिताः || १-१४-२०_END
BEGIN_
Day by day those expert Brahmans have performed all ritual works as encouraged by Vashishta, 
and others and as contained in scriptures. [1-14-20]_END

B_1_C_16_7
BEGIN_
स चाप्यपुत्रो नृपतिस्तस्मिन् काले महाद्युतिः |
अयजत् पुत्रियामिष्टिं पुत्रेप्सुररिसूदनः ||१-१६-९_END
BEGIN_
During that time the great resplendent king and an enemy subduer Dasharatha is performing
putrakaameSTi ritual, desiring progeny as he is sonless. [1-16-9]_END

B_1_C_15_14
BEGIN_
एतच्छ्रुत्वा प्रियं वाक्यं ब्रह्मणा समुदाहृतम् |
देवा महर्षयः सर्वे प्रहृष्टास्तेऽभवंस्तदा ||१-१५-१५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Brahma explaining himself, then all those gods and great sages became adequately 
happy. [1-15-15]_END

B_1_C_13_30
BEGIN_
तथा वसिष्ठवचनादृष्यशृङ्गस्य चोभयोः |
शुभे दिवसनक्षत्रे निर्यातो जगतीपतिः || १-१३-३९_END
BEGIN_
Thus, on a good day while the ruling star of the day is favourable, King Dasharatha came forth 
towards the ritual hall according to the advice of both the sages Vashishta and Rishyasringa. 
[1-13-39]_END

B_1_C_14_20
BEGIN_
नाषडङ्गविदत्रासीत् नाव्रतो नाबहुश्रुतः |
सदस्यास्तस्य वै राज्ञो नावादकुशला द्विजाः || १-१४-२१_END
BEGIN_
There is no scholar without the knowledge of the six branches of Vedas, none who is an unavowed 
scholar, none who heard learnt less scriptures, and none among the members of the ritual of 
that king Dasharatha is an inexpert in debating, thus all are scholarly Brahmans. [1-14-21]_END

B_1_C_16_8
BEGIN_
स कृत्वा निश्चयं विष्णुरामन्त्र्य च पितामहम् |
अन्तर्धानं गतो देवैः पूज्यमानो महर्षिभिः || १-१६-१०_END
BEGIN_
On taking a decision Vishnu took leave of Forefather Brahma, and vanished while he is still 
being extolled by gods and sages. [1-16-10]_END

B_1_C_15_15
BEGIN_
एतस्मिन्नन्तरे विष्णुरुपयातो महाद्युतिः |
श्ङ्खचक्रगदापाणिः पीतवासा जगत्पतिः || १-११५-१६
वैनतेयं समारुह्य भास्करस्तोयदं यथा |
तप्तहाटककेयूरो वन्द्यमानः सुरोत्तमैः || १-१५-१७_END
BEGIN_
In the meanwhile the great resplendent Vishnu, the Lord of the Universe, arrived there mounted 
on his Eagle-vehicle Garuda, handling conch-shell, disc, and mace in his three of four hands, 
clad in yellow-ochre robes, wearing golden bracelets, and while best gods eulogised him, and 
his arrival there is like the arrival of sun mounted on black cloud to accord the gratuitous 
gift called the rain. [1-15-16, 17]_END

B_1_C_13_31
BEGIN_
ततो वसिष्ठप्रमुखाः सर्व एव द्विजोत्तमाः |
ऋष्यशृङ्गं पुरस्कृत्य यज्ञकर्मारभंस्तदा || १-१३-४०_END
BEGIN_
Then Sage Vashishta and other eminent Brahmans keeping the Sage Rishyasringa ahead of them 
entered the ritual hall, to commence the ritual works thus. [1-13-40]_END

B_1_C_14_21
BEGIN_
प्राप्ते यूपोच्छ्रये तस्मिन् षड्बैल्वाः खादिरास्तथा |
तावन्तो बिल्वसहिताः पर्णिनश्च तथापरे || १-१४-२२
श्लेष्मातकमयो दिष्टो देवदारुमयस्तथा |
द्वावेव तत्र विहितौ बाहुव्यस्तपरिग्रहौ || १-१४-२३_END
BEGIN_
When the time came to stake wooden ritual posts, six posts of bilwa wood, six posts of khadira 
wood, and further the same number of posts of parnina wood are staked. One post of sleshmaataka 
wood and two of devadaaru wood as stipulated are staked. Then the distance between each post 
is maintained at the length of extended arms. [1-14-22,23]_END

B_1_C_16_9
BEGIN_
ततो वै यजमानस्य  पावकादतुलप्रभम् |
प्रादुर्भूतं महद्भूतं महावीर्यं महाबलम् || १-१६-११_END
BEGIN_
Then, from Fire of Altar Dasharatha's ritual there emerged a greatly vigorous and energetic 
Divine Being with an unparalleled resplendence, called yajna-puruSa. 
[1-16-11]_END

B_1_C_15_16
BEGIN_
ब्रह्मणा च समागम्य तत्र तस्थौ समाहितः |
तमब्रुवन् सुराः सर्वे समभिष्टूय संनताः || १-१५-१८_END
BEGIN_
Vishnu having met Brahma stood there contemplating, and then all of the gods on bowing down 
and offering prayers addressed Vishnu. [1-15-18]_END

B_1_C_13_32
BEGIN_
यज्ञवाटं गताः सर्वे यथाशास्त्रं यथाविधि |
श्रीमांश्च सह पत्नीभी राजा दीक्षामुपाविशत् || १-१३-४१_END
BEGIN_
When all have entered the ritual hall as per canons and custom, that glorious king Dasharatha 
along with his wives undertook vow of ritual. [1-13-41]_END

B_1_C_16_10
BEGIN_
कृष्णं रक्ताम्बरधरं रक्तास्यं दुन्दुभिस्वनम् |
स्निग्धहर्यक्षतनुजश्मश्रुप्रवरमूर्धजम् || १-१६-१२_END
BEGIN_
He is clad in black and red garments and his face is red and his voice resembled the drumbeat. 
His moustache and hairdo are soft like that of a lion's mane. [1-16-12]_END

B_1_C_14_22
BEGIN_
कारिताः सर्व एवैते शास्त्रज्ञैर्यज्ञकोविदैः |
शोभार्थं तस्य यज्ञस्य कांचनालंकृताभवन् || १-१४-२४_END
BEGIN_
All of those the posts are made by the authorities on scriptures and ritual scholars, and 
they are gold-pleated and decorated for the purpose of elegance to that ritual. [1-14-24]_END

B_1_C_15_17
BEGIN_
त्वां नियोक्ष्यामहे विष्णो लोकानां हितकाम्यया |
राज्ञो दशरथस्य त्वमयोध्याधिपतेः विभोः || १-१५-१९
धर्मज्ञस्य वदान्यस्य महर्षिसमतेजसः |
अस्य भार्यासु तिसृषु ह्रीश्रीकीर्त्युपमासु च || १-१५-२०
विष्णो पुत्रत्वमागच्छ कृत्वात्मानं चतुर्विधम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh! Vishnu, desiring prosperity in all the worlds we nominate you to become the son of the 
ruler and lord of Ayodhya, namely Dasharatha, who is a virtuous one, renowned one and one 
whose resplendence equals that of the sages, and oh, Vishnu, through the wives of such a king 
Dasharatha, who are in similitude with the hrii, the virtue, shrii, the 
affluence, and kiirti, the glory, you have a fourfold transformation and take birth 
as their son. [1-15-19, 20, 21a]_END

B_1_C_16_11
BEGIN_
शुभलक्षणसंपन्नं दिव्याभरणभूषितम् |
शैलशृङ्गसमुत्सेधं दृप्तशार्दूलविक्रमम् || १-१६-१३_END
BEGIN_
And he is endowed with auspicious features and decorated with divine ornaments, in height 
he is like a mountain peak, and in valiance he is like an imperious tiger. [1-16-13]_END

B_1_C_14_23
BEGIN_
एकविंशतियूपास्ते एकविंशत्यरत्नयः |
वासोभिरेकविंशद्भिरेकैकं समलंकृताः || १-१४-२५_END
BEGIN_
They are altogether twenty-one posts, each post is twenty-one cubits in height, and each is 
decoratively clothed with each cloth. [1-14-25]_END

B_1_C_15_18
BEGIN_
तत्र त्वं मानुषो भूत्वा प्रवृद्धं लोककण्टकम् || १-१५-२१
अवध्यं दैवतैर्विष्णो समरे जहि रावणम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh! Vishnu, on your taking birth as human through the wives of Dasharatha you eliminate Ravana 
in war, who has become exacerbating and thorny to all worlds, and who is otherwise not eliminable 
for gods. [1-15-21b, 22a]_END

B_1_C_16_12
BEGIN_
दिवाकरसमाकारं दीप्तानलशिखोपमम् |
तप्तजाम्बूनदमयीं राजतान्तपरिच्छदाम् || १-१६-१४
दिव्यपायससंपूर्णां पात्रीं पत्नीमिव प्रियाम् |
प्रगृह्य विपुलां दोर्भ्यां स्वयं मायामयीमिव || १-१६-१५_END
BEGIN_
That great ritual being personally brought a big golden vessel carrying it with both of his 
hands as if he would personally handle his own wife, which vessel is made from the molten 
gold and covered with a silver lid, and which appeared to be crafted out of a divine illusion, 
since it is dazzling like sun and glowing like the tongues of flame, and that vessel is full 
with the divine dessert. [1-16-14, 15]_END

B_1_C_14_24
BEGIN_
विन्यस्ता विधिवत्सर्वे शिल्पिभिः सुकृता दृढाः |
अष्टाश्रयः सर्व एव श्लक्ष्णरूपसमन्विताः || १-१४-२६_END
BEGIN_
Carpenters have carved all the posts well, and built them strongly with octahedral surfaces 
that are smoothened, and thereby they are implanted procedurally. [1-14-26]_END

B_1_C_15_19
BEGIN_
स हि देवान् सगन्धर्वान् सिद्धांश्च ऋषिसत्तमान् || १-१५-२२
राक्षसो रावणो मूर्खो वीर्योद्रेकेण बाधते |_END
BEGIN_
"He that preposterous demon Ravana with his invigorated doggedness is torturing gods along 
with eminent saints, gandharva-s, and siddha-s. [1-15-22b, 23a]_END

B_1_C_16_13
BEGIN_
समवेक्ष्याब्रवीद्वाक्यमिदं दशरथं नृपम् |
प्राजापत्यं नरं विद्धि मामिहाभ्यागतं नृप || १-१६-१६_END
BEGIN_
That divine person on observing king Dasharatha said these words "oh, king, you may know me 
as the being sent by Prajapati." [1-16-16]_END

B_1_C_14_25
BEGIN_
आच्छादितास्ते वासोभिः पुष्पैर्गन्धैश्च पूजिताः |
सप्तर्षयो दीप्तिमन्तो विराजन्ते यथा दिवि || १-१४-२७_END
BEGIN_
Those posts draped in cloths and worshipped with flowers and perfumery are irradiant, and 
they shone forth like the constellation of Seven Sages in the sky. [1-14-27]_END

B_1_C_16_14
BEGIN_
ततः परं तदा राजा प्रत्युवाच कृताञ्जलिः |
भगवन् स्वागतं तेऽस्तु किमहं करवाणि ते || १-१६-१७_END
BEGIN_
There after, king Dasharatha greeted that divine being with palms adjoining and said in reply, 
"oh, god, welcome to you, and what shall I do for you?" [1-16-17]_END

B_1_C_15_20
BEGIN_
ऋषयश्च ततस्तेन गन्धर्वाप्सरसस्तथा || १-१५-२३
क्रीडन्तो नन्दनवने रौद्रेण विनिपातिताः |_END
BEGIN_
"He that furious one with his insolence is knocking down sages from their celestial abodes, 
and like that he is knocking down the gandharva-s and apsara celestials too from the heavenly 
gardens Nandana, where they will be taking delight. [1-15-23b, 24a]_END

B_1_C_14_26
BEGIN_
इष्टकाश्च यथान्यायं कारिताश्च प्रमाणतः |
चितोऽग्निर्ब्राह्मणैस्तत्र कुशलैः शिल्पकर्मणि || १-१४-२८_END
BEGIN_
The bricks for Altar of Fire are well designed and made according to rules and standard measurements. 
The Brahmans who are experts in the architecture of laying Fire Altar, by calculating the 
ritual field with a one-ply rope and decide where and how the that shall be, the Altar of 
Fire is layered well with bricks in that ritual. [1-14-28]_END

B_1_C_16_15
BEGIN_
अथो पुनरिदं वाक्यं प्राजापत्यो नरोऽब्रवीत् |
राजन्नर्चयता देवानद्य प्राप्तमिदं त्वया || १-१६-१८_END
BEGIN_
Then again, that divine being sent by Prajapati said these words, "oh, king, now you have 
obtained this dessert in golden vessel as you have propitiated gods. [1-16-18]_END

B_1_C_14_27
BEGIN_
स चित्यो राजसिंहस्य संचितः कुशलैर्द्विजैः |
गरुडो रुक्मपक्षो वै त्रिगुणोऽष्टादशात्मकः || १-१४-२९_END
BEGIN_
That Altar of Fire of that King, the Lion, is layered by expert Brahmans in the shape of an 
eagle with golden wings, with its size being three folds bigger than the altars of other rituals, 
thus it has eighteen separators, and fire is laid on it. [1-14-29]_END

B_1_C_15_21
BEGIN_
वधार्थं वयमायातास्तस्य वै मुनिभिः सह || १-१५-२४
सिद्धगन्धर्वयक्षाश्च ततस्त्वां शरणं गताः |_END
BEGIN_
"We the celestial beings like siddha-s, gandharva-s, yaksha-s along with sages have actually 
come for his elimination, and thereby we seek shelter in you. [1-15-24b, 25a]_END

B_1_C_14_28
BEGIN_
नियुक्तास्तत्र पशवस्तत्तदुद्दिश्य दैवतम् |
उरगाः पक्षिणश्चैव यथाशास्त्रं प्रचोदिताः || १-१४-३०_END
BEGIN_
In that ritual animals, serpents and birds designated to such and such deities are readied 
according to the scriptural directives. [1-14-30]_END

B_1_C_16_16
BEGIN_
इदं तु नृपशार्दूल पायसं देवनिर्मितम् |
प्रजाकरं गृहाण त्वं धन्यमारोग्य वर्धनम् || १-१६-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, tigerly king, take this dessert prepared by divinities, this is a blessed dessert that 
enriches progeny and health. [1-16-19]_END

B_1_C_15_22
BEGIN_
त्वं गतिः परमा देव सर्वेषां नः परंतप || १-१५-२५
वधाय देवशतॄणां नृणां लोके मनः कुरु |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, enemy tormentor, oh, Vishnu, you are the ultimate recourse for all us in eliminating 
enemies of divinity, hence you make up your mind to take birth in human world." The gods appealed 
to Vishnu that way. [1-15-25b, 26a]_END

B_1_C_14_29
BEGIN_
शामित्रे तु हयस्तत्र तथा जलचराश्च ये |
ऋषिभिः सर्वमेवैतन्नियुक्तं शास्त्रतस्तदा || १-१४-३१_END
BEGIN_
The sages have arranged those animals that are to be there in animal sacrifices, like horse 
and other aquatic animals, in that ritual according to scriptures. [1-14-31]_END

B_1_C_16_17
BEGIN_
भार्याणामनुरूपाणामश्नीतेति प्रयच्छ वै |
तासु त्वं लप्स्यसे पुत्रान् यदर्थं यजसे नृप || १-१६-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, king, let this be consumed" saying so he further said, "for which purpose you have performed 
this ritual that childbearing will be fructified in your wives by bearing sons, hence give 
this among your eligible wives." So said the divine being to Dasharatha. [1-16-20]_END

B_1_C_15_23
BEGIN_
एवं स्तुतस्तु देवेशो विष्णुस्त्रिदशपुंगवः || १-१५-२६
पितामहपुरोगांस्तान् सर्वलोकनमस्कृतः
अब्रवीत् त्रिदशान् सर्वान् समेतान् धर्मसंहितान् || १-१५-२७_END
BEGIN_
When the god of gods Vishnu, the supreme one among deities, one who is revered by all worlds 
is eulogised this way, then he spoke to all of those celestials that abide in the righteousness 
and that are in the assemblage, keeping the Forefather Brahma at their helm. [1-15-26a, 27]_END

B_1_C_14_30
BEGIN_
पशूनां त्रिशतं तत्र यूपेषु नियतं तदा |
अश्वरत्नोत्तमं तस्य राज्ञो दशरथस्य च || १-१४-३२_END
BEGIN_
Three hundred animals are tied to the ritual posts, along with the gemlike best ritual horse 
of that King Dasharatha. [1-14-32]_END

B_1_C_15_24
BEGIN_
भयं त्यजत भद्रं वो हितार्थं युधि रावणम् | 
सपुत्रपौत्रं सामात्यं समित्रज्ञातिबान्धवम् || १-१५-२८
हत्वा क्रूरं दुराधर्षं देवर्षीणां भयावहम् |
दश वर्ष सहस्राणि दश वर्ष शतानि च || १-१५-२९
वत्स्यामि मानुषे लोके पालयन् पृथिवीमिमाम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Get rid off the fear, let safety be upon you, on eliminating that cruel and evil-minded Ravana 
who became dreadful to deities and sages, along with his sons, grandsons, friends, cousins 
and relatives, ministers and forces too in war for your welfare, I will then reside in human 
world ruling this earth for eleven thousand years." Thus Vishnu assured the gods. [1-15-28, 
29, 30a]_END

B_1_C_16_18
BEGIN_
तथेति नृपतिः प्रीतः शिरसा प्रतिगृह्य ताम् |
पात्रीं देवान्नसंपूर्णां देवदत्तां हिरण्मयीम् || १-१६-२१_END
BEGIN_
Agreeing to that the king wholeheartedly took that god-given golden vessel full with divine 
food. [1-16-21]_END

B_1_C_14_31
BEGIN_
कौसल्या तं हयं तत्र परिचर्य समंततः |
कृपाणैर्विशशासैनं त्रिभिः परमया मुदा || १-१४-३३_END
BEGIN_
With great delight coming on her Queen Kausalya reverently made circumambulations to the horse, 
and symbolically killed the horse with three knives. [1-14-33]_END

B_1_C_15_25
BEGIN_
एवं दत्वा वरं देवो देवानां विष्णुरात्मवान् || १-१५-३०
मानुषे चिन्तयामास जन्मभूमिमथात्मनः |_END
BEGIN_
On giving boon to all gods in that way the kind-hearted god Vishnu started to think about 
the instituting base for his birth in human world. [1-15-30b, 31a]_END

B_1_C_16_19
BEGIN_
अभिवाद्य च तद् भूतमद्भुतं प्रियदर्शनम् |
मुदा परमया युक्तश्चकाराभिप्रदक्षिणम् || १-१६-२२_END
BEGIN_
With high ecstasy Dasharatha revered that Ritual Being, the Prajaapati- 
PuruSha or yaj~na-puruSha , an astonishing and delightful 
being in his appearance, and performed circumambulations around him. [1-16-22]_END

B_1_C_14_32
BEGIN_
पतत्रिणा तदा सार्धं सुस्थितेन च चेतसा |
अवसद्रजनीमेकां कौसल्या धर्मकाम्यया || १-१४-३४_END
BEGIN_
Queen Kausalya desiring the results of ritual disconcertedly resided one night with that horse 
that flew away like a bird. [1-14-34]_END

B_1_C_16_20
BEGIN_
ततो दशरथः प्राप्य पायसं देवनिर्मितम् |
बभूव परमप्रीतः प्राप्य वित्तमिवाधनः || १-१६-२३_END


B_1_C_15_26
BEGIN_
ततः पद्मपलाशाक्षः कृत्वात्मानं चतुर्विधम् || १-१५-३१
पितरं रोचयामास तदा दशरथं नृपम् |_END
BEGIN_
And then that lotus-petal-eyed one agreeing to manifest himself in fourfold way is predisposed 
towards Dasharatha to be his father. [1-15-31b, 32a]_END

B_1_C_14_33
BEGIN_
होताध्वर्युस्तथोद्गाता हस्तेन समयोजयन् |
महिष्या परिवृत्त्या च वावातामपरां तथा || १-१४-३५_END
BEGIN_
Thus, the officiating priests of the ritual, namely hotaa adhwaryu and udgaataa 
have received in their hand the Crowned Queen, the neglected wife, and a concubine of the 
king, next as a symbolic donation in the ritual by the performer, the king. [1-14-35]_END

B_1_C_15_27
BEGIN_
तदा देवर्षिगन्धर्वाः सरुद्राः साप्सरो गणाः |
स्तुतिभिर्दिव्यरूपाभिस्तुष्टुवुर्मधुसूदनम् || १-१५-३२_END
BEGIN_
Then all the groups of gods, sages, gandharva-s, with rudraa-s, and apsarasa-s, extolled Vishnu 
with prayers of divine exposition. [1-15-32b, c]_END

B_1_C_16_21
BEGIN_
ततस्तदद्भुतप्रख्यं भूतं परमभास्वरम् |
संवर्तयित्वा तत्कर्म तत्रैवान्तरधीयत || १-१६-२४_END
BEGIN_
On completing his work of giving the golden vessel with dessert then that divine being who 
is astonishing by his form and highly glowing by his physique, disappeared then and there 
itself. [1-16-24]_END

B_1_C_14_34
BEGIN_
पतत्रिणस्तस्य वपामुद्धृत्य नियतेन्द्रियः |
ऋत्विक् परमसंपन्नः श्रपयामास शास्त्रतः || १-१४-३६_END
BEGIN_
Then the priest, one with controlled senses and rich in scriptural wealth, took up the omentum 
[fat] of the horse and cooked it as per scriptures while dropping into the altar of fire to 
bake as a food to the celestials. [1-14-36]_END

B_1_C_15_28
BEGIN_
तमुद्धतं रावणमुग्रतेजसम्
प्रवृद्धदर्पं त्रिदशेश्वरद्विषम् |
विरावणं साधुतपस्विकण्टकम्
तपस्विनामुद्धर तं भयावहम् || १-१५-३३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh! Vishnu, he that fiery one who is renowned for evil acts and who is the hater of Indra, 
that Ravana is uprising furiously with his heightened arrogance, and he has become a thorn in the 
side of hermits hence he is a fright to sages, afor he tortures insubordinates to the the extent of 
loud wailing; hence we pray you to eliminate that Ravana." [1-15-33]_END

B_1_C_16_22
BEGIN_
हर्षरश्मिभिरुद्द्योतं तस्यान्तःपुरमाबभौ |
शारदस्याभिरामस्य चंद्रस्येव नभोंशुभिः || १-१६-२५_END
BEGIN_
Lit up with beams of happiness Dasharatha's palace chambers shone forth like the autumnal 
sky brightened with moonbeams. [1-16-25]_END

B_1_C_17_0
BEGIN_
			पुत्रत्वं तु गते विष्णौ राज्ञस्तस्य महात्मनः |
			उवाच देवताः सर्वाः स्वयंभूर्भगवानिदम् || १-१७-१_END
BEGIN_
			When Vishnu attained the sonship of the great-souled king Dasharatha, then Brahma 
			the self-created addressed all of the gods this way. [1-17-1]_END

B_1_C_14_35
BEGIN_
धूमगन्धं वपायास्तु जिघ्रति स्म नराधिपः |
यथाकालं यथान्यायं निर्णुदन् पापमात्मनः || १-१४-३७_END
BEGIN_
The king Dasharatha smelt the smell of smoke as per time and procedure to cleanse his own 
sin. [1-14-37]_END

B_1_C_15_29
BEGIN_
तमेव हत्वा सबलं सबान्धवम्
विरावणं रावणमुग्रपौरुषम् |
स्वर्लोकमागच्छ गतज्वरश्चिरम्
सुरेन्द्रगुप्तं गतदोषकल्मषम् || १-१५-३४_END


B_1_C_16_23
BEGIN_
सोऽन्तःपुरं प्रविश्यैव कौसल्यामिदमब्रवीत् |
पायसं प्रतिगृह्णीष्व पुत्रीयमिदमात्मनः || १-१६-२६_END
BEGIN_
Then Dasharatha on entering palace chambers spoke this to queen Kausalya, "Receive this dessert 
to beget your son." [1-16-26]_END

B_1_C_17_1
BEGIN_
			सत्यसंधस्य वीरस्य सर्वेषां नो हितैषिणः |
			विष्णोः सहायान् बलिनः सृजध्वं कामरूपिणः || १-१७-२_END
BEGIN_
			"Let mighty and guise changing helpmates be procreated to that truth abiding and 
			valorous Vishnu who is the well-wisher of all of us. [1-17-2]_END

B_1_C_14_36
BEGIN_
हयस्य यानि चांगानि तानि सर्वाणि ब्राह्मणाः |
अग्नौ प्रास्यन्ति विधिवत् समस्ताः षोडशर्त्विजः || १-१४-३८_END
BEGIN_
Those remaining body parts that horse are there, the sixteen officiating priests have procedurally 
oblated all of them into fire. [1-14-38]_END

B_1_C_15_30

BEGIN_
"On eliminating that furiously vainglorious Ravana with all his forces and with all his kinsmen 
neutralise the pandemonium created by him in all the worlds, and for a long time to come you 
get rid of your febrility, and you please return to your heavenly abode, namely your blameless 
and faultless Vaikuntha. [1-15-34]_END

B_1_C_16_24
BEGIN_
कौसल्यायै नरपतिः पायसार्धं ददौ तदा |
अर्धादर्धं ददौ चापि सुमित्रायै नराधिपः || १-१६-२७
कैकेय्यै चावशिष्टार्धं ददौ पुत्रार्थकारणात् |
प्रददौ चावशिष्टार्धं पायसस्यामृतोपमम् || १-१६-२८
अनुचिन्त्य सुमित्रायै पुनरेव महीपतिः |
एवं तासां ददौ राजा भार्याणां पायसं पृथक् || १-१६-२९_END
BEGIN_
The king then gave half of the dessert to queen Kausalya, and he gave half of the half, i.e., 
one fourth to queen Sumitra. And to Kaikeyi he gave half of the remaining half, i.e., one 
eight of the dessert, with a desire to beget sons. Then thinking for a while gave the remaining, 
i.e., one-eighth portion again to queen Sumitra. Thus, the king distributed the dessert to 
his wives differently. [1-16-27, 28, 29]_END

B_1_C_17_2
BEGIN_
			मायाविदश्च शूरांश्च वायुवेगसमान् जवे |
			नयज्ञान् बुद्धिसंपन्नान् विष्णुतुल्यपराक्रमान् || १-१७-३
			असंहार्यानुपायज्ञान् दिव्यसंहननान्वितान् |

			सर्वास्त्रगुणसंपन्नानमृतप्राशनानिव || १-१७-४
			अप्सरस्सु च मुख्यासु गन्धर्वीणां तनूषु च |
			यक्षपन्नगकन्यासु ऋक्षविद्याधरीषु च || १-१७-५
			किंनरीणां च गात्रेषु वानरीणां तनूषु च |
			सृजध्वं हरिरूपेण पुत्रांस्तुल्यपराक्रमान् || १-१७-६_END
BEGIN_
			"Let monkey-shaped progeny equalling Vishnu's valour be procreated from the physiques 
			of prominent apsara-s and gandharva-s, from the girls of yaksha-s and pannaga-s, 
			and also thus from the bodies of kinnaraa-s, she-vidyaadharaa-s, she-riksha-s 
			and she-monkeys, and they shall be wizards of miracles and audacious ones, in 
			travel they shall have air's speed, bestowed with intellect they shall be the 
			knowers of ideation, and with their divine physique they shall be ineliminable, 
			they shall be endowed with all the assaultive aspects of all missiles, and they 
			shall be untiring in their efforts, like you who thrive on amrita, the ambrosia, 
			unmindful of thirst and hunger. [1-17-3, 4, 5, 6]_END

B_1_C_14_37
BEGIN_
प्लक्षशाखासु यज्ञानामन्येषां क्रियते हविः |
अश्वमेधस्य यज्ञस्य वैतसो भाग इष्यते || १-१४-३९_END
BEGIN_
In other rituals the oblations will be offered into sacrificial fire with spoon-like sticks 
of plaksha tree, but in Horse-sacrifice ritual they are offered through the vetasa creeper, 
a rattan plant, cane. [1-14-39]_END

B_1_C_16_25
BEGIN_
ताश्चैवं पायसं प्राप्य नरेन्द्रस्योत्तमाः स्त्रियः |
सम्मानं मेनिरे सर्वाः प्रहर्षोदितचेतसः || १-१६-३०_END
BEGIN_
On getting the dessert all of those best ladies of the king, whose hearts are exuberant with 
happiness, deemed it as a reward. [1-16-30]_END

B_1_C_17_3
BEGIN_
			पूर्वमेव मया सृष्टो जांबवानृक्षपुङ्गवः |
			जृंभमाणस्य सहसा मम वक्रादजायत || १-१७-७_END
BEGIN_
			"I have already created the eminent bear Jambavanta in earlier times, as he suddenly 
			came forth from my yawning face. [1-17-7]_END

B_1_C_14_38
BEGIN_
त्र्यहोऽश्वमेधः संख्यातः कल्पसूत्रेण ब्राह्मणैः |
चतुष्टोममहस्तस्य प्रथमं परिकल्पितम् || १-१४-४०_END
BEGIN_
The Horse Ritual is to be performed for three days as laid down in kalpasutra-s, 
the rules governing such rituals, and by braahmaNa-s, the penultimate parts of Veda-s, 
and the one performed on the first day is called chatuSToma ritual. [1-14-40]_END

B_1_C_16_26
BEGIN_
ततस्तु ताः प्राश्य तदुत्तमस्त्रियो
महीपतेरुत्तमपायसं पृथक् |
हुताशनादित्यसमानतेजसोऽ-
चिरेण गर्भान् प्रतिपेदिरे तदा || १-१६-३१_END
BEGIN_
Then on consuming dessert those best ladies of the king whose resplendence then vied with 
that Fire and Sun became pregnant after some time. [1-16-31]_END

B_1_C_17_4
BEGIN_
			ते तथोक्ता भगवता तत् प्रतिश्रुत्य शासनम् |
			जनयामासुरेवं ते पुत्रान् वानररूपिणः || १-१७-८_END
BEGIN_
			When Brahma addressed them thus, those gods have agreed to his order and accordingly 
			started to parent sons in the resemblance of monkeys. [1-17-8]_END

B_1_C_14_39
BEGIN_
उक्थ्यं द्वितीयं संख्यातमतिरात्रं तथोत्तरम् |
कारितास्तत्र बहवो विहिताः शास्त्रदर्शनात् || १-१४-४१_END
BEGIN_
The ritual on the second day is called ukthyam , and the next one performed on third 
day is called atiraatra. These apart many of the preordained rituals are performed 
there in that ritual as envisaged in scriptures. [1-14-41]_END

B_1_C_16_27
BEGIN_
ततस्तु राजा प्रतिवीक्ष्य ताः स्त्रियः
प्ररूढगर्भाः प्रतिलब्धमानसः |
बभूव हृष्टस्त्रिदिवे यथा हरिः
सुरेन्द्रसिद्धर्षिगणाभिपूजितः || १-१६-३२_END
BEGIN_
Then on seeing his queens with confirmed pregnancies Dasharatha regained his lost heart for 
sons, and he is gladdened like Vishnu, who will always be gladsome when worshipped by gods, 
namely Indra and others, as well as by the assemblages of great souls, sages. [1-16-32]_END

B_1_C_17_5
BEGIN_
			ऋषयश्च महात्मानः सिद्धविद्याधरोरगाः |
			चारणाश्च सुतान् वीरान् ससृजुर्वनचारिणः || १-१७-९_END
BEGIN_
			The great-souled celestial groups, namely the sages, siddha-s, vidyaadharaa-s, 
			caarana-s have created valiant sons that are forest rangers. [1-17-9]_END

B_1_C_14_40
BEGIN_
ज्योतिष्टोमायुषी चैवमतिरात्रौ विनिर्मितौ |
अभिजिद्विश्वजिच्चैवमप्तोर्यामो महाक्रतुः || १-१४-४२_END
BEGIN_
The rituals called jyothiSToma, aayuSi, and atiraatra rituals are performed. 
And also rituals of great kind like abhijit, vishwajit, aptoryaama are performed. 
[1-14-42]_END

B_1_C_17_6
BEGIN_
			वानरेन्द्रं महेद्राभमिन्द्रो वालिनमात्मजम् |
			सुग्रीवं जनयामास तपनस्तपतां वरः || १-१७-१०_END
BEGIN_
			Indra procreated the lord of vanara-s, namely Vali, who by his physique is like 
			Mt. Mahendra, and the highest humidifier among all the humidifiers, namely the 
			Sun, procreated Sugreeva. [1-17-10]_END

B_1_C_14_41
BEGIN_
प्राचीं होत्रे ददौ राजा दिशं स्वकुलवर्धनः
अध्वर्यवे प्रतीचीं तु ब्रह्मणे दक्षिणां दिशम् || १-१४-४३
उद्गात्रे च ततोदीचीं दक्षिणैषा विनिर्मिता |
अश्वमेधे महायज्ञे स्वयंभुविहिते पुरा || १-१४-४४_END
BEGIN_
As the promoter of his own dynasty that king Dasharatha donated eastern side to hotaa, 
western to adhvaryu, and southern to brahmaa. And to udgaataa northern 
side is given in donation. These were the donations stipulated in that great ritual, ashwamedha, 
by the Self-Created Brahma from earlier times. [1-14-44,43]_END

B_1_C_18_0
BEGIN_
निर्वृत्ते तु क्रतौ तस्मिन् हयमेधे महात्मनः |
प्रतिगृह्य सुरा भागान् प्रतिजग्मुर्यथागतम् || १-१८-१_END
BEGIN_
On the competition of the horse ritual of high-souled Dasharatha, the golds having received 
their portion of sacrificial oblation returned to their abodes as they have come. [1-18-1]_END

B_1_C_17_7
BEGIN_
			बृहस्पतिस्त्वजनयत्तारं नाम महाकपिम् |
			सर्ववानरमुख्यानां बुद्धिमन्तमनुत्तमम् || १-१७-११_END
BEGIN_
			Brihaspati, the Jupiter, gave rise to a great monkey named Tara, who is the most 
			important one among all vanara-s, and who excels all by his intelligence. [1-17-11]_END

B_1_C_14_42
BEGIN_
क्रतुं समाप्य तु तदा न्यायतः पुरुषर्षभः |
ऋत्विग्भ्यो हि ददौ राजा धरां तां कुलवर्धनः || १-१४-४५_END
BEGIN_
On completing the ritual thus that best man Dasharatha justifiably donated those lands to 
the officiating priests, called ritwiks, to promote his dynasty. [1-14-45]_END

B_1_C_18_1
BEGIN_
समाप्तदीक्षानियमः पत्नीगणसमन्वितः |
प्रविवेश पुरीं राजा सभृत्यबलवाहनः || १-१८-२_END
BEGIN_
The king completing his consecratory vows held for horse ritual, entered Ayodhya city along 
with the company of his queens, servants, guards and vehicles. [1-18-2]_END

B_1_C_17_8
BEGIN_
			धनदस्य सुतः श्रीमान् वानरो गन्धमादनः |
			विश्वकर्मा त्वजनयन्नलं नाम महाकपिम् || १-१७-१२_END
BEGIN_
			The brilliant Gandhamaadana is the son of Kubera, while the divine architect Vishvakarma 
			procreated the great monkey called Nala. [1-17-12]_END

B_1_C_14_43
BEGIN_
एवं दत्त्वा प्रहृष्टोऽभूत् श्रीमानिक्ष्वाकुनन्दनः |
ऋत्विजस्त्वब्रुवन् सर्वे राजानं गतकिल्बिषम् || १-१४-४६_END
BEGIN_
Thus on giving away the vast expanses of his kingdom he that glorious one born in Ikshvaku 
dynasty is gladdened, but all the officiating priests said to the king who by now is rid of 
his sins. [1-14-46]_END

B_1_C_18_2
BEGIN_
यथार्हं पूजितास्तेन राज्ञा च पृथिवीश्वराः |
मुदिताः प्रययुर्देशान् प्रणम्य मुनिपुंगवम् || १-१८-३_END
BEGIN_
The other kings who arrived for the ritual are delighted when befittingly honoured by the 
king Dasharatha, and they too returned to their countries, after suitably adoring the eminent 
sage Vashishta. [1-18-3]_END

B_1_C_17_9
BEGIN_
			पावकस्य सुतः श्रीमान्नीलोऽग्नि सदृशप्रभः |
			तेजसा यशसा वीर्यादत्यरिच्यत वानरान् || १-१७-१३_END
BEGIN_
			The bright son of Fire is Neela whose blaze is like that of fire and who excels 
			other monkeys by his resplendence, renown and courage. [1-17-13]_END

B_1_C_14_44
BEGIN_
भवानेव महीं कृत्स्नामेको रक्षितुमर्हति |
न भूम्या कार्यमस्माकं न हि शक्ताः स्म पालने || १-१४-४७_END
BEGIN_
"You alone are capable to protect the earth in its entirety, and there is no use for us with 
these lands, and we are not capable to rule it, either." Thus the priests are addressing the 
king. [1-14-47]_END

B_1_C_18_3
BEGIN_
श्रीमतां गच्छतां तेषां स्वगृहाणि पुरात्ततः |
बलानि राज्ञां शुभ्राणि प्रहृष्टानि चकाशिरे || १-१८-४_END
BEGIN_
The entourages of those kings who set forth homeward from that city are highly gladdened and 
shone forth in fine fettle. [1-18-4]_END

B_1_C_17_10
BEGIN_
			रूपद्रविणसंपन्नावश्विनौ रूपसंमतौ |
			मैन्दं च द्विविदं चैव जनयामासतुः स्वयम् || १-१७-१४_END
BEGIN_
			The Ashwin twin gods whose wealth is their beautiful appearance have personally 
			procreated two vanara-s namely Mainda and Dvivida, blessing them with beautiful 
			appearance.[1-17-14]_END

B_1_C_14_45
BEGIN_
रताः स्वाध्यायकरणे वयं नित्यं हि भूमिप |
निष्क्रयं किंचिदेवेह प्रयच्छतु भवानिति || १-१४-४८_END
BEGIN_
"We are always preoccupied with self-study and teaching of scriptures, oh, king, thus you 
may give us something else in barter, any modest thing. " [1-14-48]_END

B_1_C_18_4
BEGIN_
गतेषु पृथिवीशेषु राजा दशरथस्तदा |
प्रविवेश पुरीं श्रीमान् पुरस्कृत्य द्विजोत्तमान् || १-१८-५_END
BEGIN_
On the departure of visiting kings, then that fortunate king Dasharatha entered the city Ayodhya, 
keeping eminent Brahman priests ahead of him in the procession. [1-18-5]_END

B_1_C_17_11
BEGIN_
			वरुणो जनयामास सुषेणं नाम वानरम् |
			शरभं जनयामास पर्जन्यस्तु महाबलम् || १-१७-१५_END
BEGIN_
			The Rain-god procreated the vanara named Sushena, and Thunder-god gave rise 
			to the great mighty Sharabha. [1-17-15]_END

B_1_C_14_46
BEGIN_
मणिरत्नं सुवर्णं वा गावो यद्वा समुद्यतम् |
तत्प्रयच्छ नरश्रेष्ठ धरण्या न प्रयोजनम् || १-१४-४९_END
BEGIN_
"Let best gems, gold, or cows or anything else that is available you may give us, what is 
the use of these vast expanses to us." So said the scholars. [1-14-49]_END

B_1_C_17_12
BEGIN_
			मारुतस्यौरसः श्रीमान् हनुमान्नाम वानरः |
			वज्रसंहननोपेतो वैनतेयसमो जवे || १-१७-१६
			सर्ववानरमुख्येषु बुद्धिमान् बलवानपि |_END
BEGIN_
			The direct son of Air-god is the marvellous and adventurous Hanuma with an indestructible 
			body, and one identical in the speed of lady Vinata's son, namely Garuda, the 
			divine eagle vehicle of Vishnu, and among all monkey chiefs he is the intelligent 
			and the indefatigable one too. [1-17-16, 17a]_END

B_1_C_18_5
BEGIN_
शांतया प्रययौ सार्धमृष्यशृङ्गः सुपूजितः |
अनुगम्यमानो राज्ञा च सानुयात्रेण धीमता || १-१८-६_END
BEGIN_
Well adored by king Dasharatha sage Rishyasringa also travelled along with his wife Shanta, 
followed by his father-in-law King Romapada, and along with other co-travellers, namely the 
entourage of Romapada. [1-18-6]_END

B_1_C_17_13
BEGIN_
			ते सृष्टा बहुसाहस्रा दशग्रीववधोद्यताः || १-१७-१७
			अप्रमेयबला वीरा विक्रान्ताः कामरूपिणः |_END
BEGIN_
			Thus the gods have procreated many thousands of such valorous and guise changing 
			monkeys who with their immeasurable strength and bravery are manifest for the 
			elimination of the decahedral demon Ravana. [1-17-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_18_6
BEGIN_
एवं विसृज्य तान् सर्वान् राजा संपूर्णमानसः |
उवास सुखितस्तत्र पुत्रोत्पत्तिं विचिंतयन् || १-१८-७_END
BEGIN_
On dispersing all of them king Dasharatha gratifyingly dwelled there in Ayodhya, with a satiated 
heart dwelling upon the birth of his sons. [1-18-7]_END

B_1_C_14_47
BEGIN_
एवमुक्तो नरपतिर्ब्राह्मणैर्वेदपारगैः |
गवां शतसहस्राणि दश तेभ्यो ददौ नृपः || १-१४-५०
दशकोटीः सुवर्णस्य रजतस्य चतुर्गुणम् |_END
BEGIN_
The king Dasharatha, the lord of people, thus requested by the scholarly Vedic Brahmans gave 
them millions of cows, ten of ten million gold coins, and the silver four times thereof. [1-14-50, 
51a]_END

B_1_C_19_0
BEGIN_
			तच्छ्रुत्वा राजसिंहस्य वाक्यमद्भुतविस्तरम् |
			हृष्टरोमा महातेजा विश्वामित्रोऽभ्यभाषत || १-१९-१_END
BEGIN_
			On listening the grand and detailed sentences of that King the lion Dasharatha, 
			the great resplendent Sage Vishvamitra is thrilled with happiness and spoke this 
			way. [1-19-1]_END

B_1_C_17_14
BEGIN_
			ते गजाचलसंकाशा वपुष्मंतो महाबलाः || १-१७-१८
			ऋक्षवानरगोपुच्छाः क्षिप्रमेवाभिजज्ञिरे |_END
BEGIN_
			And they with their elephantine, mountainous and prodigious bodies quickly took 
			birth in bears, monkeys, sacred langoors. [1-17-18b, 19a]_END

B_1_C_18_7
BEGIN_
ततो यज्ञे समाप्ते तु ऋतूनां षट् समत्ययुः |
ततश्च द्वादशे मासे चैत्रे नावमिके तिथौ || १-१८-८
नक्षत्रेऽदितिदैवत्ये स्वोच्चसंस्थेषु पंचसु |
ग्रहेषु कर्कटे लग्ने वाक्पताविंदुना सह || १-१८-९
प्रोद्यमाने जगन्नाथं सर्वलोकनमस्कृतम् |
कौसल्याजनयद्रामं सर्वलक्षणसंयुतम् || १-१८-१०
विष्णोरर्धं महाभागं पुत्रमैक्ष्वाकुनंदनम् |
लोहिताक्षं महाबाहुं रक्तौष्ठं दुंदुभिस्वनम् || १-१८-११_END


B_1_C_14_48
BEGIN_
ऋत्विजश्च ततः सर्वे प्रददुः सहिता वसु || १-१४-५१
ऋष्यशृङ्गाय मुनये वसिष्ठाय च धीमते |_END
BEGIN_
Then all those officiating priests collectively gave that wealth to sage Rishyasringa and 
to the enlightened sage Vashishta. [1-14-51b, 52a]_END

B_1_C_19_1
BEGIN_
			सदृशं राजशार्दूल तवैतद्भुवि नान्यथा |
			महावंशप्रसूतस्य वसिष्ठव्यपदेशिनः || १-१९-२_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, tigerly king, to you befitting are these words and to none else, as you are 
			born in a great dynasty and tutored by Vashishta. [1-19-2]_END

B_1_C_17_15
BEGIN_
			यस्य देवस्य यद्रूपं वेषो यश्च पराक्रमः || १-१७-१९
			अजायत समं तेन तस्य तस्य पृथक् पृथक् |_END
BEGIN_
			Those that are procreated have attained the shape, getup and valour of the god 
			that has fathered them, and thus the monkey race is procreated separately and 
			individually. [1-17-19b, 20a]_END

B_1_C_18_8



B_1_C_14_49
BEGIN_
ततस्ते न्यायतः कृत्वा प्रविभागं द्विजोत्तमाः || १-१४-५२
सुप्रीतमनसः सर्वे प्रत्यूचुर्मुदिता भृशम् |_END
BEGIN_
Then all of those Brahmans are well satisfied at heart and distributed among themselves the 
wealth passed on by Rishyasringa and Vashishta, and then they said, "We are highly gladdened." 
[1-14-52a, 53a]_END

B_1_C_19_2
BEGIN_
			यत्तु मे हृद्गतं वाक्यं तस्य कार्यस्य निश्चयम् |
			कुरुष्व राजशार्दूल भव सत्यप्रतिश्रवाः || १-१९-३_END
BEGIN_
			"What concerns I have in my heart I am going to say, and you take decision thereof, 
			oh, tigerly-king, and become truthful to your promises. [1-19-3]_END

B_1_C_17_16
BEGIN_
			गोलांगूलीषु चोत्पन्नाः केचिदुन्नतविक्रमाः || १-१७-२०
			ऋक्षीषु च तथा जाता वानराः किंनरीषु च |_END
BEGIN_
			Some of the vanara-s endowed with superior valour are born to female langoors, 
			and like that some more to female bears and kinnaraa-s. [1-17-20b, 21a]_END

B_1_C_18_9



B_1_C_14_50
BEGIN_

जांबूनदं कोटिसंंख्यं ब्राह्मणेभ्यो ददौ तदा |_END
BEGIN_
Then to the other Brahmans who arrived there to see the ritual, King Dasharatha sincerly donated 
ten million gold coins. [1-14-53b, 54a]_END

B_1_C_19_3
BEGIN_
			अहं नियममातिष्ठे सिद्ध्यर्थं पुरुषर्षभ |
			तस्य विघ्नकरौ द्वौ तु राक्षसौ कामरूपिणौ || १-१९-४_END
BEGIN_
			"These days I am abiding by a sacrificial vow to attain a spiritual goal but, 
			oh, best one among men, two guise changing demons as causing obstacles to that 
			ritual. [1-19-4]_END

B_1_C_17_17
BEGIN_
			देवा महर्षिगन्धर्वास्तार्क्ष्या यक्षा यशस्विनः || १-१७-२१
			नागाः किंपुरुषाश्चैव सिद्धविद्याधरोरगाः |
			बहवो जनयामासुर्हृष्टास्तत्र सहस्रशः || १-१७-२२
			चारणाश्च सुतान् वीरान् ससृजुर्वनचारिणः |
			वानरान् सुमहाकायान् सर्वान् वै वनचारिणः || १-१७-२३
			अप्सरस्सु च मुख्यासु तदा विद्यधरीषु च |
