			नागकन्यासु च तथा गन्धर्वीणां तनूषु च |_END
BEGIN_
			Several of the gods, great-sages, gandharva-s, eagles, yaksha-s, and the celebrated 
			reptiles, kimpurusha-s, siddha-s, vidyaadharaa-s, uraga-s and caarana-s and even 
			the prominent maidens of apsara-s, she-vidyaadharaa-s, naaga, gandharva-s then 
			gladly procreated all of the thousands of forest-ranging and valiant vanara sons 
			from their bodies that are forest rangers. [21b, 22, 23, 24a, b]_END

B_1_C_18_10



B_1_C_14_51
BEGIN_
दरिद्राय द्विजायाथ हस्ताभरणमुत्तमम् || १-१४-५४
कस्मैचिद्याचमानाय ददौ राघवनंदनः |_END
BEGIN_
That descendent of Raghava dynasty gave an excellent hand ornament to someone who is an impoverished 
Brahman and who is beseeching. [1-14-54a, 55a]_END

B_1_C_19_4
BEGIN_
			व्रते मे बहुशश्चीर्णे समाप्त्यां राक्षसाविमौ |
			मारीचश्च सुबाहुश्च वीर्यवन्तौ सुशिक्षितौ || १-१९-५
			तौ मांसरुधिरौघेण वेदिं तामभ्यवर्षताम् |_END
BEGIN_
			"At the near end of almost completed ritual of mine two valiant and well-trained 
			demons, namely Mareecha and Subaahu, are drenching the Altar of Fire with streams 
			of meat and blood. [1-19-5, 6a]_END

B_1_C_17_18
BEGIN_
			कामरूपबलोपेता यथाकामं विचारिणः || १-१७-२४
			सिंहशार्दूलसदृशा दर्पेण च बलेन च |_END
BEGIN_
			They are endowed with guise changing faculties, with bodily might and by their 
			pride and might are identical to lions and tigers, and they are born-free in their 
			movement in forests. [1-17-24c, 25a]_END

B_1_C_18_11



B_1_C_14_52
BEGIN_
ततः प्रीतेषु विधिवत् द्विजेषु द्विजवत्सलः || १-१४-५५
प्रणाममकरोत्तेषां हर्षव्याकुलितेन्द्रियः |_END
BEGIN_
While those Brahmans are becoming happy then that king and the patron of Brahmans venerated 
them dutifully with his senses fluttering with happiness. [1-14-55b, 56a]_END

B_1_C_19_5
BEGIN_
			अवधूते तथाभूते तस्मिन्नियमनिश्चये || १-१९-६
			कृतश्रमो निरुत्साहस्तस्माद्देशादपाक्रमे |_END
BEGIN_
			"When the ritual vow is thus ravaged I, as the one who exerted myself for the 
			ritual, had to depart from that place, unenthusiastically. [1-19-6n, 7a]_END

B_1_C_17_19
BEGIN_
			शिलाप्रहरणाः सर्वे सर्वे पादपयोधिनः || १-१७-२५
			नखदंष्ट्रायुधाः सर्वे सर्वे सर्वास्त्रकोविदाः |_END
BEGIN_
			All of them are the assaulters with stones, and all are the attackers with trees, 
			and all have their nails and claws as their weapons, yet all are experts in missiles. 
			[1-17-25b, 26a]_END

B_1_C_18_12



B_1_C_14_53
BEGIN_
तस्याशिषोऽथ विविधा ब्राह्मणैः समुदाहृताः || १-१४-५६
उदारस्य नृवीरस्य धरण्यां पतितस्य च |_END
BEGIN_
Then that benevolent and valiant King Dasharatha prostrated on ground venerating the Brahmans, 
and the Brahmans too chanted various blessing hymns on that prostrating king. [1-14-56b, 57a]_END

B_1_C_20_0
BEGIN_
तच्छ्रुत्वा राजशार्दूलो विश्वामित्रस्य भाषितम् |
मुहूर्तमिव निस्सज्ञः सज्ञावानिदमब्रवीत् || १-२०-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing what is spoken by Vishvamitra the tigerly-king Dasharatha became insensate for 
a time, and on redeeming senses he said this. [1-20-1]_END

B_1_C_19_6
BEGIN_
			न च मे क्रोधमुत्स्रष्टुं बुद्धिर्भवति पार्थिव || १-१९-७
			तथाभूता हि सा चर्या न शापस्तत्र मुच्यते |_END
BEGIN_
			"And to me there is no will to let loose my anger, oh, king, as no curse shall 
			be issued under vows, and like that the activity during rituals shall be inoffensive, 
			isn't it. [1-19-7b, 8a]_END

B_1_C_17_20
BEGIN_
			विचालयेयुः शैलेन्द्रान् भेदयेयुः स्थिरान् द्रुमान् || १-१७-२६
			क्षोभयेयुश्च वेगेन समुद्रं सरितां पतिम् |_END
BEGIN_
			They can rock greatest mountains, rip firm rooted trees, and with their speed 
			they can agitate the of lord of rivers, namely the ocean. [1-17-26b, 27a]_END

B_1_C_18_13



B_1_C_14_54
BEGIN_
ततः प्रीतमना राजा प्राप्य यज्ञमनुत्तमम् || १-१४-५७
पापापहं स्वर्नयनं दुस्तरं पार्थिवर्षभैः |_END
BEGIN_
Then that king is gladdened at heart for the successful achievement of the completion of that 
excellent ritual that removes sin and that leads to heaven as well, and that which cannot 
be undertaken by many of the best kings. [1-14-57b, 58a]_END

B_1_C_20_1
BEGIN_
ऊनषोडशवर्षो मे रामो राजीवलोचनः |
न युद्धयोग्यतामस्य पश्यामि सह राक्षसैः || १-२०-२_END
BEGIN_
""Less than sixteen years of age is my lotus-eyed Rama, and I see no warring aptitude to him 
with the demons. [1-20-2]_END

B_1_C_19_7
BEGIN_
			स्वपुत्रं राजशार्दूल रामं सत्यपराक्रमम् || १-१९-८
			काकपक्षधरं शूरं ज्येष्ठं मे दातुमर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
			"As such, oh, tigerly king, it will be apt of you spare the services of that brave 
			one whose valour itself is his truthfulness, that youngling whose hair locks are 
			all the more jet black like crow wings on either side of his head, spare that 
			eldest son of yours, namely Rama. [1-19-8b, 9a]_END

B_1_C_17_21
BEGIN_
			दारयेयुः क्षितिं पद्भ्यामाप्लवेयुर्महार्णवम् || १-१७-२७
			नभस्थलं विशेयुश्च गृह्णीयुरपि तोयदान् |_END
BEGIN_
			They can shatter the ground with their two feet, leap and cross over great oceans, 
			and they can seize the clouds entering arch of heaven. [1-17-27b, 28a]_END

B_1_C_14_55
BEGIN_
ततोऽब्रवीदृष्यशृंगं राजा दशरथस्तदा || १-१४-५८
कुलस्य वर्धनं त्वं तु कर्तुमर्हसि सुव्रत |_END
BEGIN_
Thereafter king Dasharatha said to sage Rishyasringa thus, "oh, sage with best vows, you alone 
are eligible to perform the ritual for the expansion of my dynasty." [1-14-58b, 59a]_END

B_1_C_18_14

BEGIN_
On completion of the ritual, six seasons have passed by; then in the twelfth month, i.e., 
in chaitra-mAsa, and on the ninth day of that chaitra month [April-May], 
when it is punarvasunakShatrayukta-navamI tithi, i.e., when the ruling star of that 
ninth day is punarvasu, 
for which Aditi is the presiding deity; and when five of the nine planets - sUrya, kuja, guru, 
shukra, shani are in ucChasthAna-s, namely, when those planets are in 
ascension in their respective houses - meSha, makara, karkaTa, mIna, tula - rAshI-s; and when chandrayukta- 
guru, karkaTalagne - Jupiter in conjuction with Moon is ascendant in Cancer, and when day is advancing, 
Queen Kausalya gave birth to a son with all the divine attributes like lotus-red eyes, 
lengthy arms, roseate lips, voice like drumbeat, and who took birth to delight the Ikshwaku 
dynasty and adored by all the worlds, and who is the greatly blessed epitome of Vishnu, 
namely Rama. [1-18-8, 9, 10, 11]_END

B_1_C_20_2
BEGIN_
इयमक्षौहिणी पूर्णा यस्याहं पतिरीश्वरः |
अनया संवृतो गत्वा योद्धाहं तैर्निशाचरैः || १-२०-३_END
BEGIN_
"Here is the full-fledged battalion, called akShouhiNii senaa , 
for which I am the leader and controller, and fortified by this army I will go there to encounter 
those demons. [1-20-3]_END

B_1_C_19_8
BEGIN_
			शक्तो ह्येष मया गुप्तो दिव्येन स्वेन तेजसा || १-१९-९
			राक्षसा ये विकर्तारस्तेषामपि विनाशने |_END
BEGIN_
			"Indeed, he is capable to eradicate those demons that are thwarting the ritual 
			by his own divine resplendence, and protected by me as well. [1-19-9b, 10a]_END

B_1_C_17_22
BEGIN_
			गृह्णीयुरपि मातंगान् मत्तान् प्रव्रजतो वने || १-१७-२८
			नर्दमानाश्च नादेन पातयेयुर्विहंगमान् |_END
BEGIN_
			They can catch ruttish elephants that tumultuously move in forests, and just with 
			the sound of their blare they make sky flying birds to fall. [1-17-28b, 29a]_END

B_1_C_14_56
BEGIN_
तथेति च स राजानमुवाच द्विजसत्तमः |
भविष्यन्ति सुता राजंश्चत्वारस्ते कुलोद्वहाः || १-१४-५९_END
BEGIN_
That best Brahman Rishyasringa saying yes to the proposal, said this to king Dasharatha, "oh, 
king, there will be four sons to you that ennoble your dynasty. [1-14-59b, c]_END

B_1_C_18_15
BEGIN_
कौसल्या शुशुभे तेन पुत्रेणामिततेजसा |
यथा वरेण देवानामदितिर्वज्रपाणिना || १-१८-१२_END
BEGIN_
Kausalya shone forth with such a son whose resplendence is unlimited, as with lady Aditi who 
once stood out with her son Indra, the best one among gods. [1-18-12]_END

B_1_C_20_3
BEGIN_
इमे शूराश्च विक्रान्ता भृत्या मेऽस्त्रविशारदाः |
योग्या रक्षोगणैर्योद्धुं न रामं नेतुमर्हसि || १-२०-४_END
BEGIN_
"Brave and daring are these soldiers of mine, and as experts in weaponry they are the appropriate 
ones to combat the hordes of demons, but, it will be ungentle of you to take Rama with you. 
[1-20-4]_END

B_1_C_19_9
BEGIN_
			श्रेयश्चास्मै प्रदास्यामि बहुरूपं न संशयः || १-१९-१०
			त्रयाणामपि लोकानां येन ख्यातिं गमिष्यति |_END
BEGIN_
			"I will also accord many kinds of benefits to him by which he acquires renown 
			in all the three worlds, no doubt about it. [1-19-10b, 11a]_END

B_1_C_17_23
BEGIN_
			ईदृशानां प्रसूतानि हरीणां कामरूपिणाम् || १-१७-२९
			शतं शतसहस्राणि यूथपानां महात्मनाम् |_END
BEGIN_
			Thus the gods and others have procreated millions of such noble souled Vaanaras 
			as the chiefs of warriors who can change their guise at their wish. [1-17-29b, 
			30a]_END

B_1_C_14_57
BEGIN_
स तस्य वाक्यं मधुरं निशम्य
प्रणम्य तस्मै प्रयतो नृपेन्द्र |
जगाम हर्षं परमं महात्मा
तं ऋष्यशृङ्गं पुनरप्युवाच || १-१४-६०_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the sweet words of Sage Rishyasringa, he that king of kings Dasharatha went into 
a state of ecstasy and venerating that great soul, Rishyasringa, again said this to him. [1-14-60]_END

B_1_C_18_16
BEGIN_
भरतो नाम कैकेय्यां जज्ञे सत्यपराक्रमः |
साक्षाद्विष्णोश्चतुर्भागः सर्वैः समुदितो गुणैः || १-१८-१३_END
BEGIN_
Queen Kaikeyi gave birth to Bharata, one embodied with all merits, and whose truthfulness 
itself is his valour and who is fourth component of manifest Vishnu, namely Rama. [1-18-13]_END

B_1_C_20_4
BEGIN_
अहमेव धनुष्पाणिर्गोप्ता समरमूर्धनि |
यावत् प्राणान् धरिष्यामि तावद्योत्स्ये निशाचरैः || १-२०-५_END
BEGIN_
"I alone with bow in my hand can protect your ritual, and as long as I bear my lives so long 
I war with those nightwalkers staying in the van of war. [1-20-5]_END

B_1_C_19_10
BEGIN_
			न च तौ राममासाद्य शक्तौ स्थातुं कथञ्चन || १-१९-११
			न च तौ राघवादन्यो हन्तुमुत्सहते पुमान् |_END
BEGIN_
			"Those two demons will be rendered incapable to stand fast on affronting Rama 
			in anywise, and none other than Raghava has the fortitude to eliminate those two. 
			[1-19-11b, 12a]_END

B_1_C_17_24
BEGIN_
			ते प्रधानेषु यूथेषु हरीणां हरियूथपाः || १-१७-३०
			बभूवुर्यूथपश्रेष्ठा वीरांश्चाजनयन् हरीन् |_END
BEGIN_
			Those vanara generals who took birth thus became the prominent generals among 
			the principle battalions of monkeys, and they have also procreated brave monkeys 
			on their own. [1-17-30a, 31b]_END

B_1_C_18_17
BEGIN_
अथ लक्ष्मणशत्रुघ्नौ सुमित्राजनयत् सुतौ |
वीरौ सर्वास्त्रकुशलौ विष्णोरर्धसमन्वितौ | १-१८-१४_END
BEGIN_
Queen Sumitra then gave birth to two sons who are the embodied epitomes of Vishnu, namely 
Lakshmana, and Shatrughna, who are valiant ones and experts in all kinds of weaponry. [1-18-14]_END

B_1_C_20_5
BEGIN_
निर्विघ्ना व्रतचर्या सा भविष्यति सुरक्षिता |
अहं तत्रागमिष्यामि न रामं नेतुमर्हसि || १-२०-६_END
BEGIN_
" I myself wish to come over there thereby the works of ritual will be well-guarded and unimpeded, 
but, taking Rama with you will be ungracious of you. [1-20-6]_END

B_1_C_19_11
BEGIN_
			वीर्योत्सिक्तौ हि तौ पापौ कालपाशवशं गतौ || १-१९-१२
			रामस्य राजशार्दूल न पर्याप्तौ महात्मनः |_END
BEGIN_
			"Those two sinners that are berserk by their vigour have gone into the subjection 
			of death's noose, oh tigerly king, cannot counterbalance the great-souled Rama. 
			[1-19-12b, 13a]_END

B_1_C_17_25
BEGIN_
			अन्ये ऋक्षवतः प्रस्थानुपतस्थुः सहस्रशः || १-१७-३१
			अन्ये नानाविधान् शैलान् काननानि च भेजिरे |_END
BEGIN_
			Some thousands of them stayed on the ridges of Mt. Rikshavat while others reached 
			many kinds of other mountains and forests. [1-17-31b, 32a]_END

B_1_C_18_18
BEGIN_
पुष्ये जातस्तु भरतो मीनलग्ने प्रसन्नधीः |
सार्पे जातौ तु सौमित्री कुळीरेऽभ्युदिते रवौ || १-१८-१५_END
BEGIN_
			With the dawn of sun on the next day, fair-minded Bharata is born under Pisces where puSyami 
			is the star of day, later the sons of Sumitra, namely Lakshmana and Shatrughna are 
			born under Cancer, where aashleSa is the star of the 
			day, i.e., the tenth of chaitra month, [1-18-15]_END

B_1_C_20_6
BEGIN_
बालो ह्यकृतविद्यश्च न च वेत्ति बलाबलम् |
न चास्त्रबलसंयुक्तो न च युद्धविशारदः || १-२०-७
न चासौ रक्षसां योग्यः कूटयुद्धा हि ते ध्रुवम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Why because, Rama is boy! And he is unschooled in his princely education; does he know the 
strengths and weaknesses of opponents - no; has he got the equipage of arsenal - no; has he 
any expertise in warfare - no; is he an equal to the demons - no; be that as it may, those 
demons definitely conduct a deceitful warfare, isn't it. [1-19-7, 8a]_END

B_1_C_19_12
BEGIN_
			न च पुत्रगतं स्नेहं कर्तुमर्हसि पार्थिव || १-१९-१३
			अहं ते प्रतिजानामि हतौ तौ विद्धि राक्षसौ |_END
BEGIN_
			"It will be unapt of you to show your paternal fondness, oh, king, upon my oath, 
			be assured that those two demons are eradicated. [1-19-13b, 14a]_END

B_1_C_17_26
BEGIN_
			सूर्यपुत्रं च सुग्रीवं शक्रपुत्रं च वालिनम् || १-१७-३२
			भ्रातरावुपतस्थुस्ते सर्वे च हरियूथपाः |
			नलं नीलं हनूमन्तमन्यांश्च हरियूथपान् || १-१७-३३_END
BEGIN_
			All of the monkeys stood by the brothers, namely the son of Indra Vali, and the 
			son of sun Sugreeva, and even with the monkey generals like Nala, Neela and Hanuma 
			et al. [1-17-32b, 33]_END

B_1_C_18_19
BEGIN_
राज्ञः पुत्रा महात्मानश्चत्वारो जज्ञिरे पृथक् |
गुणवंतोऽनुरूपाश्च रुच्या प्रोष्ठपदोपमाः || १-१८-१६_END
BEGIN_
Thus there are four great-souled sons of Dasharatha, born on separate instances, who are virtuous, 
charming, and by brilliance they are in similitude with two stars of each of the asterisms 
called puurvaabhaadra and uttaraabhaadra. 
[1-18-16]_END

B_1_C_21_0
BEGIN_
			तच्छ्रुत्वा वचनं तस्य स्नेहपर्याकुलाक्षरम् |
			समन्युः कौशिको वाक्यं प्रत्युवाच महीपतिम् || १-२१-१_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing the wavery words of Dasharatha that are full of fond for his son, 
			Vishvamitra wrathfully replied this sentence to the king. [1-21-1]_END

B_1_C_20_7
BEGIN_
विप्रयुक्तो हि रामेण मुहूर्तमपि नोत्सहे || १-२०-८
जीवितुं मुनिशार्दूल न रामं नेतुमर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
"Alienated from Rama I am disinclined to live even for a moment, oh, tigerly sage, hence taking 
Rama with you will be unjust. [1-20-8b, 9a]_END

B_1_C_19_13
BEGIN_
			अहं वेद्मि महात्मानं रामं सत्यपराक्रमम् || १-१९-१४
			वसिष्ठोऽपि महातेजा ये चेमे तपसि स्थिताः |_END
BEGIN_
			"I am sensible of that sublime-soul Rama, whose valour is his truthfulness, and 
			even this great resplendent Vashishta and these saints that are here are aware. 
			[1-19-14b, 15a]_END

B_1_C_17_27
BEGIN_
			ते तार्क्ष्यबलसंपन्नाः सर्वे युद्धविशारदाः |
			विचरन्तोऽर्दयन् दर्पात् सिंहव्याघ्रमहोरगान् || १-१७-३४_END
BEGIN_
			All of those who are well-versed in warfare and endowed with the might of divine 
			eagle Garuda, used to thwart the pride of lions, tigers and great snakes just 
			by their own prideful subjugation while they move about the forests. [1-17-34]_END

B_1_C_21_1
BEGIN_
			पूर्वमर्थं प्रतिश्रुत्य प्रतिज्ञां हातुमिच्छसि |
			राघवाणामयुक्तोऽयं कुलस्यास्य विपर्ययः || १-२१-२_END
BEGIN_
			"On promising me to fulfil my object in the first instance you wish to repudiate 
			it now, undeserving is this kind of deviation for the kings of Raghava dynasty. 
			[1-21-2]_END

B_1_C_18_20
BEGIN_
जगुः कलं च गंधर्वा ननृतुश्चाप्सरोगणाः |
देवदुंदुभयो नेदुः पुष्पवृष्टिश्च खात्पतत् || १-१८-१७
उत्सवश्च महानासीदयोध्यायां जनाकुलः |_END
BEGIN_
The celestial singers sang melodiously, paradisiacal dancing parties danced, divine drums 
drummed and heavens rained flowers, with all this there is a great festivity in Ayodhya with 
thronging people. [1-18-17, 18a]_END

B_1_C_20_8
BEGIN_
यदि वा राघवं ब्रह्मन्नेतुमिच्छसि सुव्रत || १-२०-९
चतुरंगसमायुक्तं मया सह च तं नय |_END
BEGIN_
"Otherwise, oh, Brahman with best vows, if you so wish to take Rama along with you, you lead 
him off along with me, and along with my four kinds of troops. [1-20-9b, 10a]_END

B_1_C_19_14
BEGIN_
			यदि ते धर्मलाभं तु यशश्च परमं भुवि || १-१९-१५
			स्थिरमिच्छसि राजेन्द्र रामं मे दातुमर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
			"If you wish to gain in value of probity, a long-lasting and paramount renown 
			on earth it will be apt of you to handover Rama to me. [1-19-15b, 16a]_END

B_1_C_17_28
BEGIN_
			महाबलो महाबाहुर्वाली विपुलविक्रमः |
			जुगोप भुजवीर्येण ऋक्षगोपुच्छवानरान् || १-१७-३५_END


B_1_C_21_2
BEGIN_
			यदीदं ते क्षमं राजन् गमिष्यामि यथागतम् |
			मिथ्याप्रतिज्ञः काकुत्स्थ सुखी भव सबान्धवः || १-२१-३_END
BEGIN_
			"If this is worth while to you, oh, king, I wish to go away as I have come, and 
			you with your feigned promises be nonchalantly happy with your kinsmen." So said 
			Vishvamitra to the king. [1-21-3]_END

B_1_C_18_21
BEGIN_
रथ्याश्च जनसंबाधा नटनर्तकसंकुलाः || १-१८-१८
गायनैश्च विराविण्यो वादनैश्च तथापरैः |
विरेजुर्विपुलास्तत्र सर्वरत्नसमन्विताः || १-१८-१९_END
BEGIN_
Hilarity filled the streets with people stampeding them and with the flurry of actors, dancers, 
singers and instrumentalists, as well by other onlookers, and there on the streets widely 
strewn are all kinds of gems appreciating the artists. [1-18-18b, 19]_END

B_1_C_20_9
BEGIN_
षष्टिर्वर्षसहस्राणि जातस्य मम कौशिक || १-२०-१०
कृच्छ्रेणोत्पादितश्चायं न रामं नेतुमर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
"Sixty thousand years have passed from my birth, oh! Vishvamitra, and this Rama is engendered 
at this age, that too with tribulations, hence taking Rama with you will be inappropriate 
of you. [1-20-10b, 11a]_END

B_1_C_19_15
BEGIN_
			यद्यभ्यनुज्ञां काकुत्स्थ ददते तव मंत्रिणः || १-१९-१६
			वसिष्ठप्रमुखाः सर्वे ततो रामं विसर्जय |_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, Dasharatha, you may send Rama if only your ministers and all the other elite 
			headed by Vashishta are going to give assent. [1-19-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_17_29
BEGIN_
			तैरियं पृथिवी शूरैः सपर्वतवनार्णवा |
			कीर्णा विविधसंस्थानैर्नानाव्यंजनलक्षणैः || १-१७-३६_END
BEGIN_
			The earth with its mountains, forests and oceanward places is overspread with 
			those brave ones that possess diverse physiques and peculiar indication marks 
			of their stock. [1-17-36]_END

B_1_C_21_3
BEGIN_
			तस्य रोषपरीतस्य विश्वामित्रस्य धीमतः |
			चचाल वसुधा कृत्स्ना विवेश च भयं सुरान् || १-२१-४_END
BEGIN_
			When that prudent sage Vishvamitra is thus enwrapped in fury, then the whole earth 
			trembled and the gods are scared. [1-21-4]_END

B_1_C_18_22
BEGIN_
प्रदेयांश्च ददौ राजा सूतमागधवंदिनाम् |
ब्राह्मणेभ्यो ददौ वित्तं गोधनानि सहस्रशः || १-१८-२०_END
BEGIN_
The king gave worthy gifts to eulogisers, bard singers, and panegyrists, and to Brahmans he 
gave funds and wealth in the form of thousands of cows. [1-18-20]_END

B_1_C_20_10
BEGIN_
चतुर्णामात्मजानां हि प्रीतिः परमिका मम || १-२०-११
ज्येष्ठे धर्मप्रधाने च न रामं नेतुमर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
"I will have exceptional affection for all of my four sons, isn't it, and among them Rama 
has a significance in the matter of his descent as an eldest son, hence taking Rama with you 
will be unjust of you. [1-20-11b, 12a]_END

B_1_C_19_16
BEGIN_
			अभिप्रेतमसंसक्तमात्मजं दातुमर्हसि || १-१९-१७
			दशरात्रं हि यज्ञस्य रामं राजीवलोचनम् |_END
BEGIN_
			"It will be apt of you to send your choicest son, the lotus-eyed Rama, just for 
			ten days of the ritual without temporising. [1-19-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_17_30
BEGIN_
			तैर्मेघबृन्दाचलकूटसंनिभैः
			महाबलैर्वानरयूथपाधिपैः |
			बभूव भूर्भीमशरीररूपैः
			समावृता रामसहायहेतोः || १-१७-३७_END
BEGIN_
			The earth is thus suffused with those mighty army generals of Vanara race whose 
			physiques resembled the clusters of clouds and peaks of mountains, and who have 
			emerged for the reason of helping Rama. [1-17-37]_END

B_1_C_21_4
BEGIN_
			त्रस्तरूपं तु विज्ञाय जगत्सर्वं महानृषिः |
			नृपतिं सुव्रतो धीरो वसिष्ठो वाक्यमब्रवीत् || १-२१-५_END
BEGIN_
			On knowing the appalled appearance of the entire world at the fury of Vishvamitra, 
			Vashishta the great sage with high vows and an insightful one too, said these 
			words to the king. [1-21-5]_END

B_1_C_18_23
BEGIN_
अतीत्यैकादशाहं तु नामकर्म तथाकरोत् |
ज्येष्ठं रामं महात्मानं भरतं कैकयीसुतम् || १-१८-२१
सौमित्री लक्ष्मणमिति शत्रुघ्नमपरं तथा |
वसिष्ठः परमप्रीतो नामानि कुरुते तदा || १-१८-२२_END
BEGIN_
Elapsed are eleven days and the naming ceremony is performed, then Vashishta, the chief priest, 
named the high-souled elder one as Rama, Kaikeyi's son as Bharata, and one son of Sumitra 
as Lakshmana and the other as Shatrughna [1-18-21, 22]_END

B_1_C_20_11
BEGIN_
किं वीर्या राक्षसास्ते च कस्य पुत्राश्च के च ते || १-२०-१२
कथं प्रमाणाः के चैतान् रक्षन्ति मुनिपुंगव |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, eminent sage, of what fortitude are those demons? Whose sons are they? Who are they? 
How is their size and shape? Also who protects all of them? [1-20-12b, 13a]_END

B_1_C_19_17
BEGIN_
            नात्येति कालो यज्ञस्य यथायं मम राघव || १-१९-१८
			तथा कुरुष्व भद्रं ते मा च शोके मनः कृथाः |_END
BEGIN_
			"I wish you to take decision as to how my ritual's time is not lapsed, and 
			let safety betide you, let not your heart be rendered to grieve." Thus Vishvamitra 
			said to Dasharatha. [1-19-18b, 19a]_END

B_1_C_21_5
BEGIN_
			इक्ष्वाकूणां कुले जातः साक्षाद्धर्म इवापरः |
			धृतिमान् सुव्रतः श्रीमान्न धर्मं हातुमर्हसि || १-२१-६_END
BEGIN_
			"Born in Ikshwaku dynasty you are apparently the other god of ethics on earth, 
			a staunch one with righteous vows and a glorious one too, such as you are, it 
			will be unapt of you to forsake ethics." [1-21-6]_END

B_1_C_18_24
BEGIN_
ब्राह्मणान् भोजयामास पौरान् जानपदानपि |
अददद्ब्राह्मणानां च रत्नौघममितं बहु || १-१८-२३
तेषां जन्मक्रियादीनि सर्वकर्माण्यकारयत् |_END
BEGIN_
The king feasted Brahmans, urbanites and villagers and he gifted many valuable gems to Brahmans 
in an unlimited way, and all the rituals of birth and ceremonies sequel to it like naming 
ceremony, first-food-feeding ceremony, first-hair-removal ceremony, and sacred thread ceremony 
are performed in respect of the princes. [1-18-23, 24a]_END

B_1_C_20_12
BEGIN_
कथं च प्रतिकर्तव्यं तेषां रामेण रक्षसाम् || १-२०-१३
मामकैर्वा बलैर्ब्रह्मन् मया वा कूटयोधिनाम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Brahman, how Rama, or my forces, or I myself have to retaliate those demons that are 
deceitful militants. [1-20-13b, 14a]_END

B_1_C_19_18
BEGIN_
			इत्येवमुक्त्वा धर्मात्मा धर्मार्थसहितं वचः || १-१९-१९
			विरराम महातेजा विश्वामित्रो महामतिः |_END
BEGIN_
			On saying those words that comprise fairness and meaningfulness that virtue-souled 
			great saint with great resplendence paused. [1-19-19b, 20a]_END

B_1_C_21_6
BEGIN_
			त्रिषु लोकेषु विख्यातो धर्मात्मा इति राघव |
			स्वधर्मं प्रतिपद्यस्व नाधर्मं वोढुमर्हसि || १-२१-७_END
BEGIN_
			"In three worlds you are renowned as the right-minded one, oh, Raghava, hence 
			adhere to your own uprightness, and adhering to unrighteousness will be unapt 
			of you. [1-21-7]_END

B_1_C_18_25
BEGIN_
तेषां केतुरिव ज्येष्ठो रामो रतिकरः पितुः |१-१८-२४
बभूव भूयो भूतानां स्वयंभूरिव सम्मतः |_END
BEGIN_
Among those princes the eldest one Rama is like a flagstaff and a delight of his father Dasharatha, 
and he became acceptable to all beings like the self-created Brahma. [1-18-24b, 25a]_END

B_1_C_20_13
BEGIN_
सर्वं मे शंस भगवन् कथं तेषां मया रणे|| १-२०-१४
स्थातव्यं दुष्टभावानां वीर्योत्सिक्ता हि राक्षसाः |
तस्य तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा विश्वामित्रोऽभ्यभाषत || १-२०-१५_END
BEGIN_
"Tell me all that, oh, god, how I have to carry on when warring with those evil minded demons, 
for the demons will be delirious by their audacity, isn't it..." Thus Dasharatha asked Vishvamitra 
insistently. On hearing those words Sage Vishvamitra replied this way. [1-20-14b, 15]_END

B_1_C_19_19
BEGIN_
			स तन्निशम्य राजेन्द्रो विश्वामित्रवचः शुभम् || १-१९-२०
			शोकेन महताविष्टश्चचाल च मुमोह च |
			लब्धसंज्ञस्तथोत्थाय व्यषीदत भयान्वितः || १-१९-२१_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing the propitious words of sage Vishvamitra that best king Dasharatha 
			shuddered and swooned as he is muffled up with profound adversity, and after that 
			on regaining consciousness he sunk down in fear. [1-19-20b, 21]_END

B_1_C_18_26
BEGIN_
सर्वे वेदविदः शूराः सर्वे लोकहिते रताः || १-१८-२५
सर्वे ज्ञानोपसंपन्नाः सर्वे समुदिता गुणैः |_END
BEGIN_
All the princes are scholars in Veda-s, valiant ones, all are interested in the welfare of 
the world, all are intellectuals and all of them possess an air of probity. [1-18-25b, 26a]_END

B_1_C_21_7
BEGIN_
			प्रतिश्रुत्य करिष्येति उक्तं वाक्यमकुर्वतः |
			इष्टापूर्तवधो भूयात्तस्माद्रामं विसर्जय || १-२१-८_END
BEGIN_
			"Promising to effectuate something in any way and not effectuating the given word 
			results in the perdition to the merits of iSTaapuurta 
			Vedic rituals, hence oh, Raghava, leave hold of Rama. [1-21-8]_END

B_1_C_20_14
BEGIN_
पौलस्त्यवंशप्रभवो रावणो नाम राक्षसः |
स ब्रह्मणा दत्तवरस्त्रैलोक्यं बाधते भृशम् || १-२०-१६
महाबलो महावीर्यो राक्षसैर्बहुभिर्वृतः |_END
BEGIN_
"One born in Paulastya dynasty, an extremely mighty and exceedingly brave demon named Ravana 
is there, and he with the boon given by Brahma, and accompanied with many other demons is 
torturing the triad of worlds, contemptuously. [1-20-16, 17a]_END

B_1_C_19_20
BEGIN_
			इति हृदयमनोविदारणं
			मुनिवचनं तदतीव शुश्रुवान् |
			नरपतिरभवन्महान् महात्मा
			व्यथितमनाः प्रचचाल चासनात् || १-१९-२२_END
BEGIN_
			This way on hearing that word of the saint Vishvamitra which is explicitly slitting 
			his mind and heart that illustrious and noble-souled king Dasharatha then became 
			highly annoyed at heart, and flustered extremely in his throne. [1-19-22]_END

B_1_C_22_0
BEGIN_
			तथा वसिष्ठे ब्रुवति राजा दशरथः स्वयम् |
			प्रहृष्टवदनो राममाजुहाव सलक्ष्मणम् || १-२२-१_END
BEGIN_
			When Vashishta said that way king Dasharatha with an air of satisfaction personally 
			fetched Rama along with Lakshmana. [1-22-1]_END

B_1_C_18_27
BEGIN_
तेषामपि महातेजा रामः सत्यपराक्रमः || १-१८-२६
इष्टः सर्वस्य लोकस्य शशांक इव निर्मलः |_END
BEGIN_
Among them the great resplendent Rama, whose valour itself is his truthfulness, is the dear 
one to all the world like the tranquil moon. [1-18-26b, 27a]_END

B_1_C_20_15
BEGIN_
श्रूयते च महाराजा रावणो राक्षसाधिपः || १-२०-१७
साक्षाद्वैश्रवणभ्राता पुत्रो विश्रवसो मुनेः |_END
BEGIN_
"Unequivocally that chief of demons is the brother of Kubera and the son of sage Vishravasa, 
thus we hear. [1-20-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_21_8
BEGIN_
			कृतास्त्रमकृतास्त्रं वा नैनं शक्ष्यन्ति राक्षसाः |
			गुप्तं कुशिकपुत्रेण ज्वलनेनामृतं यथा || १-२१-९_END
BEGIN_
			"Whether Rama is trained in weaponry or not, demons cannot trounce Rama as long 
			as Kushi's son Vishvamitra protects him, like the heavenly firewall that protects 
			divine nectar. [1-21-9]_END

B_1_C_22_1
BEGIN_
			कृतस्वस्त्ययनं मात्रा पित्रा दशरथेन च |
			पुरोधसा वसिष्ठेन मङ्गलैरभिमंत्रितम् || १-२२-२
			सपुत्रं मूर्ध्न्युपाघ्राय राजा दशरथस्तदा |
			ददौ कुशिकपुत्राय सुप्रीतेनान्तरात्मना || १-२२-३_END
BEGIN_
			Rama is blessed for a propitious travel firstly by his mother Kausalya and then 
			by his father king Dasharatha, thereupon the royal priest Vashishta rendered Vedic 
			hymns blessing the journey, then Dasharatha well pleased in his heart of hearts 
			kissed his son Rama on forehead and entrusted him to Vishvamitra. [1-22-2, 3]_END

B_1_C_18_28
BEGIN_
गजस्कन्धेऽश्वपृष्ठे च रथचर्यासु सम्मतः || १-१८-२७
धनुर्वेदे च निरतः पितृशुश्रूषणे रतः |_END
BEGIN_
Rama is admittedly a champion of riding elephants and horses, also in tactical charioting, 
and he rejoices in the art of archery, and absorbed in the obedient service of his father. 
[1-18-27b, 28a]_END

B_1_C_20_16
BEGIN_
यदा न खलु यज्ञस्य विघ्नकर्ता महाबलः || १-२०-१८
तेन संचोदितौ तौ तु राक्षसौ च महाबलौ |
मारीचश्च सुबाहुश्च यज्ञविघ्नं करिष्यतः || १-२०-१९_END
BEGIN_
"That formidable Ravana is not a devastator of rituals by himself, even so, two very mighty 
demons called Mareecha and Subaahu will cause devastating hindrances to rituals, instigated 
by him." Thus Sage Vishvamitra said to Dasharatha. [1-20-18b, 19]_END

B_1_C_21_9
BEGIN_
			एष विग्रहवान् धर्म एष वीर्यवतां वरः |
			एष बुद्ध्याधिको लोके तपसश्च परायणम् || १-२१-१०_END
BEGIN_
			"He is an embodiment of virtue, matchless among the venturesome, peerless in intellect 
			among all in the world, and flawless in ascesis. [1-21-10]_END

B_1_C_22_2
BEGIN_
			ततो वायुः सुखस्पर्शो नीरजस्को ववौ तदा |
			विश्वामित्रगतं रामं दृष्ट्वा राजीवलोचनम् || १-२२-४_END
BEGIN_
			Then on seeing the lotus-eyed Rama following Vishvamitra, dustless 
			and pleasant for touch breeze blew. [1-22-4]_END

B_1_C_18_29
BEGIN_
बाल्यात् प्रभृति सुस्निग्धो लक्ष्मणो लक्ष्मिवर्धनः || १-१८-२८
रामस्य लोकरामस्य भ्रातुर्ज्येष्ठस्य नित्यशः |_END
BEGIN_
Right from childhood Lakshmana, the enhancer of prosperity, is always amiable towards his 
world-charming elder brother Rama. [1-18-28b, 29a]_END

B_1_C_20_17
BEGIN_
इत्युक्तो मुनिना तेन राजोवाच मुनिं तदा |
न हि शक्तोऽस्मि संग्रामे स्थातुं तस्य दुरात्मनः || १-२०-२०_END
BEGIN_
Thus when he is said so by that sage Vishvamitra, then the king Dasharatha spoke to the sage, 
"I myself am not capable of standing against that evil minded Ravana, in truth, where is the 
question of deputing my young Rama to confront him? [1-20-20]_END

B_1_C_21_10
BEGIN_
			एषोऽस्त्रान् विविधान् वेत्ति त्रैलोक्ये सचराचरे |
			नैनमन्यः पुमान् वेत्ति न च वेत्स्यन्ति केचन || १-२१-११_END
BEGIN_
			"He is in the know-how of various missiles, and no other person is there in the 
			triad of worlds, inclusive of sessile and mobile worlds, who is knowledgeable 
			about him, or someone who can know him will be there in future, excepting myself. 
			[1-21-11]_END

B_1_C_22_3
BEGIN_
			पुष्पवृष्टिर्महत्यासीद्देवदुन्दुभिनिःस्वनैः |
			शङ्खदुन्दुभिनिर्घोषः प्रयाते तु महात्मनि || १-२२-५_END
BEGIN_
			When the great-souled Rama forged ahead there occurred an abounding downpour of 
			flowers with the booming of divine drums, together with the boom and blare of 
			drums and conch-shells of Ayodhya. [1-22-5]_END

B_1_C_18_30
BEGIN_
सर्वप्रियकरस्तस्य रामस्यापि शरीरतः || १-१८-२९
लक्ष्मणो लक्ष्मिसंपन्नो बहिःप्राण इवापरः |_END
BEGIN_
Lakshmana who is endowed with the wealth of dedication dedicated himself to Rama with bodily 
service, and while performing all agreeable deeds in respect of Rama, he behaved like Rama's 
alter ego. [1-18-29b, 30a]_END

B_1_C_20_18
BEGIN_
स त्वं प्रसादं धर्मज्ञ कुरुष्व मम पुत्रके |
मम चैवाल्पभाग्यस्य दैवतं हि भवान् गुरुः || १-२०-२१_END
BEGIN_
"You are the knower of probity, such as you are, you may please bestow benevolence upon my 
boyish son, as well on a less fortunate one like me too, and as our mentor you are indeed 
a god of ours. [1-20-21]_END

B_1_C_21_11
BEGIN_
			न देवा नर्षयः केचिन्नामरा न च राक्षसाः |
			गन्धर्वयक्षप्रवराः सकिन्नरमहोरगाः || १-२१-१२_END
BEGIN_
			"While Gods cannot know Vishvamitra, can anybody from sages - no; immortals- no; demons 
			- no; the gandharva-s and eminent yaksha-s together with the kinnaraa-s and great 
			reptile beings - no, they cannot know him. [1-21-12]_END

B_1_C_22_4
BEGIN_
			विश्वामित्रो ययावग्रे ततो रामो महायशाः |
			काकपक्षधरो धन्वी तं च सौमित्रिरन्वगात् || १-२२-६_END
BEGIN_
			Rama with jet-black hair-locks handling his bow followed Vishvamitra who walked 
			ahead, while Lakshmana handling his own bow followed Rama. [1-22-6]_END

B_1_C_20_19
BEGIN_
देवदानवगंधर्वा यक्षाः पतगपन्नगाः|
न शक्ता रावणं सोढुं किं पुनर्मानवा युधि || १-२०-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Gods, demons, celestial beings like gandharva-s, yaksha-s, winged and reptile beings 
are incapable to bear the brunt of that Ravana in fight, why tell again about humans. [1-20-22]_END

B_1_C_18_31
BEGIN_
न च तेन विना निद्रां लभते पुरुषोत्तमः || १-१८-३०
मृष्टमन्नमुपानीतमश्नाति न हि तं विना |_END
BEGIN_
That best one among the men Rama does not get his sleep without Lakshmana and he would 
not eat food brought for him, however delicious it may be, without Lakshmana. [1-18-30b, 31a]_END

B_1_C_21_12
BEGIN_
			सर्वास्त्राणि कृशाश्वस्य पुत्राः परमधार्मिकाः |
			कौशिकाय पुरा दत्ता यदा राज्यं प्रशासति || १-२१-१३_END
BEGIN_
			"All the missiles known to Vishvamitra are the highly righteous children of Krishaashva 
			Prajapati, where Prajapati-s were the earliest ruler of mankind, and god Shiva 
			gave them to Vishvamitra when was ruling kingdom. [1-21-13]_END

B_1_C_22_5
BEGIN_
			कलापिनौ धनुष्पाणी शोभयानौ दिशो दश |
			विश्वामित्रं महात्मानं त्रिशीर्षाविव पन्नगौ |
			अनुजग्मतुरक्षुद्रौ पितामहमिवाश्विनौ || १-२२-७_END
BEGIN_
			Rama and Lakshmana, with two quivers each and two bows in their hands, and making 
			all the ten directions of compass lambent followed Vishvamitra, as if three headed 
			serpents followed Vishvamitra, and with their highly dynamic physiques and spiritedness 
			they look as if like the Ashwin twin gods of unequal charm following Brahma, the 
			Forefather. [1-22-7]_END

B_1_C_20_20
BEGIN_
स तु वीर्यवतां वीर्यमादत्ते युधि रावणः |
तेन चाहं न शक्तोऽस्मि संयोद्धुं तस्य वा बलैः || १-२०-२३
सबलो वा मुनिश्रेष्ठ सहितो वा ममात्मजैः |_END
BEGIN_
"But that Ravana depletes the valour of valorous opponents in a battle, oh, eminent sage, 
either with my entire forces, or with all my sons I am inadequate to grapple with all his 
forces, or with him, individually. [1-20-23, 24a]_END

B_1_C_18_32
BEGIN_
यदा हि हयमारूढो मृगयां याति राघवः || १-१८-३१
तदैनं पृष्ठतोऽभ्येति स धनुः परिपालयन् |_END
BEGIN_
Whenever Raghava mounts a horse and goes on a hunting game Lakshmana rushes after him wielding 
his bow as a squire. [1-18-31b, 32a]_END

B_1_C_21_13
BEGIN_
			तेऽपि पुत्रा कृशाश्वस्य प्रजापतिसुतासुताः |
			नैकरूपा महावीर्या दीप्तिमंतो जयावहाः || १-२१-१४_END
BEGIN_
			"Those missiles are the sons of Daksha Prajaapati's daughters and her husband 
			Krishaasva Prajapati, and they are disparate in their form, intrepid, dazzling, 
			and victory-oriented missiles. [1-21-14]_END

B_1_C_23_0
BEGIN_
प्रभातायां तु शर्वर्यां विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः |
अभ्यभाषत काकुत्स्थौ शयानौ पर्णसंस्तरे || १-२३-१_END
BEGIN_
At dawn after that night the great saint Vishvamitra spoke to the legatees of Kakutstha, Rama 
and Lakshmana, those that are sleeping on a grass bed. [1-23-1]_END

B_1_C_22_6
BEGIN_
			तदा कुशिकपुत्रं तु धनुष्पाणी स्वलंकृतौ |
			बद्धगोधांगुलित्राणौ खड्गवन्तौ महाद्युती || १-२२-८
			कुमारौ चारुवपुषौ भ्रातरौ रामलक्ष्मणौ |
			अनुयातौ श्रिया दीप्तौ शोभयेतामनिन्दितौ || १-२२-९
			स्थाणुं देवमिवाचिन्त्यं कुमाराविव पावकी |_END
BEGIN_
			Those two youngsters with charming and bejewelled physiques are handling bows 
			and swords and their fingers have leathern covers. Both the unreprovable brothers 
			Rama and Lakshmana are highly resplendent and effulgent by their worth. While 
			they are following Vishvamitra they looked like the sons of Fire-god, namely Skanda 
			and Vishakha, following the great god with inscrutable potential, namely Shiva, 
			and thus the brothers have made Vishvamitra to shine forth in even pose with god 
			Shiva. [1-22-8, 9, 10a]_END

B_1_C_20_21
BEGIN_
कथमप्यमरप्रख्यं संग्रामाणामकोविदम् || १-२०-२४
बालं मे तनयं ब्रह्मन्नैव दास्यामि पुत्रकम् |_END
BEGIN_
"My boyish son is godlike and unfledged in warfare, oh, Brahman, and he is the one who alleviates 
me from punnama naraka the hell of sonless fathers... no, I cannot 
spare my son in anyway. [1-20-24b, 25a]_END

B_1_C_18_33
BEGIN_
भरतस्यापि शत्रुघ्नो लक्ष्मणावरजो हि सः || १-१८-३२
प्राणैः प्रियतरो नित्यं तस्य चासीत्तथा प्रियः |_END
BEGIN_
Lakshmana's younger brother Shatrughna is a dear one to Bharata, like that Bharata too held 
Shatrughna dearer than his own lives. [1-18-32b, 33a]_END

B_1_C_21_14
BEGIN_
			जया च सुप्रभा चैव दक्षकन्ये सुमध्यमे |
			ते सुवातेऽस्त्रशस्त्राणि शतं परमभास्वरम् || १-२१-१५_END
BEGIN_
			"Jaya and Suprabha, the daughters of Daksha Prajapati, endowed with best waists 
			gave birth to a hundred missiles and weaponry whose flare is supreme. [1-21-15]_END

B_1_C_23_1
BEGIN_
कौसल्या सुप्रजा राम पूर्वा संध्या प्रवर्तते |
उत्तिष्ठ नरशार्दूल कर्तव्यं दैवमाह्निकम् || १-२३-२_END
BEGIN_
"Fortunate is Kausalya to beget you as her son Rama... get up oh, tigerly-man, eastern aurora 
is emerging, daytime tasks towards gods are to be performed." [1-23-2]_END

B_1_C_22_7
BEGIN_
			अध्यर्धयोजनं गत्वा सरय्वा दक्षिणे तटे | १-२२-१०
			रामेति मधुरां वाणीं विश्वामित्रोऽभ्यभाषत |_END
BEGIN_
			And on going one and half yojana distance Vishvamitra addressed Rama in a harmonious 
			voice calling, 'oh, Rama', on the southern riverbank of Sarayu. [1-22-10b, 11a]_END

B_1_C_20_22
BEGIN_
अथ कालोपमौ युद्धे सुतौ सुन्दोपसुन्दयोः || १-२०-२५
यज्ञविघ्नकरौ तौ ते नैव दास्यामि पुत्रकम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Further, those saboteurs of your ritual namely Mareecha and Subaahu, are similar to Death-god 
and the descendents of the earliest demons and subverters of rituals, namely Sunda and Upasunda, 
no, I cannot spare my son, in any case. [1-20-25b, 26a]_END

B_1_C_18_34
BEGIN_
स चतुर्भिर्महाभागैः पुत्रैर्दशरथः प्रियैः || १-१८-३३
बभूव परमप्रीतो देवैरिव पितामहः |_END
BEGIN_
King Dasharatha is highly gladdened with four of his highly fortunate sons like the Forefather 
Brahma with gods in heaven. [1-18-33]_END

B_1_C_21_15
BEGIN_
            पंचाशतं सुतान् लेभे जया लब्धवरा वरान् | 
            वधायासुरसैन्यानामप्रमेयानरूपिणः || १-२१-१६_END
BEGIN_
			"On getting a boon Jaya named wife of Krishaasva Prajapati is benefited with fifty 
			best and formless sons with immeasurable fortitude for the destruction of ungodly 
			beings. [1-21-16]_END

B_1_C_23_2
BEGIN_
तस्यर्षेः परमोदारं वचः श्रुत्वा नरोत्तमौ |
स्नात्वा कृतोदकौ वीरौ जेपतुः परमं जपम् || १-२३-३_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the benign words of the sage those valorous and best ones among men got up, bathed, 
and on offering water oblation they meditated upon the supreme hymn, namely Gayatri. [1-23-3]_END

B_1_C_22_8
BEGIN_
			गृहाण वत्स सलिलं मा भूत् कालस्य पर्ययः || १-२२-११
			मंत्रग्रामं गृहाण त्वं बलामतिबलां तथा |_END
BEGIN_
			" "Take water, my boy, and like that you receive a group of hymns,
			bala and atibala from 
			me, and let no time lapse. [1-22-11b, 12a]_END

B_1_C_20_23
BEGIN_
मारीचश्च सुबाहुश्च वीर्यवन्तौ सुशिक्षितौ || १-२०-२६
तयोरन्यतरं योद्धुं यास्यामि ससुहृद्गणः |
अन्यथा त्वनुनेष्यामि भवन्तं सह बान्धवैः || १-२०-२७_END
BEGIN_
"Mareecha and Subaahu are well-trained and valorous ones, hence I will proceed with all my 
friendly forces to war with either of those two demons, otherwise, I along with all my relatives 
implore upon you for your exoneration in my failure to comply my own promises. [1-20-26b, 
27]_END

B_1_C_18_35
BEGIN_
ते यदा ज्ञानसंपन्नाः सर्वे समुदिता गुणैः || १-१८-३४
ह्रीमन्तः कीर्तिमन्तश्च सर्वज्ञा दीर्घदर्शिनः |
तेषामेवं प्रभावाणां सर्वेषां दीप्ततेजसाम् || १-१८-३५
पिता दशरथो हृष्टो ब्रह्मा लोकाधिपो यथा |_END
BEGIN_
When all of the four sons are thus prospering with prudence, gifted with all the merits, self-conscious 
to do wrong deeds, well-known for their gentility, knowers of pros and cons and even the conscientious 
princes, then their father Dasharatha is contented in respect of all of them who are such 
radiantly brilliant and potential princes, like Brahma. [1-18-34b, 35, 36a]_END

B_1_C_21_16
BEGIN_
			सुप्रभाजनयत् चापि पुत्रान् पंचाशतं पुनः |
			संहारान्नाम दुर्धर्षान् दुराक्रामान् बलीयसः || १-२१-१७_END
BEGIN_
			"Suprabha, another wife of Krishaasva Prajapati, gave birth to another fifty unassailable, 
			unconquerable and mighty sons named the Eliminators. [1-21-17]_END

B_1_C_23_3
BEGIN_
कृताह्निकौ महावीर्यौ विश्वामित्रं तपोधनम् |
अभिवाद्यातिसंहृष्टौ गमनायाभितस्थतुः || १-२३-४_END
BEGIN_
On performing their dawn time duties those two stalwarts, Rama and Lakshmana, enthusiastically 
presented themselves before the ascetically rich sage Vishvamitra for further journey, duly 
venerating him. [1-23-4]_END

B_1_C_22_9
BEGIN_
			न श्रमो न ज्वरो वा ते न रूपस्य विपर्ययः || १-२२-१२
			न च सुप्तं प्रमत्तं वा धर्षयिष्यन्ति नैरृताः |_END
BEGIN_
			"On receiving these hymns neither tiredness nor fever, nor disfiguring of personality 
			can effect you, nor the demons can charge you either you are sleeping or unvigilant. 
			[1-11-12b, 13a]_END

B_1_C_20_24
BEGIN_
इति नरपतिजल्पनाद्द्विजेन्द्रं
कुशिकसुतं सुमहान् विवेश मन्युः |
सुहुत इव मखेऽग्निराज्यसिक्तः
समभवदुज्वलितो महर्षिवह्निः || १-२०-२८_END
BEGIN_
Thus, by the incongruous talk of Dasharatha, the outstanding Brahman and son of Sage Kushi, 
namely sage Vishvamitra is overwhelmed with outrageous anger by his mentation, and that fire-like 
glorious sage looked like the ritual fire into which many inflammable oblations are offered, 
and which is drenched with a lot of clarified butter, whereby it is flaring up its tongues. 
[1-20-28]_END

B_1_C_18_36
BEGIN_
ते चापि मनुजव्याघ्रा वैदिकाध्ययने रताः || १-१८-३६
पितृशुश्रूषणरता धनुर्वेदे च निष्ठिताः |_END
BEGIN_
Even those tigerly-men, namely the princes, are engrossed in the studies of Veda-s, delighted 
to render service to their father and they are also the experts in art of archery. [1-18-36b, 
37a]_END

B_1_C_21_17
BEGIN_
			तानि चास्त्राणि वेत्त्येष यथावत् कुशिकात्मजः |
			अपूर्वाणां च जनने शक्तो भूयः स धर्मवित् || १-२१-१८_END
BEGIN_
			"And this sage Vishvamitra is in the precise know of the said missiles, and this 
			principled one is also capable of creating hitherto unavailable missiles. [1-21-18]_END

B_1_C_23_4
BEGIN_
तौ प्रयान्तौ महावीर्यौ दिव्यां त्रिपथगां नदीम् |
ददृशाते ततस्तत्र सरय्वाः संगमे शुभे || १-२३-५_END
BEGIN_
Then on travelling some more distance those two great valiant ones, there they have seen the 
divine river that courses in three ways, namely Ganga, at the auspicious confluence of River 
Sarayu. [1-23-5]_END

B_1_C_22_10
BEGIN_
			न बाह्वोः सदृशो वीर्ये पृथिव्यामस्ति कश्चन || १-२२-१३
			त्रिषु लोकेषु वा राम न भवेत्सदृशस्तव |_END
BEGIN_
			"As it is none whosoever on earth can equal you in dexterity, Rama, and by reciting 
			these hymns none can equal you in the three worlds. [1-22-13b, 14a]_END

B_1_C_18_37
BEGIN_
अथ राजा दशरथस्तेषां दारक्रियां प्रति || १-१८-३७
चिंतयामास धर्मात्मा सोपाध्यायः सबान्धवः |_END
BEGIN_
Then the noble souled Dasharatha contemplated along with his priestly teachers and relatives 
about the matrimonial alliances of his sons. [1-18-37b, 38a]_END

B_1_C_21_18
BEGIN_
			तेनास्य मुनिमुख्यस्य धर्मज्ञस्य महात्मनः |
			न किंचिदस्त्यविदितं भूतं भव्यं च राघव || १-२१-१९_END
BEGIN_
			"Thereby, oh, Raghava, nothing whatsoever is unknown to this great-souled Vishvamitra, 
			who is a distinguished sage and the knower of virtue, either that has happened 
			or that is happening. [1-21-19]_END

B_1_C_23_5
BEGIN_
तत्राश्रमपदं पुण्यं ऋषीणां भावितात्मनाम् |
बहुवर्षसहस्राणि तप्यतां परमं तपः || १-२३-६_END
BEGIN_
There they have seen the merited hermitage of sages with contemplative souls, and who are 
practising supreme ascesis for many thousand years. [1-23-6]_END

B_1_C_22_11
BEGIN_
			बलामतिबलां चैव पठतस्तात राघव || १-२२-१४
			न सौभाग्ये न दाक्षिण्ये न ज्ञाने बुद्धिनिश्चये |
			नोत्तरे प्रतिवक्तव्ये समो लोके तवानघ || १-२२-१५_END
BEGIN_
			"My dear Raghava, if bala atibala hymns are practised, oh, impeccable one, none 
			can equal you in the world by your handsomeness, calibre, erudition, by your discernment, 
			and even in replying or rebutting you. [1-22-14b, 15]_END

B_1_C_18_38
BEGIN_
तस्य चिन्तयमानस्य मन्त्रि मध्ये महात्मनः || १-१८-३८
अभ्यागच्छन्महातेजा विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः |_END
BEGIN_
While the great souled Dasharatha is discussing the marriages of princes among his ministers, 
the highly powerful sage Vishvamitra arrived. [1-18-38b, 39a]_END

B_1_C_21_19
BEGIN_
			एवंवीर्यो महातेजा विश्वामित्रो महायशाः |
			न रामगमने राजन् संशयं गन्तुमर्हसि || १-२१-२०_END
BEGIN_
			"Thus, the highly renowned and great resplendent sage Vishvamitra has this sort 
			of enterprise, oh, king, allowing a doubt enter your mind in Rama's accompanying 
			the sage will be unapt of you. [1-21-20]_END

B_1_C_23_6
BEGIN_
तं दृष्ट्वा परमप्रीतौ राघवौ पुण्यमाश्रमम् |
ऊचतुस्तं महात्मानं विश्वामित्रमिदं वचः || १-२३-७_END
BEGIN_
On seeing that merited hermitage Rama and Lakshmana are highly pleased and said this word 
to that great-soul Sage Vishvamitra. [1-23-7]_END

B_1_C_22_12
BEGIN_
			एतद्विद्याद्वये लब्धे न भवेत्सदृशस्तव |
			बला चातिबला चैव सर्वज्ञानस्य मातरौ || १-२२-१६_END
BEGIN_
			"On receiving these two teachings there will be none similar to you, for bala 
			and atibala are the mothers of all knowledge. [1-22-16]_END

B_1_C_18_39
BEGIN_
स राज्ञो दर्शनाकांक्षी द्वाराध्यक्षानुवाच ह || १-१८-३९
शीघ्रमाख्यात मां प्राप्तं कौशिकं गाधिनः सुतम् |_END
BEGIN_
Desirous to have an audience with king Vishvamitra said to the doorkeeper, "Let the king be 
informed quickly that I, the son of Gadhi from the dynasty of Kushi, have come" [1-18-39b, 
40a]_END

B_1_C_21_20
BEGIN_
			तेषां निग्रहणे शक्तः स्वयं च कुशिकात्मजः |
			तव पुत्रहितार्थाय त्वामुपेत्याभियाचते || १-२१-२१_END
BEGIN_
			"This son of Kushi, Vishvamitra, can as well control those demons by himself, 
			but intending to accord beneficence to your son he approached you and imploring 
			upon you. [1-21-21]_END

B_1_C_23_7
BEGIN_
कस्यायमाश्रमः पुण्यः को न्वस्मिन्वसते पुमान् |
भगवन् श्रोतुमिच्छावः परं कौतूहलं हि नौ || १-२३-८_END
BEGIN_
"Whose hermitage is this merited one? Indeed who is the celebrity that lives therein? Oh, 
godly sage, we are interested to listen, and we are truly inquisitive about it." Thus they 
asked. [1-23-8]_END

B_1_C_22_13
BEGIN_
			क्षुत्पिपासे न ते राम भविष्येते नरोत्तम |
			बलामतिबलां चैव पठतस्तात राघव || १-२२-१७_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, best one among men, Raghava, if you go on reciting bala and atiblala hymns, 
			my dear Rama, there will be no hunger or thirst to you. [1-22-17]_END

B_1_C_18_40
BEGIN_
तच्छ्रुत्वा वचनं तस्य राज्ञो वेश्म प्रदुद्रुवुः || १-१८-४०
संभ्रान्तमनसः सर्वे तेन वाक्येन चोदिताः |_END
BEGIN_
On listening those words all the doorkeepers are dumbfounded, and ushered by those words they 
quickly rushed to the place of Dasharatha. [1-18-40b, 41a]_END

B_1_C_21_21
BEGIN_
			इति मुनिवचनात् प्रसन्नचित्तो
			रघुवृषभश्च मुमोद पार्थिवाग्र्यः |
			गमनमभिरुरोच राघवस्य
			प्रथितयशाः कुशिकात्मजाय बुद्ध्या || १-२१-२२_END
BEGIN_
			Thus the prominent king from Raghu dynasty, namely Dasharatha, became serene-minded 
			by sage Vashishta's words, and he who is supreme among other kings and who has 
			pronounced renown, that Dasharatha then gladly and wholeheartedly consented to 
			the travel of Rama along with the sage Vishvamitra. [1-21-22]_END

B_1_C_23_8
BEGIN_
तयोस्तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा प्रहस्य मुनिपुंगवः |
अब्रवीच्छ्रूयतां राम कस्यायं पूर्व आश्रमः || १-२३-९_END
BEGIN_
On hearing their words the eminent sage Viswamitra said smilingly, " whose hermitage is this 
in earlier times that may be listened." Thus Vishvamitra started to narrate. [1-23-9]_END

B_1_C_24_0
BEGIN_
ततः प्रभाते विमले कृताह्निकमरिन्दमौ |
विश्वामित्रं पुरस्कृत्य नद्यास्तीरमुपागतौ || १-२४-१_END
BEGIN_
Then, in the fresh of the morning those enemy destroyers, Rama and Lakshmana, arrived at the 
riverbank of Ganga keeping sage Vishvamitra ahead of them, which sage has just completed his 
ritualistic chores of dawn. [1-24-1]_END

B_1_C_22_14
BEGIN_
			गृहाण सर्वलोकस्य गुप्तये रघुनन्दन |
			विद्याद्वयमधीयाने यशश्चाप्यतुलं भुवि |
			पितामहसुते ह्येते विद्ये तेजःसमन्विते || १-२२-१८
			प्रदातुं तव काकुत्स्थ सदृशस्त्वं हि धार्मिक |_END
BEGIN_
			"And if these twin teachings are practised an inestimable renown will also accrue, 
			oh, Raghu's legatee, these two hymns that possess brilliance are the daughters 
			of Forefather Brahma, and oh, Rama of Kakutstha, I intend to impart these hymns 
			to you, oh virtuous one, as you are the most eligible one, hence take the teachings 
			that are kept safe from the world. [1-22-18, 19a]_END

B_1_C_18_41
BEGIN_
ते गत्वा राजभवनं विश्वामित्रमृषिं तदा || १-१८-४१
प्राप्तमावेदयामासुर्नृपायेक्ष्वाकवे तदा |_END
BEGIN_
Then on their arriving at the king's palace the doorkeepers have announced to the king of 
Ikshvaku-s, namely Dasharatha, about the arrival of sage Vishvamitra. [1-18-41b, 42a]_END

B_1_C_23_9
BEGIN_
कन्दर्पो मूर्तिमानासीत् काम इत्युच्यते बुधैः |
तपस्यन्तमिह स्थाणुं नियमेन समाहितम् || १-२३-१०
कृतोद्वाहं तु देवेशं गच्छन्तं समरुद्गणम् |
धर्षयामास दुर्मेधा हुंकृतश्च महात्मना || १-२३-११_END
BEGIN_
"When Love-god was with his body wise men used to call him Kama, the passion. At this place, 
that Love-god with his naughty intent braved god of gods Shiva who had been practising ascesis 
and who concentrated observantly, and who was returning after his marriage along with his 
followers, namely the Wind-gods, and that great soul Shiva disapprovingly roared at Love-god. 
[1-23-10, 11]_END

B_1_C_24_1
BEGIN_
ते च सर्वे महात्मानो मुनयः संश्रितव्रताः |
उपस्थाप्य शुभां नावं विश्वामित्रमथाब्रुवन् || १-२४-२_END
BEGIN_
All those sages of Kaama's hermitage that are the great souls and scrupulous ones in their 
vows, have positioned an auspicious ferryboat within the reach in the river, and then they 
said to sage Vishvamitra. [1-24-2]_END

B_1_C_22_15
BEGIN_
			कामं बहुगुणाः सर्वे त्वय्येते नात्र संशयः |१-२२-१९
			तपसा संभृते चैते बहुरूपे भविष्यतः |_END
BEGIN_
			"Though all of these numerous qualities are undoubtedly available with you, that 
			too in abundance, yet these hymns if ascetically nurtured will yield various results." 
			Thus spoke Sage Vishvamitra to Rama. [1-22-19b, 20a]_END

B_1_C_18_42
BEGIN_
तेषां तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा सपुरोधाः समाहितः || १-१८-४२
प्रत्युज्जगाम संहृष्टो ब्रह्माणमिव वासवः |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that message from doorkeepers Dasharatha is highly pleased and he has gone towards 
Vishvamitra in a self-possessed manner along with royal priests, as Indra would ceremoniously 
go towards Brahma. [1-18-42b, 43a]_END

B_1_C_23_10
BEGIN_
अवध्यतश्च रौद्रेण चक्षुषा रघुनन्दन |
व्यशीर्यन्त शरीरात् स्वात् सर्वगात्राणि दुर्मतेः || १-२३-१२_END
BEGIN_
"And Rama, the wrathful third-eye of Shiva destroyed the lewd-minded Love-god making all his 
limbs to fall down from his body. [1-23-12]_END

B_1_C_24_2
BEGIN_
आरोहतु भवान्नावं राजपुत्रपुरस्कृतः |
अरिष्टं गच्छ पन्थानं मा भूत्कालविपर्ययः || १-२४-३_END
BEGIN_
"You may board the boat keeping the princes ahead of you, and we wish you to proceed on a 
prosperous route without the shift of time." So said the sages. [1-24-3]_END

B_1_C_22_16
BEGIN_
			ततो रामो जलं स्पृष्ट्वा प्रहृष्टवदनः शुचिः | १-२२-२०
			प्रतिजग्राह ते विद्ये महर्षेर्भावितात्मनः |_END
BEGIN_
			Then Rama on touching water to purify himself received those teachings from the 
			contemplative soul Vishvamitra with gladness beaming on his face. [1-22-20b, 21a]_END

B_1_C_18_43
BEGIN_
तं दृष्ट्वा ज्वलितं दीप्त्या तापसं संशितव्रतम् || १-१८-४३
प्रहृष्टवदनो राजा ततोऽर्घ्यमुपहारयत् |_END
BEGIN_
Then on seeing the resplendent sage Vishvamitra, whose radiance is by his own ascesis and 
who has severe self-discipline, the king offered water with a gladsome aspect, as first customary 
hospitality in receiving unexpected guest. [1-18-43b, 44a]_END

B_1_C_23_11
BEGIN_
तत्र गात्रं हतं तस्य निर्दग्धस्य महात्मनः |
अशरीरः कृतः कामः क्रोधाद्देवेश्वरेण ह || १-२३-१३_END
BEGIN_
"There the body of Love-god is evanesced when that great soul Shiva burnt it down, and by 
the anger of that god of gods Shiva, Love-god is rendered as a bodiless entity. [1-23-13]_END

B_1_C_24_3
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रस्तथेत्युक्त्वा तानृषीन्प्रतिपूज्य च |
ततार सहितस्ताभ्यां सरितं सागरंगमाम् || १-२४-४_END
BEGIN_
Sage Vishvamitra on saying 'it must be so,' to those sages and revering them in his turn, 
cruised the river that itself is cruising towards ocean, along with both the princes. [1-24-4]_END

B_1_C_22_17
BEGIN_
			विद्यासमुदितो रामः शुशुभे भूरिविक्रमः || १-२२-२१
			सहस्ररश्मिर्भगवान् शरदीव दिवाकरः |
			गुरुकार्याणि सर्वाणि नियुज्य कुशिकात्मजे |
			ऊषुस्तां रजनीं तत्र सरय्वाः सुसुखं त्रयः || १-२२-२२_END
BEGIN_
			Rama, the one with marvellous valiance, on obtaining those teachings performed 
			all his duties of a student in respect of a teacher and then shone forth like 
			the thousand rayed sun on a cloudless sky of autumn. Then those three very happily 
			stayed on the riverbank of Sarayu for that night. [1-22-21b, 22]_END

B_1_C_18_44
BEGIN_
स राज्ञः प्रतिगृह्यार्घ्यं शास्त्रदृष्टेन कर्मणा || १-१८-४४
कुशलं चाव्ययं चैव पर्यपृच्छन्नराधिपम् |_END
BEGIN_
On receiving water from the king scripturally and customarily Vishvamitra enquired after the 
well-being and welfare of king Dasharatha. [1-18-44b, 45a]_END

B_1_C_23_12
BEGIN_
अनङ्ग इति विख्यातस्तदाप्रभृति राघव |
स चाङ्गविषयः श्रीमान् यत्राङ्गं स मुमोच ह || १-२३-१४_END
BEGIN_
Then onwards Love-god is renowned as Ananga, as he is without body, and where his body is 
given up that is renowned as Anga province. [1-23-14]_END

B_1_C_24_4
BEGIN_
तत्र शुश्राव वै शब्दं तोयसंरम्भवर्धितम् |
मध्यमागम्य तोयस्य तस्य शब्दस्य निश्चयम् || १-२४-५
ज्ञातुकामो महातेजा सह रामः कनीयसा |_END
BEGIN_
On coming to the midstream of water there Rama heard an unusual and increasing noise of gushy 
waters along with his younger brother, and that brilliant one Rama desired to know its significance. 
[1-24-5, 6a]_END

B_1_C_22_18
BEGIN_
			दशरथनृपसूनुसत्तमाभ्यां
			तृणशयनेऽनुचिते सहोषिताभ्याम् |
			कुशिकसुतवचोऽनुलालिताभ्यां |
			सुखमिव सा विबभौ विभावरी च || १-२२-२३_END
BEGIN_
			Though both Rama and Lakshmana slept on an undeserving grass bed, nestled by the 
			comfortable words of Vishvamitra that night is as though pleasant to the noteworthy 
			children of Dasharatha. [1-22-24]_END

B_1_C_18_45
BEGIN_
पुरे कोशे जनपदे बान्धवेषु सुहृत्सु च || १-१८-४५
कुशलं कौशिको राज्ञः पर्यपृच्छत् सुधार्मिकः |_END
BEGIN_
That highly righteous sage Vishvamitra asked the king after the well-being of city, exchequer, 
rural areas, friends and relatives. [1-18-45b, 46a]_END

B_1_C_23_13
BEGIN_
तस्यायमाश्रमः पुण्यस्तस्येमे मुनयः पुरा |
शिष्या धर्मपरा वीर तेषां पापं न विद्यते || १-२३-१५_END
BEGIN_
"This merited hermitage thus belongs to Shiva and, oh, brave Rama, these sages abiding in 
virtue are Shiva's disciples at one time, thus sin is unverifiable with them. [1-23-15]_END

B_1_C_24_5
BEGIN_
अथ रामः सरिन्मध्ये पप्रच्छ मुनिपुङ्गवम् || १-२४-६
वारिणो भिद्यमानस्य किमयं तुमुलो ध्वनिः |_END
BEGIN_
Rama then asked the eminent sage Vishvamitra in the midst of the river, "what is this turbulent 
sound sire, as though slashing water?" [1-24-6b, 7a]_END

B_1_C_18_46
BEGIN_
अपि ते संनताः सर्वे सामन्ता रिपवो जिताः || १-१८-४६
दैवं च मानुषं चैव कर्म ते साध्वनुष्ठितम् |_END
BEGIN_
Sage Vishvamitra asked Dasharatha, "Are all of the provincial kings acquiescent to you, and 
all your enemies conquered? Are you properly performing the devotional and social works?" 
[1-18-46b, 47a]_END

B_1_C_23_14
BEGIN_
इहाद्य रजनीं राम वसेम शुभदर्शन |
पुण्ययोः सरितोर्मध्ये श्वस्तरिष्यामहे वयम् || १-२३-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Let us stay for this night in this hermitage situated in between two meritorious rivers Ganga 
and Sarayu, oh, Rama with auspicious mien, tomorrow we will cross over the River Ganga. [1-23-16]_END

B_1_C_24_6
BEGIN_
राघवस्य वचः श्रुत्वा कौतूहलसमन्वितम् || १-२४-७
कथयामास धर्मात्मा तस्य शब्दस्य निश्चयम् |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the inquisitive words of Raghava that virtue-souled sage Vishvamitra started to 
tell the significance of that sound. [1-24-7b, 8a]_END

B_1_C_25_0
BEGIN_
अथ तस्याप्रमेयस्य मुनेर्वचनमुत्तमम् |
श्रुत्वा पुरुषशार्दूलः प्रत्युवाच शुभां गिरम् || १-२५-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the worthy words of that sage with inestimable power, then the tigerly man Rama 
replied him with estimable words. [1-25-1]_END

B_1_C_18_47
BEGIN_
वसिष्ठं च समागम्य कुशलं मुनिपुंगवः || १-१८-४७
ऋषींश्च तान् यथान्यायं महाभागानुवाच ह |_END
BEGIN_
And on meeting the eminent sage Vashishta and with them the other exalted sages according 
to custom Vishvamitra asked after their well-being. [1-18-47b, 48a]_END

B_1_C_24_7
BEGIN_
कैलासपर्वते राम मनसा निर्मितं परम् || १-२४-८
ब्रह्मणा नरशार्दूल तेनेदं मानसं सरः |_END
BEGIN_
"On Mt. Kailash Brahma created a great lake at his will, oh, tigerly-man Rama, hence that 
is called Maanasa Lake. [1-24-8b, 9a]_END

B_1_C_23_15
BEGIN_
अभिगच्छामहे सर्वे शुचयः पुण्यमाश्रमम् |
इह वासः परोऽस्माकं सुखं वस्त्यामहे वयम् || १-२३-१७
स्नाताश्च कृतजप्याश्च हुतहव्या नरोत्तम |_END
BEGIN_
"Let us all purify ourselves by taking our bath, performing our meditations, offering our 
daily oblations, and then let us enter this meritorious hermitage, thus our stay in here will 
be comforting to us." So said Vishvamitra to Rama and Lakshmana. [1-23-17, 18a]_END

B_1_C_25_1
BEGIN_
अल्पवीर्या यदा यक्षी श्रूयते मुनिपुङ्गव |
कथं नागसहस्रस्य धारयत्यबला बलम् || १-२५-२_END
BEGIN_
"It is said that yaksha's strength is trivial, and this is an yakshii, more so a female, how 
then this yakshii frail by her femineity can exert the strength of a thousand elephants? [1-25-2]_END

B_1_C_18_48
BEGIN_
ते सर्वे हृष्टमनसस्तस्य राज्ञो निवेशनम् || १-१८-४८
विविशुः पूजितास्तेन निषेदुश्च यथार्हतः |_END
BEGIN_
Then adoringly invited by the king Dasharatha all of them gladly entered the palace and they 
took their seats according to protocol. [1-18-48b, 49a]_END

B_1_C_24_8
BEGIN_
तस्मात् सुस्राव सरसः सायोध्यामुपगूहते || १-२४-९
सरः प्रवृत्ता सरयूः पुण्या ब्रह्मसरश्च्युता |
तस्यायमतुलः शब्दो जाह्नवीमभिवर्तते || १-२४-१०
वारिसंक्षोभजो राम प्रणामं नियतः कुरु |_END
BEGIN_
"That river which spontaneously flows out of that Maanasa Lake surrounds Ayodhya city is this 
one, the River Sarayu. Because this has originated from a lake, saraH, 
this is known as Sarayu. And because it flows from Brahma's Lake it is a merited river. This 
is the remarkable noise of such a Sarayu River in its coursing towards River Ganga, generated 
by the collision of their waters, and Rama, offer regards to these rivers, respectfully." 
So said Vishvamitra to the princes. [1-24-9b, 10, 11a]_END

B_1_C_23_16
BEGIN_
तेषां संवदतां तत्र तपोदीर्घेण चक्षुषा || १-२३-१८
विज्ञाय परमप्रीता मुनयो हर्षमागमन् |
अर्घ्यं पाद्यं तथातिथ्यं निवेद्य कुशिकात्मजे || १-२३-१९_END
BEGIN_
When they are discussing there the sages of that hermitage are highly gladdened to perceive 
them with their sixth-sense, and on approaching them enchantedly they offered water for hands 
and feet wash and then offered hospitality firstly to Sage Vishvamitra. [1-23-18, 19]_END

B_1_C_25_2
BEGIN_
इत्युक्तं वचनं श्रुत्वा राघवस्यामितोजसा |
हर्षयन् श्लक्ष्णया वाचा सलक्ष्मणमरिन्दमम् || १-२५-३
विश्वामित्रोऽब्रवीद्वाक्यं शृणु येन बलोत्कटा |
वरदानकृतं वीर्यं धारयत्यबला बलम् || १-२५-४_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the sentence of Raghava with illimitable dynamism, Vishvamitra said this sentence 
to the enemy subduer Rama along with Lakshmana, cheering them up with his pleasant words, 
"Listen by which a female became outstanding by her strength... she assumes strength by the 
bestowal of a boon. [1-25-3, 4]_END

B_1_C_18_49
BEGIN_
अथ हृष्टमना राजा विश्वामित्रं महामुनिम् || १-१८-४९
उवाच परमोदारो हृष्टस्तमभिपूजयन् |_END
BEGIN_
Then the very generous king Dasharatha is gladdened at heart at the arrival of Vishvamitra, 
and he spoke this way feeling happy to adore that sage. [1-18-49b, 50a]_END

B_1_C_24_9
BEGIN_
ताभ्यां तु तावुभौ कृत्वा प्रणाममतिधार्मिकौ || १-२४-११
तीरं दक्षिणमासाद्य जग्मतुर्लघुविक्रमौ |_END
BEGIN_
Offering their salutations to River Sarayu and Ganga those two most virtuous and agile footed 
princes proceeded further on reaching the southern riverbank. [1-24-11b, 12a]_END

B_1_C_23_17
BEGIN_
रामलक्ष्मणयोः पश्चादकुर्वन्नतिथिक्रियाम् |
सत्कारं समनुप्राप्य कथाभिरभिरंजयन् ||१-२३-२०_END
BEGIN_
Afterwards those sages of that hermitage have accorded reception to Rama and Lakshmana, and 
applauded by Vishvamitra for their hospitality those sages have entertained Rama and other 
guests with myths and legends. [1-23-20]_END

B_1_C_25_3
BEGIN_
पूर्वमासीन्महायक्षः सुकेतुर्नाम वीर्यवान् |
अनपत्यः शुभाचारः स च तेपे महत्तपः || १-२५-५_END
BEGIN_
"Once there was a formidable yaksha named Suketu, but he was childless, and he who had devout 
conduct performed a great ascesis. [1-25-5]_END

B_1_C_18_50
BEGIN_
यथामृतस्य संप्राप्तिर्यथा वर्षमनूदके || १-१८-५०
यथा सदृशदारेषु पुत्रजन्माप्रजस्य वै |
प्रणष्टस्य यथा लाभो यथा हर्षो महोदये || १-१८-५१
तथैवागमनं मन्ये स्वागतं ते महामुने |_END
BEGIN_
"I deem your arrival is in the vein of mortals attaining ambrosia, rainfall in a droughty 
land, a barren father begetting a son through his deserving wife, a regain of long lost treasures, 
and the gladness at a great happening, oh, great saint, welcome to you." [1-18-50b, 51, 52a]_END

B_1_C_24_10
BEGIN_
स वनं घोरसंकाशं दृष्ट्वा नरवरात्मजः || १-२४-१२
अविप्रहतमैक्ष्वाकः पप्रच्छ मुनिपुंगवम् |_END
BEGIN_
On seeing a horrendous and uninhibited forest, Rama, the son of the best king Dasharatha asked 
the eminent sage Vishvamitra. [1-24-12b, 13a]_END

B_1_C_23_18
BEGIN_
यथार्हमजपन् संध्यामृषयस्ते समाहिताः |
तत्र वासिभिरानीता मुनिभिः सुव्रतैः सह || १-२३-२१
न्यवसन् सुसुखं तत्र कामाश्रमपदे तथा |_END
BEGIN_
Those sages with concentrated minds and according to one's own aptitude have meditated upon 
the deity of sunset when it is sundown, followed by Rama and others. Then led into hermitage 
by those sages who are with pious commitments and who are dwelling there, Rama and others 
have very comfortably stayed in the precincts of Shiva's hermitage. [1-23-21]_END

B_1_C_25_4
BEGIN_
पितामहस्तु सुप्रीतस्तस्य यक्षपतेस्तदा |
कन्यारत्नं ददौ राम ताटकां नाम नामतः || १-२५-६_END
BEGIN_
"Gladdening at his ascesis, Rama, then the Forefather Brahma gave him a gemlike daughter who 
is renowned by the name of Tataka. [1-25-6]_END

B_1_C_18_51
BEGIN_
कं च ते परमं कामं करोमि किमु हर्षितः || १-१८-५२
पात्रभूतोऽसि मे ब्रह्मन् दिष्ट्या प्राप्तोऽसि मानद |
अद्य मे सफलं जन्म जीवितं च सुजीवितम् || १-१८-५३
यस्माद् विप्रेन्द्रमद्राक्षं सुप्रभाता निशा मम |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Brahman, as I am the one who is delighted for your arrival, and as you are the most eligible 
recipient from me, what is that choicest object of yours to be fulfilled by me, and in which 
way. Oh, endower of respect, for me your arrival is fortunate whereby my birth is fructified 
and my life flourished today, and wherefore I could see a great Brahman like you visiting 
my home, therefore the sun appears to have dawned in my night. [1-18-52b, 53, 54a]_END

B_1_C_24_11
BEGIN_
अहो वनमिदं दुर्गं झिल्लिकागणसंयुतम् || १-२४-१३
भैरवैः श्वापदैः कीर्णं शकुनैर्दारुणारवैः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, impenetrable is this forest fraught with swarms of crickets, brutish predators, and vultures, 
which are all horribly strident. [1-24-13b, 14a]_END

B_1_C_23_19
BEGIN_
कथाभिरभिरामभिरभिरामौ नृपात्मजौ | - 
रमयामास धर्मात्मा कौशिको मुनिपुङ्गवः || १-२३-२२_END
BEGIN_
Staying very comfortably in the precincts of Kaama hermitage, 
then that virtuous sage Vishvamitra, saint the eminent, delighted the delightful princes with delighting stories.....[1-23-22]_END

B_1_C_25_5
BEGIN_
ददौ नागसहस्रस्य बलं चास्याः पितामहः |
न त्वेव पुत्रं यक्षाय ददौ ब्रह्मा महायशाः || १-२५-७_END
BEGIN_
"Forefather Brahma also gave the strength of a thousand elephants to her, but he that highly 
remarkable Brahma did not give a son to that yaksha, anticipating male to be more hazardous. 
[1-25-7]_END

B_1_C_26_0
BEGIN_
मुनेर्वचनमक्लीबं श्रुत्वा नरवरात्मजः |
राघवः प्राञ्जलिर्भूत्वा प्रत्युवाच दृढव्रतः || १-२६-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of that unfaltering sage about demoness Tataka, Raghava, best 
man's son who is firm in his vows, reverently adjoining his palms replied the sage. 
[1-26-1]_END

B_1_C_18_52
BEGIN_
पूर्वं राजर्षिशब्देन तपसा द्योतितप्रभः || १-१८-५४
ब्रह्मर्षित्वमनुप्राप्तः पूज्योऽसि बहुधा मया |_END
BEGIN_
"Originally your glory was explicit by your title kingly-sage, and subsequently you 
attained the Absolute-sainthood by your ascesis, and you are venerable to me, in many 
ways." [1-18-54b, 55a]_END

B_1_C_24_12
BEGIN_
नानाप्रकारैः शकुनैर्वाश्यद्भिर्भैरवस्वनैः || १-२४-१४
सिंहव्याघ्रवराहैश्च वारणैश्चापि शोभितम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Various vultures are screeching with fierce sonority, and tigers, wild boars, and elephants 
render this forest atypical. [1-24-14b, 15a]_END

B_1_C_25_6
BEGIN_
तां तु बालां विवर्धन्तीं रूपयौवनशालिनीम् |
जंभपुत्राय सुन्दाय ददौ भार्यां यशस्विनीम् || १-२५-८_END
BEGIN_
"When that bright girl is growing up into a youthful beauty her father Suketu gave her to 
Jambha's son Sunda as wife. [1-25-8]_END

B_1_C_26_1
BEGIN_
पितुर्वचननिर्देशात् पितुर्वचनगौरवात् |
वचनं कौशिकस्येति कर्तव्यमविशङ्कया || १-२६-२_END
BEGIN_
"Upon my father's order, upon my honour to my father's word, and looking upon this 
as the word of sage Kushi's son, my mentor, this task is definitely to be implemented. 
[1-26-2]_END

B_1_C_18_53
BEGIN_
तदद्भुतमभूत् विप्र पवित्रं परमं मम || १-१८-५५
शुभक्षेत्रगतश्चाहं तव संदर्शनात् प्रभो |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Brahman, thereby your arrival at my place is surprising and ideally sacred to me, and 
by your very appearance I have become one who has gone on a quiet pilgrimage. [1-18-55b, 56a]_END

B_1_C_24_13
BEGIN_
धवाश्वकर्णककुभैर्बिल्वतिन्दुकपाटलैः || १-२४-१५
संकीर्णं बदरीभिश्च किंन्वेतद्दारुणं वनम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed, what is this wretched forest that is dense with Dhava, Ashvakarna, Arjuna, Bilva, 
Tinduka, Patala, and Badari trees." Thus Rama asked Vishvamitra. [1-24-15b, 16a]_END

B_1_C_25_7
BEGIN_
कस्यचित्त्वथ कालस्य यक्षी पुत्रं व्यजायत |
मारीचं नाम दुर्धर्षं यः शापाद्राक्षसोऽभवत् ||१-२५-९_END
BEGIN_
"Then after sometime that yakshii Tataka delivered an indomitable son named Mareecha, who 
by curse became a demon. [1-25-9]_END

B_1_C_26_2
BEGIN_
सोऽहं पितुर्वचः श्रुत्वा शासनाद्ब्रह्मवादिनः |
करिष्यामि न संदेहस्ताटकावधमुत्तमम् || १-२६-४_END
BEGIN_
"Such as I am, I will undertake the primary duty of eliminating Tataka, according 
as the follower of father's words, and according to the instruction of a Brahma 
scholar, such as your are, without a doubt. [1-26-4]_END

B_1_C_18_54
BEGIN_
ब्रूहि यत् प्रार्थितं तुभ्यं कार्यमागमनं प्रति || १-१८-५६
इच्छाम्यनुगृहीतोऽहं त्वदर्थं परिवृद्धये |_END
BEGIN_
"You may tell me, entreating which work your arrival chanced here and I feel that I am indeed 
blessed and wish to make it happen to achieve results. [1-18-56b, 57a]_END

B_1_C_24_14
BEGIN_
तमुवाच महातेजा विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः || १-२४-१६
श्रूयतां वत्स काकुत्स्थ यस्यैतद्दारुणं वनम् |_END
BEGIN_
The resplendent and the great saint Vishvamitra then said to Rama, "I will tell you, oh, my 
boy Rama, whose is this wretched forest. [1-24-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_25_8
BEGIN_
सुन्दे तु निहते राम सागस्त्यमृषिसत्तमम् |
ताटका सह पुत्रेण प्रधर्षयितुमिच्छति || १-२५-१०_END
BEGIN_
"But when Sunda is eliminated by sage Agastya's curse, she that Tataka wished to retaliate 
that eminent sage along with her son Mareecha. [1-25-10]_END

B_1_C_26_3
BEGIN_
गोब्राह्मणहितार्थाय देशस्यास्य हिताय च |
तव चैवाप्रमेयस्य वचनं कर्तुमुद्यतः || १-२६-५_END
BEGIN_
"I am ready to effectuate the bidding of an inestimable sage like you, for the welfare 
of cows and Brahmans, and for the advantage of this province." So said Rama to sage 
Vishvamitra. [1-26-5]_END

B_1_C_18_55
BEGIN_
कार्यस्य न विमर्शं च गंतुमर्हसि सुव्रत || १-१८-५७
कर्ता चाहमशेषेण दैवतं हि भवान् मम |_END
BEGIN_
"It is unapt of you to deliberate about the feasibility of the work, oh, sage with blest vows, 
while I am the fulfiller of it without any reminder, since you are god to me, indeed. [1-18-57b, 
58a]_END

B_1_C_24_15
BEGIN_
एतौ जनपदौ स्फीतौ पूर्वमास्तां नरौत्तम || १-२४-१७
मलदाश्च करूषाश्च देवनिर्माणनिर्मितौ |_END
BEGIN_
"Once these were vast provinces, oh, best one among men, designed by gods and known as Malada 
and Karuusha. [1-24-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_25_9
BEGIN_
भक्षार्थं जातसंरम्भा गर्जन्ती साभ्यधावत |
आपतन्तीं तु तां दृष्ट्वा अगस्त्यो भगवानृषिः || १-२५-११
राक्षसत्वं भजस्वेति मारीचं व्याजहार सः |_END
BEGIN_
"With desperation brewing in her she roaringly rushed towards the sage as though to eat him 
away, and on seeing her rushing along with her son Mareecha towards him, the godly saint Agastya 
firstly cursed Mareecha saying, 'you will attain demon-hood.' [1-25-11, 12a]_END

B_1_C_26_4
BEGIN_
एवमुक्त्वा धनुर्मध्ये बध्वा मुष्टिमरिन्दमः |
ज्याघोषमकरोत्तीव्रं दिशः शब्देन नादयन् || १-२६-६_END
BEGIN_
Saying thus, Rama, the enemy-destroyer, clenched his left fist on the handgrip in 
the middle of the bow, and with the right he made a thunderous sound of the bowstring 
making all the directions to blast. [1-26-6]_END

B_1_C_18_56
BEGIN_
मम चायमनुप्राप्तो महानभ्युदयो द्विज |
तवागमनजः कृत्स्नो धर्मश्चानुत्तमो द्विज || १-१८-५८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Brahman, this is the great prosperity that bechanced on me, and this is propriety in 
its entirety that bechanced on me, as a result of your arrival. [1-18-58b, c]_END

B_1_C_24_16
BEGIN_
पुरा वृत्रवधे राम मलेन समभिप्लुतम् || १-२४-१८
क्षुधा चैव सहस्राक्षं ब्रह्महत्या समाविशत् |_END
BEGIN_
"Once upon a time, oh, Rama, mortal impurities of filth and hunger completely stained Indra 
when he eliminated demon Vritra, as he committed the sin of killing of a Brahman, where the 
demon Vritra was incidentally a Brahman. [1-24-18b, 19a]_END

B_1_C_25_10
BEGIN_
अगस्त्यः परमामर्षस्ताटकामपि शप्तवान् || १-२५-१२
पुरुषादी महायक्षी विरूपा विकृतानना |
इदं रूपं विहायाशु दारुणं रूपमस्तु ते || १-२५-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Highly infuriated sage Agastya even cursed Tataka saying, 'forthwith divested of this form 
of a beautiful female, oh, great yakshii, you shall become a man eater with your form distorted, 
face contorted, and shape monstrous.' [1-25-12b, 13]_END

B_1_C_26_5
BEGIN_
तेन शब्देन वित्रस्तास्ताटकावनवासिनः |
ताटका च सुसंक्रुद्धा तेन शब्देन मोहिता || १-२६-७_END
BEGIN_
By that sound the inhabitants of Tataka forest are startled, and even Tataka is 
stupefied by that sound, and she is intolerably infuriated at it. [1-26-7]_END

B_1_C_18_57
BEGIN_
इति हृदयसुखं निशम्य वाक्यम्
श्रुतिसुखमात्मवता विनीतमुक्तम् |
प्रथितगुणयशा गुणैर्विशिष्टः
परमऋषिः परमं जगाम हर्षम् || १-१८-५९_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of high-minded Dasharatha, said that way in all his humbleness, and those 
that are pleasant to ears as well to heart, he who is a renowned for his personal attributes 
and a reputed one by his exceptional qualities, that sublime sage Vishvamitra obtained high 
rejoice. [1-18-59]_END

B_1_C_24_17
BEGIN_
तमिन्द्रं मलिनं देवा ऋषयश्च तपोधनाः || १-२४-१९
कलशैः स्नापयामासुर्मलं चास्य प्रमोचयन् |_END
BEGIN_
"The gods and ascetically rich sages then started to bathe feculent Indra with their handy 
vessels for the riddance of his defilement. [1-24-19b, 20a]_END

B_1_C_25_11
BEGIN_
सैषा शापकृतामर्षा ताटका क्रोधमूर्च्छिता |
देशमुत्सादयत्येनमगस्त्याचरितं शुभम् || १-२५-१४_END
BEGIN_
"Frenzied by the curse and convulsed in fury she that Tataka is thus vandalising this auspicious 
province, in which sage Agastya once sauntered. [1-25-14]_END

B_1_C_26_6
BEGIN_
तं शब्दमभिनिध्याय राक्षसी क्रोधमूर्च्छिता |
श्रुत्वा चाभ्यद्रवत् क्रुद्धा यतः शब्दो विनिस्सृतः || १-२६-८_END
BEGIN_
She who is convulsed in anger to hear that sound gave attention to the direction 
wherefrom it emerged and she rancorously rushed thereto. [1-26-8]_END

B_1_C_24_18
BEGIN_
इह भूम्यां मलं दत्त्वा देवाः कारूषमेव च || १-२४-२०
शरीरजं महेन्द्रस्य ततो हर्षं प्रपेदिरे |_END
BEGIN_
"On giving filth and hunger emerged out of the body of Mahendra here on the earth then the 
gods were gladdened. [1-24-20b, 21a]_END

B_1_C_25_12
BEGIN_
एनां राघवदुर्वृत्तां यक्षीं परमदारुणाम् |
गोब्राह्मणहितार्थाय जहि दुष्टपराक्रमाम् || १-२५-१५_END
BEGIN_
"She that highly atrocious one is with horrific behaviour and malefic valour, hence you shall 
eliminate this yakshii for the welfare of Brahmans and cows. [1-25-15]_END

B_1_C_26_7
BEGIN_
तां दृष्ट्वा राघवः क्रुद्धां विकृतां विकृताननाम् |
प्रमाणेनातिवृद्धां च लक्ष्मणं सोऽभ्यभाषत || १-२६-९_END
BEGIN_
Raghava on seeing that monstrous-looking demoness with a distorted face and who 
by proportions is very gigantic, furthermore infuriated, spoke to Lakshmana. [1-26-9]_END

B_1_C_24_19
BEGIN_
निर्मलो निष्करूषश्च शुचिरिन्द्रो यथाभवत् || १-२४-२१
ततो देशस्य सुप्रीतो वरं प्रादादनुत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_
"As and when Indra was without desecration and hunger as well, and thus purified, then gladdened 
about this place he gave it an unexcelled boon. [1-24-21b, 22a]_END

B_1_C_25_13
BEGIN_
न ह्येनां शापसंसृष्टां कश्चिदुत्सहते पुमान् |
निहन्तुं त्रिषु लोकेषु त्वामृते रघुनन्दन || १-२५-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Excepting you there is none to eliminate her who is indomitably sheathed in a curse, oh, 
Raghu's legatee, and none in the three worlds can possibly brave her. [1-25-16]_END

B_1_C_26_8
BEGIN_
पश्य लक्ष्मण यक्षिण्या भैरवं दारुणं वपुः |
भिद्येरन् दर्शनादस्या भीरूणां हृदयानि च || १-२६-१०_END
BEGIN_
"Lakshmana, see that yakshii's grisly and ghastly physique, seeing which hearts 
of cowards are prone to burst. [1-26-10]_END

B_1_C_24_20
BEGIN_
इमौ जनपदौ स्फीतौ ख्यातिं लोके गमिष्यतः || १-२४-२२
मलदाश्च करूषाश्च ममांगमलधारिणौ |_END
BEGIN_
"These provinces that bear the impurity of my body shall become resourceful and they shall 
attain renown in world as Malada and Karusha." Thus Indra gave boon to this place. [1-24-22b, 
23a]_END

B_1_C_25_14
BEGIN_
न हि ते स्त्रीवधकृते घृणा कार्या नरोत्तम |
चातुर्वर्ण्यहितार्थाय कर्तव्यम् राजसूनुना || १-२५-१७_END
BEGIN_
"Compassion regarding the elimination of a female is ungermane, oh, best one among men, since 
a prince has to effectuate it intending the welfare of four categories of society. [1-25-17]_END

B_1_C_26_9
BEGIN_
एतां पश्य दुराधर्षां मायाबलसमन्विताम् |
विनिवृत्तां करोम्यद्य हृतकर्णाग्रनासिकाम् || १-२६-११_END
BEGIN_
" She is unstoppable and has magical powers, is't, you may see now how I will make 
her to readily retreat by lopping off her ears and the tip of nose. [1-26-11]_END

B_1_C_24_21
BEGIN_
साधु साध्विति तं देवाः पाकशासनमब्रुवन् || १-२४-२३
देशस्य पूजां तां दृष्ट्वा कृतां शक्रेण धीमता |_END
BEGIN_
"On observing the honour accorded by wise Indra to these places gods praised the controller 
of demon Paaka, namely Indra saying, 'splendid, splendid it is.' [1-24-23b, 24a]_END

B_1_C_25_15
BEGIN_
नृशंसमनृशंसं वा प्रजारक्षणकारणात् |
पातकं वा सदोषं वा कर्तव्यं रक्षता सदा || १-२५-१८_END
BEGIN_
"For the reason of protecting people, a protector always has to execute such deed, either 
it is ruthless or humane, sinful or vilifying. [1-25-18]_END

B_1_C_26_10
BEGIN_
न ह्येनामुत्सहे हन्तुं स्त्रीस्वभावेन रक्षिताम् |
वीर्यं चास्या गतिं चापि हन्यतामिति मे मतिः || १-२६-१२_END
BEGIN_
"As it is her femininess is protecting her, and I too I do not really attempt 
to kill her, but I intend to terminate her impudence and mobility. [1-26-12]_END

B_1_C_24_22
BEGIN_
एतौ जनपदौ स्फीतौ दीर्घकालमरिन्दम || १-२४-२४
मलदाश्च करूषाश्च मुदितौ धनधान्यतः |_END
BEGIN_
"For a long time these habitations Malada and Karuusha were affluent, oh, enemy subjugator 
Rama, and people were happy with wealth and provisions. [1-24-24b, 25a]_END

B_1_C_25_16
BEGIN_
राज्यभारनियुक्तानामेष धर्मः सनातनः |
अधर्म्यां जहि काकुत्स्थ धर्मो ह्यस्यां न विद्यते || १-२५-१९_END
BEGIN_
"To the nominee who bears the burden of kingdom this is the age-old duty, and hence oh, Rama, 
the legatee of Kakutstha, eliminate this infamy, as goodness is inevident in her, isn't it. 
[1-25-19]_END

B_1_C_26_11
BEGIN_
एवं ब्रुवाणे रामे तु ताटका क्रोधमूर्च्छिता |
उद्यम्य बाहू गर्जन्ती राममेवाभ्यधावत || १-२६-१३_END
BEGIN_
While Rama is still speaking that way, convulsed in anger Tataka roaringly rushed 
towards Rama alone, swinging her arms. [1-26-13]_END

B_1_C_24_23
BEGIN_
कस्यचित्त्वथ कालस्य यक्षी वै कामरूपिणी || १-२४-२५
बलं नागसहस्रस्य धारयन्ती तदा ह्यभूत् |
ताटका नाम भद्रं ते भार्या सुन्दस्य धीमतः || १-२४-२६
मारीचो राक्षसः पुत्रो यस्याः शक्रपराक्रमः |_END
BEGIN_
"Later at sometime, a yaksha female who is a guise changer at her wish, possessor of the strength 
of a thousand elephants, wife of clever Sunda, and she whose son is demon Mareecha, the 
one equal to Indra in his bravery, prevailed here, let you be safe Rama. [1-24-25b, 26, 27a]_END

B_1_C_25_17
BEGIN_
श्रूयते हि पुरा शक्रो विरोचनसुतां नृप |
पृथिवीं हन्तुमिच्छन्तीं मन्थरामभ्यसूदयत् || १-२५-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, the protector of people, we have heard that Indra once eliminated Manthara, the 
daughter of Virochana, when she wished to annihilate earth, haven't we. [1-25-20]_END

B_1_C_26_12
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रस्तु ब्रह्मर्षिर्हुंकारेणाभिभर्त्स्य ताम् |
स्वस्ति राघवयोरस्तु जयं चैवाभ्यभाषत || १-२६-१४_END
BEGIN_
But the Brahma-sage Vishvamitra daunted sounded her off and said to Rama and Lakshmana, 
"let you be safe, and be victorious." [1-26-14]_END

B_1_C_24_24
BEGIN_
वृत्तबाहुर्महाशीर्षो विपुलास्यतनुर्महान् || १-२४-२७
राक्षसो भैरवाकारो नित्यं त्रासयते प्रजाः |_END
BEGIN_
"That demon Mareecha is round shouldered, huge headed, cavernous mouthed, and gigantic bodied 
one, and he is always terrifying the people. [1-24-27b, 28a]_END

B_1_C_25_18
BEGIN_
विष्णुना च पुरा राम भृगुपत्नी पतिव्रता |
अनिन्द्रं लोकमिच्छन्ती काव्यमाता निषूदिता || १-२५-२१_END
BEGIN_
"And Rama, once Vishnu wiped out even the wife of sage Bhrigu and sage Shukracarya's mother 
when she wished the world to become one without a governing factor, namely Indra. [1-25-21]_END

B_1_C_26_13
BEGIN_
उद्धुन्वाना रजो घोरं ताटका राघवावुभौ |
रजो मेघेन महता मुहूर्तं सा व्यमोहयत् || १-२६-१५_END
BEGIN_
Flinging up dreadful dust on those two Raghavaa-s, Tataka baffled them for a while 
with a massive cloud of dust. [1-26-15]_END

B_1_C_24_25
BEGIN_
इमौ जनपदौ नित्यं विनाशयति राघव || १-२४-२८
मलदांश्च करूषांश्च ताटका दुष्टचारिणी |_END
BEGIN_
"And Raghava, that malevolent Tataka is always destroying the inhabitations at Malada and 
Karusha. [1-24-28b, 29a]_END

B_1_C_25_19
BEGIN_
एतैरन्यैश्च बहुभी राजपुत्रैर्महात्मभिः |
अधर्मसहिता नार्यो हताः पुरुषसत्तमैः |
तस्मादेनां घृणां त्यक्त्वा जहि मच्छासनान्नृप || १-२५-२२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, prince, these great souls and many other celebrated personalities have eliminated females 
who deported themselves with unrighteousness, and hence, oh, Rama, the protector of people, 
by my decree you leave off compassion and eliminate her." Thus said sage Vishvamitra to Rama 
regarding Tataka's elimination. [1-25-22]_END

B_1_C_26_14
BEGIN_
ततो मायां समास्थाय शिलावर्षेण राघवौ |
अवाकिरत् सुमहता ततश्चुक्रोध राघवः || १-२६-१६_END
BEGIN_
Then taking hold of witchery she inundated both the Raghava-s with highly torrential 
stone rain, by which Rama became indignant. [1-26-16]_END

B_1_C_24_26
BEGIN_
सेयं पन्थानमावृत्य वसत्यध्यर्धयोजने || १-२४-२९
अतैव च गन्तव्यं ताटकाया वनं यतः |_END
BEGIN_
"She lives about one and half yojana distance from here, and by which reason this became the 
forest of Tataka, owing to her gruesome activities, for that reason only a headway is to be 
made, to eradicate her and her activities. [1-24-29b, 30a]_END

B_1_C_26_15
BEGIN_
शिलावर्षं महत्तस्याः शरवर्षेण राघवः |
प्रतिवार्योपधावन्त्याः करौ चिच्छेद पत्रिभिः || १-२६-१७_END
BEGIN_
On forestalling her effusive stone storming with his arrow storm, Rama even mutilated 
both of her arms with arrows while she rushed towards them. [1-26-17]_END

B_1_C_24_27
BEGIN_
स्वबाहुबलमाश्रित्य जहीमां दुष्टचारिणीम् || १-२४-३०
मन्नियोगादिमं देशं कुरु निष्कण्टकं पुनः |_END
BEGIN_
"Depending upon the strength of your own self-confidence you have to eradicate this evildoer, 
and assigned by me you have to make this province free from thorniness. [1-24-30b, 31a]_END

B_1_C_26_16
BEGIN_
ततश्च्छिन्नभुजां श्रान्तामभ्याशे परिगर्जतीम् |
सौमित्रिरकरोत् क्रोधाद् हृतकर्णाग्रनासिकाम् || १-२६-१८_END
BEGIN_
With her arms severed and fatigued she started to roar extremely at the nearby, 
and then provoked Lakshmana made her to loose her ears and the tip of nose by cutting 
them off. [1-26-18]_END

B_1_C_24_28
BEGIN_
न हि कश्चिदिमं देशं शक्तो ह्यागन्तुमीदृशम् || १-२४-३१
यक्षिण्या घोरया राम उत्सादितमसह्यया |_END
BEGIN_
"Indeed, none is able to enter this sort of province, Rama, destroyed by the hazardous 
and invincible unearthly being who turned into a demoness, namely Tataka, hence you have to 
make the provinces habitable. [1-24-31b, 32a]_END

B_1_C_26_17
BEGIN_
कामरूपधरा सा तु कृत्वा रूपाण्यनेकशः |
अन्तर्धानं गता यक्षी मोहयन्ती स्वमायया || १-२६-१९
अश्मवर्षं विमुंचन्ती भैरवं विचचार सा ||_END
BEGIN_
That guise changer vanished after variously altering her aspects, and then on baffling 
them with her illusoriness and discharging stone storms she moved about appallingly. 
[1-26-19, 20a]_END

B_1_C_24_29
BEGIN_
एतत्ते सर्वमाख्यातं यथैतद्दारुणं वनम् |
यक्ष्या चोत्सादितं सर्वमद्यापि न निवर्तते || १-२४-३२_END
BEGIN_
"As to how that ghoulish Tataka destroyed this entire forest, rendering it as a devastated 
place, without refraining from it even today, all that is narrated." So said Vishvamitra to 
Rama. [1-24-32]_END

B_1_C_26_18
BEGIN_
