मुदितैर्मुनिशार्दूलैः प्रशस्तः कुशिकात्मजः |
निद्रामुपागमच्छ्रीमानस्तं गत इवांशुमान् || १-३४-२२_END
BEGIN_
Sage Vishvamitra is pleased when those tigerly sages have laude him, and then that 
magnificent sage Vishvamitra lapsed into the lap of sleep, as the sun lapses into 
lap of dusk for that day. [1-34-22]_END

B_1_C_36_4
BEGIN_
			पुरा रामकृतोद्वाहः शितिकण्ठो महातपाः || १-३६-५
			दृष्ट्वा च भगवान् देवीं मैथुनायोपचक्रमे |_END
BEGIN_
			"On his getting married to Uma, oh, Rama, the sublime-ascetic and bluish 
			throated god Shiva, as his throat became blue when he consumed poison 
			during the churning of Milky Ocean, at one time with a predilection 
			towards her he has started lovemaking with her. [1-36-5b, 6a]_END

B_1_C_34_22
BEGIN_
रामोऽपि सहसौमित्रिः किंचिदागतविस्मयः |
प्रशस्य मुनिशार्दूलं निद्रां समुपसेवते || १-३४-२३_END
BEGIN_
Even Rama with a little astonishment coming upon him, applauding that tigerly-sage, 
and glided into the lap of sleep along with Soumitri. [1-34-23]_END

B_1_C_35_15
BEGIN_
			अथ ज्येष्ठां सुराः सर्वे देवकार्यचिकीर्षया |
			शैलेन्द्रं वरयामासुर्गंगां त्रिपथगां नदीम् || १-३५-१७_END
BEGIN_
			"Later, all of the divinities intending to fulfil a divine purpose have 
			sought the lordly mountain Himavan to spare Ganga, who is scheduled 
			to become a tri-way-cruising river. [1-35-17]_END

B_1_C_36_5
BEGIN_
			तस्य संक्रीडमानस्य महादेवस्य धीमतः |
			शितिकण्ठस्य देवस्य दिव्यं वर्षशतं गतम् || १-३६-६
			न चापि तनयो राम तस्यामासीत्परंतप |_END
BEGIN_
			"While that sublime, sagacious and blue-throated God Shiva is in lovemaking, 
			oh, enemy-scorcher Rama, a hundred divine years have elapsed, even then 
			he had no son in her, namely Goddess Uma. [1-36-6b, c, 7]_END

B_1_C_35_16
BEGIN_
			ददौ धर्मेण हिमवांस्तनयां लोकपावनीम् |
			स्वच्छंदपथगां गंगां त्रैलोक्यहितकाम्यया || १-३५-१८_END
BEGIN_
			"With a righteous thinking and hopeful of the welfare in triadic world, 
			Himavan then spared his daughter Ganga whose flow is at her own volition. 
			[1-35-18]_END

B_1_C_36_6
BEGIN_
			सर्वे देवाः समुद्युक्ताः पितामहपुरोगमाः || १-३६-७
			यदिहोत्पद्यते भूतं कः तत्प्रतिसहिष्यति |_END


B_1_C_37_0
BEGIN_
			तप्यमाने तदा देवे सेन्द्राः साग्निपुरोगमाः |
			सेनापतिमभीप्सन्तः पितामहमुपागमन् || १-३७-१_END
BEGIN_
			"While god Shiva is undertaking ascesis thus, then the gods desiring an Army Chief 
			for celestial forces have arrived in the audience of Forefather Brahma, along 
			with Indra and keeping Fire-god at their fore." Sage Vishvamitra continued his 
			narration to Rama. [1-37-1]_END

B_1_C_35_17
BEGIN_
			प्रतिगृह्य त्रिलोकार्थं त्रिलोकहितकांक्षिणः |
			गंगामादाय तेऽगच्छन् कृतार्थेनान्तरात्मना || १-३५-१९_END
BEGIN_
			"Those divinities who are the well-wishers of the well-being of tri-world 
			welcomed Ganga, who is incidentally intended for the purpose of the 
			tri-world, and they came back to heaven fetching Ganga with them, with 
			a heartfelt joy for their purpose is fulfilled. [1-35-19]_END

B_1_C_36_7
BEGIN_
			अभिगम्य सुराः सर्वे प्रणिपत्येदमब्रुवन् || १-३६-८
			देव देव महादेव लोकस्यास्य हिते रत |
			सुराणां प्रणिपातेन प्रसादं कर्तुमर्हसि || १-३६-९_END
BEGIN_
			"All of the gods on approaching and paying their deference to Shiva 
			spoke this to him, 'oh, God of Gods, oh, one who is interested in the 
			welfare of these worlds, oh, Great-God, considering the supplication 
			of all gods it will be apt of you to bestow grace.' [1-36-8b, 9]_END

B_1_C_37_1
BEGIN_
			ततोऽब्रुवन् सुराः सर्वे भगवन्तं पितामहम् |
			प्रणिपत्य सुराः राम सेन्द्राः साग्निपुरोगमाः || १-३७-२_END
BEGIN_
			"On approaching the Forefather Brahma, oh, Rama, all of the celestials headed 
			by Fire-god and along with Indra have venerated and then spoke this to him. [1-37-2]_END

B_1_C_35_18
BEGIN_
			या चान्या शैलदुहिता कन्यासीद्रघुनंदन |
			उग्रं सा व्रतमास्थाय तपस्तेपे तपोधना || १-३५-२०_END
BEGIN_
			"The other daughter of Himavanta, oh, Raghu's descendent, that unmarried 
			girl namely Uma, she performed a rigorous sacrament taking hold of a 
			supreme devoutness as her ascesis itself is her wealth. [1-35-20]_END

B_1_C_36_8
BEGIN_
			न लोका धारयिष्यन्ति तव तेजः सुरोत्तम |
			ब्राह्मेण तपसा युक्तो देव्या सह तपश्चर || १-३६-१०
			त्रैलोक्यहितकामार्थं तेजस्तेजसि धारय |
			रक्ष सर्वानिमान् लोकान्नालोकं कर्तुमर्हसि || १-३६-११_END
BEGIN_
			" 'Worlds cannot capably bear your offspring born out of your effulgence, 
			oh, Supreme-God, hence you may practice yogic asceticism along with 
			your consort Goddess Uma in unison with Vedic postulates of Yoga, rather 
			than progeniture, and desiring the welfare of the three worlds you may 
			please retain your refulgent seed within your own radiance, thus protect 
			this universe, since it will not be apt of you to render it devoid of 
			worlds with the efflux of the unmanageable potence of yours .' So said 
			gods to Shiva. [1-36-10, 11]_END

B_1_C_37_2
BEGIN_
			येन सेनापतिर्देव दत्तो भगवता पुरा |
			स तपः परमास्थाय तप्यते स्म सहोमया || १-३७-३_END
BEGIN_
			" 'Oh, god Brahma, he who has hypothetically given a Chief of Celestial Army in 
			the form of his potence that god Shiva is undertaking a supreme ascesis, indeed 
			along with Goddess Uma. [1-37-3]_END

B_1_C_35_19
BEGIN_
			उग्रेण तपसा युक्तां ददौ शैलवरः सुताम् |
			रुद्रायाप्रतिरूपाय उमां लोकनमस्कृताम् || १-३५-२१_END
BEGIN_
			"As for Uma who is unified with her rigorous sacrament and who is adored 
			by all the world, that best one among mountains Himavanta gave such 
			a daughter to the unique god Rudra. [1-35-21]_END

B_1_C_36_9
BEGIN_
			देवतानां वचः श्रुत्वा सर्वलोकमहेश्वरः |
			बाढमित्यब्रवीत् सर्वान् पुनश्चेदमुवाच ह || १-३६-१२_END
BEGIN_
			"On listening the words of gods that Rarefied-God of Universe, namely 
			Shiva said, 'so be it,' and further spoke this to all of the gods, indeed. 
			[1-36-12]_END

B_1_C_37_3
BEGIN_
			यदत्रानंतरं कार्यं लोकानां हितकाम्यया |
			संविधत्स्व विधानज्ञ त्वं हि नः परमा गतिः || १-३७-४_END
BEGIN_
			" 'Looking forward for the welfare of the worlds, oh, knower of the procedures, 
			Brahma, you may order us clearly what is to be done next, as you alone are our 
			ultimate recourse. [1-37-4]_END

B_1_C_35_20
BEGIN_
			एते ते शैलराजस्य सुते लोकनमस्कृते |
			गंगा च सरितां श्रेष्ठा उमादेवी च राघव || १-३५-२२_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, Raghava, the prominent one among rivers namely Ganga and Uma Devi 
			as well, these are the two daughters of the king of mountains that are 
			highly revered by the world. [1-35-22]_END

B_1_C_36_10
BEGIN_
			धारयिष्याम्यहं तेजस्तेजस्येव सहोमया |
			त्रिदशाः पृथिवी चैव निर्वाणमधिगच्छतु || १-३६-१३_END
BEGIN_
			" 'I wish to bear my sperm in my virility and Uma in hers, let the immortals 
			and mortals as well, derive a perfect bliss. [1-36-13]_END

B_1_C_37_4
BEGIN_
			देवतानां वचः श्रुत्वा सर्वलोकपितामहः |
			सान्त्वयन् मधुरैर्वाक्यैस्त्रिदशानिदमब्रवीत् || १-३७-५_END
BEGIN_
			"On listening the words of gods, Brahma, the Forefather of all the worlds, soothingly 
			spoke this to the celestials with sweet words. [1-37-5]_END

B_1_C_35_21
BEGIN_
			एतत्ते सर्वमाख्यातं यथा त्रिपथगामिनी |
			खं गता प्रथमं तात गतिं गतिमतां वर || १-३५-२३_END
BEGIN_
			"Dear boy Rama with beautiful gait, as to how the triply coursing Ganga 
			has cruised to heaven in the first phase, I have related all about that 
			cruise to you. [1-35-23]_END

B_1_C_36_11
BEGIN_
			यदिदं क्षुभितं स्थानान्मम तेजो ह्यनुत्तमम् |
			धारयिष्यति कस्तन्मे ब्रुवन्तु सुरसत्तमाः || १-३६-१४_END
BEGIN_
			" 'But that part which has already stirred up from its place is irrestrainable, 
			as such, oh gods of eminence, you tell me who can contain that part 
			of the unexcelled potence.' So said Shiva to gods. [1-36-14]_END

B_1_C_37_5
BEGIN_
			शैलपुत्र्या यदुक्तं तन्न प्रजाः स्वासु पत्निषु |
			तस्या वचनमक्लिष्टं सत्यमेव न संशयः || १-३७-६_END
BEGIN_
			" 'What the Daughter of Mountain, namely Goddess Uma, has said that 'you shall 
			have no posterity in your own wives' is true and it cannot be decried, and it 
			is unambiguous too. [1-37-6]_END

B_1_C_35_22
BEGIN_
			सैषा सुरनदी रम्या शैलेन्द्रतनया तदा |
			सुरलोकं समारूढा विपापा जलवाहिनी || १-३५-२४_END
BEGIN_
			"As such, that marvellous and sinless daughter of the lordly mountain 
			Himavanta, ever-flowing in the form of water, ascended to the abode 
			of divinities and became devaganga , Divine 
			River. [1-35-24]_END

B_1_C_36_12
BEGIN_
			एवमुक्तास्ततो देवाः प्रत्यूचुर्वृषभध्वजम् |
			यत्तेजः क्षुभितं ह्यद्य तद्धरा धारयिष्यति || १-३६-१५_END
BEGIN_
			"Thus spoken by Shiva, then the gods in reply spoke to him whose banner 
			is Divine-Bull, namely Shiva, 'that part of the potence which has already 
			stirred up, the earth indeed endures that now. [1-3-15]_END

B_1_C_37_6
BEGIN_
			इयमाकाशगंगा यस्यां पुत्रं हुताशनः |
			जनयिष्यति देवानां सेनापतिमरिंदमम् || १-३७-७_END
BEGIN_
			" 'In whom the Fire-god can procreate an enemy-destroying Chief of Celestial Armies, 
			such an empyreal Ganga is there. [1-37-7]_END

B_1_C_38_0
BEGIN_
            तां कथां कौशिको रामे निवेद्य मधुराक्षरम् |
			पुन रेवापरं वाक्यं काकुत्स्थमिदमब्रवीत् || १-३८-१_END
BEGIN_
			Describing that legend of Kaartikeya to Rama, the descendent of Kaushi, 
			namely sage Vishvamitra has further spoken this best sentence worded 
			melodiously to Rama, the descendent of Kakutstha. [1-38-1]_END

B_1_C_36_13
BEGIN_
			एवमुक्तः सुरपतिः प्रमुमोच महाबलः |
			तेजसा पृथिवी येन व्याप्ता सगिरिकानना || १-३६-१६_END
BEGIN_
			"Thus said by the gods that Yogi of par excellence and the God of Gods, 
			Shiva, discharged his refulgent semen with which the earth together 
			with its mountains and forests is overspread. [1-36-16]_END

B_1_C_37_7
BEGIN_
			ज्येष्ठा शैलेन्द्रदुहिता मानयिष्यति तं सुतम् |
			उमायास्तद्बहुमतं भविष्यति न संशयः || १-३७-८_END
BEGIN_
			" 'The elder daughter King of Mountains, namely Ganga, will graciously welcome 
			the offspring from Fire-god, and that act of Ganga in welcoming the offspring 
			through Fire-god will also be pleasurable in many ways to the younger daughter 
			of King of Mountains, namely Uma, no doubt about it.' So said Brahma to all the 
			gods. [1-37-8]_END

B_1_C_38_1
BEGIN_
			अयोध्याधिपतिर्वीरः पूर्वमासीन्नराधिपः |
			सगरो नाम धर्मात्मा प्रजाकामः स चाप्रजः || १-३८-२_END
BEGIN_
			"Once there was a valiant and virtue-souled king of Ayodhya named Sagara, 
			who is without offspring, as such he was longing for offspring. [1-38-2]_END

B_1_C_36_14
BEGIN_
			ततो देवाः पुनरिदमूचुश्चापि हुताशनम् |
			आविश त्वं महातेजो रौद्रं वायुसमन्वितः || १-३६-१७_END
BEGIN_
			"Thereby the gods in their turn said even to Fire-god, 'you enter the 
			great-potence of Rudra along with Wind-god, lest that potence may annihilate 
			the earth and earthlings, because you can consume anything that comes 
			in touch with you. [1-36-17]_END

B_1_C_37_8
BEGIN_
			तच्छ्रुत्वा वचनं तस्य कृतार्था रघुनन्दन |
			प्रणिपत्य सुराः सर्वे पितामहमपूजयन् || १-३७-९_END
BEGIN_
			"On hearing those words of Brahma, oh, Rama, the delight of Raghu's dynasty, all 
			the gods have praisefully worshipped him, as their ends are achieved at the bidding 
			fair of Brahma. [1-37-9]_END

B_1_C_38_2
BEGIN_
			वैदर्भदुहिता राम केशिनी नाम नामतः |
			ज्येष्ठा सगरपत्नी सा धर्मिष्ठा सत्यवादिनी || १-३८-३_END
BEGIN_
			"The daughter of King of Vidarbha, renowned by name Keshini, is the 
			eldest wife of Sagara, and she was virtue-minded, and an advocate of 
			truth. [1-38-3]_END

B_1_C_36_15
BEGIN_
			तदग्निना पुनर्व्याप्तं संजातं श्वेतपर्वतम् |
			दिव्यं शरवणं चैव पावकादित्यसंनिभम् || १-३६-१८
			यत्र जातो महातेजाः कार्तिकेयोऽग्निसंभवः |_END
BEGIN_
			"And when Fire-god invaded that great-potence of Shiva it has emerged 
			as White-mountain, also thus it has become as a divine forest of reeds 
			equalling the Sun and Fire in its resplendence, wherefrom the highly 
			brilliant Kumara has emerged. [1-36-18, 19a]_END

B_1_C_37_9
BEGIN_
			ते गत्वा परमं राम कैलासं धातुमण्डितम् |
			अग्निं नियोजयामासुः पुत्रार्थं सर्वदेवताः || १-३७-१०_END
BEGIN_
			"On going to that supreme Mt. Kailash, oh, Rama, which is heaped up with many 
			ores, all of those gods have assigned the Fire-god to father a son. [1-37-10]_END

B_1_C_38_3
BEGIN_
			अरिष्ठनेमिदुहिता सुपर्णभगिनी तु सा |
			द्वितीया सगरस्यासीत् पत्नी सुमतिसंज्ञिता || १-३८-४_END
BEGIN_
			"The daughter of Arishtanemi, namely sage Kashyapa, and who is also 
			the sister of Garuda, the Divine-Eagle-vehicle of Vishnu, is the second 
			wife of Sagara, who is known by the name Sumati. [1-38-4]_END

B_1_C_36_16
BEGIN_
			अथोमां च शिवं चैव देवाः सर्षिगणास्तदा || १-३६-१९
			पूजयामासुरत्यर्थं सुप्रीतमनसस्ततः |_END
BEGIN_
			"Later on, the gods together with the assemblages of sages are well 
			pleased at heart as it has happened according to their prayer, thereby 
			they fulsomely adored Shiva and even Uma. [1-36-19b, 20a]_END

B_1_C_37_10
BEGIN_
			देवकार्यमिदं देव समाधत्स्व हुताशन |
			शैलपुत्र्यां महातेजो गंगायां तेज उत्सृज || १-३७-११_END
BEGIN_
			" 'Oh, Fire-god, you please coordinate the mission of gods, oh, great-resplendent 
			god of Fire, you may release the potence of Shiva, which you have contained so 
			far, in the daughter of King of Mountains, namely River Ganga.' Thus, all gods 
			have requested the Fire-god. [1-37-11]_END

B_1_C_38_4
BEGIN_
			ताभ्यां सह महाराजा पत्नीभ्याम् तप्तवांस्तपः |
			हिमवंतं समासाद्य भृगुप्रस्रवणे गिरौ || १-३८-५_END
BEGIN_
			"Reaching the Himalayan Mountains along with his two wives that 
			great King Sagara practised asceticism on a mountain called Brugu-prsravana 
			for progeny. [1-38-5]_END

B_1_C_36_17
BEGIN_
			अथ शैलसुता राम त्रिदशानिदमब्रवीत् || २०
			समन्युरशपत् सर्वान् क्रोधसंरक्तलोचना |_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, Rama, but the daughter of Himalayan Mountain, namely Uma, while 
			irefully saying this to the divinities she cursed them all with her 
			eyes reddened in anger. [1-36-20b, 21a]_END

B_1_C_37_11
BEGIN_
			देवतानां प्रतिज्ञाय गंगामभ्येत्य पावकः |
			गर्भं धारय वै देवि देवतानामिदं प्रियम् || १-३७-१२_END
BEGIN_
			"On assuring the gods that he will do his best, the Fire-god approached Ganga 
			entreating, 'Oh, Goddess Ganga, you verily bear pregnancy with the potence of 
			Shiva, since this is the select process of all the gods.' So said Fire-god to 
			River Ganga. [1-37-12]_END

B_1_C_38_5
BEGIN_
			अथ वर्षशते पूर्णे तपसाराधितो मुनिः |
			सगराय वरं प्रादाद् भृगुः सत्यवतां वरः || १-३८-६_END


B_1_C_36_18
BEGIN_
			यस्मान्निवारिता चाहं संगता पुत्रकाम्यया || १-३६-२१
			अपत्यं स्वेषु दारेषु नोत्पादयितुमर्हथ |_END
BEGIN_
			" 'Wherefore, I who am desirous of a son had been prevented from the 
			intimacy with my husband, therefore you shall be infecund to beget progeny 
			through your own wives. [1-36-21b, 22a]_END

B_1_C_37_12
BEGIN_
			इत्येतद्वचनं श्रुत्वा दिव्यं रूपमधारयत् |
			स तस्या महिमां दृष्ट्वा समंतादवकीर्यत || १-३७-१३_END
BEGIN_
			"On listening that sentence of Fire-god, River Ganga adopted a celestial form 
			readying herself, and on seeing her glorious mien the Fire-god seeped throughout 
			her. [1-37-13]_END

B_1_C_38_6
BEGIN_
			अपत्यलाभः सुमहान् भविष्यति तवानघ |
			कीर्तिं चाप्रतिमां लोके प्राप्स्यसे पुरुषर्षभ || १-३८-७_END
BEGIN_
			" 'Oh, merited one, you will achieve very admirable progeny, and 
			oh, best one among men, you will also acquire an unparalleled renown 
			in the world. [1-38-7]_END

B_1_C_36_19
BEGIN_
			अद्य प्रभृति युष्माकमप्रजाः सन्तु पत्नयः || १-३६-२२
			एवमुक्त्वा सुरान्सर्वान् शशाप पृथिवीमपि |_END
BEGIN_
			" 'And from now onwards you wives shall remain infertile...' and on 
			saying this way to all of the gods she also gave a curse to the earth. 
			[1-36-22, 23a]_END

B_1_C_37_13
BEGIN_
			समंततस्तदा देवीमभ्यषिंचत पावकः |
			सर्वस्रोतांसि पूर्णानि गंगाया रघुनन्दन || १-३७-१४_END
BEGIN_
			"The Fire-god then drenched River Ganga from all over with the potence of Shiva 
			which he contained so far, oh, Raghu's delight Rama, and every rill and channel 
			of Ganga is replete with it. [1-37-14]_END

B_1_C_38_7
BEGIN_
			एका जनयिता तात पुत्रं वंशकरं तव |
			षष्टिं पुत्रसहस्राणि ह्यपरा जनयिष्यति || १-३८-८_END
BEGIN_
			" 'One of your wives will mother a son who enriches your dynasty, oh, 
			dear sire, and the other mothers sixty thousand sons.' Said Sage Bhrigu 
			to Sagara. [1-38-8]_END

B_1_C_36_20
BEGIN_
			अवने नैकरूपा त्वं बहुभार्या भविष्यसि || १-३६-२३
			न च पुत्रकृतां प्रीतिं मत्क्रोधकलुषीकृता |
			प्राप्स्यसि त्वं सुदुर्मेधे मम पुत्रमनिच्छती || १-३६-२४_END
BEGIN_
			" 'Oh, Earth, your appearance shall be bizarre and you will be a wife 
			to many. And oh, verily base-minded earth, rendered sully by my anger 
			you shall have no gratification caused by the children as you are bigoted 
			against my son. [1-36-23b, 24]_END

B_1_C_37_14
BEGIN_
			तमुवाच ततो गंगा सर्वदेवपुरोगमम् |
			अशक्ता धारणे देव तेजस्तव समुद्धतम् || १-३७-१५
			दह्यमानाग्निना तेन संप्रव्यथितचेतना |_END
BEGIN_
			"River Ganga then spoke this to the Fire-god who is in the lead of all gods, 'oh, 
			god, I am incapable to bear up the rampant fervour of yours, and while being burnt 
			with the fire of god Shiva compounded with that of yours my life-force is very 
			highly tortured.' [1-37-15, 16a]_END

B_1_C_38_8
BEGIN_
			भाषमाणं महात्मानं राजपुत्र्यौ प्रसाद्य तम् |
			ऊचतुः परमप्रीते कृतांजलिपुटे तदा || १-३८-९_END
BEGIN_
			Highly gladdened are the daughters of kings of Vidarbha and Aristanemi, 
			i.e., the queens of Sagara, and on making palm-fold in supplication 
			at the sage who is speaking that way, and on gaining the grace of that 
			sage they spoke to him. [1-38-9]_END

B_1_C_39_0
BEGIN_
			विश्वामित्रवचः श्रुत्वा कथान्ते रघुनंदन |
			उवाच परमप्रीतो मुनिं दीप्तमिवानलम् || १-३९-१_END
BEGIN_
			On listening the narration of Vishvamitra, Rama, the delighter of Raghu's 
			dynasty is highly rejoiced, and at the end of the episode he spoke to 
			sage whose glow is fire like. [1-39-1]_END

B_1_C_36_21
BEGIN_
			तान् सर्वान् पीडितान् दृष्ट्वा सुरान् सुरपतिस्तदा |
			गमनायोपचक्राम दिशं वरुणपालिताम् || १-३६-२५_END
BEGIN_
			"That God of Gods Shiva becoming ill at ease to look at all of the distressed 
			gods, equally feeling small to convince his consort Uma, he has started 
			to journey towards the western quarter which is ruled by Rain-god. [1-36-25]_END

B_1_C_37_15
BEGIN_
			अथाब्रवीदिदं गङ्गां सर्वदेवहुताशनः || १-३७-१६
			इह हैमवते पार्श्वे गर्भोऽयं संनिवेश्यताम् |_END
BEGIN_
			"He who consumes fire-oblations on behalf of all the gods, that Fire-god seeing 
			the miserable condition of River Ganga then spoke this to her, ''you may lay away 
			that embryo here at the side of Himalayan Mountains.' So said Fire-god to River 
			Ganga. [1-37-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_38_9
BEGIN_
			एकः कस्याः सुतो ब्रह्मन् का बहून् जनयिष्यति |
			श्रोतुमिच्छावहे ब्रह्मन् सत्यमस्तु वचस्तव || १-३८-१०_END
BEGIN_
			" 'Which of us will carry one son, oh, Brahma-sage, and which of us 
			begets numerous sons, we two wish to listen about that, oh, Brahman, 
			let your word betide truth.' Thus, the queens of Sagara spoke to the 
			sage. [1-38-10]_END

B_1_C_39_1
BEGIN_
			श्रोतुमिच्छामि भद्रं ते विस्तरेण कथामिमाम् |
			पूर्वजो मे कथं ब्रह्मन् यज्ञं वै समुपाहरत् || १-३९-२_END
BEGIN_
			I am interested to listen this episode exhaustively, oh, Brahman, let 
			good betide you, how my ancestor Sagara had completed the Vedic-ritual, 
			really. [1-39-2]_END

B_1_C_36_22
BEGIN_
			स गत्वा तप आतिष्ठत् पार्श्वे तस्योत्तरे गिरेः |
			हिमवत्प्रभवे शृंगे सह देव्या महेश्वरः || १-३६-२६_END
BEGIN_
			"On going to the northern side of Himalayan Mountains, that God of Gods, 
			Shiva settled down in ascesis along with his consort Uma on the peak 
			of a mountain emerged from Himalayas. [1-36-26]_END

B_1_C_37_16
BEGIN_
			श्रुत्वा त्वग्निवचो गंगा तं गर्भमतिभास्वरम् || १-३७-१७
			उत्ससर्ज महातेजाः स्रोतोभ्यो हि तदानघ |_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, great-resplendent Rama, on hearing the words of Fire-god, oh, charming prince 
			Rama, River Ganga indeed ejected that great-radiant embryo of Shiva from all her 
			rills and channels. [1-37-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_38_10
BEGIN_
			तयोस्तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा भृगुः परमधार्मिकः |
			उवाच परमां वाणीं स्वच्छन्दोऽत्र विधीयताम् || १-३८-११_END
BEGIN_
			On listening their words the Sage Bhrigu spoke in a glorious tone, 'let 
			your freewill be brought to bear this issue'. [1-38-11]_END

B_1_C_39_2
BEGIN_
			तस्य तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा कौतूहलसमन्वितः |
			विश्वामित्रस्तु काकुत्स्थमुवाच प्रहसन्निव || १-३९-३
			श्रूयतां विस्तरो राम सगरस्य महात्मनः |_END
BEGIN_
			On listening the words of Rama that are inclusive of his inquisitiveness, 
			Sage Vishvamitra smilingly spoke to that descendent of Kakutstha, "oh, 
			Rama, let the episode of the great-souled Sagara be listened vividly." 
			Vishvamitra thus commenced to narrate that episode. [1-39-3, 4a]_END

B_1_C_36_23
BEGIN_
			एष ते विस्तरो राम शैलपुत्र्या निवेदितः |
			गङ्गायाः प्रभवं चैव शृणु मे सहलक्ष्मणः || १-३६-२७_END
BEGIN_
			"This is the legend of mountain's daughter, namely Goddess Uma vividly 
			narrated to you, oh, Rama, and now listen from me along with Lakshmana 
			about the emergence of Ganga. [1-36-27]_END

B_1_C_37_17
BEGIN_
			यदस्या निर्गतं तस्मात्तप्तजांबूनदप्रभम् || १-३७-१८
			कांचनं धरणीं प्राप्तं हिरण्यमतुलप्रभम् |_END
BEGIN_
			"Which refulgent embryo with the glitter of molten gold has emerged from River 
			Ganga is there that has reached earth, and from that the silver, and even the 
			gold with its matchless dazzle have emerged. [1-37-18]_END

B_1_C_38_11
BEGIN_
			एको वंशकरो वास्तु बहवो वा महाबलाः |
			कीर्तिमन्तो महोत्साहाः का वा कं वरमिच्छति || १-३८-१२_END
BEGIN_
			 'Whether one wants one son who enriches dynasty, or whether numerous 
			sons who will be highly energetic, highly renowned, and highly enthusiastic. 
			Who wants which boon from either of them?' Thus, the Sage gave them 
			the option. [1-38-12]_END

B_1_C_39_3
BEGIN_
			शंकरश्वशुरो नाम हिमवानिति विश्रुतः || १-३९-४
			विंध्यपर्वतमासाद्य निरीक्षेते परस्परम् |_END
BEGIN_
			The father-in-law of god Shankara who is well-known by the name of 
			Himavan sets eyes on Mt. Vindhya, which stands as loftily as Himalayas, 
			and those two mountains peer at each other. [1-39-4b, 5a]_END

B_1_C_37_18
BEGIN_
			ताम्रं कार्ष्णायसं चैव तैक्ष्ण्यादेवाभिजायत || १-३७-१९
			मलं तस्याभवत्तत्र त्रपु सीसकमेव च |
			तदेतद्धरणीं प्राप्य नानाधातुरवर्धत || १-३७-२०_END
BEGIN_
			"In that process, copper and iron are also generated from that combustion of fires 
			of Shiva and Fire-god, and the residua have become tin and lead, and thus that 
			embryo on reaching the earth has evolved itself into various other elements also. 
			[1-37-19b, 20]_END

B_1_C_38_12
BEGIN_
			मुनेस्तु वचनं श्रुत्वा केशिनी रघुनंदन |
			पुत्रं वंशकरं राम जग्राह नृपसंनिधौ || १-३८-१३_END
BEGIN_
			"On listening the words of the sage, oh, Rama, oh, delighter of Raghu's 
			dynasty, the first queen Keshini has chosen one son who enriches the 
			dynasty in the presence of King Sagara. [1-38-13]]_END

B_1_C_39_4
BEGIN_
			तयोर्मध्ये प्रवृत्तोऽभूद्यज्ञः स पुरुषोत्तम|| १-३९-५
			स हि देशो नरव्याघ्र प्रशस्तो यज्ञकर्मणि|_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, best one among men, Rama, that Vedic-ritual of Sagara started 
			in between those two mountains, namely Himalayas and Vindhya ranges, 
			and oh, tigerly-man Rama, that area is renowned for Vedic-rituals, isn't 
			it! [1-39-5b, 6a]_END

B_1_C_37_19
BEGIN_
			निक्षिप्तमात्रे गर्भे तु तेजोभिरभिरंजितम् |
			सर्वं पर्वतसंनद्धं सौवर्णमभवद्वनम् || १-३७-२१_END
BEGIN_
			"But, just when that embryo is laid down on Himalayan mountains, entire reed-garden 
			sprouted on that mountain is made brilliant by that glittering embryo and the 
			reed-garden itself has become golden. [1-37-21]_END

B_1_C_38_13
BEGIN_
			षष्टिं पुत्रसहस्राणि सुपर्णभगिनी तदा |
			महोत्साहान् कीर्तिमतो जग्राह सुमतिः सुतान् || १-३८-१४_END
BEGIN_
			"Sumati, the sister of mighty-winged Garuda and the second queen of 
			Sagara has then chosen sixty thousand sons with great enthusiasm and 
			high reputation. [1-38-14]_END

B_1_C_39_5
BEGIN_
			तस्याश्वचर्यां काकुत्स्थ दृढधन्वा महारथः || १-३९-६
			अंशुमानकरोत्तात सगरस्य मते स्थितः |_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, dear sire Rama, the grandson of Sagara and the son of exiled Asamanja 
			is Amshuman, oh, descendant of Kakutstha, which Anshuman's bow will 
			be unfaltering and who is a top-speeded chariot-rider, and he has escorted 
			ritual-horse released. [1-39-6b, 7a]_END

B_1_C_37_20
BEGIN_
			जातरूपमिति ख्यातं तदा प्रभृति राघव |
			सुवर्णं पुरुषव्याघ्र हुताशनसमप्रभम् |
			तृणवृक्षलतागुल्मं सर्वं भवति कांचनम् || १-३७-२२_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, tigerly-man, from then onwards the gold with its brilliance equalling that 
			of the Fire-god is renowned by the name of jaataruupa 
			, one that retains its birth-time form, and oh, Raghava, everything on the mountain, 
			say grass, trees, climbers, and shrubs, all have become golden. [1-37-22]_END

B_1_C_38_14
BEGIN_
			प्रदक्षिणमृषिं कृत्वा शिरसाभिप्रणम्य च |
			जगाम स्वपुरं राजा सभार्या रघुनन्दन || १-३८-१५_END
BEGIN_
			"On performing circumambulations to the Sage Bhrigu along with wives, 
			oh, Raghu's scion, also on reverencing him head-bent, the king Sagara 
			proceeded to his own city. [1-38-15]_END

B_1_C_39_6
BEGIN_
			तस्य पर्वणि तं यज्ञं यजमानस्य वासवः || १-३९-७
			राक्षसीं तनुमास्थाय यज्ञीयाश्वमपाहरत् |_END
BEGIN_
			And on the day of a sacred function called ukthyam 
			, Indra assumed the form of a demon and stole the ritual horse of the 
			chief of the ritual, namely Sagara. [1-39-7b, 8a]_END

B_1_C_37_21
BEGIN_
            तं कुमारं ततो जातं सेन्द्राः सहमरुद्गणाः |
			क्षीरसंभावनार्थाय कृत्तिकाः समयोजयन् || १-३७-२३_END
BEGIN_
			"Then for the boy who took birth from the embryo deposited in Himalayas, the Wind-gods 
			along with Indra have arranged Krittika stars to simultaneously suckle him. [1-37-23]_END

B_1_C_38_15
BEGIN_
			अथ काले गते तस्मिन् ज्येष्ठा पुत्रं व्यजायत |
			असमंज इति ख्यातं केशिनी सगरात्मजम् || १-३८-१६_END
BEGIN_
			When the time rolled by then the elder wife Keshini gave birth to the 
			son of Sagara who is reputed by the name Asamanja. [1-38-16]_END

B_1_C_39_7
BEGIN_
			ह्रियमाणे तु काकुत्स्थ तस्मिन्नश्वे महात्मनः ||१-३९-८
			उपाध्यायगणाः सर्वे यजमानमथाब्रुवन् |_END
BEGIN_
			While that ritual-horse of the great-souled Sagara is stolen, all the 
			congregations of the Ritviks, the religious-teachers, then spoke to 
			the chief propitiator, namely Sagara. [1-39-8b, 9a]_END

B_1_C_37_22
BEGIN_
			ताः क्षीरं जातमात्रस्य कृत्वा समयमुत्तमम् |
			ददुः पुत्रोऽयमस्माकं सर्वासामिति निश्चिताः || १-३७-२४_END
BEGIN_
			"Those Krittika stars have decided among themselves that 'this boy shall be the 
			son for all of us,' and on making such a best resolve they suckled the just born 
			boy. [1-37-24]_END

B_1_C_38_16
BEGIN_
			सुमतिस्तु नरव्याघ्र गर्भतुंबं व्यजायत |
			षष्टिः पुत्रसहस्राणि तुंबभेदाद्विनिःसृताः || १-३८-१७_END
BEGIN_
			But the second queen Sumati on part, oh, tigerly-man Rama, verily 
			delivered a round and long egg which is like a single gourd, and on 
			breaking it up sixty thousand sons are issued forth from that cucumber 
			like egg. [1-38-17]_END

B_1_C_39_8
BEGIN_
			अयं पर्वणि वेगेन यज्ञियाश्वोऽपनीयते ||१-३९-९
			हर्तारं जहि काकुत्स्थ हयश्चैवोपनीयताम् |_END
BEGIN_
			'Oh, Sagara,the descendent of Kakutstha, at this auspicious time the 
			ritual horse is hastily diverted, you kill him who stole the horse, 
			and let that horse be fetched'. [1-39-9b, 10a]_END

B_1_C_37_23
BEGIN_
			ततस्तु देवताः सर्वाः कार्तिकेय इति ब्रुवन् |
			पुत्रस्त्रैलोक्यविख्यातो भविष्यति न संशयः || १-३७-२५_END
BEGIN_
			"All the gods have then said, 'this boy will be renowned in all the three world 
			as Kaarthikeya, as Krittika-stars have suckled him, with any doubt.' [1-37-25]_END

B_1_C_40_0
BEGIN_
			देवतानां वचः श्रुत्वा भगवान्वै पितामहः |
			प्रत्युवाच सुसंत्रस्तान् कृतान्तबलमोहितान् || १-४०-१_END
BEGIN_
			"On hearing the words of gods, the esteemed Forefather Brahma spoke 
			to them, who are very highly scared, and bewildered by the might of 
			Sagara's sons for they are effectuating the end of all beings." Vishvamitra 
			thus continued his narration. [1-40-1]_END

B_1_C_38_17
BEGIN_
			घृतपूर्णेषु कुंभेषु धात्र्यस्तान् समवर्धयन् |
			कालेन महता सर्वे यौवनं प्रतिपेदिरे || १-३८-१८_END
BEGIN_
			The childminders brought up those siblings in vessels filled with ghee, 
			the clarified butter, and after a protracted time all of the children 
			have attained youthfulness. [1-38-18]_END

B_1_C_39_9
BEGIN_
			यज्ञश्च्छिद्रं भवत्येतत्सर्वेषामशिवाय नः || १-३९-१०
			तत्तथा क्रियतां राजन् यज्ञोऽच्छिद्रः क्रतुर्भवेत् |_END
BEGIN_
			'This hindrance in Vedic-ritual will become inauspicious for all of 
			us, thereby, oh, king, action may be taken as to how there can be no 
			fault in proceedings of the ritual.' The religious-teachers of Sagara 
			have advised him in this way. [1-39-10b, 11a]_END

B_1_C_37_24
BEGIN_
			तेषां तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा स्कन्नं गर्भपरिस्रवे |
			स्नापयन् परया लक्ष्म्या दीप्यमानं यथानलम् || १-३७-२६_END


B_1_C_40_1
BEGIN_
			यस्येयं वसुधा कृत्स्ना वासुदेवस्य धीमतः|
			महिषी माधवस्यैषा स एव भगवान् प्रभुः|| १-४०-२
			कापिलं रूपमास्थाय धारयत्यनिशं धराम् |
			तस्य कोपाग्निना दग्धा भविष्यन्ति नृपात्मजाः || १-४०-३_END
BEGIN_
			To whom this Mother Earth belongs in all her entirety, he is that 
			prescient Vasudeva, and she is also the consort of that Maadhava, and 
			that Vishnu eternally props up Mother Earth. Hence, that reverential 
			Vishnu donning the semblance of Sage Kapila will burn down the sons 
			of emperor Sagara to ashes in a fire of fury. [1-40-2, 3]_END

B_1_C_38_18
BEGIN_
			अथ दीर्घेण कालेन रूपयौवनशालिनः |
			षष्टिः पुत्रसहस्राणि सगरस्याभवंस्तदा || १-३८-१९_END
BEGIN_
			After a long time the sixty thousand sons of king Sagara have become 
			youthful, and handsome in their aspects. [1-38-19]_END

B_1_C_39_10
BEGIN_
			सोऽपाध्यायवचः श्रुत्वा तस्मिन्सदसि पार्थिवः ||१-३९-११
			षष्टिं पुत्रसहस्राणि वाक्यमेतदुवाच ह |_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing the words of religious-teachers that king Sagara indeed 
			spoke this much to his sixty thousand sons in that religious-council. 
			[1-39-11b, 12a]_END

B_1_C_37_25

BEGIN_
"On hearing that blessing of gods Krittika stars gave a wash to that excellently 
auspicious boy who is radiant like fire, and who slid down from the secretion of 
the womb of Ganga. [1-37-26]_END

B_1_C_40_2
BEGIN_
			पृथिव्याश्चापि निर्भेदो दृष्ट एव सनातनः |
			सगरस्य च पुत्राणां विनाशो दीर्घदर्शिनाम् ||१-४०-४_END
BEGIN_
			'Even the complete cleavage of the earth, and the complete ruination 
			of Sagara's sons as well, are envisaged by the providentially farsighted 
			ancients." So said Brahma to gods. [1-40-4]_END

B_1_C_38_19
BEGIN_
			स च ज्येष्ठो नरश्रेष्ठ सगरस्यात्मसंभवः |
			बालान् गृहीत्वा तु जले सरय्वा रघुनंदन || १-३८-२०
			प्रक्षिप्य प्रहसन् नित्यं मज्जतस्तान् निरीक्ष्य वै |_END
BEGIN_
			But, oh, best one among men, oh, Rama, the elder son of the king Sagara, 
			namely Asamanja, always used to grab and hurl children into the waters 
			of River Sarayu, and on seeing the drowning children he used to enjoy 
			with laughter. [1-38-20, 21a]_END

B_1_C_39_11
BEGIN_
			गतिं पुत्रा न पश्यामि रक्षसां पुरुषर्षभाः ||१-३९-१२
			मंत्रपूतैर्महाभागैरास्थितो हि महाक्रतुः |_END
BEGIN_
			'Oh, sons, I do not envisage any way in for demons into this ritual, 
			since oh, best ones among men, holy-sanctifiers who themselves are sanctified 
			by the Vedic-hymns are conducting this glorious Vedic-ritual, isn't 
			it. [1-39-12b, 13a]_END

B_1_C_37_26
BEGIN_
			स्कंद इत्यब्रुवन् देवाः स्कन्नं गर्भपरिस्रवात् |
			कार्तिकेयं महाबाहुं काकुत्स्थ ज्वलनोपमम् || १-३७-२७_END
BEGIN_
			"And gods called that boy, oh, Rama of Kakutstha, whose glow is like that of flaring 
			fire and who is ambidextrous as 'Skanda' for he slid down from the secretions 
			of a womb. [1-37-27]_END

B_1_C_40_3
BEGIN_
			पितामह वचः श्रुत्वा त्रयस्त्रिंशदरिन्दम |
			देवाः परमसंहृष्टाः पुनर्जग्मुर्यथागतम् || १-४०-५_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing the words of the Forefather Brahma all the thirty three 
			gods went away with utmost satisfaction, as they have came. [1-40-5]_END

B_1_C_38_20
BEGIN_
			एवं पापसमाचारः सज्जनप्रतिबाधकः || १-३८-२१
			पौराणामहिते युक्तः पित्रा निर्वासितः पुरात् |_END
BEGIN_
			This way, when that son Asamanja is with sinister activity, a torturer 
			of goodmen, and delighter in the undesirable activities towards citizens, 
			his father king Sagara expatriated him from the city. [1-38-21b, 22a]_END

B_1_C_39_12
BEGIN_
			तद्गच्छत विचिन्वध्वं पुत्रका भद्रमस्तु वः ||१-३९-१३
			समुद्रमालिनीं सर्वां पृथिवीमनुगच्छत |_END
BEGIN_
			'Oh, sons, you may therefore proceed to search for the horse and its 
			thief on entire earth as far as it is garlanded by the ocean, and safety 
			betides you all. [1-39-13]_END

B_1_C_37_27
BEGIN_
			प्रादुर्भूतं ततः क्षीरं कृत्तिकानामनुत्तमम् |
			षण्णां षडाननो भूत्वा जग्राह स्तनजं पयः || १-३७-२८_END
BEGIN_
			"Then an unexcelled milk instantly came forth from the breasts of the six Krittika-stars, 
			and becoming a six-faced one that boy too sucked that milk from the six Krittika-stars 
			at the same time. [1-37-28]_END

B_1_C_40_4
BEGIN_
			सगरस्य च पुत्राणां प्रादुरासीन्महास्वनः |
			पृथिव्यां भिद्यमानायां निर्घातसमनिःस्वनः || १-४०-६_END
BEGIN_
			When the sons of Sagara are digging the earth then there emerged an 
			unbearable noise similar to the crashing of a thunder. [1-40-6]_END

B_1_C_39_13
BEGIN_
			एकैकं योजनं पुत्रा विस्तारमभिगच्छत || १-३९-१४
			यावत्तुरगसंदर्शस्तावत्खनत मेदिनीम् |
			तमेव हयहर्तारं मार्गमाणा ममाज्ञया ||१-३९-१५_END
BEGIN_
			'Oh, sons, let each prince advance searching one square yojana of 
			earth, by my order you dig up the earth until the appearance of the 
			horse, while searching for the stealer of that horse. [1-39-14b, 15]_END

B_1_C_38_21
BEGIN_
			तस्य पुत्रोंऽशुमान्नाम असमंजस्य वीर्यवान् || १-३८-२२
			सम्मतः सर्वलोकस्य सर्वस्यापि प्रियंवदः |_END
BEGIN_
			But Asamanja's son is a valorous one, who by name is Anshuman, and who 
			is an acceptable one for all people and who fondly converses with all. 
			[1-38 -22b, 23a]_END

B_1_C_37_28
BEGIN_
			गृहीत्वा क्षीरमेकाह्ना सुकुमारवपुस्तदा |
			अजयत् स्वेन वीर्येण दैत्यसैन्यगणान्विभुः || १-३७-२९_END
BEGIN_
			"On sipping the milk just for one day he became an adolescent boy on that day 
			itself, and even though he is of delicate constitution as a boy, that taskmaster 
			triumphed over the army troops of demons by his own vigour. [1-37-29]_END

B_1_C_40_5
BEGIN_
			ततो भित्त्वा महीं सर्वां कृत्वा चापि प्रदक्षिणम् |
			सहिताः सगराः सर्वे पितरं वाक्यमब्रुवन् || १-४०-७_END
BEGIN_
			Then on hollowing the entire earth, and on making trips around her 
			without finding the horse, all of the sons of Sagara have come together 
			and on going to their father they spoke these words to him. [1-40-7]_END

B_1_C_41_0
BEGIN_
			पुत्रांश्चिरगतान् ज्ञात्वा सगरो रघुनंदन |
			नप्तारमब्रवीद्राजा दीप्यमानं स्वतेजसा || १-४१-१_END
BEGIN_
			"On observing that his sons have gone long time back in search of ritual-horse, 
			oh, Rama, king Sagara spoke this to his grandson, Amshuman, who is radiant 
			with his own self-resplendence." Thus Vishvamitra continued his narration 
			about Sagara. [1-41-1]_END

B_1_C_39_14
BEGIN_
			दीक्षितः पौत्रसहितः सोपाध्यायगणस्त्वहम् |
			इह स्थास्यामि भद्रं वो यावत्तुरगदर्शनम् ||१-३९-१६_END
BEGIN_
			'As for myself, I will stay here only along with my grandson, namely 
			Amshuman, and with the congregation of religious-teachers till the horse 
			appears, as I am under vow of the ritual.' Thus Sagara instructed to 
			his sixty thousand sons and stayed back at the ritual place. [1-39-16]_END

B_1_C_38_22
BEGIN_
			ततः कालेन महता मतिः समभिजायत || १-३८-२३
			सगरस्य नरश्रेष्ठ यजेयमिति निश्चिता |_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, best one among men, Rama, then after along time a decided thought 
			has occurred to king Sagara that, 'I shall perform a Vedic-ritual.'[1-38-23b, 
			24a]_END

B_1_C_37_29
BEGIN_
			सुरसेनागणपतिमभ्यषिंचन्महाद्युतिम् |
			ततस्तममराः सर्वे समेत्याग्निपुरोगमाः || १-३७-३०_END
BEGIN_
			"All of the celestial have then come together under the leadership of Fire-god 
			and they anointed that highly resplendent boy, Skanda, or Kaarthikeya, as the 
			Chief of Celestial Army troops. [1-37-30]_END

B_1_C_40_6
BEGIN_
			परिक्रांता मही सर्वा सत्त्ववन्तश्च सूदिताः |
			देवदानवरक्षांसि पिशाचोरगपन्नगाः || १-४०-८
			न च पश्यामहेऽश्वं तमश्वहर्तारमेव च |
			किं करिष्याम भद्रं ते बुद्धिरत्र विचार्यताम् || १-४०-९_END
BEGIN_
			'Entire earth is trekked and mighty beings like gods, demons, monsters, 
			evil-spirits, fiends, serpents, naga-s are also eliminated, but we have 
			not seen the ritual-horse or its stealer. What we have to do next. Let 
			a thought be given in this matter. Let safeness betide you.' So said 
			those princes to their father Sagara. [1-40-8, 9]_END

B_1_C_41_1
BEGIN_
			शूरश्च कृतविद्यश्च पूर्वैस्तुल्योऽसि तेजसा |
			पितृणां गतिमन्विच्छ येन चाश्वोऽपहारितः || १-४१-२_END
BEGIN_
			'You are brave one and completed your education in warfare, such as 
			you are, you are a coequal to your paternal-uncles in magnificence, 
			thus you search the course of your paternal uncles, also him by whom 
			the horse is stolen.' Thus King Sagara started speaking to his grandson 
			Amshuman. [1-41-2]_END

B_1_C_39_15
BEGIN_
			ते सर्वे हृष्टमनसो राजपुत्रा महाबलाः |
			जग्मुर्महीतलं राम पितुर्वचनयंत्रिताः ||१-३९-१७_END
BEGIN_
			Animated by their father's words those great-mighty princes enthusiastically 
			proceeded onto earth's surface in the preliminary round of search. [1-39-1]_END

B_1_C_38_23
BEGIN_
			स कृत्वा निश्चयं राजा सोपाध्यायगणस्तदा |
			यज्ञकर्मणि वेदज्ञो यष्टुं समुपचक्रमे || १-३८-२४_END
BEGIN_
			That king Sagara who is an expert in Vedic-procedures has then taken 
			a decision along with the assemblages of his religious-teachers insofar 
			as the procedures of the ritual are concerned, and he commenced to perform 
			the Vedic-ritual. [1-38-24b, c]_END

B_1_C_37_30
BEGIN_
			एष ते राम गंगाया विस्तरोऽभिहितो मया |
			कुमारसंभवश्चैव धन्यः पुण्यस्तथैव च || १-३७-३१_END
BEGIN_
			"This way, I have vividly narrated the legend of Ganga to you, oh, Rama, like 
			that the Divine and Meritorious legend of the emergence of Kumara, namely Skanda 
			is also narrated. [1-37-31]_END

B_1_C_40_7
BEGIN_
			तेषां तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा पुत्राणां राजसत्तमः |
			समन्युरब्रवीद्वाक्यं सगरो रघुनंदन || १-४०-१०_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing that sentence of his sons, oh, Rama, descendent of Raghu, 
			that exalted king Sagara infuriately spoke these words. [1-40-10]_END

B_1_C_41_2
BEGIN_
			अन्तर्भौमानि सत्त्वानि वीर्यवन्ति महान्ति च |
			तेषां त्वं प्रतिघातार्थं सासिं गृह्णीष्व कार्मुकम् || १-४१-३_END
BEGIN_
			The living beings in netherworlds of earth are intrepid and they 
			are extraordinary also, hence you take your bow along with your sword 
			to retaliate them in the event of their attacking you. [1-41-3]_END

B_1_C_39_16
BEGIN_
			गत्वा तु पृथिवीं सर्वमदृष्टा तं महबलाः |
			योजनायामविस्तारमेकैको धरणीतलम् |
			बिभिदुः पुरुषव्याघ्र वज्रस्पर्शसमैर्भुजैः ||१-३९-१८_END
BEGIN_
			But, oh, tigerly-man Rama, on going round the earth in its entirety 
			those great-mighty princes did not find that horse, then as said by 
			their father they mapped the earth to a unit of one square yojana for 
			each of them, and each of them hollowed out each and every area on the 
			surface of earth with their arms that have the touch of the diamonds. 
			[1-39-18]_END

B_1_C_37_31
BEGIN_
			भक्तश्च यः कार्तिकेये काकुत्स्थ भुवि मानवः |
			आयुष्मान् पुत्र पौत्रश्च स्कन्दसालोक्यतां व्रजेत् || १-३७-३२_END
BEGIN_
			"He who is a devotee of Kartikeyaa, oh, Rama of Kakutstha, he thrives with longevity, 
			also with sons, grandsons on this humanly earth in his mortal life, and on its 
			conclusion he becomes one with Skanda on journeying to Skanda's abode. [1-37-32]_END

B_1_C_40_8
BEGIN_
			भूयः खनत भद्रं वो विभेद्य वसुधातलम्
			अश्वहर्तारमासाद्य कृतार्थाश्च निवर्तत || १-४०-११_END
BEGIN_
			'Let the earth be dug further, may safety be with you, and verily 
			splitting open the surface of the earth you catch hold of the thief 
			of the horse, and on achieving your purpose you may return to me.' In 
			this way Sagara ordered his sons. [1-40-11]_END

B_1_C_41_3
BEGIN_
			अभिवाद्याभिवाद्यांस्त्वां हत्वा विघ्नकरानपि |
			सिद्धार्थः संनिवर्तस्व मम यज्ञस्य पारगः || १-४१-४_END
BEGIN_
			'On saluting them that are worthy for salutations, and on eliminating 
			them that are the causer of obstructions, you shall achieve your purpose 
			of tracking the ritual-horse, and thus you comeback safely and let my 
			Vedic-ritual be crossed over to the other shore of mortality by you.' 
			Thus king Sagara told his grandson Amshuman. [1-41-4]_END

B_1_C_39_17
BEGIN_
			शूलैरशनिकल्पैश्च हलैश्चापि सुदारुणैः |
			भिद्यमाना वसुमती ननाद रघुनंदन ||१-३९-१९_END
BEGIN_
			Mother Earth bewailed while she is ruptured with spears also that are 
			similar to thunderbolts, besides with very gruelling ploughs. [1-39-19]_END

B_1_C_40_9
BEGIN_
			पितुर्वचनमासाद्य सगरस्य महात्मनः |
			षष्टिः पुत्रसहस्राणि रसातलमभिद्रवन् || १-४०-१२_END
BEGIN_
			On catching up the words of their father, the great-souled Sagara, 
            his sixty thousand sons rushed towards the surface of the rasaatala, 
            the netherworld. [1-40-12]_END

B_1_C_41_4
BEGIN_
			एवमुक्तो ंऽशुमान् सम्यक्सगरेण महात्मना |
			धनुरादाय खड्गं च जगाम लघुविक्रमः || १-४१-५_END
BEGIN_
			When the great-souled king Sagara has thoroughly said in this way, 
			that adroitly agile Amshuman proceeded wielding a bow and a sword. [1-41-5]_END

B_1_C_39_18
BEGIN_
			नागानां वध्यमानानामसुराणां च राघव |
			राक्षसानां च दुर्धर्षः सत्त्वानां निनदोऽभवत् ||१-३९-२०_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, Raghava, there emerged an unbearable rumpus from the serpents, 
			asura-s, demons, and other beings living underneath the surface of earth, 
			while they are killed during hollowing the earth. [1-39-20]_END

B_1_C_40_10
BEGIN_
			खन्यमाने ततस्तस्मिन् ददृशुः पर्वतोपमम् |
			दिशागजं विरूपाक्षं धारयन्तं महीतलम् || १-४०-१३_END
BEGIN_
			While digging the earth there they beheld a mountain similar easterly 
			elephant named Viruupaaksha, which is bearing the eastern side of earth's 
			surface on its head. [1-40-13]_END

B_1_C_41_5
BEGIN_
			स खातं पितृभिर्मार्गमन्तर्भौमं महात्मभिः |
			प्रापद्यत नरश्रेष्ठ तेन राज्ञाभिचोदितः || १-४१-६_END
BEGIN_
			Motivated by the King Sagara, oh, Rama, the best one among men, Amshuman 
			progressed on the walkway that was hollowed out by his great-souled 
			paternal-uncles inside the earth. [1-41-6]_END

B_1_C_39_19
BEGIN_
			योजनानां सहस्राणि षष्टिं तु रघुनंदन |
			बिभिदुर्धरणीं राम रसातलमनुत्तमम् ||१-३९-२१_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, Rama, the legatee of Raghu's dynasty, thus sixty thousand square 
			yojana-s of the earth is dug over, so as to make the earth's outermost 
			plane as the unsurpassed rasaatala, the 
			sixth subterranean and the nethermost plane. [1-39-21]_END

B_1_C_40_11
BEGIN_
			सपर्वतवनां कृत्स्नां पृथिवीं रघुनंदन |
			धारयामास शिरसा विरूपाक्षो महागजः || १-४०-१४_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, Rama, the legatee of Raghu, that great easterly elephant Viruupaaksha 
			is bearing the entire eastern earth along with its mountains and forests 
			on its head. [1-40-14]_END

B_1_C_41_6
BEGIN_
			देवदानवरक्षोभिः पिशाचपतगोरगैः |
			पूज्यमानं महातेजा दिशागजमपश्यत || १-४१-७_END
BEGIN_
			And he that resplendent Amshuman beheld one of the four directional 
			elephant of the earth which is being venerated by gods, monsters, demons, 
			imps, vultures and serpents. [1-41-7]_END

B_1_C_39_20
BEGIN_
			एवं पर्वतसंबाधं जम्बूद्वीपं नृपात्मजाः |
			खनन्तो नृपशार्दूल सर्वतः परिचक्रमुः ||१-३९-२२_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, the tigerly king Rama, the sons of Sagara have endeavoured everywhere 
			digging over the Jambu Island which is verily congested with mountains 
			in this way. [1-39-22]_END

B_1_C_42_0
BEGIN_
			कालधर्मं गते राम सगरे प्रकृतीजनाः |
			राजानं रोचयामासुरंशुमन्तं सुधार्मिकम् || १-४२-१_END
BEGIN_
			"When King Sagara passed away owing to the irrefutable virtue of Time, 
			the ministers and subjects of that kingdom are predisposed towards the 
			highly honourable Amshuman to become their king and they enthroned him 
			accordingly." Thus Vishvamitra continued narration about the predecessors 
			of Rama. [1-42-1]_END

B_1_C_40_12
BEGIN_
			यदा पर्वणि काकुत्स्थ विश्रमार्थं महागजः |
			खेदाच्चालयते शीर्षं भूमिकंपस्तदा भवेत् || १-४०-१५_END
BEGIN_
			On certain occasions, oh, Rama of Kakutstha, when that great-elephant 
			moves its head desiring respite in tiresomeness then earthquakes will 
			occur on earth. [1-40-15]_END

B_1_C_41_7
BEGIN_
			स तं प्रदक्षिणं कृत्वा पृष्ट्वा चैव निरामयम् |
			पितृन् स परिपप्रच्छ वाजिहर्तारमेव च || १-४१-८_END
BEGIN_
			On circumambulating that elephant in supplication, and even on enquiring 
			after its well-being, he that Amshuman has enquired in detail with it 
			for his paternal-uncles and even about the robber of the ritual-horse. 
			[1-41-8]_END

B_1_C_39_21
BEGIN_
			ततो देवाः सगंधर्वाः सासुराः सहपन्नगाः |
			संभ्रांतमनसः सर्वे पितामहमुपागमन् ||१-३९-२३_END
BEGIN_
			All the gods along with gandharva-s, asura-s, and reptiles who are 
			distraught at heart for the plight of earth have approached the Forefather, 
			Brahma. [1-39-23]_END

B_1_C_42_1
BEGIN_
			स राजा सुमहानासीदंशुमान् रघुनंदन |
			तस्य पुत्रो महानासीद्दिलीप इति विश्रुतः || १-४२-२_END
BEGIN_
			"He that Amshuman turned out to be a very great king, and oh, Rama of 
			Raghu's delight, he begot a marvellous son who is renowned as Dileepa. 
			[1-42-2]_END

B_1_C_40_13
BEGIN_
			ते तं प्रदक्षिणं कृत्वा दिशापालं महागजम् |
			मानयन्तो हि ते राम जग्मुर्भित्त्वा रसातलम् || १-४०-१६_END
BEGIN_
			They circumambulated the great elephant in supplication, oh Rama, and 
			on worshipping that elephant which is the protector of easterly direction 
			they proceeded to netherworld duly splitting the earth. [1-40-16]_END

B_1_C_41_8
BEGIN_
			दिशागजस्तु तच्छ्रुत्वा प्रत्युवाच महामतिः |
			आसमंज कृतार्थस्त्वं सहाश्वः शीघ्रमेष्यसि || १-४१-९_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing that enquiry of Amshuman that directional elephant with 
			great perception replied on its part saying, 'oh Amshuman, son of Asamanja, 
			on achieving your mission you will return expeditiously along with the 
			horse'. [1-41-9]_END

B_1_C_39_22
BEGIN_
			ते प्रसाद्य महात्मानं विषण्णवदनास्तदा |
			ऊचुः परमसंत्रस्ताः पितामहमिदं वचः ||१-३९-२४_END
BEGIN_
			They the gods who are very highly scared, and who are chap-fallen, 
			then spoke this sentence to the great-souled Forefather Brahma on gaining 
			his grace. [1-39-24]_END

B_1_C_40_14
BEGIN_
			ततः पूर्वां दिशं भित्त्वा दक्षिणां बिभिदुः पुनः |
			दक्षिणस्यामपि दिशि ददृशुस्ते महागजम् || १-४०-१७
			महापद्मं महात्मानं सुमहत्पर्वतोपमम् |
			शिरसा धारयन्तं गां विस्मयं जग्मुरुत्तमम् || १-४०-१८_END
BEGIN_
			After splitting the eastern direction then they split opened the southern 
			direction, and even in southern direction they beheld an elephant that 
			is similar to a very great mountain, and that is sustaining southerly 
			side of earth on its head, and on seeing that mammoth elephant of venerable 
			character, namely Mahapadma, they went into an inordinate astonishment. 
			[1-40-17, 18]_END

B_1_C_42_2
BEGIN_
			तस्मै राज्यं समादिश्य दिलीपे रघुनंदन |
			हिमवच्छिखरे रम्ये तपस्तेपे सुदारुणम् || १-४२-३_END
BEGIN_
			Assigning the kingdom to Dileepa, oh, Rama of Raghu's dynasty, Amshuman 
			undertook very stern ascesis on a pleasant peak of Himalayas desiring 
			the descent of River Ganga to earth. [1-42-3]_END

B_1_C_41_9
BEGIN_
			तस्य तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा सर्वानेव दिशागजान् |
			यथाक्रमं यथान्यायं प्रष्टुं समुपचक्रमे || १-४१-१०_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing that word of that directional elephant he departed from 
			there, and on sequentially reaching other directional elephants that 
			are abiding in other directions of earth, he commenced to ask the same 
			enquiry which he made with the first, according to the positioning of 
			elephants in directions, and according to the established procedures 
			of their venerability. [1-41-10]_END

B_1_C_39_23
BEGIN_
			भगवन् पृथिवी सर्वा खन्यते सगरात्मजैः |
			बहवश्च महात्मानो वध्यन्ते जलचारिणः ||१-३९-२५_END
BEGIN_
			'Oh, god Brahma, the sons of Sagara are digging entire earth, thus 
			aquatic beings and many great-souls are being destroyed. [1-39-25]_END

B_1_C_42_3
BEGIN_
			द्वात्रिंशच्च सहस्राणि वर्षाणि सुमहायशाः |
			तपोवनगतो राजा स्वर्गं लेभे तपोधनः || १-४२-४_END
BEGIN_
			On practising ascesis in ascetic-woods for thirty-two thousand years 
			that highly renowned king Amshuman achieved heaven as he acquired only 
			the wealth of practising the ascesis. [1-42-4]_END

B_1_C_40_15
BEGIN_
			ते तं प्रदक्षिणं कृत्वा सगरस्य महात्मनः |
			षष्टिः पुत्रसहस्राणि पश्चिमां बिभिदुर्दिशम् || १-४०-१९_END
BEGIN_
			On circumabulating that elephant Mahaapada in supplication, they the 
			sixty thousand sons of great-souled Sagara scooped out the westerly 
			direction. [1-40-19]_END

B_1_C_41_10
BEGIN_
			तैश्च सर्वैर्दिशापालैर्वाक्यज्ञैर्वाक्यकोविदैः |
			पूजितः सहयश्चैव गन्तासीत्यभिचोदितः || १-४१-११_END
BEGIN_
			All the elephants that safeguard the directions of earth which have 
			the faculties of articulation and eloquence have adored Amshuman and 
			motivated him by saying, 'you will be going from here taking the horse.' 
			[1-41-11]_END

B_1_C_39_24
BEGIN_
			अयं यज्ञ हरोऽस्माकमनेनाश्वोऽपनीयते |
			इति ते सर्वभूतानि हिंसन्ति सगरात्मजाः ||१-३९-२६_END
BEGIN_
            " 'This one is the destroyer of our ritual... this one has carried off 
			our ritual horse...' thinking thus and suspecting everyone those sons 
			of Sagara are torturing all the living beings.' Thus all the gods have 
			appealed to Brahma." So said Sage Vishvamitra to Rama and others. [1-39-26]_END

B_1_C_40_16
BEGIN_
			पश्चिमायामपि दिशि महांतमचलोपमम् |
			दिशागजं सौमनसं ददृशुस्ते महाबलाः || १-४०-२०_END
BEGIN_
			Even in the westerly direction those great mighty sons of Sagara beheld 
			an infinite and mountain similar elephant of western direction, called 
			Sumanasa. [1-40-20]_END

B_1_C_42_4
BEGIN_
			दिलीपस्तु महातेजाः श्रुत्वा पैतामहं वधम् |
			दुःखोपहतया बुद्ध्या निश्चयं नाध्यगच्छत || १-४२-५_END
BEGIN_
			The great resplendent Dileepa on hearing the elimination of his grandfathers, 
			the sixty thousand sons of Sagara at the hand of sage Kapila, and with 
			a mind that is marred by the plight of his father Amshuman in absolving 
			the souls of Sagara's sons, he that Dileepa could not arrive at any 
			decision concerning the descent of Ganga. [1-42-5]_END

B_1_C_41_11
BEGIN_
			तेषां तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा जगाम लघुविक्रमः |
			भस्मराशीकृता यत्र पितरस्तस्य सागराः || १-४१-१२_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing that common blessing of all the directional-elephants, he 
			that nimble-footed Amshuman has gone to the place where his paternal-uncles, 
			sons of Sagara, were rendered as mounds of ashes. [1-41-12]_END

B_1_C_40_17
BEGIN_
			ते तं प्रदक्षिणं कृत्वा पृष्ट्वा चापि निरामयम् |
			खनंतः समुपक्रांता दिशं सोमवतीं तदा || १-४०-२१_END
BEGIN_
			Circumambulating that elephant namely Sumanasa in western side, and 
			even on asking about its well-being, then they reached the northern 
			direction duly digging the earth. [1-40-21]_END

B_1_C_42_5
BEGIN_
			कथं गंगावतरणं कथं तेषां जलक्रिया |
			तारयेयं कथं चैतानिति चिंतापरोऽभवत् || १-४२-६_END
BEGIN_
			Dileepa became worried as to how River Ganga is to be alighted onto 
			earth from heaven, how water-oblations are to be offered for the souls 
			of Sagara's sons, and how to cross them, the souls, over this mortal 
			world. [1-42-6]_END

B_1_C_41_12
BEGIN_
			स दुःखवशमापन्नस्त्वसमंजसुतस्तदा |
			चुक्रोश परमार्तस्तु वधात्तेषां सुदुःखितः || १-४१-१३_END
BEGIN_
			But he on whom the control of anguish has chanced for not physically 
			seeing his paternal-uncles, that son of Asamanja then wept, as he is 
			highly agonised and extremely anguished at their destruction. [1-41-13]_END

B_1_C_40_18
BEGIN_
			उत्तरस्यां रघुश्रेष्ठ ददृशुर्हिमपाण्डुरम् |
			भद्रं भद्रेण वपुषा धारयन्तं महीमिमाम् || १-४०-२२_END
BEGIN_
			In the northern direction, oh, Rama, they beheld Bhadra, a snow-white 
			elephant with an auspicious body bearing northern side of this earth. 
			[1-40-22]_END

B_1_C_42_6
BEGIN_
			तस्य चिंतयतो नित्यं धर्मेण विदितात्मनः |
			पुत्रो भगीरथो नाम जज्ञे परमधार्मिकः ||१-४२-७_END
BEGIN_
			To him who is self-mortified and who is always thinking righteously 
			about the alight of Ganga onto earth, to such a Dileepa a most-virtuous 
			son is born who is renowned by his name Bhageeratha. [1-42-7]_END

B_1_C_41_13
BEGIN_
			यज्ञियं च हयं तत्र चरन्तमविदूरतः |
			ददर्श पुरुषव्याघ्रो दुःखशोकसमन्वितः || १-४१-१४_END
BEGIN_
			That tigerly-man Amshuman who is overwhelmed by agony and anguish, 
			also beheld there the horse of Vedic-ritual that is grazing nearby. 
			[1-41-14]_END

B_1_C_40_19
BEGIN_
			समालभ्य ततः सर्वे कृत्वा चैनं प्रदक्षिणम् |
			षष्टिः पुत्रसहस्राणि बिभिदुर्वसुधातलम् || १-४०-२३_END
BEGIN_
			On touching that elephant reverently and also circumambulating it, 
			those sixty thousands sons of Sagara further burrowed to the surface 
			of the earth. [1-40-23]_END

B_1_C_42_7
BEGIN_
			दिलीपस्तु महातेजा यज्ञैर्बहुभिरिष्टवान् |
			त्रिंशद्वर्षसहस्राणि राजा राज्यमकारयत् || १-४२-८_END
BEGIN_
			That great-resplendent king Dileepa on his part performed numerous 
			Vedic-rituals, and he ruled the kingdom for thirty thousand years - 
			to the delight of each of his subjects, but could not find a way to 
			fetch Ganga. [1-42-8]_END

B_1_C_41_14
BEGIN_
			स तेषां राजपुत्राणां कर्तुकामो जलक्रियाम् |
			स जलार्थं महातेजा न चापश्यज्जलाशयम् || १-४१-१५_END
BEGIN_
			When he that great resplendent Amshuman wanted to offer obsequial waters 
			to the departed sons of Sagara and searched for water he has not found 
			any fount of water. [1-41-15]_END

B_1_C_40_20
BEGIN_
			ततः प्रागुत्तरां गत्वा सागराः प्रथितां दिशम् |
			रोषादभ्यखनन्सर्वे पृथिवीं सगरात्मजाः || १-४०-२४_END
BEGIN_
			The sons of Sagara have then gone to the auspicious northeast direction,
			iishaana-digbhaaga, Shiva-sthaana, and 
			all those sons of Sagara have tunnelled the earth rancorously. [1-40-24]_END

B_1_C_42_8
BEGIN_
			अगत्वा निश्चयं राजा तेषामुद्धरणं प्रति |
			व्याधिना नरशार्दूल कालधर्ममुपेयिवान् || १-४२-९_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, tigerly-man Rama, that king Dileepa by not attaining any choice 
			towards the uplifting the souls of his grandparents to heaven by bringing 
			Ganga to earth, he took to illness, and he attained the ultimate virtue 
			of Time, namely the demise. [1-42-9]_END

B_1_C_41_15
BEGIN_
			विसार्य निपुणां दृष्टिं ततोऽपश्यत् खगाधिपम् |
			पितृणां मातुलं राम सुपर्णमनिलोपमम् || १-४१-१६_END
BEGIN_
			Spanning his expert glances, oh, Rama, he then saw the rapid-winged 
			king of birds, namely Garuda, the Eagle-vehicle of Vishnu, who is the 
			maternal uncle of his father and other paternal-uncles, and whose flight 
			will be similar to that of the Wind-god. [1-41-16]_END

B_1_C_40_21
BEGIN_
			ते तु सर्वे महत्मानो भीमवेगा महबलाः |
			ददृशुः कपिलं तत्र वासुदेवं सनातनम् || १-४०-२५
			हयं च तस्य देवस्य चरन्तमविदूरतः |
			प्रहर्षमतुलं प्राप्ताः सर्वे ते रघुनंदन || १-४०-२६_END


B_1_C_42_9
BEGIN_
			इन्द्रलोकं गतो राजा स्वार्जितेनैव कर्मणा |
			राज्ये भगीरथं पुत्रमभिषिच्य नरर्षभः || १-४२-१०_END
BEGIN_
			That best one among men, namely king Dileepa, on anointing his son 
			Bhageeratha in the kingdom went to the abode of Indra, namely the heaven, 
			only by his self-acquired merits of deeds. [1-42-10]_END

B_1_C_41_16
BEGIN_
			स चैनमब्रवीद्वाक्यं वैनतेयो महाबलः |
			मा शुचः पुरुषव्याघ्र वधोऽयं लोकसम्मतः || १-४१-१७_END
BEGIN_
			That great-mighty son of Lady Vinata, namely Garuda, also spoke this 
			word to Amshuman, 'do not bemoan, oh, tigerly-man, this eradication 
			of your paternal-uncles is worthwhile to the worlds'. [1-41-17]_END

B_1_C_40_22
BEGIN_
			ते तं हयहरं ज्ञात्वा क्रोधपर्याकुलेक्षणाः |
			खनित्रलांगलधरा नानावृक्षशिलाधराः || १-४०-२७
			अभ्यधावन्त संक्रुद्धास्तिष्ठ तिष्ठेति चाब्रुवन् |_END
BEGIN_
			The eyes of the princes are agitated in fury in construing the sage 
			Kapila as the stealer of ritual-horse, and they furiously dashed towards 
			him wielding crowbars, ploughs, and various trees and boulders, and 
			shouting at him, 'stay, stay.' [1-40-27, 28a]_END

B_1_C_42_10
BEGIN_
			भगीरथस्तु राजर्षिर्धार्मिको रघुनंदन |
			अनपत्यो महाराजः प्रजाकामः स च प्रजाः || १-४२-११_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, Rama, the legatee of Raghu, but on his part that self-righteous 
			and kingly-sage Bhageeratha is childless, and that great king longed-for 
			offspring. [1-42-11]_END

B_1_C_43_0
BEGIN_
			देवदेवे गते तस्मिन् सोंऽगुष्ठाग्रनिपीडिताम् |
			कृत्वा वसुमतीं राम वत्सरं समुपासत || १-४३-१_END
BEGIN_
			"When the god of gods Brahma left from there Bhageeratha stood on the 
			tip of his big-toe praying for the mercy of Lord Shiva for one year, 
			while that tip of his big-toe pressurised the earth." Thus Vishvamitra 
			continued his narration about Bhageeratha's effort to bring Ganga to 
			earth. [1-43-1]_END

B_1_C_41_17
BEGIN_
			कपिलेनाप्रमेयेण दग्धा हीमे महाबलाः |
			सलिलं नार्हसि प्राज्ञ दातुमेषां हि लौकिकम् || १-४१-१८_END
BEGIN_
			In fact, Kapila, the Imponderable Sage, has burnt down those great-mighty 
			paternal-uncles of yours, oh, observant Amshuman, as such it will not 
			be apt of you to offer the mundane obsequial water-oblations to them, 
			indeed. [1-41-18]_END

B_1_C_40_23
BEGIN_
			अस्माकं त्वं हि तुरगं यज्ञियं हृतवानसि || १-४०-२८
			दुर्मेधस्त्वं हि संप्राप्तान् विद्धि नः सगरात्मजान् |_END
BEGIN_
			You the malicious one, you have indeed stolen our ritual-horse, and 
			in fact, you should know that we who arrived here are the sons of Sagara.' 
			Thus Sagara's sons shouted at sage Kapila. [1-40-28b, 29a]_END

B_1_C_42_11
BEGIN_
			मंत्रिष्वाधाय तद्राज्यं गङ्गावतरणे रतः|
			तपो दीर्घं समातिष्ठद्गोकर्णे रघुनंदन || १-४२-१२
			ऊर्ध्वबाहुः पंचतपा मासाहारो जितेन्द्रियः |_END
BEGIN_
			Interested in the alighting of River Ganga on earth, oh, Rama, the 
			descendent of Raghu, king Bhageeratha delegated his kingdom to the custody 
			of his ministers and people and firmed up himself in sustained asceticism 
			on Mt. Gokarna in Himalayas, and he practise ascesis standing amid five-fires, 
			upraising his hands, with a monthly sustenance and with his sense conquered. 
			[1-42-12, 13a]_END

B_1_C_43_1
BEGIN_
			अथ संवत्सरे पूर्णे सर्वलोकनमस्कृतः |
			उमापतिः पशुपती राजानमिदमब्रवीत् || १-४३-२_END
BEGIN_
			On completion of one year, he who is venerated by all worlds, the consort 
			of Uma and the god of animals from insects to humans, that god Shiva 
			revealed himself and spoke this to the king. [1-43-2]_END

B_1_C_41_18
BEGIN_
			गंगा हिमवतो ज्येष्ठा दुहिता पुरुषर्षभ |
			तस्यां कुरु महाबाहो पितॄणां तु जलक्रियाम् || १-४१-१९_END
BEGIN_
			'Oh, best one among men, River Ganga is the elder daughter of 
			Himavanta, and oh, dextrous one, you have to offer water-oblation to 
			the departed paternal-uncles of yours in her waters, namely the holy 
			waters of River Ganga'. [1-41-19]_END

B_1_C_40_24
BEGIN_
			श्रुत्वा तद्वचनं तेषां कपिलो रघुनंदन || १-४०-२९
			रोषेण महताविष्टो हुं कारमकरोत्तदा |_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing their words, oh, Rama, the descendant of Raghu, then sage 
			Kapila is beset with high wrath, and he boomed a 'hum' sound at them. 
			[1-40-29b, 30a]_END

B_1_C_42_12
BEGIN_
			तस्य वर्षसहस्राणि घोरे तपसि तिष्ठतः || १-४२-१३
			अतीतानि महाबहो तस्य राज्ञो महात्मनः |
			सुप्रीतो भगवान्ब्रह्मा प्रजानां पतिरीश्वरः || १-४२-१४_END
BEGIN_
			Thousands of years have rolled by while Bhageeratha stood practising 
			his severe ascesis, oh, dextrous Rama, and then the lord and master 
			of all beings, namely god Brahma, is well pleased with that great-souled 
			king's ascesis. [1-42-13b, 14]_END

B_1_C_43_2
BEGIN_
			प्रीतस्तेऽहं नरश्रेष्ठ करिष्यामि तव प्रियम् |
			शिरसा धारयिष्यामि शैलराजसुतामहम् ||१-४३-३_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, best one among humans, I am delighted with your unwavering effort, 
			and I will fulfil your cherish. I will therefore sustain Ganga, the 
			daughter of king of mountains by my head. [1-43-3]_END

B_1_C_41_19
BEGIN_
			भस्मराशीकृतानेतान् प्लावयेल्लोकपावनी |
			तया क्लिन्नमिदं भस्म गंगया लोककान्तया |
			षष्टिं पुत्रसहस्राणि स्वर्गलोकं गमिष्यति || १-४१-२०_END
BEGIN_
			World purifier River Ganga will drift them who are rendered as mounds 
			of ashes to heaven, and when she who is much adored by all worlds drenches 
			this ash, that River Ganga herself will lead the sixty-thousand sons 
			of Sagara to heaven. [1-41-20]_END

B_1_C_40_25
BEGIN_
			ततस्तेनाप्रमेयेण कपिलेन महात्मना |
			भस्मराशीकृताः सर्वे काकुत्स्थ सगरात्मजाः || १-४०-३०_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, Rama of Kakutstha, then that great-souled sage Kapila, rather Vishnu 
			with unimaginable power, has rendered all of those sons of Sagara as 
			heaps of ashes by virtue of his 'hum' sound." Thus Sage Vishvamitra 
			is narrating the legend of Sagara to Rama and others. [1-40-30b, c]_END

B_1_C_43_3
BEGIN_
			ततो हैमवती ज्येष्ठा सर्वलोकनमस्कृता |
			तदा सातिमहद्रूपं कृत्वा वेगं च दुःसहम् ||१-४३-४
			आकाशादपतद्राम शिवे शिवशिरस्युत |_END
BEGIN_
			Afterwards, she who is reverenced by all the worlds and who is the 
			elder daughter of Himavanta, that Ganga assuming an unendurable form 
			and an insupportable rapidity, they say, then plunged from the sky onto 
			the auspicious head of Shiva. [1-43-4, 5a]_END

B_1_C_42_13
BEGIN_
			ततः सुरगणैः सार्धमुपागम्य पितामहः |
			भगीरथं महात्मानं तप्यमानमथाब्रवीत् || १-४२-१५_END
BEGIN_
			Forefather Brahma then arrived along with assemblages of gods, and 
			spoke this way to the great-souled Bhageeratha who is deep in the practise 
			of ascesis. [1-42-15]_END

B_1_C_41_20
BEGIN_
			गच्छ चाश्वं महाभाग संगृह्य पुरुषर्षभ |
			यज्ञं पैतामहं वीर निर्वर्तयितुमर्हसि || १-४१-२१_END
BEGIN_
			'Oh, great fortunate one, oh, best one among men, you may proceed 
			from here with the horse, oh, brave one, it will be apt of you to carry 
			out the Vedic-ritual of your grandfather.' Thus Garuda said to Amshuman. 
			[1-41-21]_END

B_1_C_43_4
BEGIN_
			अचिन्तयच्च सा देवी गङ्गा परमदुर्धरा ||१-४३-५
			विशाम्यहं हि पातालं स्त्रोतसा गृह्य शंकरम् |_END
BEGIN_
			She who is an extremely unendurable river that goddess Ganga even speculated 
			saying to herself, 'let me enter netherworld, indeed whisking Shiva 
			with my streams.' [1-43-5b, 6a]_END

B_1_C_42_14
BEGIN_
			भगीरथ महाराग प्रीतस्तेऽहं जनाधिप |
			तपसा च सुतप्तेन वरं वरय सुव्रत || १-४२-१६_END
BEGIN_
		  Oh, great king Bhageeratha, oh, lord of the people, I am delighted 
			with the perfectly conducted ascesis of yours, hence oh, truly committed 
			one, you may beseech for a boon. [1-42-16]_END

B_1_C_41_21
BEGIN_
			सुपर्णवचनं श्रुत्वा सोंऽशुमानतिवीर्यवान् |
			त्वरितं हयमादाय पुनरायान्महायशाः || १-४१-२२_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing the words of that great-winged eagle, Garuda, he that highly 
			brave and well-renowned Amshuman swiftly took the horse, and returned 
			to the ritual place of his grandfather, king Sagara. [1-41-22]_END

B_1_C_43_5
BEGIN_
			तस्या वलेपनं ज्ञात्वा क्रुद्धस्तु भगवान् हरः || १-४३-६
			तिरोभावयितुं बुद्धिं चक्रे त्रिनयनस्तदा |_END
BEGIN_
			Discerning her egotism god Shiva is infuriated, and then on his part 
			that Three-eyed god Shiva thought to pent her up in the tufts of his 
			head-hair. [1-43-6b, 7a]_END

B_1_C_42_15
BEGIN_
			तमुवाच महातेजाः सर्वलोकपितामहम् |
			भगीरथो महाबाहुः कृतांजलिपुटः स्थितः || १-४२-१७_END
BEGIN_
			That great resplendent and highly fortunate king Bhageeratha then remaining 
			with suppliantly adjoined palm fold spoke to him who is the Forefather 
			of all worlds, namely Brahma. [1-42-17]_END

B_1_C_41_22
BEGIN_
			ततो राजानमासाद्य दीक्षितं रघुनंदन |
			न्यवेदयद्यथावृत्तं सुपर्णवचनं तथा || १-४१-२३_END
BEGIN_
			Then on reaching the King Sagara, who is under the vow of the ritual, 
			oh, Rama, Amshuman described what all has happened and even the words 
			of Garuda. [1-41-23]_END

B_1_C_43_6
BEGIN_
			सा तस्मिन् पतिता पुण्या पुण्ये रुद्रस्य मूर्धनि||१-४३-७
			हिमवत्प्रतिमे राम जटामण्डलगह्वरे |_END
BEGIN_
			And oh, Rama, she that holy River Ganga swooped down into the cavernous 
			curls of matted hair-tufts on the holy head of God Shiva, and she became 
			a detainee in them. [1-43-7b, 8a]_END

B_1_C_42_16
BEGIN_
			यदि मे भगवान्प्रीतो यद्यस्ति तपसः फलम् |
			सगरस्यात्मजाः सर्वे मत्तः सलिलस्याप्नुयुः || १-४२-१८_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, god, if you are satisfied with my ascesis, and if there is any 
			fruition to the ascesis of mine, let all the sons of Sagara get water 
			oblations through me. [1-42-18]_END

B_1_C_41_23
BEGIN_
			तच्छ्रुत्वा घोरसंकाशं वाक्यमंशुमतो नृपः |
			यज्ञं निर्वर्तयामास यथाकल्पं यथाविधि || १-४१-२४_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing those unendurable words from Amshuman, the king Sagara firstly 
			completed the Vedic-ritual scripturally and procedurally. [1-41-24]_END

B_1_C_42_17
BEGIN_
			गङ्गायाः सलिलक्लिन्ने भस्मन्येषां महात्मनाम् |
			स्वर्गं गच्छेयुरत्यन्तं सर्वे मे प्रपितामहाः || १-४२-१९_END
BEGIN_
			While the ashes of these great souls are drenched with the waters 
			of Ganga, let all of those great-grandfathers of mine depart to heaven, 
			eternally. [1-42-19]_END

B_1_C_43_7
BEGIN_
			सा कथञ्चिन्महीं गन्तुं नाशक्नोद्यत्नमास्थिता ||१-४३-८
			नैव सा निर्गमं लेभे जटामण्डलमन्ततः |_END
BEGIN_
			Though she strove hard in one way or another to reach the earth that 
			Ganga is rendered incapable, as she could not gain access for an outlet 
			from any edge of the coils of matted hair-tufts of Shiva, hence she 
			is held there in durance vile. [1-43-8b, 9a]_END

B_1_C_41_24
BEGIN_
			स्वपुरं चागमच्छ्रीमानिष्टयज्ञो महीपतिः |
			गंगायाश्चागमे राजा निश्चयं नाध्यगच्छत || १-४१-२५_END
BEGIN_
			On completing the Vedic-ritual King Sagara arrived at his capital, 
			but that king could not arrive at a decision about the arrival of Ganga 
			to the earth. [1-41-25]_END

B_1_C_42_18
BEGIN_
			देव याचे ह संतत्यै नावसीदेत्कुलं च नः |
			इक्ष्वाकूणां कुले देव एष मेऽस्तु वरः परः || १-४२-२०_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, god, I indeed pray for offspring in our Ikshvaku dynasty, let 
			not our dynasty dwindle as I am issueless, and oh, god, let this be 
			the other boon to me. [1-42-20]_END

B_1_C_43_8
BEGIN_
			तत्रैवाबंभ्रमद्देवी संवत्सरगणान्बहून् ||१-४३-९
			तामपश्यन् पुनस्तत्र तपः परममास्थितः |_END
BEGIN_
			Goddess Ganga whirled round and round in the coils of tufts alone for 
			many number of years, and when Ganga's emanation from those coils is 
			intangible Bhageeratha again firmed up in a marvellous penance in the 
			matter of her descent to earth. [1-43-9b, 10a]_END

B_1_C_41_25
BEGIN_
			अगत्वा निश्चयं राजा कालेन महता महान् |
			त्रिंशद्वर्षसहस्राणि राज्यं कृत्वा दिवं गतः || १-४१-२६_END
BEGIN_
			"That great king Sagara could not get at any resolve in getting Ganga 
			to earth even after a long time, and on ruling kingdom for thirty-thousand 
			years he went to heaven." Thus Vishvamitra continued his narration about 
			the ancestors of Rama. [1-41-26]_END

B_1_C_42_19
BEGIN_
			उक्तवाक्यं तु राजानं सर्वलोकपितामहः |
			प्रत्युवाच शुभां वाणीं मधुरं मधुराक्षराम् || १-४२-२१_END
BEGIN_
			The Forefather of all the worlds, Brahma, then replied the king who 
			has spoken in that way, in an auspicious tongue that is sweet-sounding 
			and sweetly worded, as well. [1-42-21]_END

B_1_C_43_9
BEGIN_
			स तेन तोषितश्चासीदत्यन्तं रघुनंदन || १-४३-१०
			विससर्ज ततो गङ्गां हरो बिन्दुसरः प्रति |_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, Rama, the legatee of Raghu, with that ascesis of Bhageeratha god 
			Shiva is very much delighted, and thereupon he has also released Ganga 
			aiming at Bindu Lake in Himalayas. [1-43-10b, 11a]_END

B_1_C_42_20
BEGIN_
			मनोरथो महानेष भगीरथ महारथ |
			एवं भवतु भद्रं ते इक्ष्वाकुकुलवर्धन || १-४२-२२_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, top-speeded chariot-rider Bhageeratha, this aspiration of yours 
			is sublime, and oh, the furtherer of Ikshvaku dynasty, so be it, let 
			safeness betide you. [1-42-22]_END

B_1_C_43_10
BEGIN_
			तस्यां विसृज्यमानायां सप्त स्रोतंसि जज्ञिरे || १-४३-११
			ह्लादिनी पावनी चैव नलिनी च तथैव च |
			तिस्रः प्राचीं दिशं जग्मुर्गंगाः शिवजलाः शुभाः || १-४३-१२_END
BEGIN_
			While god Shiva released Ganga into Bindu Lake seven streams have emerged 
			out of it, and thus three auspicious Ganga-s with holy waters have cruised 
			eastward which are known as Hlaadini, Paavani, and Nalini. [1-43-11b, 
			12]_END

B_1_C_44_0
BEGIN_
			स गत्वा सागरं राजा गंगयानुगतस्तदा |
			प्रविवेश तलं भूमेर्यत्र ते भस्मसात्कृताः || १-४४-१_END
BEGIN_
            "King Bhageeratha followed by Ganga has gone to the ocean-like ditch 
			which is dredged up by the sons of Sagara, and entered the subterranean 
			of earth where the sons of Sagara are rendered to ashes." Thus Vishvamitra 
			continued his narration about the Descent of Ganga. [1-44-1]_END

B_1_C_42_21
BEGIN_
			इयं हैमवती ज्येष्ठा गंगा हिमवतः सुता |
			तां वै धारयितुं राजन् हरस्तत्र नियुज्यताम् || १-४२-२३_END
BEGIN_
			This Ganga is the one with snow-broth, the elder daughter of Himavanta, 
			and oh, king Bhageeratha, god Shiva alone is capable to sustain her 
			force in the course of her alighting onto earth, and in fact, he is 
			to be commissioned for that purpose. [1-42-23]_END

B_1_C_43_11
BEGIN_
			सुचक्षुश्चैव सीता च सिन्धुश्चैव महानदी |
			तिस्रस्त्वेता दिशं जग्मुः प्रतीचीं तु शुभोदकाः ||१-४३-१३_END
BEGIN_
			Also thus Sucakshu, Seetha, and the excellent river Sindhu are the 
			other three rivers which streamed to the westward direction with their 
			holy waters. [1-43-13]_END

B_1_C_44_1
BEGIN_
			भस्मन्यथाप्लुते राम गंगायाः सलिलेन वै |
			सर्वलोकप्रभुर्ब्रह्मा राजानमिदमब्रवीत् || १-४४-२_END
BEGIN_
			While the waters of Ganga are inundating those ashes, oh, Rama, then 
			Brahma, the lord of all worlds, indeed spoke this to the king Bhageeratha. 
			[1-44-2]_END

B_1_C_42_22
BEGIN_
			गंगायाः पतनं राजन् पृथिवी न सहिष्यते |
			तां वै धारयितुं राजन् नान्यं पश्यामि शूलिनः || १-४२-२४_END
BEGIN_
			'Oh, king Bhageeratha, the earth cannot endure the downfall of Ganga 
			and to sustain Ganga, oh, king, indeed I do not behold none other than 
			the Trident-wielder, god Shiva.' Thus Brahma spoke to Bhageeratha. [1-42-24]_END

B_1_C_43_12
BEGIN_
			सप्तमी चान्वगात्तासां भगीरथरथं तदा |
			भगीरथोऽपि रजर्षिर्दिव्यं स्यंदनमास्थितः || १-४३-१४
			प्रायादग्रे महातेजा गङ्गा तं चाप्यनुव्रजत् |_END
BEGIN_
			Of them the seventh Ganga flowed towards the path of Bhageeratha' chariot, 
			and that great-resplendent and kingly sage Bhageeratha sitting in a 
			divine chariot moved ahead and even Ganga followed him. [1-43-14, 15a]_END

B_1_C_44_2
BEGIN_
			तारिता नरशार्दूल दिवं याताश्च देववत् |
			षष्टिः पुत्रसहस्राणि सगरस्य महात्मनः || १-४४-३_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, tigerly-man Bhageeratha, the sixty thousands sons of great souled 
			Sagara have crossed over the sea of mortality, and on a par with the 
			gods they have also transited to heaven. [1-44-3]_END

B_1_C_42_23
BEGIN_
			तमेवमुक्त्वा राजानं गङ्गां चाभाष्य लोककृत् |
			जगाम त्रिदिवं देवैः सह सर्वैर्मरुद्गणैः || १-४२-२५_END
BEGIN_
			"Speaking this way to the king Bhageeratha and informally greeting Ganga 
			also, that Creator of Worlds, Brahma, left for heaven along with all 
			the groups of gods and Wind-gods." Thus Vishvamitra continued narration 
			about the arrival of River Ganga to earth. [1-42-25]_END

B_1_C_43_13
BEGIN_
			गगनाच्छङ्करशिरस्ततो धरणिमागता || १-४३-१५
			व्यसर्पत जलं तत्र तीव्रशब्दपुरस्कृतम् |_END
BEGIN_
			Thus Ganga came from heavens onto Shankara's head and from there onto 
			the earth, and there on earth her waters advanced with a tumultuous 
			sound advancing them. [1-43-15b, 16a]_END

B_1_C_44_3
BEGIN_
			सागरस्य जलं लोके यावत् स्थास्यति पार्थिव |
			सगरस्यात्मजाः सर्वे दिवि स्थास्यन्ति देववत् ||१-४४-४_END
BEGIN_
			As long as the water of the ocean abides in the world, oh, king, 
			so long the sons of Sagara will abide in heaven like gods. [1-44-4]_END

B_1_C_43_14
BEGIN_
			मत्स्यकच्छपसंघैश्च शिंशुमारगणैस्तथा || १-४३-१६
			पतद्भिः पतितैश्चैव व्यरोचत वसुंधरा |_END
BEGIN_
			The earth then verily shone forth with the shoals of fish, schools 
			of tortoises, and scores of porpoises and other aquatic beings that 
			have already fallen and that are still falling in step with the spates 
			of Ganga. [1-43-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_44_4
BEGIN_
			इयं च दुहिता ज्येष्ठा तव गंगा भविष्यति |
			त्वत्कृतेन च नाम्नाथ लोके स्थास्यति विश्रुता ||१-४४-५_END
BEGIN_
			This Ganga will become your eldest daughter and hereafter she will 
			remain renowned in the world with the name associated with your deed 
			of bringing her onto earth. [1-44-5]_END

B_1_C_43_15
BEGIN_
			ततो देवर्षिगंधर्वा यक्षा सिद्धगणास्तथा || १-४३-१७
			व्यलोकयन्त ते तत्र गगनाद्गां गतां तदा |_END
BEGIN_
			Later, they the gods, sages, gandharva-s, yaksha-s, and the assemblages 
			of siddha-s have then seen there the swoop of Ganga in that way from 
			heaven to earth, with curiosity. [1-43-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_44_5
BEGIN_
			गंगा त्रिपथगा नाम दिव्या भागीरथीति च |
			त्रीन्पथो भावयन्तीति तस्मत्त्रिपथगा स्मृता || १-४४-६_END
BEGIN_
			Henceforth heavenly Ganga will be renowned as 'Triple-path-cruiser' 
			and 'Bhaageerathi,' as well, and as this river is sanctifying three 
			worlds, namely, svarga, bhuu, paataala loka-s, 
			'heaven, earth and netherworld' she will be remembered as the traveller 
			on triple path. [1-44-6]_END

B_1_C_43_16
BEGIN_
			विमानैर्नगराकारैर्हयैर्गजवरैस्तथा ||१-४३-१८
			पारिप्लवगताश्चापि देवतास्तत्र विष्ठिताः |_END
BEGIN_
			Some of the gods with aircrafts that are like cities in their shape 
			and size, and some with horses that are prancing, and some with best 
			elephants that are staggering, at the very sight of plunging Ganga, 
			have entered the firmament at that place. [1-43-18b, 19a]_END

B_1_C_44_6
BEGIN_
			पितामहानां सर्वेषां त्वमत्र मनुजाधिप |
			कुरुष्व सलिलं राजन् प्रतिज्ञामपवर्जय || १-४४-७_END
BEGIN_
			You may now offer water-oblations to all of your forefathers in the 
			waters of Ganga, oh, king, the lord of people, thus you may fulfil and 
			do away with the pledge of your requiescat. [1-44-7]_END

B_1_C_43_17
BEGIN_
			तदद्भुततमं लोके गंगापतनमुत्तमम् ||१-४३-१९
			दिदृक्षवो देवगणाः समीयुरमितौजसः |_END
BEGIN_
			The gods whose animation is unlimited, and who are anxious to see the 
			plunge of Ganga, have come together in assemblages, which plunge is 
			a highest marvel in the universe by a better degree of her illimitable 
			animation than that of gods who came to see, and even benignant to the 
			world in according water and salving souls, which those gods cannot 
			do. [1-43-19b, 20a]_END

B_1_C_44_7
BEGIN_
			पूर्वकेण हि ते राजंस्तेनातियशसा तदा |
			धर्मिणां प्रवरेणाथ नैष प्राप्तो मनोरथः || १-४४-८_END
BEGIN_
		    Your ancestor Sagara is a highly glorious one and a best one 
			among righteous persons, oh, king, even then he has not achieved this 
			aspiration of alighting Ganga in his lifetime, but you have achieved 
			it. [1-44-8]_END

B_1_C_43_18
BEGIN_
			संपतद्भिः सुरगणैस्तेषां चाभरणौजसा || १-४३-२०
			शतादित्यमिवाभाति गगनं गततोयदम् |_END
BEGIN_
			"The glitter of the ornaments of hosts of gods who are in stampede, 
			made the cloudless sky to shine as if it is with a hundred of suns. 
			[1-43-20b, 21a]_END

B_1_C_45_0
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रवचः श्रुत्वा राघवः सहलक्ष्मणः |
विस्मयं परमं गत्वा विश्वामित्रमथाब्रवीत् || १-४५-१_END
BEGIN_
On listening the narration of Sage Vishwamitra about Ganga's descent along with 
Lakshmana, Rama went into a great astonishment, and then addressed Vishvamitra. 
[1-45-1]_END

B_1_C_44_8
BEGIN_
			तथैवांशुमता वत्स लोकेऽप्रतिमतेजसा |
			गङ्गां प्रार्थयता नेतुं प्रतिज्ञा नापवर्जिता || १-४४-९_END
BEGIN_
			Like that, your grandfather Amshuman, who is unequalled in his resplendence 
			in this world and who had been praying for the descent of Ganga, he 
			also could not dispense with this vow on fulfilling it. [1-44-9]_END

B_1_C_43_19
BEGIN_
			शिंशुमारोरगगणैर्मीनैरपि च चंचलैः || १-४३-२१
			विद्युद्भिरिव विक्षिप्तैराकाशमभवत्तदा |_END
BEGIN_
			At that time, with the falling and rising of scores of porpoises and 
			reptiles, even with the wriggling fishes, the sky became flashy as if 
			flashes of lightning are strewn over it. [1-43-21b, 22a]_END

B_1_C_45_1
BEGIN_
अत्यद्भुतमिदं ब्रह्मन् कथितं परमं त्वया |
गंगावतरणं पुण्यं सागरस्यापि पूरणम् || १-४५-२_END
BEGIN_
The blessed legend you have narrated about the digging of an ocean at the behest 
of Sagara, Ganga's alighting, and Bhageeratha filling it with the water of Ganga 
is sacrosanct and even highly amazing. [1-45-2]_END

B_1_C_44_9
BEGIN_
			राजर्षिणा गुणवता महर्षिसमतेजसा |
			मत्तुल्यतपसा चैव क्षत्रधर्मे स्थितेन च || १-४४-१०
			दिलीपेन महाभाग तव पित्रातितेजसा |
			पुनर्न शङ्किता नेतुं गङ्गां प्रार्थयतानघ || १-४४-११_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, impeccable Bhageeratha, even by the kingly-sage Dileepa whose 
			resplendence is kindred to great sages, who is equal to me in his ascesis, 
			who is abided by the observances of ruling Kshatriya class, even by 
			such a highly fortunate and highly resplendent father of yours it was 
			impossible to bring Ganga in his turn, even though he had been supplicating 
			for the descent of Ganga throughout his lifetime. [1-44-10, 11]_END

B_1_C_43_20
BEGIN_
			पाण्डुरैः सलिलोत्पीडैः कीर्यमाणैः सहस्रधा ||१-४३-२२
			शारदाभ्रैरिवाकीर्णं गगनं हंससंप्लवैः |_END
BEGIN_
			Spattered innumerably with the whitish froth from the splashes of Ganga, 
			and stippled with the flights of swans, the sky is as though overspread 
			with silver-clouds of autumn. [1-43-22b, 23a]_END

B_1_C_44_10
BEGIN_
			सा त्वया समतिक्रान्ता प्रतिज्ञा पुरुषर्षभ |
			प्राप्तोऽसि परमं लोके यशः परमसंमतम् || १-४४-१२_END
BEGIN_
			But, you have accomplished that pledge, oh, the best one among men, 
			and in the world you have achieved highest renown which is highly adorable 
			by all. [1-44-12]_END

B_1_C_45_2
BEGIN_
क्षणभूतेव नौ रात्रिः संवृत्तेयं परंतप |
इमां चिंतयतोः सर्वां निखिलेन कथां तव || १-४५-३_END
BEGIN_
Oh, enemy-inflamer, for two of us entire night rolled by as if it is a single moment 
while we were thinking about the episode you have narrated in its entirety. [1-45-3]_END

B_1_C_43_21
BEGIN_
			क्वचिद् द्रुततरं याति कुटिलं क्वचिदायतम् ||१-४३-२३
			विनतं क्वचिदुद्धूतं क्वचिद्याति शनैः शनैः |_END
BEGIN_
			Somewhere Ganga is coursing precipitately, elsewhere sinuously, somewhere 
			else straightly, elsewhere sloppily, somewhere gushingly, and somewhere 
			else her cruise is leisurely and tardily. [1-43-23b, 24a]_END

B_1_C_44_11
BEGIN_
			तच्च गंगावतरणं त्वया कृतमरिन्दम |
			अनेन च भवान् प्राप्तो धर्मस्यायतनं महत् || १-४४-१३_END
BEGIN_
			That 'Descent of Ganga' is perfected by you, oh, enemy-represser, 
			and by this you have acquired a genuine basis for righteousness in this 
			world, and thereby a base for yourself in my world, namely Abode of 
			Brahma. [1-44-13]_END

B_1_C_45_3
BEGIN_
तस्य सा शर्वरी सर्वा मम सौमित्रिणा सह |
जगाम चिंतयानस्य विश्वामित्रकथां शुभाम् ||१-४५-४_END
BEGIN_
While thinking about the auspicious legend of Ganga along with Lakshmana, oh, friend 
of the universe, Vishvamitra, whole night rolled by." Thus Rama is addressing Vishvamitra. 
[1-45-4]_END

B_1_C_43_22
BEGIN_
			सलिलेनैव सलिलं क्वचिदभ्याहतं पुनः || १-४३-२४
			मुहुरूर्ध्वपथं गत्वा पपात वसुधां पुनः |_END
BEGIN_
			Somewhere her water repeatedly knocking against her own water is recurrently 
			billowing upwards only to make nosedive onto earth. [1-43-24b, 25a]_END

B_1_C_44_12
BEGIN_
			प्लावयस्व त्वमात्मानं नरोत्तम सदोचिते |
			सलिले पुरुषश्रेष्ठ शुचिः पुण्यफलो भव || १-४४-१४_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, phenomenal one, you may always take dip-baths in the holy water 
			of Ganga and oh, persona grata, thereby get purified of sins and thus 
			let your merit be fructified. [1-44-14]_END

B_1_C_45_4
BEGIN_
ततः प्रभाते विमले विश्वामित्रं तपोधनम्|
उवाच राघवो वाक्यं कृताह्निकमरिन्दमः || १-४५-५_END
BEGIN_
