Thereafter on the next fresh dawn the enemy-oppressor Raghava spoke these words 
to sage Vishvamitra, whose affluence is nothing but asceticism, and who by now has 
performed his daily chores of rituals. [1-45-5]_END

B_1_C_43_23
BEGIN_
			तच्छङ्करशिरोभ्रष्टं भ्रष्टं भूमितले पुनः ||१-४३-२५
			व्यरोचत तदा तोयं निर्मलं गतकल्मषम् |_END
BEGIN_
			That impeccable and immaculate water of Ganga then became outstanding 
			as it has flounced down from heaven primarily onto the head of Shankara, 
			and therefrom it has coasted down onto the earth. [1-43-25b, 26a]_END

B_1_C_44_13
BEGIN_
			पितामहानां सर्वेषां कुरुष्व सलिलक्रियाम् |
			स्वस्ति तेऽस्तु गमिष्यामि स्वं लोकं गम्यतां नृप || १-४४-१५_END
BEGIN_
			'You may now perform water-oblations to your forefathers with the 
			water of Ganga, let there be wellbeing to you, and oh, king, here I 
			go to my abode and you too may depart to yours.' Thus Brahma said to 
			Bhageeratha. [1-44-15]_END

B_1_C_45_5
BEGIN_
गता भगवती रात्रिः श्रोतव्यं परमं श्रुतम् |
तराम सरितं श्रेष्ठं पुण्यां त्रिपथगां नदीम् ||१-४५-६_END
BEGIN_
We have listened the praiseworthy legend of River Ganga, and the deific night 
has also passed by while listening such a legend, we may now cross over the very 
same prominent and merited River Ganga, the tri-path-cruiser. [1-45-6]_END

B_1_C_43_24
BEGIN_
			तत्रर्षिगणगन्धर्वा वसुधातलवासिनः ||१-४३-२६
			भवाङ्गपतितं तोयं पवित्रमिति पस्पृशुः |_END
BEGIN_
			And asserting that the water as holy, because it descended touching 
			the body of Shiva, viz., the head of Shiva, the assemblages of sages, 
			gandharva-s, and those that are residents on the plane of earth have 
			sipped that water at that place. [1-43-26b, 27a]_END

B_1_C_44_14
BEGIN_
			इत्येवमुक्त्वा देवेशः सर्वलोकपितामहः |
			यथागतं तथागच्छद्देवलोकं महायशाः || १-४४-१६_END
BEGIN_
			On saying in this way, the forefather of all the worlds, and the great 
			glorious lord of all gods, namely Brahma, went away to his empyrean 
			world as he has came. [1-44-16]_END

B_1_C_45_6
BEGIN_
नौरेषा हि सुखास्तीर्णा ऋषीणां पुण्यकर्मणाम् |
भगवन्तमिह प्राप्तं ज्ञात्वा त्वरितमागता || १-४५-७_END
BEGIN_
"This boat which is suitable for the embarkation of the sages whose deeds are pious, 
and which is comfortably blanketed with mats in its deck has come here, and indeed 
on knowing about the visit of your holiness to this place the sages have fetched 
it." Thus Rama spoke to Vishvamitra. [1-45-7]_END

B_1_C_46_0
BEGIN_
			हतेषु तेषु पुत्रेषु दितिः परमदुःखिता |
			मारीचं काश्यपं राम भर्तारमिदमब्रवीत् || १-४६-१_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, Rama, Lady Diti was highly anguished for those sons that are killed 
			and said this to her husband, Sage Kashyapa, the son of Sage Maareechi." 
			Thus Vishvamitra continued narration. [1-46-1]_END

B_1_C_43_25
BEGIN_
			शापात् प्रपतिता ये च गगनाद्वसुधातलम् ||१-४३-२७
			कृत्वा तत्राभिषेकं ते बभूवुर्गतकल्मषाः |_END
BEGIN_
			Also those that have fallen from heaven onto the surface of earth by 
			some curse or the other, they too became blemishless on taking head-bath 
			in the water of Ganga. [1-43-27b, 28a]_END

B_1_C_44_15
BEGIN_
			भगीरथस्तु राजर्षिः कृत्वा सलिलमुत्तमम् |
			यथाक्रमं यथान्यायं सागराणां महायशाः || १-४४-१७
			कृतोदकः शुची राजा स्वपुरं प्रविवेश ह |
			समृद्धार्थो नरश्रेष्ठ स्वराज्यं प्रशशास ह ||१-४४-१८_END
BEGIN_
			On according those best water-oblations that endow superior realms 
			to the souls of sons of Sagara, according to precedency and the rationale 
			of scriptures, and even on offering water-oblations to other manes that 
			kingly-sage and greatly renowned Bhageeratha is sanctified, and then 
			only that king re-entered his own city, indeed when his purpose is completely 
			achieved, and oh, outstanding man Rama, thus that king Bhageeratha ruled 
			his kingdom well. [1-44-17, 18]_END

B_1_C_45_7
BEGIN_
तस्य तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा राघवस्य महात्मनः |
संतारं कारयामास सर्षिसंघस्य कौशिकः || १-४५-८_END
BEGIN_
Hearing the words of great-souled Raghava, Vishvamitra of Kusha dynasty, started 
to cross over the River Ganga along with the assemblage of sages, and with both 
the Raghava-s. [1-45-8]_END

B_1_C_46_1
BEGIN_
			हतपुत्रास्मि भगवंस्तव पुत्रैर्महाबलैः |
			शक्रहन्तारमिच्छामि पुत्रं दीर्घतपोऽर्जितम् ||१-४६-२_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, god, I am bereaved of my sons who are killed by your great mighty 
			sons, the sons of your second wife Aditi, as such I wish to bear a son, 
			who is achievable by sustained penance, for he shall be the exterminator 
			of Indra. [1-46-2]_END

B_1_C_43_26
BEGIN_
			धूतपापाः पुनस्तेन तोयेनाथ शुभान्विता || १-४३-२८
			पुनराकाशमाविश्य स्वान् लोकान् प्रतिपेदिरे |_END
BEGIN_
			When sins are washed away with the hallowing water of Ganga, they again 
			transited skyward and then obtained their own empyrean worlds once again. 
			[1-43-28b, 29a]_END

B_1_C_44_16
BEGIN_
			प्रमुमोद च लोकस्तं नृपमासाद्य राघव |
			नष्टशोकः समृद्धार्थो बभूव विगतज्वरः || १-४४-१९_END
BEGIN_
			On regaining him as their king the subjects of the kingdom are overjoyed, 
			and oh, Raghava, that king Bhageeratha too is relieved of his febrility 
			as his purpose is achieved and he is happy when devoid of haunting grief 
			of getting Ganga to earth. [1-44-19]_END

B_1_C_45_8
BEGIN_
उत्तरं तीरमासाद्य संपूज्यर्षिगणं ततः |
गंगाकूले निविष्टास्ते विशालां ददृशुः पुरिम् || १-४५-९_END
BEGIN_
Arriving at the northern bank of River Ganga they have honoured the group of sages 
who ferried them up to here and sent them off. Then sojourning on the riverbank 
of Ganga they have seen the city called Vishaala. [1-45-9]_END

B_1_C_46_2
BEGIN_
			साहं तपश्चरिष्यामि गर्भं मे दातुमर्हसि |
			ईश्वरं शक्रहन्तारं त्वमनुज्ञातुमर्हसि || १-४६-३_END
BEGIN_
			'Such a bereaved mother as I am, I wish to undertake asceticism for 
			a son who shall become an exterminator of Indra, and who shall be the 
			ruler of worlds. As such, it will be apt of you to permit me for asceticism, 
			and further it will be apt of you to accord me pregnancy with such a 
			son.' Thus Diti spoke to her husband Kaashyapa. [1-46-3]_END

B_1_C_43_27
BEGIN_
			मुमुदे मुदितो लोकस्तेन तोयेन भास्वता || १-४३-२९
			कृताभिषेको गंगायां बभूव विगतक्लमः |_END
BEGIN_
			With her splendorous water people are blissful, and on taking dip-baths 
			in Ganga they are totally removed of the strains of their sins, and 
			they lived blissfully ever after. [1-43-29b, 30a]_END

B_1_C_44_17
BEGIN_
			एष ते राम गंगाया विस्तरोऽभिहितो मया |
			स्वस्ति प्राप्नुहि भद्रं ते संध्याकालोऽतिवर्तते || १-४४-२०_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, Rama, this way I described to you about 'The Decent of Ganga' in 
			detail, thus you be blest and prosperous, and as the visceral time is 
			elapsing no more questions from you for now, and let us meditate on 
			Gayatri. But listen to the fruits of listening the legend of 
			ganga avataraNa, 'The Descent of Ganga' [1-44-20]_END

B_1_C_45_9
BEGIN_
ततो मुनिवरस्तूर्णं जगाम सहराघवः |
विशालां नगरीं रम्यां दिव्यां स्वर्गोपमां तदा || १-४५-१०_END
BEGIN_
The great sage Vishvamitra then quickly started along with Rama and Lakshmana to 
the charming and admirable city Vishaala, which in comparison is like heaven. [1-45-10]_END

B_1_C_46_3
BEGIN_
			तस्यास्तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा मारीचः कश्यपस्तदा |
			प्रत्युवाच महातेजा दितिं परमदुःखिताम् || १-४६-४_END
BEGIN_
			On hearing her request the great resplendent sage Kaashyapa, the son 
			of Sage Mareechi, replied Diti, who is deeply mournful. [1-46-4]_END

B_1_C_43_28
BEGIN_
			भगीरथोऽपि राजर्षिर्दिव्यं स्यंदनमास्थितः ||१-४३-३०
			प्रायादग्रे महातेजास्तं गंगा पृष्ठतोऽन्वगात् |_END
BEGIN_
			In this way, the great-resplendent and kingly sage Bhageeratha sitting 
			in a divine chariot continuously moved ahead and Ganga continually followed 
			him at his behind. [1-43-30b, 31a]_END

B_1_C_44_18
BEGIN_
			धन्यं यशस्यमायुष्यं पुत्र्यं स्वर्ग्यमथापि च |
			यः श्रावयति विप्रेषु क्षत्रियेष्वितरेषु च || १-४४-२१
			प्रीयन्ते पितरस्तस्य प्रीयन्ते दैवतानि च |_END
BEGIN_
			This legend is conducive to achieve prosperity, fame, longevity, progeny 
			and even heaven, and he who narrates this legend to others, whether 
			he is from Brahmans or from Kshatriya-s, or for that matter of fact 
			from any other class, his manes will be satisfied, and gods too will 
			be gladdened. [1-44-21, 22a]_END

B_1_C_45_10
BEGIN_
अथ रामो महाप्राज्ञो विश्वामित्रं महामुनिम् |
पप्रच्छ प्रांजलिर्भूत्वा विशालामुत्तमां पुरीम् || १-४५-११_END
BEGIN_
Then Rama, whose flair for knowing everything is high, became suppliant duly adjoining 
his palms, and enquired about the prominent city Vishala with the great Sage Vishvamitra. 
[1-45-11]_END

B_1_C_46_4
BEGIN_
			एवं भवतु भद्रं ते शुचिर्भव तपोधने |
			जनयिष्यसि पुत्रं त्वं शक्रहन्तारमाहवे ||१-४६-५_END
BEGIN_
			" 'So be it... oh, ascetically wealthy lady, you be blest, if you abide 
			by the propriety of the practises of asceticism, then you will be delivering 
			a son who can become an exterminator of Indra in war. [1-46-5]_END

B_1_C_43_29
BEGIN_
			देवाः सर्षिगणाः सर्वे दैत्यदानवराक्षसाः || १-४३-३१
			गन्धर्वयक्षप्रवराः सकिंनरमहोरगाः |
			सर्पाश्चाप्सरसो राम भगीरथरथानुगाः || १-४३-३२
			गंगामन्वगमन् प्रीताः सर्वे जलचराश्च ये |_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, Rama, all of the gods along with the assemblages of sages, ogres, 
			monsters, demons, and even great reptiles with kinnara-s, and gandharva-s 
			with best yaksha-s, and even serpents and apsara-s, have delightfully 
			moved after Ganga who is following the chariot of Bhageeratha, and why 
			they, in fact, all of the aquatic beings have followed Ganga. [31b, 
			32, 33a]_END

B_1_C_44_19
BEGIN_
			इदमाख़्यनमायुष्यं गंगावतरणं शुभम् || १-४४-२२
			यः श्रुणोति च काकुत्स्थ सर्वान् कामानवाप्नुयात् |
			सर्वे पापाः प्रणश्यन्ति आयुः कीर्तिश्च वर्धते || १-४४-२३_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, Rama of Kakutstha-s, he who listens to this auspicious legend named 
			'The Descent of Gang,' which is an endower of longevity, all his wishes 
			are achieved, all his sins are obliterated, and his reputation and longevity 
			are also enhanced." Thus Vishvamitra concluded the episode of 'The Descent 
			of Ganga.' [1-44-22b, 23]_END

B_1_C_45_11
BEGIN_
कतमो राजवंशोऽयं विशालायां महामुने |
श्रोतुमिच्छामि भद्रं ते परं कौतूहलं हि मे || १-४५-१२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, great sage, which dynasty of kings is ruling from this city of Vishaala? Let 
safeness betide you, I am interested to hear of it and indeed I am highly inquisitive 
about it." Thus Rama spoke to Vishvamitra. [1- 45-12]_END

B_1_C_46_5
BEGIN_
			पूर्णे वर्षसहस्रे तु शुचिर्यदि भविष्यसि |
			पुत्रं त्रैलोक्यहन्तारं मत्तस्त्वं जनयिष्यसि ||१-४६-६_END
BEGIN_
			'If you can complete a thousand years of asceticism punctiliously, 
			by my grace you can deliver a son who can be a husbander of three worlds.' 
			Thus Sage Kaashyapa advised his wife Diti. [1-46-6]_END

B_1_C_43_30
BEGIN_
			यतो भगीरथो राजा ततो गंगा यशस्विनी || १-४३-३३
			जगाम सरितां श्रेष्ठा सर्वपापप्रणाशिनी |_END
BEGIN_
			In whichever direction king Bhageeratha has advanced, that glorious 
			River Ganga, who is the prominent river among all the rivers and the 
			complete obliterator of sins, has also moved at his behind in that direction. 
			[1-43-33b, 34a]_END

B_1_C_45_12
BEGIN_
तस्य तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा रामस्य मुनिपुंगवः |
आख्यातुं तत्समारेभे विशालस्य पुरातनम् || १-४५-१३_END
BEGIN_
Hearing that sentence of Rama then the eminent sage Vishvamitra has commenced to 
narrate the legend of ancient Vishaala. [1-45-13]_END

B_1_C_46_6
BEGIN_
			एवमुक्त्वा महातेजाः पाणिना स ममार्ज ताम् |
			तमालभ्य ततः स्वस्तीत्युक्त्वा तपसे ययौ ||१-४६-७_END
BEGIN_
			Saying thus that great resplendent sage patted her, and then on his 
			touching her she is consecrated, and then that sage Kaashyapa departed 
			for his ascetic practises, saying 'be blest.' [1-46-7]_END

B_1_C_43_31
BEGIN_
			ततो हि यजमानस्य जह्नोरद्भुतकर्मणः ||१-४३-३४
			गङ्गा संप्लावयामास यज्ञवाटं महत्मनः |_END
BEGIN_
			While in flow she started to completely inundate the field of Vedic-ritual 
			belonging to the great-souled sage Jahnu, who is of marvellous deeds 
			and who is presently an officiator of an ongoing Vedic-ritual. [1-43-34b, 
			35a]_END

B_1_C_45_13
BEGIN_
श्रूयतां राम शक्रस्य कथां कथयतः श्रुताम् |
अस्मिन् देशे हि यद्वृत्तं शृणु तत्त्वेन राघव || १-४५-१४_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, I will tell you about the auspicious legend of Indra as I was told, and 
you listen to it as I tell. Oh, Raghava, indeed you may now listen to the quintessence 
of what has happened in this country. [1-45-14]_END

B_1_C_46_7
BEGIN_
			गते तस्मिन्नरश्रेष्ठ दितिः परमहर्षिता |
			कुशप्लवं सामासाद्य तपस्तेपे सुदारुणम् ||१-४६-८_END
BEGIN_
			On the exit of Sage Kaashyapa, oh, best one among men Rama, highly 
			elated Diti reached the sacred place called Kushaplava, on which the 
			present City of Vishala is now standing, and practised a highly rigorous 
			asceticism. [1-46-8]_END

B_1_C_43_32
BEGIN_
			तस्यावलेपनं ज्ञात्वा क्रुद्धो जह्नुश्च राघव || १-४३-३५
			अपिबत्तु जलं सर्वं गङ्गायाः परमाद्भुतम् |_END
BEGIN_
			But on knowing her hubris, oh, Raghava, that sage Jahnu has become 
			irritated and causing an extreme marvel he drank off all the water of 
			Ganga. [1-43-35b, 36a]_END

B_1_C_45_14
BEGIN_
पूर्वं कृतयुगे राम दितेः पुत्रा महाबलाः |
अदितेश्च महाभागा वीर्यवन्तः सुधार्मिकाः || १-४५-१५_END
BEGIN_
Once in Krita era, oh, Rama, the sons of Lady Diti were extremely energetic, whereas 
the sons of her younger sister Lady Aditi were vigorous and highly righteous. [1-45-15]_END

B_1_C_46_8
BEGIN_
			तपस्तस्यां हि कुर्वत्यां परिचर्यां चकार ह |
			सहस्राक्षो नरश्रेष्ठ परया गुणसंपदा || १-४६-९_END
BEGIN_
			While she is truly practising asceticism, oh, the best among men Rama, 
			that Thousand-eyed god Indra has indeed rendered services with his abundant 
			and surpassing veracities to her, who is none other than his maternal-aunt. 
			[1-46-9]_END

B_1_C_43_33
BEGIN_
			ततो देवाः सगन्धर्वा ऋषयश्च सुविस्मिताः || १-४३-३६
			पूजयन्ति महात्मानं जह्नुं पुरुषसत्तमम् |
			गङ्गां चापि नयन्ति स्म दुहितृत्वे महात्मनः || १-४३-३७_END
BEGIN_
			Thereupon, the gods along with gandharva-s and sages at that extremely 
			marvellous feat of Sage Jahnu are highly astounded, and they then started 
			to worship that ablest human and great-souled sage Jahnu, and even deigned 
			for the daughterhood of Ganga to that high-souled sage Jahnu. [1-43-36b, 
			37]_END

B_1_C_45_15
BEGIN_
ततस्तेषां नरव्याघ्र बुद्धिरासीन्महात्मनाम् |
अमरा निर्जराश्चैव कथं स्यामो निरामयाः || १-४५-१६_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, tigerly-man, Rama, then those great-souls speculated as to 'how we can thrive 
without ageing, illness, and likewise without death.' [1-45-16]_END

B_1_C_46_9
BEGIN_
			अग्निं कुशान् काष्ठमपः फलं मूलं तथैव च |
			न्यवेदयत् सहस्राक्षो यच्चान्यदपि कांक्षितम् ||१-४६-१०_END
BEGIN_
			The Thousand-eyed god Indra made available fire, firewood, water, the 
			sacred Kusha grass, fruits and like that tubers also, and whatever other 
			items she required in her ascetic practise. [1-46-10]_END

B_1_C_43_34
BEGIN_
			ततस्तुष्टो महातेजाः श्रोत्राभ्यामसृजत् प्रभुः |
			तस्माज्जह्नुसुता गङ्गा प्रोच्यते जाह्नवीति च || १-४३-३८_END
BEGIN_
			That greatly radiant and godly sage Jahnu is then delighted and released 
			Ganga from both of his ears. Therefore Ganga became the daughter of 
			sage Jahnu, and she is also renowned as Jahnavi, after the name of that 
			sage. [1-43-38]_END

B_1_C_47_0
BEGIN_सप्तधा तु कृते गर्भे दितिः परमदुःखिता |सहस्राक्षं दुराधर्षं वाक्यं सानुनयाब्रवीत् || १-४७-१_END
BEGIN_"Diti was highly anguished when her foetus is rendered into sevenfold, and spoke these 
appeasing words to the indomitable Thousand-eyed Indra." Thus Vishvamitra continued his narration about 
City Vishala. [1-47-1]_END

B_1_C_45_16
BEGIN_
तेषां चिंतयतां तत्र बुद्धिरासीद्विपश्चिताम् |
क्षीरोदमथनं कृत्वा रसं प्राप्स्याम तत्र वै || १-४५-१७_END
BEGIN_
A thought occurred to those masterminds who were thinking on that matter clueing 
them up, 'we indeed can get elixir of life by churning the Milky Ocean.' [1-45-17]_END

B_1_C_46_10
BEGIN_
			गात्रसंवाहनैश्चैव श्रमापनयनैस्तथा |
			शक्रः सर्वेषु कालेषु दितिं परिचचार ह || १-४६-११_END
BEGIN_
			All the time Indra indeed served Diti by massaging her body, and other 
			means of removing her bodily strain resulting from her arduous practises. 
			[1-46-11]_END

B_1_C_43_35
BEGIN_
			जगाम च पुनर्गङ्गा भगीरथरथानुगा |
			सागरं चापि संप्राप्ता सा सरित्प्रवरा तदा ||१-४३-३९
			रसातलमुपागच्छत् सिद्ध्यर्थं तस्य कर्मणः |_END
BEGIN_
			Even though Ganga again proceeded moving behind the chariot of Bhageeratha 
			and reached the ocean, therefrom she had to wend her way to netherworld, 
			once dug by the sons of Sagara, only to accomplish the mission of Bhageeratha, 
			namely drenching the ashes of Sagara's sons. [1-43-39, 40a]_END

B_1_C_47_1
BEGIN_ममापराधाद्गर्भोऽयं सप्तधा शकलीकृतः | नापराधो हि देवेश तवात्र बलसूदन || 
१-४७-२_END
BEGIN_ 'Oh, Indra, the eliminator of demon Bala, this foetus of mine is sliced into seven 
segments owing to my own misdeed, oh, ruler of gods, Indra, indeed there is no iniquity of yours in 
this matter.' Thus Diti started speaking to Indra. [1-47-2]_END

B_1_C_45_17
BEGIN_
ततो निश्चित्य मथनं योक्त्रं कृत्वा च वासुकिम् |
मन्थानं मन्दरं कृत्वा ममन्थुरमितौजसः || १-४५-१८_END
BEGIN_
Deciding upon to churn the Milky Ocean then made Vasuki, Thousand-headed King of 
Snakes, as the churning rope and Mt. Mandara as stirrer, and those brothers whose 
energy is unlimited have started churning the Milky Ocean thoroughly. [1-45-18]_END

B_1_C_46_11
BEGIN_
			पूर्णे वर्षसहस्रे तु दशोने रघुनंदन |
			दितिः परमसंहृष्टा सहस्राक्षमथाब्रवीत् ||१-४६-१२_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, Rama, the descendent of Raghu, when ten years are less to complete 
			the thousand years span of her ascetics, Diti is highly rejoiced as 
			her ambition is going to fructify in just ten more years, and then she 
			spoke to the Thousand-eyed god, Indra. [1-46-12]_END

B_1_C_43_36
BEGIN_
			भगीरथोऽपि रजार्षिर्गङ्गामादाय यत्नतः || १-४३-४०
			पितामहान् भस्मकृतानपश्यद्गतचेतनः |_END
BEGIN_
			Even kingly-sage Bhageeratha making every effort ushered Ganga to netherworld, 
			but on seeing his grandparents rendered to ashes he has became doleful. 
			[1-43-40b, 41a]_END

B_1_C_47_2
BEGIN_प्रियं त्वत्कृतमिच्छामि मम गर्भविपर्यये |मरुतां सप्तसप्तानां स्थानपाला 
भवन्तु ते || १-४७-३_END
BEGIN_Though a reversal has happened against my thinking in the matter of my pregnancy, 
let these seven segments become your seven Wind-gods, the rulers of seven ethereal-places, under your 
ruler-ship. [1-47-3]_END

B_1_C_45_18
BEGIN_
अथ वर्षसहस्रेण योक्त्रं सर्पशिरांसि च |
वमन्त्यतिविषं तत्र ददंशुर्दशनैः शिलाः || १-४५-१९_END
BEGIN_
After a thousand years, the Thousand-headed serpent Vaasuki, which is being 
used as churning rope, is incapacitated to bear the friction of churning and fanged 
the cliffs of Mt. Mandara. Thereby a great lot of venom is disgorged from the heads 
of that serpent Vaasuki, which venom on melting the rocks of Mt. Mandara became 
the holocaustic poison called haalaahala. [1-45-19]_END

B_1_C_46_12
BEGIN_
			तपश्चरन्त्या वर्षाणि दश वीर्यवतां वर |
			अवशिष्टानि भद्रं ते भ्रातरं द्रक्ष्यसे ततः ||१-४६-१३_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, best one among the valiant ones, Indra, to me who am practising 
			asceticism ten years are remaining to complete, then you can see your 
			brother, you be safe. [1-46-13]_END

B_1_C_43_37
BEGIN_
			अथ तद्भस्मनां राशिं गङ्गासलिलमुत्तमम् |
			प्लावयत् पूतपाप्मानः स्वर्गं प्रप्ता रघूत्तम ||१-४३-४१_END
BEGIN_
			"Oh, Rama, the best of Raghu's dynasty, then Ganga inundated that mound 
			of ashes of Sagara's six-thousand sons, by which those souls obtained 
			heaven, while the sins of souls are cleansed with the water of Ganga." 
			Thus Vishvamitra continued his narration. [1-43-41b, c]_END

B_1_C_47_3
BEGIN_वातस्कंधा इमे सप्त चरन्तु दिवि पुत्रक |मारुता इति विख्याता दिव्यरूपा ममात्मजाः 
||१-४७-४_END
BEGIN_Oh, son Indra, let these seven sons of mine become the seven presiding deities of 
Cosmic Air Divisions and let them move in heaven with heavenly forms. [1-47-4]_END

B_1_C_45_19
BEGIN_
उत्पपाताग्निसंकाशं हालाहलमहाविषम् |
तेन दग्धं जगत्सर्वं सदेवासुरमानुषम् || १-४५-२०_END
BEGIN_
A lethal poison similar to inferno known as haalaahala has started to fulminate 
therefrom, by which whole universe of gods, non-gods and humans is burnt down. [1-45-20]_END

B_1_C_46_13
BEGIN_
			यमहं त्वत्कृते पुत्र तमाधास्ये जयोत्सुकम् |
			त्रैलोक्यविजयं पुत्र सह भोक्ष्यसि विज्वरः || १-४६-१४_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, son Indra, whom I am bringing up for your reason, I will bring 
			him up as a victory-enthusiast, and oh, son, Indra, along with him conquering 
			the three worlds you can enjoy them, without febrility from your enemies._END

B_1_C_47_4
BEGIN_ब्रह्मलोकं चरत्वेक इन्द्रलोकं तथापरः |दिव्यवायुरिति ख्यातः तृतीयोऽपि 
महायशाः ||१-४७-५_END
BEGIN_One from the seven may permeate Brahma's abode, likewise another may permeate the 
heaven of Indra, and even the third one, let him become a greatly celebrated and reputed as Divine Wind, 
and he may circulate in entire universe. [1-47-5]_END

B_1_C_45_20
BEGIN_
अथ देवा महादेवं शंकरं शरणार्थिनः |
जग्मुः पशुपतिं रुद्रं त्राहि त्राहीति तुष्टुवुः || १-४५-२१_END
BEGIN_
The gods seeking shelter then approached Rudra, the Cardinal God, Endower of Solace, 
and who husbands all the created animals inclusive of human-animals, namely Shiva, 
and they prayed to him saying 'save, save us.' [1-45-21]_END

B_1_C_46_14
BEGIN_
			याचितेन सुरश्रेष्ट पित्रा तव महात्मना |
			वरो वर्षसहस्रान्ते मम दत्तः सुतं प्रति || १-४६-१५_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, best one among gods, Indra, on my prayer your high-souled father 
			Sage Kaashyapa bestowed this boon on me for a son, which materialises 
			at the end of thousand years, and only ten more years are to slip by. 
			[1-46-15]_END

B_1_C_47_5
BEGIN_चत्वारस्तु सुरश्रेष्ठ दिशो वै तव शासनात् |संचरिष्यन्ति भद्रं ते कलेन हि ममात्मजाः ||१-४७-६
    त्वत्कृतेनैव नाम्ना वै मारुता इति विश्रुताः |_END
BEGIN_'Oh, chief of gods, Indra, let four of my sons permeate four directions according to 
time and at your command, let safety betide you, and let them be renowned verily by the name given by 
you as 'Marut,' because you have coaxed the crying fragments of foetus saying, 'maa ruda, maa ruda, 
'do not cry, do not cry...' Thus Diti said to Indra. [1-47-6, 7a]_END

B_1_C_45_21
BEGIN_
एवमुक्तस्ततो देवैर्देवदेवेश्वरः प्रभुः |
प्रादुरासीत् ततोऽत्रैव शंखचक्रधरो हरिः || १-४५-२२_END
BEGIN_
This way while the gods are praying the Lord and God of Gods, namely Shiva, then 
handling his disc and conch-shell Vishnu has also revealed himself at that place. 
[1-45-22]_END

B_1_C_46_15
BEGIN_
			इत्युक्त्वा च दितिस्तत्र प्राप्ते मध्यन्दिनेश्वरे |
			निद्रयापहृता देवी पादौ कृत्वाथ शीर्षतः ||१-४६-१६_END
BEGIN_
			When Diti was saying thus, the noontime sun was reigning high that 
			lady is stolen over by sleep keeping her feet headward. [1-46-16]_END

B_1_C_47_6
BEGIN_तस्यास्तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा सहस्राक्षः पुरंदरः ||१-४७-७उवाच प्रांजलिर्वाक्यं 
दितिं बलनिषूदनः |_END
BEGIN_On hearing her words, the Thousand-eyed destroyer of enemy's citadels and a demon named 
Bala, namely Indra, spoke this word to Diti, humbly adjoining his palms. [1-47-7b, 8a]_END

B_1_C_46_16
BEGIN_
			दृष्ट्वा तामशुचिं शक्रः पादयोः कृतमूर्धजाम् |
			शिरःस्थाने कृतौ पादौ जहास च मुमोद च || १-४६-१७_END
BEGIN_
			On observing her who has become impious by placing her head at feet-side 
			and braid falling on feet, Indra is gladdened and laughed at her failed 
			asceticism. [1-46-17]_END

B_1_C_45_22
BEGIN_
उवाचैनं स्मितं कृत्वा रुद्रं शूलधरं हरिः |
दैवतैर्मथ्यमाने तु तत्पूर्वं समुपस्थितम् || १-४५-२३
तत्त्वदीयं सुरश्रेष्ठ सुराणामग्रतो हि यत् |
अग्रपूजामिह स्थित्वा गृहाणेदं विषं प्रभो || १-४५-२४_END
BEGIN_
And Vishnu smilingly spoke to wielder of trident Rudra, 'oh, god the best, whatever 
element that has emerged from the churning of Milk Ocean by gods, that shall belong 
to you, isn't it. By virtue of your position as the foremost god among gods, oh, 
omnicompetent god Shiva, you please accept this poison applying yourself to that 
position of foremost god, and deeming this poison, haalahala, as a foremost oblation 
to your godhood'. [1-45-23, 24]_END

B_1_C_48_0
BEGIN_
पृष्ट्वा तु कुशलं तत्र परस्परसमागमे |
कथान्ते सुमतिर्वाक्यं व्याजहार महामुनिम् || १-४८-१_END
BEGIN_
When those two, Vishvamitra and Sumati, have met one another there at that place, 
king Sumati raised the topic of Rama and Lakshmana, after exchanging greetings and 
enquiring about the well-being of the great-saint Vishvamitra. [1-48-1]_END

B_1_C_47_7
BEGIN_सर्वमेतद्यथोक्तं ते भविष्यति न संशयः ||१-४७-८विचरिष्यन्ति भद्रं ते देवरूपास्तवात्मजाः |
एवं तौ निश्चयं कृत्वा मातापुत्रौ तपोवने ||१-४७-९जग्मतुस्त्रिदिवं राम कृतार्थाविति नः श्रुतम् |_END
BEGIN_" 'All this will happen as you have said, undoubtedly, and your offspring, the Maaruta-s, 
would be pervading in the forms of gods, you be safe.' Thus Indra assured Diti. Those two, the stepmother 
Diti and the stepson Indra, on arriving at a decision in that ascetic forest, departed to heaven fulfilling 
their purposes. Thus we heard the legend." Thus Vishvamitra continued his narration. [1-47-8b, 9, 10a]_END

B_1_C_46_17
BEGIN_
			तस्याः शरीरविवरं प्रविवेश पुरंदरः |
			गर्भं च सप्तधा राम चिच्छेद परमात्मवान् ||१-४६-१८_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, Rama, being a highly courageous one, Indra the destroyer of enemy 
			fastnesses, entered the body of Diti through her vaginal aperture and 
			rent her foetus asunder into seven fragments. [1-46-18]_END

B_1_C_45_23
BEGIN_
इत्युक्त्वा च सुरश्रेष्ठस्तत्रैवान्तरधीयत |
देवतानां भयं दृष्ट्वा श्रुत्वा वाक्यं तु शार्ङ्गिणः || १-४५-२५
हालाहलं विषं घोरं संजग्राहामृतोपमम् |_END
BEGIN_
Saying so Vishnu, the best one among gods, has disappeared then and there only. 
And on observing the scare of gods and also on paying heed to the words of the Wielder 
of Bow called shaar~Nga, namely Vishnu, god Shiva gulped that lethal poison,
haalaahala , as if it is ambrosia. [1-45-25, 26a]_END

B_1_C_48_1
BEGIN_
इमौ कुमारौ भद्रं ते देवतुल्यपराक्रमौ |
गजसिंहगती वीरौ शार्दूलवृषभोपमौ || १-४८-२
पद्मपत्रविशालाक्षौ खड्गतूणीधनुर्धरौ |
अश्विनाविव रूपेण समुपस्थितयौवनौ || १-४८-३
यदृच्छयैव गां प्राप्तौ देवलोकादिवामरौ |
कथं पद्भ्यामिह प्राप्तौ किमर्थं कस्य वा मुने || १-४८-४_END
BEGIN_  
"These two youngsters, oh, sage, let safety betide you, striding like audacious 
elephants and arrogant lions, bearing a similitude to adventurous tigers and adamantine 
bulls, and wielding quivers, swords, and bows, are valorous with their valour matching 
that of Vishnu, and with their eyes broad like lotus-petals and with youthfulness 
in the offing they look like the exceptionally beautiful twin-gods, Ashwin-brothers, 
by their physique. How these two have footslogged and chanced here as though immortals 
have chanced on earth from the abode of gods at their pleasure? What for they have 
come here, and whose scions are they? [1-48-2, 3, 4]_END

B_1_C_47_8
BEGIN_एष देशः स काकुत्स्थ महेन्द्राध्युषितः पुरा || १-४७-१०दितिं यत्र तपःसिद्धामेवं
परिचचार सः |_END
BEGIN_Oh, Rama of Kakutstha, this province is that one which was once presided over by Indra, 
and where he rendered services to that accomplished one in her asceticism, namely lady Diti. [1-47-10b, 
11a]_END

B_1_C_46_18
BEGIN_
			भिद्यमानस्ततो गर्भो वज्रेण शतपर्वणा |
			रुरोद सुस्वरं राम ततो दितिरबुध्यत || १-४६-१९_END
BEGIN_
			Oh, Rama, then that foetus wailed clamorously while being sliced with 
			Thunderbolt that has hundred cutting edges, and then Diti woke up. [1-46-19]_END

B_1_C_45_24
BEGIN_
देवान् विसृज्य देवेशो जगाम भगवान् हरः॥ १-४५-२६
ततो देवासुराः सर्वे ममन्थू रघुनन्दन।_END
BEGIN_
The god of gods Hara then left for his abode Kailash parting with other gods, and 
oh, Rama, the joy of Raghu's dynasty, the gods and non-gods have continued to churn 
the Milky Ocean. [1-45-26b, 27a]_END

B_1_C_48_2
BEGIN_
भूषयन्ताविमं देशं चन्द्रसूर्याविवाम्बरम् |
परस्परेण सदृशौ प्रमाणेङ्गितचेष्टितैः || १-४८-५
किमर्थं च नरश्रेष्ठौ संप्राप्तौ दुर्गमे पथि |
वरायुधधरौ वीरौ श्रोतुमिच्छामि तत्त्वतः || १-४८-६_END
BEGIN_
"These two best ones among men are identical to one another by their bodily proportion, 
facial-language, and by bodily gestures, and with their presence they refurbish 
this province like the Moon and Sun brightening the firmament. In truth, I would 
like to know for what reason these valiant ones who are wielding best weapons have 
arrived here travelling on an arduous path." Thus, king Sumati asked Vishvamitra. 
[1-48-5, 6]_END

B_1_C_47_9
BEGIN_इक्ष्वाकोस्तु नरव्याघ्र पुत्रः परमधार्मिकः || १-४७-११अलंबुषायामुत्पन्नो विशाल 
इति विश्रुतः |तेन चासीदिह स्थाने विशालेति पुरी कृता || १-४७-१२_END
BEGIN_To king Ikshvaku of Vishaala, oh, tigerly-man Rama, a highly righteous son was born 
through queen Alambusa, and he was renowned as Vishaala. There is a city in this place constructed by 
him and known by his own name, Vishaala. [1-47-11b, 12]_END

B_1_C_46_19
BEGIN_
			मा रुदो मा रुदश्चेति गर्भं शक्रोऽभ्यभाषत |
			बिभेद च महातेजा रुदन्तमपि वासवः || १-४६-२०_END
BEGIN_
			'Do not scream, do not scream...' thus Indra was coaxing the foetus, 
			and even though that foetus is screaming piteously the great resplendent 
			Indra has gone on fragmenting it. [1-46-20]_END

B_1_C_45_25
BEGIN_
प्रविवेशाथ पातालं मन्थानः पर्वतोत्तमः॥ १-४५-२७
ततो देवाः सगन्धर्वाः तुष्टुवुर्मधुसूदनम्।_END
BEGIN_
Now the loftiest mountain that is being used as stirrer, namely Mt. Mandara, has 
caved into the netherworld, thereby the gods along with gandharva-s have prayed 
to Madhusuudana, the other name of Vishnu. [1-45-27b, 28a]_END

B_1_C_48_3
BEGIN_
तस्य तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा यथावृत्तं न्यवेदयत् |
सिद्धाश्रमनिवासं च राक्षसानां वधं तथा | १-४८-७_END
BEGIN_
On hearing those words of King Sumati, Vishvamitra informed him about the visit 
of Rama and Lakshmana to the Hermitage of Accomplishment, also about the elimination 
of demons, as it has happened. [1-48-7a, 7b]_END

B_1_C_47_10
BEGIN_विशालस्य सुतो राम हेमचन्द्रो महाबलः |सुचन्द्र इति विख्यातो हेमचन्द्रादनंतरः 
|| १-४७-१३_END
BEGIN_"Oh, Rama, Vishaala's son is the great-mighty Hemachandra, and Hemachandra's son is highly 
renowned as Suchandra.. [1-47-13]_END

B_1_C_46_20
BEGIN_
			न हन्तव्यं न हन्तव्यमित्येवं दितिरब्रवीत् |
			निष्पपात ततः शक्रो मातुर्वचनगौरवात् ||१-४६-२१_END
BEGIN_
			'Unkillable, unkillable is my foetus...' thus Diti raved in that way, 
			and then Indra fell out of the womb honouring his stepmother's entreaty. 
			[1-46-21]_END

B_1_C_45_26
BEGIN_
त्वं गतिः सर्वभूतानां विशेषेण दिवौकसाम्॥ १-४५-२८
पालयास्मान् महाबाहो गिरिमुद्धर्तुमर्हसि।_END
BEGIN_
 'You alone are the recourse to all beings, especially to the dwellers in heavens, 
oh ambidextrous god Vishnu, you safeguard us, it will be apt of you elevate the 
mountain.' So prayed gods to Vishnu. [1-45-28b, 29a]_END

B_1_C_48_4
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रवचः श्रुत्वा राजा परमविस्मितः || १-४८-७
अतिथी परमौ प्राप्तं पुत्रौ दशरथस्य तौ |
पूजयामास विधिवत् सत्कारार्हौ महाबलौ || १-४८-८_END
BEGIN_
King Sumati is highly astonished to hear the words of Vishvamitra about the visit 
of Rama and Lakshmana, and treating them to have come as the most prominent and 
honour-worthy guests that king started to honour those two great-mighty sons of 
Dasharatha customarily. [1-48-7c, 8]_END

B_1_C_47_11
BEGIN_सुचन्द्रतनयो राम धूम्राश्व इति विश्रुतः |धूम्राश्वतनयश्चापि सृंजयः समपद्यत 
|| १-४७-१४_END
BEGIN_"The son of Suchandra became famous as Dhuumraashva, and oh, Rama, Dhuumraashva derived 
his son named Srinjaya. [1-47-14]_END

B_1_C_46_21
BEGIN_
			प्रांजलिर्वज्रसहितो दितिं शक्रोऽभ्यभाषत |
			अशुचिर्देवि सुप्तासि पादयोः कृतमूर्धजा|| १-४६-२२_END
BEGIN_
			Indra humbly folding his palms that are still handling his bloody Thunderbolt 
			spoke to Diti, 'oh, lady, you have become impious when your braid touched 
			your feet and when you have gone to sleep in midday, and you vow is 
			thwarted.' [1-46-22]_END

B_1_C_45_27
BEGIN_
इति श्रुत्वा हृषीकेशः कामठं रूपमास्थितः॥ १-४५-२९
पर्वतं पृष्ठतः कृत्वा शिश्ये तत्रोदधौ हरिः।_END
BEGIN_
Hearing the prayer of gods Vishnu, Hrisheekesha, the controller of senses, adopting 
the form of a tortoise and positioning the stirring Mt. Mandara on that tortoiseshell, 
he lay recumbent at the bottom of Milky Ocean as a base to the stirrer. [1-45-29b, 
30a]_END

B_1_C_48_5
BEGIN_
ततः परमसत्कारं सुमतेः प्राप्य राघवौ |
उष्य तत्र निशामेकां जग्मतुर्मिथिलां ततः || १-४८-९_END
BEGIN_
On getting high honours from King Sumati, Raghava-s stayed there along with Vishvamitra 
and with the community of sages for one night, and then they all have moved on to 
Mithila. [1-48-9]_END

B_1_C_47_12
BEGIN_सृंजयस्य सुतः श्रीमान् सहदेवः प्रतापवान् |कुशाश्वः सहदेवस्य पुत्रः परमधार्मिकः 
|| १-४७-१५_END
BEGIN_The fortunate and valorous son of Srinjaya is Sahadeva, and the son of Sahadeva is the 
most righteous Kushaashva. [1-47-15]_END

B_1_C_46_22
BEGIN_
			तदन्तरमहं लब्ध्वा शक्रहन्तारमाहवे |
			अभिदं सप्तधा देवि तन्मे त्वम् क्षन्तुमर्हसि || १-४६-२३_END
BEGIN_
			"Thereby I gained a chance to eliminate him who can eliminate Indra 
			in a battle. Hence I fragmented your foetus into seven fragments, and 
			it will be apt of you to pardon me for that act of mine." So said 
			Indra to lady Diti. Thus, Sage Vishvamitra continued narration about 
			City of Vishaala. [1-46-23]_END

B_1_C_45_28
BEGIN_
पर्वताग्रं तु लोकात्मा हस्तेनाक्रम्य केशवः॥ १-४५-३०
देवानां मध्यतः स्थित्वा ममन्थ पुरुषोत्तमः।_END
BEGIN_
Keshava then reached out his hand and grasped the mountaintop as he is the Cosmic-Soul, 
and thus staying amid gods that Supreme Person Vishnu participated in churning the 
ocean by holding the stirring mountain upright. [1-45-30b, 31a]_END

B_1_C_49_0
BEGIN_
अफलस्तु ततः शक्रो देवानग्निपुरोगमान् |
अब्रवीत् त्रस्तनयनः सिद्धगन्धर्वचारणान् || १-४९-१_END
BEGIN_
The emasculated Indra then with panicked eyes spoke to gods, siddha-s, gandharva-s, 
and carana-s, keeping Fire-god as their helms-god. [1-49-1]_END

B_1_C_48_6
BEGIN_
तां दृष्ट्वा मुनयः सर्वे जनकस्य पुरीं शुभाम् |
साधु साध्विति शंसन्तो मिथिलां समपूजयन् || १-४८-१०_END
BEGIN_
On seeing Janaka's auspicious city Mithila, all of the saints who are accompanying 
Vishvamitra, Rama, and Lakshmana, extolled it saying, "Splendid! Splendid!" and 
admired it highly. [1-48-10]_END

B_1_C_47_13
BEGIN_कुशाश्वस्य महातेजाः सोमदत्तः प्रतापवान् |सोमदत्तस्य पुत्रस्तु काकुत्स्थ इति 
विश्रुतः ||१-४७-१६_END
BEGIN_The highly resplendent and dauntless Somadatta is the son of Kushaashva and Somadatta's 
son is highly reputed as Kakutstha. [1-47-16]_END

B_1_C_45_29
BEGIN_
अथ वर्षसहस्रेण आयुर्वेदमयः पुमान्॥ १-४५-३१
उदतिष्ठत् सुधर्मात्मा सदण्डः सकमण्डलुः।
पूर्वं धन्वन्तरिर्नाम अप्सराश्च सुवर्चसः॥ १-४५-३२_END
BEGIN_
After a thousand years of churning, then a male personality, an epitome of Life 
Sciences, namely aayurveda , a highly righteous soul, named Dhanvantari, 
has firstly surfaced with his arm-rest-stick and with his handy water-vessel, and 
then the remarkably elegant Apsara-s, angelic damsels, have emerged next to him 
from the Milky Ocean. [1-45-31b, 32]_END

B_1_C_49_1
BEGIN_
कुर्वता तपसो विघ्नं गौतमस्य महात्मनः |
क्रोधमुत्पाद्य हि मया सुरकार्यमिदं कृतम् || १-४९-२_END
BEGIN_
I have Indeed incited fury in that noble-souled Sage Gautama by effectuating 
hindrance in his asceticism, but I have accomplished a task of gods. [1-49-2]_END

B_1_C_48_7
BEGIN_
मिथिलोपवने तत्र आश्रमं दृश्य राघवः |
पुराणं निर्जनं रम्यं पप्रच्छ मुनिपुंगवम् || १-४८-११_END
BEGIN_
On seeing a hermitage in the fringes of Mithila, that appeared to be age-old, but 
now uninhabited, yet pleasing, Rama asked the eminent sage Vishvamitra. [1-48-11]_END

B_1_C_47_14
BEGIN_तस्य पुत्रो महातेजाः संप्रत्येष पुरीमिमाम् |आवसत्परमप्रख्यः सुमतिर्नाम दुर्जयः 
|| १-४७-१७_END
BEGIN_Presently that Kakutstha's son named Sumati, who is a great-resplendent one, an unconquerable 
one, and a highly celebrated one is dwelling in this city. [1-47-17]_END

B_1_C_45_30
BEGIN_
अप्सु निर्मथनादेव रसात्तस्माद्वरस्त्रियः।
उत्पेतुर्मनुजश्रेष्ठ तस्मादप्सरसोऽभवन्॥ १-४५-३३_END
BEGIN_
Choicest females have come out an elixir obtained on absolute churning of the waters 
of Milk Ocean, oh, best one among men, Rama, thereby that genera of females became 
Apsara-s. [1-45-33]_END

B_1_C_49_2
BEGIN_
अफलोऽस्मि कृतस्तेन क्रोधात् सा च निराकृता |
शापमोक्षेण महता तपोऽस्यापहृतं मया || १-४९-३_END
BEGIN_
By Gautama's anger I am rendered testicle-less and his wife Ahalya is also rejected 
by the sage, and thus by his releasing a severe curse his propriety for ascesis 
is dwindled, therefore his ascesis is pre-empted by me. [1-49-3]_END

B_1_C_48_8
BEGIN_
इदमाश्रमसंकाशं किं न्विदं मुनिवर्जितम् |
श्रोतुमिच्छामि भगवन् कस्यायं पूर्व आश्रमः || १-४८-१२_END
BEGIN_
"This is semblable to a hermitage but sages seem to have discarded it. Oh, venerable 
sage, whose is this hermitage previously, I wish to listen of it." Thus, Rama asked 
Vishvamitra. [1-48-12]_END

B_1_C_47_15
BEGIN_इक्ष्वाकोस्तु प्रसादेन सर्वे वैशालिका नृपाः |दीर्घायुषो महात्मानो वीर्यवन्तः 
सुधार्मिकाः || १-४७-१८_END
BEGIN_By the grace of Ikshvaku, the successive kings of Vishaala have longevity, intrepidity, 
well-off in generosity, and they were great-souled ones. [1-47-18]_END

B_1_C_45_31
BEGIN_
षष्टिः कोट्योऽभवंस्तासामप्सराणां सुवर्चसाम्।
असन्ख्येयास्तु काकुत्स्थ यास्तासां परिचारिकाः॥ १-४५-३४_END
BEGIN_
Six hundred millions of such Apsara-s with amazing dazzle have emerged from the 
churning of Milky Ocean, oh, descendent of Kakutstha, and their maidservants who 
emerged along with them are innumerable. [1-45-34]_END

B_1_C_49_3
BEGIN_
तन्मां सुरवराः सर्वे सर्षिसंघाः सचारणाः |
सुरकार्यकरं यूयं सफलं कर्तुमर्हथ || १-४९-४_END
BEGIN_
'Therefore, oh, all gods with the assemblages of sages and caarana-s, it will 
be apt of you to make me virile again, as I have acted for the benefit of gods.' 
Thus Indra spoke to all gods. [1-49-4]_END

B_1_C_48_9
BEGIN_
तच्छ्रुत्वा राघवेणोक्तं वाक्यं वाक्यविशारदः |
प्रत्युवाच महातेजा विश्वमित्रो महामुनिः || १-४८-१३_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that sentence spoken by Raghava, the expert in sententiousness, a great 
resplendent sage and eminent-saint Vishvamitra replied him in this way. [1-48-13]_END

B_1_C_47_16
BEGIN_इहाद्य रजनीमेकां सुखं स्वप्स्यामहे वयम् |श्वः प्रभाते नरश्रेष्ठ जनकं द्रष्टुमर्हसि || १-४७-१९_END
BEGIN_"Today we may gladly go to sleep here for a night, and oh, best one among men, and it 
will be apt of you to see Janaka, the King of Mithila tomorrow morning." Thus Sage Vishvamitra spoke 
to Rama and Lakshmana. [1-47-19]_END

B_1_C_45_32
BEGIN_
न ताः स्म प्रतिगृह्णन्ति सर्वे ते देवदानवाः।
अप्रतिग्रहणादेव ता वै साधारणाः स्मृताः॥ १-४५-३५_END
BEGIN_
Anybody either from gods or demons espoused them, and when none espoused them they 
are virtually reckoned as 'general-purpose' Apsara-females. [1-45-35]_END

B_1_C_49_4
BEGIN_
शतक्रतोर्वचः श्रुत्वा देवाः साग्निपुरोगमाः |
पितृदेवानुपेत्याहुः सह सर्वैः मरुद्गणैः || १-४९-५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of the officiator for Hundred-Vedic-rituals, namely Indra, 
all of the gods and other assemblages of celestials, together with the groups of 
Marut-gods came to the godly manes keeping the Fire-god in van, and appealed. [1-49-5]_END

B_1_C_47_17
BEGIN_सुमतिस्तु महातेजा विश्वामित्रमुपागतम् |श्रुत्वा नरवरश्रेष्ठः प्रत्यागच्छन् 
महायशाः || १-४७-२०_END
BEGIN_The best one among best men, a widely reputed and the highly resplendent king of Vishaala, 
namely Sumati, having heard that Vishvamitra has arrived at the precincts of the city, came to him for 
a warm welcome. [1-47-20]_END

B_1_C_48_10
BEGIN_
हन्त ते कथयिष्यामि शृणु तत्त्वेन राघव |
यस्यैतदाश्रमपदं शप्तं कोपान्महात्मना || १-४८-१४_END
BEGIN_
What a pleasure! You may listen as I narrate, Raghava, whose hermitage is this 
factually, and which great soul has resentfully cursed this. [1-48-14]_END

B_1_C_45_33
BEGIN_
वरुणस्य ततः कन्या वारुणी रघुनन्दन।
उत्पपात महाभागा मार्गमाणा परिग्रहम्॥ १-४५-३६_END
BEGIN_
Oh, descendent of Raghu, then the heaven-sent damsel Vaaruni came up from Milky 
Ocean searching for her espousal, who is the daughter of Varuna, the Rain-god, and 
who incidentally is the presiding deity of hard liquors and also called as sura. 
[1-45-36]_END

B_1_C_49_5
BEGIN_
अयं मेषः सवृषणः शक्रो ह्यवृषणः कृतः |
मेषस्य वृषणौ गृह्य शक्रायाशु प्रयच्छत || १-४९-६_END
BEGIN_
'This ram is with testicles and Indra is indeed rendered testicle-less. Taking 
the testicles of this ram they may be given to Indra quickly.' Thus Fire-god started 
his appeal to manes. [1-49-6]_END

B_1_C_47_18
BEGIN_पूजां च परमां कृत्वा सोपाध्यायः सबान्धवः |प्रांजलिः कुशलं पृष्ट्वा विश्वामित्रमथाब्रवीत् || १-४७-२१_END
BEGIN_King Sumati arrived along with his mentors and family members, offered an excellent veneration 
to Vishvamitra, and then spoke to the sage with adjoined palms enquiring about his well being. [1-47-21]_END

B_1_C_48_11
BEGIN_
गौतमस्य नरश्रेष्ठ पूर्वमासीन्महात्मनः |
आश्रमो दिव्यसंकाशः सुरैरपि सुपूजितः || १-४८-१५_END
BEGIN_
Oh, the best one among men Rama, this hermitage with a heavenly glisten, and highly 
hallowed even by gods, once belonged to the great-souled sage Gautama. [1-48-15]_END

B_1_C_45_34
BEGIN_
दितेः पुत्रा न तां राम जगृहुर्वरुणात्मजाम्।
अदितेस्तु सुता वीर जगृहुस्तामनिन्दिताम्॥ १-४५-३७_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, the sons of Diti, namely asuraa-s, have not espoused that daughter of 
Rain-god, but oh, brave Rama, the sons of Aditi on their part, namely sura-s, have 
espoused that impeccable Vaaruni. [1-45-37]_END

B_1_C_49_6
BEGIN_
अफलस्तु कृतो मेषः परां तुष्टिं प्रदास्यति |
भवतां हर्षणार्थाय ये च दास्यन्ति मानवाः |
अक्षयं हि फलं तेषां यूयं दास्यथ पुष्कलम् || १-४९-७_END
BEGIN_
'This ram that is being offered to you shall now be gelded to give its testes 
to Indra, and though this ram is deprived of its organ it will be complete and it 
endows complete satisfaction to you. To those humans who hereafter offer testes-less 
rams in sacrifices for the purpose of your gratification, you shall truly offer 
them plentiful and unmitigated benefits.' Thus Agni, the Fire-god spoke to manes. 
[1-49-7]_END

B_1_C_47_19
BEGIN_धन्योऽस्म्यनुगृहीतोऽस्मि यस्य मे विषयं मुने |संप्राप्तो दर्शनं चैव नास्ति 
धन्यतरो मम || १-४७-२२_END
BEGIN_"To which province you have visited that happens to be mine, thereby I could get an audience 
of yours without stirring myself from my country, hence none will be more fortunate than me." So said 
king Sumati to Vishvamitra. [1-47-22]_END

B_1_C_48_12
BEGIN_
स चात्र तप आतिष्ठदहल्यासहितः पुरा |
वर्षपूगान्यनेकानि राजपुत्र महायशः || १-४८-१६_END
BEGIN_
In this hermitage, oh, prince Rama, once that highly renowned Sage Gautama sat 
tight in asceticism for numerous cycle of years along with his wife Ahalya. [1-48-16]_END

B_1_C_45_35
BEGIN_
असुरास्तेन दैतेयाः सुरास्तेनादितेः सुताः।
हृष्टाः प्रमुदिताश्चासन् वारुणीग्रहणात् सुराः॥ १-४५-३८_END
BEGIN_
Thereby the sons of Diti are called asuraa-s, and the sons of Aditi are 
called suraa-s, and gods are delighted and rejoiced on espousing Vaaruni. 
[1-45-38]_END

B_1_C_49_7
BEGIN_
अग्नेस्तु वचनं श्रुत्वा पितृदेवाः समागताः |
उत्पाट्य मेषवृषणौ सहस्राक्षे न्यवेशयन् || १-४९-८_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Agni, the Fire-god, the manes-gods who gathered to collect 
their share of offering have extricated that ram's testes, which is not yet sacrificed 
but tethered to a sacrificial post, and offered them to the Thousand-eyed Indra. 
[1-49-8]_END

B_1_C_48_13
BEGIN_
तस्यान्तरं विदित्वा तु सहस्राक्षः शचीपतिः |
मुनिवेषधरो भूत्वाऽहल्यामिदमब्रवीत् || १-४८-१७_END
BEGIN_
On knowing the meantime of Gautama's availability at hermitage, Indra, the husband 
of Shaci Devi and the Thousand-eyed god wearing the guise of sage Gautama and becoming 
such a sage, approached Ahalya and said this to her. [1-48-17]_END

B_1_C_45_36
BEGIN_
उच्चैःश्रवा हयश्रेष्ठो मणिरत्नं च कौस्तुभम्।
उदतिष्ठन्नरश्रेष्ठ तथैवामृतमुत्तमम्॥ १-४५-३९_END
BEGIN_
Then a best horse called Ucchaishravaa has emerged, oh, Rama, the best among men, 
and then a gem of a jewel, called Kaustubha, and like that amrita, the 
Supreme ambrosial elixir of gods, have also emerged. [1-45-39]_END

B_1_C_49_8
BEGIN_
तदा प्रभृति काकुत्स्थ पितृदेवाः समागताः |
अफलान् भुंजते मेषान् फलैस्तेषामयोजयन् || १-४९-९_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama of Kakutstha, from then onwards the manes-gods who come to collect their 
share are enjoying even the goats, even if they do not have testes, to endow benefits 
thereof to those that offer those goats, and to join the testes of goats to Indra. 
[1-49-9]_END

B_1_C_48_14
BEGIN_
ऋतुकालं प्रतीक्षन्ते नार्थिनः सुसमाहिते |
संगमं त्वहमिच्छामि त्वया सह सुमध्यमे || १-४८-१८_END
BEGIN_
Oh, finely limbed lady, indulgers do not watch out for the time to conceive, 
as such oh, slender-waisted one, I desire copulation with you. [1-48-18]_END

B_1_C_45_37
BEGIN_
अथ तस्य कृते राम महानासीत् कुलक्षयः।
अदितेस्तु ततः पुत्रा दितेः पुत्रानसूदयन्॥ १-४५-४०_END
BEGIN_
Owing to the dispute regarding the possession of that ambrosia, oh, Rama, then 
there chanced a rampant ethnic havoc, and then the sons of Aditi have havocked the 
sons of Diti. [1-45-40]_END

B_1_C_49_9
BEGIN_
इन्द्रस्तु मेषवृषणस्तदा प्रभृति राघव |
गौतमस्य प्रभावेन तपसा च महात्मनः || १-४९-१०_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Raghava, owing to the efficacy of the great-souled Gautama and his ascesis, 
from then onwards Indra has became one with the testes of a goat. [1-49-10]_END

B_1_C_48_15
BEGIN_
मुनिवेषं सहस्राक्षं विज्ञाय रघुनंदन |
मतिं चकार दुर्मेधा देवराजकुतूहलात् || १-४८-१९_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, the legatee of Raghu, though knowing him as the Thousand-eyed Indra in 
the guise of her husband Gautama, she is inclined to have intercourse ill-advisedly, 
only to satisfy the impassion of the King of Gods. [1-48-19]_END

B_1_C_45_38
BEGIN_
एकतामगमन् सर्वे असुरा राक्षसैः सह।
युद्धमासीन् महाघोरं वीरत्रैलोक्यमोहनम्॥ १-४५-४१_END
BEGIN_
All the asura-s and demons have come to one side against sura-s, and there occurred 
a very gruesome war which was perplexing to all the triad of universe viz., ethereal, 
real and surreal spheres. [1-45-41]_END

B_1_C_49_10
BEGIN_
तदागच्छ महातेज आश्रमं पुण्यकर्मणः |
तारयैनां महाभागामहल्यां देवरूपिणीम् || १-४९-११_END
BEGIN_
"Therefore, oh, great-resplendent Rama, enter the hermitage of Gautama whose deeds 
are pietistic, and atone Ahalya who is highly fortunate and who is in the compose 
of a divinity." Thus Vishvamitra spoke to Rama. [1-49-11]_END

B_1_C_48_16
BEGIN_
अथाब्रवीत् सुरश्रेष्ठं कृतार्थेनान्तरात्मना |
कृतार्थास्मि सुरश्रेष्ठ गच्छ शीघ्रमितः प्रभो || १-४८-२०
आत्मानं मां च देवेश सर्वदा रक्ष गौतमात् |_END
BEGIN_
She felt fulfilled in her heart of hearts and then she said this to that best god 
Indra, 'I am gratified in complying with your wish, oh, best of gods, get going 
oh, lord, from here quickly, oh, ruler of gods, always safeguard yourself and me 
from Sage Gautama.' Thus, Ahalya said to Indra. [1-48-20, 21a]_END

B_1_C_45_39
BEGIN_
यदा क्षयं गतं सर्वं तदा विष्णुर्महाबलः।
अमृतं सोऽहरत्तूर्णं मायामास्थाय मोहिनीम्॥ १-४५-४२_END
BEGIN_
When everything is wading into annihilation then that omnicompetent Vishnu swiftly 
impounded Amrita, the Divine Elixir, by assuming his illusory power of Mohini. [1-45-42]_END

B_1_C_49_11
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रवचः श्रुत्वा राघवः सहलक्ष्मणः |
विश्वामित्रं पुरस्कृत्य आश्रमं प्रविवेश ह || १-४९-१२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing Vishvamitra's words Rama entered the hermitage along with Lakshmana and 
keeping Vishvamitra afore. [1-49-12]_END

B_1_C_48_17
BEGIN_
इन्द्रस्तु प्रहसन् वाक्यमहल्यामिदमब्रवीत् || १-४८-२१
सुश्रोणि परितुष्टोऽस्मि गमिष्यामि यथागतम् |_END
BEGIN_
Indra on his part smilingly said this word to Ahalya, 'oh, well-hipped lady, I 
am quite delighted, here I go as I have came.' [1-48-21b, 22a]_END

B_1_C_45_40
BEGIN_
ये गताभिमुखं विष्णुमक्षरं पुरुषोत्तमम्।
संपिष्टास्ते तदा युद्धे विष्णुना प्रभविष्णुना॥ १-४५-४३_END
BEGIN_
Whoever confronted that Eternal and Supreme Person, namely Vishnu, in that war, 
then Vishnu whose blaze is threefold as manifest in the sun, fire and lightning, 
has pulverised him. [1-45-43]_END

B_1_C_49_12
BEGIN_
ददर्श च महाभागां तपसा द्योतितप्रभाम् |
लोकैरपि समागम्य दुर्निरीक्ष्यां सुरासुरैः || १-४९-१३
प्रयत्नान्निर्मितां धात्रा दिव्यां मायामयीमिव |
धूमेनाभिपरीताङ्गीं दीप्तामग्निशिखामिव || १-४९-१४
सतुषारावृतां साभ्रां पूर्णचन्द्रप्रभामिव |
मध्येऽम्भसो दुराधर्षां दीप्तां सूर्यप्रभामिव || १-४९-१५_END
BEGIN_
She whose splendour is brightened by her ascesis, at whom it is impossible to raise 
an eye for a stare either for gods, or for demons, or for the worldly beings on 
coming close to her, whom the Creator has contrived with careful contemplation as 
an angelic and a completely phantasmal entity, who is like the befogged and beclouded 
moonshine of a full moon as she is hitherto enshrouded by the dried up leaves and 
dust, who is like an unwatchable sunshine mirrored in and glowing from the midst 
of water, for she is hitherto in the midst of denounce, and whose limbs are like 
the tongues of a flaring fire around which fumes are cloaking, as she is hitherto 
practising an utmost ascesis subsisting on air alone, which ascesis alone made her 
like a flaring Ritual Fir, and Rama has seen such a highly glorious Ahalya. [1-49-13, 
14, 15]_END

B_1_C_48_18
BEGIN_
एवं संगम्य तु तया निश्चक्रामोटजात्ततः || १-४८-२२
स संभ्रमात्त्वरन् राम शङ्कितो गौतमं प्रति |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, Indra then came out of the cottage flustering hurriedly after copulating 
with her with an uncertainty about the arrival of Sage Gautama. [1-48-22b, 23a]_END

B_1_C_45_41
BEGIN_
अदितेरात्मजा वीरा दितेः पुत्रान्निजघ्‌निरे।
अस्मिन् घोरे महायुद्धे दैतेयादित्ययोर्भृशम्॥ १-४५-४४_END
BEGIN_
In this horrendous war between the progeny of Diti, namely demons, and the progeny 
of Aditi, namely gods, the sons of Aditi being gods, have altogether massacred the 
demonic sons of Diti. [1-45-44]_END

B_1_C_49_13
BEGIN_
सा हि गौतमवाक्येन दुर्निरीक्ष्या बभूव ह |
त्रयाणामपि लोकानां यावद्रामस्य दर्शनम् |१-४९-१६_END
BEGIN_
Ahalya is indeed indiscernible to all the three worlds by the very word of Gautama 
until the manifestation of Rama. [1-49-16a, b]_END

B_1_C_48_19
BEGIN_
गौतमं स ददर्शाथ प्रविशन्तं महामुनिम् || १-४८-२३
देवदानवदुर्धर्षं तपोबलसमन्वितम् |
तीर्थोदकपरिक्लिन्नं दीप्यमानमिवानलम् || १-४८-२४
गृहीतसमिधं तत्र सकुशं मुनिपुंगवम् |_END
BEGIN_
Indra looked at Gautama..the one who is great saint, inaccessible to gods and demons, full of ascetic power,
purified with holy water, bright like fire, holding Samidha-s and kusha grass in hands,
and eminent Sage entering into the hermitage. [1-48-23b, 24, 25a]_END

B_1_C_45_42
BEGIN_
निहत्य दितिपुत्रांश्च राज्यं प्राप्य पुरन्दरः।
शशास मुदितो लोकान् सर्षिसन्घान् सचारणान्॥ १-४५-४५_END
BEGIN_
"On eliminating the demonic sons of Diti and on acquiring kingdom of heaven, that 
eliminator of enemy cities, namely Indra, happily ruled the worlds that are inclusive 
of sages and caarana-s." Thus Vishvamitra continued his narration about Vishaala 
city and its emergence. [1-45-45]
_END

B_1_C_49_14
BEGIN_
शापस्यान्तमुपागम्य तेषां दर्शनमागता ||
राघवौ तु ततस्तस्याः पादौ जगृहतुर्मुदा | १-४९-१७_END
BEGIN_
On reaching the end of curse she came into the view of Raghava-s, and they too gladly 
touched her feet in reverence. [1-49-16c, 17a]_END

B_1_C_48_20
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा सुरपतिस्त्रस्तो विषण्णवदनोऽभवत् || १-४८-२५
अथ दृष्ट्वा सहस्राक्षं मुनिवेषधरं मुनिः |
दुर्वृत्तं वृत्तसंपन्नो रोषाद्वचनमब्रवीत् || १-४८-२६_END
BEGIN_
On seeing the sage the lord of gods Indra is scared and became dreary-faced. Then 
the well-behaved Gautama furiously spoke these words on seeing the ill-behaved Thousand-eyed 
Indra who is donning the guise of a saint. [1-48-25b, 26]_END

B_1_C_49_15
BEGIN_
स्मरन्ती गौतमवचः प्रतिजग्राह सा च तौ ||
पाद्यमर्घ्यं तथातिथ्यं चकार सुसमाहिता |
प्रतिजग्राह काकुत्स्थो विधिदृष्टेन कर्मणा || १-४९-१८_END
BEGIN_
Reminiscing Gautama's words Ahalya received those two, and self-consciously offered 
water for feet and hand washing, and like that she also offered guestship customarily 
and dutifully, and Rama of Kakutstha on his part acquiesced her hospitality. [1-49-18]_END

B_1_C_48_21
BEGIN_
मम रूपं समास्थाय कृतवानसि दुर्मते |
अकर्तव्यमिदं यस्मात् विफलस्त्वं भविष्यति || १-४८-२७_END
BEGIN_
'Oh, dirty-minded Indra, taking hold of my form you have effectuated this unacceptable 
deed, whereby you shall become infecund.' Thus, Gautama cursed Indra. [1-48-27]_END

B_1_C_49_16
BEGIN_
पुष्पवृष्टिर्महत्यासीद्देवदुंदुभिनिस्वनैः |
गन्धर्वाप्सरसां चैव महानासीत् समुत्सवः || १-४९-१९_END
BEGIN_
There chanced an abundant floral fall form firmament to the drumbeats of god's drums, 
and the celestials like gandharva-s, apsara-s revelled in a splendid festivity that 
is superb. [1-49-19]_END

B_1_C_50_0
BEGIN_
ततः प्रागुत्तरां गत्वा रामः सौमित्रिणा सह |विश्वामित्रं पुरस्कृत्य यज्ञवाटमुपागमत् || १-५०-१_END
BEGIN_
Rama then travelled along with Lakshmana towards northeast direction keeping Vishvamitra afore and neared 
the hall of Vedic ritual of Janaka in Mithila kingdom. [1-50-1]_END

B_1_C_48_22
BEGIN_
गौतमेनैवमुक्तस्य स रोषेण महात्मना |
पेततुर्वृषणौ भूमौ सहस्राक्षस्य तत्क्षणात् || १-४८-२८_END
BEGIN_
When that great-souled sage Gautama spoke that way with rancour, the testicles 
of the cursed Thousand-eyed Indra fell down onto ground at that very moment. [1-48-28]_END

B_1_C_49_17
BEGIN_
साधु साध्विति देवास्तामहल्यां समपूजयन् |
तपोबलविशुद्धाङ्गीं गौतमस्य वशानुगाम् || १-४९-२०_END
BEGIN_
Gods have collectively reverenced her, whose limbs are depurated by the asset of 
her ascesis which is performed as a devotee of Gautama remaining in his directives, 
saying 'Gracious! Goodness!' [1-49-20]_END

B_1_C_50_1
BEGIN_
रामस्तु मुनिशार्दूलमुवाच सहलक्ष्मणः |साध्वी यज्ञसमृद्धिर्हि जनकस्य महात्मनः || १-५०-२_END
BEGIN_
Rama who is with Lakshmana spoke to the tigerly saint Vishvamitra, " the Vedic-ritual of noble-souled 
Janaka is excellent, indeed with bountifully garnered paraphernalia of the ritual. [1-50-2]_END

B_1_C_48_23
BEGIN_
तथा शप्त्वा च वै शक्रं भार्यामपि च शप्तवान् |
इह वर्षसहस्राणि बहूनि निवसिष्यसि || १-४८-२९
वायुभक्षा निराहारा तप्यन्ती भस्मशायिनी |
अदृश्या सर्वभूतानामाश्रमेऽस्मिन् निवत्स्यसि || १-४८-३०_END
BEGIN_
On cursing Indra thus the sage cursed even his wife saying, 'you shall tarry here 
for many thousands of years to come without food and consuming air alone, and unseen 
by all beings you shall live on in this hermitage while contritely recumbent in 
dust.' [1-48-29, 30]_END

B_1_C_49_18
BEGIN_
गौतमोऽपि महातेजा अहल्यासहितः सुखी |
रामं संपूज्य विधिवत्तपस्तेपे महातपाः || १-४९-२१_END
BEGIN_
Even that great-resplendent Gautama is heartened when he reunited with Ahalya after 
a long, long a time, and that sage customarily reverenced Rama for actualising his 
solemn utterance, and that great-ascetic Gautama continued his ascesis together 
with Ahalya. [1-49-21]_END

B_1_C_50_2
BEGIN_
बहूनीह सहस्राणि नानादेशनिवासिनाम् |ब्राह्मणानां महाभाग वेदाध्ययनशालिनाम् || १-५०-३ऋषि 
ऋषिवाटाश्च दृश्यन्ते शकटीशतसंकुलाः |देशो विधीयतां ब्रह्मन् यत्र वत्स्यामहे वयम् || १-५०-४_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, highly fortunate sage, this place abounds with many thousands of Brahmans who are experts in Vedic 
practises and who seem to be the dwellers of numerous provinces, and also discernable are the cottages 
of sages rife with hundreds of carts full with their ceremonial chattels, as such oh, Brahman, a campsite 
may be decided for us too, as I discern every inch is inhabited." Thus Rama spoke to Vishvamitra. [1-50-3, 
4]_END

B_1_C_48_24
BEGIN_
यदा त्वेतद्वनं घोरं रामो दशरथात्मजः |
आगमिष्यति दुर्धर्षस्तदा पूता भविष्यसि || १-४८-३१_END
BEGIN_
When that unassailable son of Dasharatha, namely Rama, arrives at this squalid 
forest, for it will be henceforth rendered so along with you, then you will be purified. 
[1-48-31]_END

B_1_C_49_19
BEGIN_
रामोऽपि परमां पूजां गौतमस्य महामुनेः |
सकाशाद्विधिवत्प्राप्य जगाम मिथिलां ततः || १-४९-२२_END
BEGIN_
Even Rama on receiving a conventionally high veneration in the manifestness of that 
great-saint Gautama himself, then moved ahead to Mithila. [1-49-22]_END

B_1_C_50_3
BEGIN_
रामस्य वचनं श्रुत्वा विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः |निवेशमकरोद्देशे विविक्ते सलिलायुते || १-५०-५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Rama that great-saint Vishvamitra arranged a camp at an unfrequented place that 
has refreshing water. [1-50-5]_END

B_1_C_48_25
BEGIN_
तस्यातिथ्येन दुर्वृत्ते लोभमोहविवर्जिता |
मत्सकाशे मुदा युक्ता स्वं वपुर्धारयिष्यसि || १-४८-३२_END
BEGIN_
'On your welcoming Rama, oh, ill-behaved woman, you will be divested of your greed 
and craze in which you lingered so far, and then you will assume your own body and 
then you can be in my proximity, rejoicingly.' Thus, Sage Gautama cursed his wife 
Ahalya. [1-48-32]_END

B_1_C_50_4
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रमनुप्राप्तं श्रुत्वा नृपवरस्तदा |शतानन्दं पुरस्कृत्य पुरोहितमनिन्दितम् || १-५०-६
प्रत्युज्जगाम सहसा विनयेन समन्वितः |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that Vishvamitra has arrived in Mithila, then the best king Janaka instantly forged ahead 
towards Vishvamitra, keeping his unreprovable priest Shataananda afore of the team, in deference to 
Vishvamitra. [1-50-6, 7a]_END

B_1_C_48_26
BEGIN_
एवमुक्त्वा महातेजा गौतमो दुष्टचारिणीम् |
इममाश्रममुत्सृज्य सिद्धचारणसेविते |
हिमवच्छिखरे रम्ये तपस्तेपे महातपाः || १-४८-३३_END
BEGIN_
"On cursing immodest Ahalya thus, that great-resplendent Sage Gautama shed this 
hermitage which was once adored by celestials like siddha-sand caarana-s, and that 
great-ascetic Gautama practised his asceticism on the pleasant peaks of Himalayas." 
Thus, Vishvamitra continued his narration about the legend of Ahalya. [1-48-33]_END

B_1_C_50_5
BEGIN_
ऋत्विजोऽपि महात्मानस्त्वर्घ्यमादाय सत्वरम् ||१-५०-७विश्वामित्राय धर्मेण ददौ धर्मपुरस्कृतम् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Even the Ritvik-s, the administrators of that Vedic-ritual, of the great souled king Janaka arrived 
with post-haste taking holy waters, and they have ritualistically offered that sanctified water to Vishvamitra. 
[1-50-7b, 8a]_END

B_1_C_50_6
BEGIN_
प्रतिगृह्य तु तां पूजां जनकस्य महात्मनः || १-५०-८पप्रच्छ कुशलं राज्ञो यज्ञस्य च निरामयम् |_END
BEGIN_
On receiving that veneration from the great souled Janaka, Vishvamitra asked after the well-being of 
the king Janaka, as well about the unhindered proceedings of that Vedic-ritual. [1-50-8b, 9a]_END

B_1_C_50_7
BEGIN_
स तांश्चाथ मुनीन् पृष्ट्वा सोपाध्यायपुरोधसः || १-५०-९यथार्हमृषिभिः सर्वैः समागच्छत् प्रहृष्टवत् 
|_END
BEGIN_
Then Vishvamitra asked after the well-being of saints, mentors, clerics, as befitting to their order, 
and joined the company of all of the sages as a happy-souled sage. [1-50-9b, 10a]_END

B_1_C_50_8
BEGIN_
अथ राजा मुनिश्रेष्ठं कृताञ्जलिरभाषत || १-५०-१०आसने भगवानास्तां सहैभिर्मुनिसत्तमैः |_END
BEGIN_
The king Janaka adjoining his palms then spoke to that eminent-sage Vishvamitra, "oh, reverend sage, 
please be seated on this high seat, along with these eminent saints in their respective seats." Thus 
Janaka spoke to Vishvamitra [1-50-10b, 11a]_END

B_1_C_50_9
BEGIN_
जनकस्य वचः श्रुत्वा निषसाद महामुनिः || १-५०-११पुरोधा ऋत्विजश्चैव राजा च सह मंत्रिभिः |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Janaka that great-sage Vishvamitra took his seat, and king Janaka also took 
seat along with his royal priest Shataananda, and the administrators of that Vedic-ritual, namely Ritvik-s, 
and along with his ministers. [1-50-11b, 12a]_END

B_1_C_50_10
BEGIN_
आसनेषु यथान्यायमुपविष्टान् समन्ततः || १-५०-१२दृष्ट्वा स नृपतिस्तत्र विश्वामित्रमथाब्रवीत् 
|_END
BEGIN_
On beholding all of them seated all about in their respective seats as demanded by procedure king Janaka 
then spoke to Vishvamitra. [1-50-12b, 13a]_END

B_1_C_50_11
BEGIN_
अद्य यज्ञसमृद्धिर्मे सफला दैवतैः कृता || १-५०-१३अद्य यज्ञफलं प्राप्तं भगवद्दर्शनान्मया |_END
BEGIN_
Today my Vedic ritual is enriched with your advent, whereby I deem that gods have fructified the ritual. 
Let the ritual be like that. I deem that I have obtained the fruit of the ritual just on seeing godlike 
you here today. [1-50-13b, 14a]_END

B_1_C_50_12
BEGIN_
धन्योऽस्म्यनुगृहीतोऽस्मि यस्य मे मुनिपुङ्गव || १-५०-१४यज्ञोपसदनं ब्रह्मन् प्राप्तोऽसि मुनिभिः 
सह |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Brahman, at which Vedic-ritual hall you have arrived along with so many sages that happens to be 
mine, whereby, oh, eminent saint, I feel that I am honoured and hallowed. [1-50-14b, 15a]_END

B_1_C_50_13
BEGIN_
द्वादशाहं तु ब्रह्मर्षे दीक्षामाहुर्मनीषिणः || १-५०-१५ततो भागार्थिनो देवान् द्रष्टुमर्हसि 
कौशिक |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Brahma-sage, the scholarly Ritvik-s conducting my Vedic-ritual are saying that only twelve more 
days are remaining to complete the observation of ritual-pledge, and then oh, Kaushika, it will be apt 
of you to see the gods who arrive at the conclusion of this Vedic-ritual expecting their due in the 
ritual." So said king Janaka to Vishvamitra. [1-50-15b, 16a]_END

B_1_C_50_14
BEGIN_
इत्युक्त्वा मुनिशार्दूलं प्रहृष्टवदनस्तदा || १-५०-१६पुनस्तं परिपप्रच्छ प्रांजलिः प्रयतो नृपः 
|_END
BEGIN_
On speaking to that tigerly sage Vishvamitra in this way, the king again asked the sage pointedly and 
inquisitively with adjoined palms and with a gladdened face. [1-50-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_50_15
BEGIN_
इमौ कुमारौ भद्रं ते देवतुल्यपराक्रमौ || १-५०-१७गजसिंहगती वीरौ शार्दूलवृषभोपमौ |
पद्मपत्रविशालाक्षौ खड्गतूणीधनुर्धरौ |अश्विनाविव रूपेण समुपस्थितयौवनौ || १-५०-१८यदृच्छयैव 
गां प्राप्तौ देवलोकादिवामरौ |कथं पद्भ्यामिह प्राप्तौ किमर्थं कस्य वा मुने || १-५०-१९_END
BEGIN_
These two youngsters, oh, sage, let safety betide you, striding like audacious elephants and arrogant 
lions, bearing a similitude to adventurous tigers and adamantine bulls, and wielding quivers, swords, 
and bows, are valorous with their valour matching that of Vishnu, and with their eyes broad like lotus-petals 
and with youthfulness in the offing they look like the exceptionally beautiful twin-gods, Ashwin-brothers, 
by their physique. How these two have footslogged and chanced here as though immortals have chanced 
on earth from the abode of gods at their pleasure? What for they have come here, and whose scions are 
they? [1-50-17b, 18, 19]_END

B_1_C_50_16
BEGIN_
वरायुधधरौ वीरौ कस्य पुत्रौ महामुने |भूषयन्ताविमं देशं चन्द्रसूर्याविवाम्बरम् || १-५०-२०
परस्परस्य सदृशौ प्रमाणेङ्गितचेष्टितैः |काकपक्षधरौ वीरौ श्रोतुमिच्छामि तत्त्वतः || १-५०-२१_END
BEGIN_
Oh, great-saint, whose sons are these two valiant youngsters who are brandishing best weapons? They 
are embellishing this province as the Sun and Moon doeth the sky. Each to each they are clonal by postural-language, 
by facial-language and by body language. They appear valorous but boyish in their appearance, as their 
curls are still jet-black like crow-wings. Thus, whether they are immature by age though mature by their 
valour or so, I wish to listen about them in actuality. [1-50-20, 21]_END

B_1_C_50_17
BEGIN_
तस्य तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा जनकस्य महात्मनः |न्यवेदयदमेयात्मा पुत्रौ दशरथस्य तौ || १-५०-२२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of great-souled Janaka, Vishvamitra whose anima is immeasurable, has announced 
that those two as the sons of king Dasharatha. [1-50-22]_END

B_1_C_50_18
BEGIN_
सिद्धाश्रमनिवासं च राक्षसानां वधं तथा |तत्रागमनमव्यग्रं विशालायाश्च दर्शनम् || १-५०-२३
अहल्यादर्शनं चैव गौतमेन समागमम् |महाधनुषि जिज्ञासां कर्तुमागमनं तथा || १-५०-२४एतत्सर्वं 
महातेजा जनकाय महात्मने |निवेद्य विररामाथ विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः || १-५०-२५_END
BEGIN_
The highly resplendent great-saint Vishvamitra has informed the high souled Janaka about the coming 
of Rama and Lakshmana to the Hermitage of Accomplishment, their stopping over there and elimination 
of demons at that place, their indefatigable travel along with him, beholding City of Vishaala, seeing 
Ahalya, her reuniting with Sage Gautama, likewise their coming hitherward to gain a grasp of great bow 
of Shiva. On informing all these incidents to Janaka as well as to Shataananda, who incidentally is 
the son of Ahalya, sage Vishvamitra paused. [1-50-23, 24, 25]_END

B_1_C_51_0
BEGIN_
तस्य तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा विश्वामित्रस्य धीमतः |
हृष्टरोमा महातेजाः शतानन्दो महातपाः || १-५१-१
गौतमस्य सुतो ज्येष्ठस्तपसा द्योतितप्रभः |
रामसंदर्शनादेव परं विस्मयमागतः || १-५१-२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that sentence of that intellectual sage Vishvamitra, the highly refulgent 
and the great ascetic Shataananda is overjoyed, and Sage Shataananda, the eldest 
son of Sage Gautama, and whose radiance is brightened by his own ascesis is highly 
amazed just on seeing Rama. [1-51-1, 2]_END

B_1_C_51_1
BEGIN_
एतौ निषण्णौ संप्रेक्ष्य सुखासीनौ नृपात्मजौ |
शतानन्दो मुनिश्रेष्ठं विश्वामित्रमथाब्रवीत् || १-५१-३_END
BEGIN_
On raptly observing those two princes who are sitting comfortably with their heads 
bending down submissively, then Shataananda spoke to the eminent sage Vishvamitra. 
[1-51-3]_END

B_1_C_51_2
BEGIN_
अपि ते मुनिशार्दूल मम माता यशस्विनी |
दर्शिता राजपुत्राय तपो दीर्घमुपागता || १-५१-४_END
BEGIN_
Oh, tigerly saint Vishvamitra, you have revealed my glorious mother Ahalya who 
meted out a marathon ascesis to the princes - Really! [1-51-4]_END

B_1_C_51_3
BEGIN_
अपि रामे महातेजो मम माता यशस्विनी |
वन्यैरुपाहरत् पूजां पूजार्हे सर्वदेहिनाम् || १-५१-५_END
BEGIN_
And the highly resplendent and celebrated mother of mine worshipped Rama, who is 
worthy of worship by every corporeal being, with forest produce, is it so! [1-51-5]_END

B_1_C_51_4
BEGIN_
अपि रामाय कथितं यद् वृत्तं तत्पुरातनम् |
मम मातुर्महातेजो दैवेन दुरनुष्ठितम् || १-५१-६_END
BEGIN_
Oh, great-resplendent Vishvamitra, you have narrated to Rama about the maltreatment 
of my mother by the Providence as has happened anciently, isn't it![1-51-6]_END

B_1_C_51_5
BEGIN_
अपि कौशिक भद्रं ते गुरुणा मम संगता |
माता मम मुनिश्रेष्ठ रामसंदर्शनादितः || १-५१-७_END
BEGIN_
Oh, the best sage Kaushika, you be safe, my mother is reunited with my father on 
beholding and giving hospitality to Rama - Really! [1-51-7]_END

B_1_C_52_0
BEGIN_
तं दृष्ट्वा परमप्रीतो विश्वामित्रो महाबलः |प्रणतो विनयाद्वीरो वसिष्ठं जपतां वरम् || १-५२-१_END
BEGIN_
On seeing at that best sage among best meditators Sage Vashishta, the great-mighty and valorous Vishvamitra 
is highly rejoiced and obediently made an obeisance to the sage. [1-52-1]_END

B_1_C_51_6
BEGIN_
अपि मे गुरुणा रामः पूजितः कुशिकात्मज |
इहागतो महातेजाः पूजां प्राप्य महात्मनः || १-५१-८_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Kaushika, my father came to my mother's place from Himalayas! Has the great 
resplendent father of mine worshipped Rama because the redemption of my mother is 
per the kindness of Rama! Has this great-souled Rama reverenced that great resplendent 
father of mine by according a redemption, ahalyaa-daana, 
the endowment of Ahalya to her husband. [1-51-8]_END

B_1_C_52_1
BEGIN_
स्वागतं तव चेत्युक्तो वसिष्ठेन महात्मना |आसनं चास्य भगवान् वसिष्ठो व्यादिदेश ह || १-५२-२_END
BEGIN_
The great-souled Vashishta spoke, "you are welcome," and that godly sage has indeed shown a high seat 
to Vishvamitra. [1-52-2]_END

B_1_C_51_7
BEGIN_

अपि शान्तेन मनसा गुरुर्मे कुशिकात्मज|
इहागतेन रामेण पुजितेनाभिवादितः || १-५१-९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Kaushika, on his arrival at my mother's place whether this reverential Rama 
reverenced my father with a pacified heart without becoming contumelious!" Thus 
sage Shataananda exclaimed at the marvel occurred through Rama. [1-51-9]_END

B_1_C_52_2
BEGIN_
उपविष्टाय च तदा विश्वामित्राय धीमते |यथान्यायं मुनिवरः फलमूलमुपाहरत् || १-५२-३_END
BEGIN_
The eminent saint Vashishta then customarily offered fruits and tuber to the courageous Vishvamitra 
who by now has assumed a seat. [1-52-3]_END

B_1_C_51_8
BEGIN_
तच्छ्रुत्वा वचनं तस्य विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः |
प्रत्युवाच शतानन्दं वाक्यज्ञो वाक्यगोविदम् || १-५१-१०_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that sentence of his, that great-saint and sentence-precisian Sage Vishvamitra, 
replied the sentence-precisionist Sage Shataananda. [1-51-10]_END

B_1_C_52_3
BEGIN_
प्रतिगृह्य तु तां पूजां वसिष्ठाद्राजसत्तमः |तपोऽग्निहोत्रशिष्येषु कुशलं पर्यपृच्छत || १-५२-४
विश्वामित्रो महातेजा वनस्पतिगणे तथा |सर्वत्र कुशलं चाह वसिष्ठो राजसत्तमः || १-५२-५_END
BEGIN_
On receiving that deference from Vashishta, then that unsurpassed king Vishvamitra asked after the well-being 
of the ascesis, Fire-rituals and disciples and their progress in that hermitage, and that great-resplendent 
Vishvamitra has also asked after the well being of flora and fauna of the hermitage, and Vashishta reported 
to the matchless king about the all round well-being of every activity. [1-52-4, 5]_END

B_1_C_51_9
BEGIN_
नातिक्रान्तं मुनिश्रेष्ठ यत् कर्तव्यं कृतं मया |
संगता मुनिना पत्नी भार्गवेणेव रेणुका || १-५१-११_END
BEGIN_
"I have done whatever good is to be done and nothing is left undone, and the wife 
of the sage, namely Ahalya, is reunited with her husband sage Gautama, as with Renuka 
who was reunited with sage Jamadagni, the descendent of Bhrigu." So said Vishvamitra. 
[1-51-11]_END

B_1_C_52_4
BEGIN_
सुखोपविष्टं राजानं विश्वामित्रं महातपाः |पप्रच्छ जपतां श्रेष्ठो वसिष्ठो ब्रह्मणः सुतः || १-५२-६_END
BEGIN_
Vashishta the supreme one among meditators, a great-ascetic, and the brainchild of Brahma has then asked 
Vishvamitra who is sitting at ease. [1-52-6]_END

B_1_C_51_10
BEGIN_
तच्छ्रुत्वा वचनं तस्य विश्वामित्रस्य धीमतः |
शतानन्दो महातेजा रामं वचनमब्रवीत् || १-५१-१२_END
BEGIN_
On hearing those words of that highly intellectual Vishvamitra, high refulgent sage 
Shataananda spoke these words to Rama. [1-51-12]_END

B_1_C_52_5
BEGIN_
कच्चित्ते कुशलं राजन् कच्चिद्धर्मेण रंजयन् |प्रजाः पालयसे राजन् राजवृत्तेन धार्मिक || १-५२-७_END
BEGIN_
I hope that you are fine! And oh, righteous king, hope that you are ruling people righteously with 
kingly righteousness to their contentment. [1-52-7]_END

B_1_C_51_11
BEGIN_
स्वागतं ते नरश्रेष्ठ दिष्ट्या प्राप्तोऽसि राघव |
विश्वामित्रं पुरस्कृत्य महर्षिमपराजितम् || १-५१-१३_END
BEGIN_
Hail to thee! Oh, best one among men Rama, your arrival is a godsend, not only 
to Mithila but to entire humanity, and oh, Raghava, as an undefeatable great-sage 
Vishvamitra spearheads you, so shall your mission be undefeatable, thus hail to 
thee! [1-51-13]_END

B_1_C_52_6
BEGIN_
कच्चित्ते सुभृता भृत्याः कच्चित्तिष्ठन्ति शासने |कच्चित्ते विजिताः सर्वे रिपवो रिपुसूदन || १-५२-८_END
BEGIN_
I hope your servants are looked after well, hope all of them are abiding by the rulership, oh, vanquisher 
of adversaries, I hope that you have surely vanquished all of your adversaries. [1-52-8]_END

B_1_C_51_12
BEGIN_
अचिन्त्यकर्मा तपसा ब्रह्मर्षिरमितप्रभः |
विश्वामित्रो महातेजा वेत्स्येनं परमां गतिम् || १-५१-१४_END
BEGIN_
This highly resplendent Vishvamitra's exploits are unimaginable. He attained the 
highest order of Brahma-sage by his ascesis, thus illimitable is his ascetic resplendence, 
and you have to know him as an ultimate course, not only to you alone, but also 
to one and all. [1-51-14]_END

B_1_C_52_7
BEGIN_
कच्चित् बले च कोशे च मित्रेषु च परंतप |कुशलं ते नरव्याघ्र पुत्रपौत्रे तथानघ || १-५२-९_END
BEGIN_
"For you are an impeccable one and an emery-inflamer, oh, tigerly-man, I hope that your forces, exchequer 
and confederates are fine, and all is well with your sons and grandsons." Thus Vashishta asked the well-being 
of Vishvamitra. [1-52-9]_END

B_1_C_51_13
BEGIN_
नास्ति धन्यतरो राम त्वत्तोऽन्यो भुवि कश्चन |
गोप्ता कुशिकपुत्रस्ते येन तप्तं महत्तपः || १-५१-१५_END
BEGIN_
None other than you is fortunate enough on earth, oh, Rama, as you are in the custodial 
care of Vishvamitra, the scion of Kushika, who has practised supreme ascesis. [1-51-15]_END

B_1_C_52_8
BEGIN_
सर्वत्र कुशलं राजा वसिष्ठं प्रत्युदाहरत् |विश्वामित्रो महातेजा वसिष्ठं विनयान्वितम् || १-५२-१०_END
BEGIN_
The great-resplendent king Vishvamitra respectfully replied Sage Vashishta saying, 'everything 
is fine.' [1-52-10]_END

B_1_C_51_14
BEGIN_
श्रूयतां चाभिधास्यामि कौशिकस्य महात्मनः |
यथा बलं यथा तत्त्वं तन्मे निगदतः शृणु || १-५१-१६_END
BEGIN_
What is the prowess of the great-souled Vishvamitra, and what the quintessence 
of his legend may be heard from me while I narrate it. [1-51-16]_END

B_1_C_52_9
BEGIN_
कृत्वा तौ सुचिरं कालं धर्मिष्ठौ ताः कथास्तदा |मुदा परमया युक्तौ प्रीयेतां तौ परस्परम् || 
१-५२-११_END
BEGIN_
Both of those celebrities of conscientious then exchanged pleasantries for a long time with their rejoice 
heightening and gladdening one another. [1-52-11]_END

B_1_C_51_15
BEGIN_
राजाऽसीदेष धर्मात्मा दिर्घकालमरिंदमः |
धर्मज्ञः कृतविद्यश्च प्रजानां च हिते रतः || १-५१-१७_END
BEGIN_
This probity-souled Vishvamitra, being a proficient in rectitude, a perfectionist 
in kingcraft, a proponent of people's welfare, more so a persecutor of enemies, 
was there as a king for a long time. [1-51-17]_END

B_1_C_52_10
BEGIN_
ततो वसिष्ठो भगवान् कथान्ते रघुनंदन |विश्वामित्रमिदं वाक्यमुवाच प्रहसन्निव || १-५२-१२_END
BEGIN_
Then at the end of discussions, oh, Rama the legatee of Raghu, that godly Sage Vashishta smilingly 
spoke this sentence to Vishvamitra. [1-52-12]_END

B_1_C_51_16
BEGIN_
प्रजापतिसुतस्त्वासीत् कुशो नाम महीपतिः |
कुशस्य पुत्रो बलवान् कुशनाभः सुधार्मिकः || १-५१-१८_END
BEGIN_
There was a king named Kusha, a brainchild of Prjaapati, and Kusha's son was the 
powerful and verily righteous Kushanaabha. [1-51-18]_END

B_1_C_52_11
BEGIN_
आतिथ्यं कर्तुमिच्छामि बलस्यास्य महाबल |तव चैवाप्रमेयस्य यथार्हं संप्रतीच्छ मे || १-५२-१३_END
BEGIN_
I wish to offer guestship befitting to your status, oh, great-forceful king Vishvamitra, to a matchless 
one like you and to this military force of yours, kindly accept it from me. [1-52-13]_END

B_1_C_51_17
BEGIN_
कुशनाभसुतस्त्वासीद्गाधिरित्येव विश्रुतः |
गाधेः पुत्रो महातेजा विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः || १-५१-१९_END
BEGIN_
One who is highly renowned by the name Gaadhi was the son of Kushanaabha, and Gaadhi's 
son is this great-saint of great resplendence, Vishvamitra. [1-51-19]_END

B_1_C_53_0
BEGIN_
एवमुक्ता वसिष्ठेन शबला शत्रुसूदन |विदधे कामधुक्कामान् यस्य यस्येप्सितं यथा || १-५३-१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, enemy-chastener Rama, when the Divine Cow Shabala is spoken in this way by Sage Vashishta, then 
that milker bestowed each and every fancy, fancied by each and every fancier, according to one's own 
fancy." Thus Sage Shataananda continued the legend of Shabala or Kaamadhenu, as a part of the legend 
of Vishvamitra to Rama and others. [1-53-1]_END

B_1_C_52_12
BEGIN_
सत्क्रियां तु भवानेतां प्रतीच्छतु मया कृताम् |राजंस्त्वमतिथिश्रेष्ठः पूजनीयः प्रयत्नतः || 
१-५२-१४_END
BEGIN_
'You may kindly accept all these hospitalities offered by me, oh king, for you are an important guest 
you ought to be reverenced effortfully.' So said Vashishta to Vishvamitra. [1-52-14]_END

B_1_C_53_1
BEGIN_
इक्षून्मधूंस्तथा लाजान् मैरेयांश्च वरासवान् |पानानि च महार्हाणि भक्ष्यांश्चोच्चावचांस्तथा || 
१-५३-२_END
BEGIN_
Shabala bestowed dishes of sugar cane and honey, and flakes of all sorts, like cornflakes, rice-flakes, 
also best arracks and liquors in best wineglasses, further, the drinks and foodstuffs that are very 
diverse and verily apposite to royalties and army-men. [1-53-2]_END

B_1_C_51_18
BEGIN_
विश्वमित्रो महातेजाः पालयामास मेदिनीम् |
बहुवर्षसहस्राणि राजा राज्यमकारयत् || १-५१-२०_END
BEGIN_
Vishvamitra ruled the earth, and this great-resplendent king ruled the kingdom 
for many thousands of years. [1-51-20]_END

B_1_C_52_13
BEGIN_
एवमुक्तो वसिष्ठेन विश्वामित्रो महामतिः |कृतमित्यब्रवीद्राजा पूजावाक्येन मे त्वया || १-५२-१५_END
BEGIN_
When sage Vashishta said in this way, that highly-intellectual king Vishvamitra said to him, 'hospitality 
is deemed to have been offered to me with your reverential words, it is enough and nothing more is necessary.' 
[1-52-15]_END

B_1_C_53_2
BEGIN_
उष्णाढ्यस्यौदनस्यापि राशयः पर्वतोपमाः |मृष्टान्नानि च सूपाश्च दधिकुल्यास्तथैव च || १-५३-३
नानास्वादुरसानां च खाण्डवानां [षाडवानां] तथैव च |भाजनानि [भोजनानि] सुपूर्णानि गौडानि च सहस्रशः 
|| १-५३-४_END
BEGIN_
There emerged mountainous stacks of steamy foodstuffs, palatable side-dishes and desserts of rice 
etc., also the dumplings of cooked pulses, like that the cascades of curds and the other milk products 
like butter, ghee, cheese etc. Thousands of silver dishes and hollowware fully replete with daintily 
soft drinks, like that full with sugar-candy preparations, and with preparations that comprise all the 
six tastes have come up together with delectable foodstuffs made out of treacly dumplings of cane sugar. 
[1-53-3, 4]_END

B_1_C_51_19
BEGIN_
कदाचित्तु महातेजा योजयित्वा वरूथिनीम् |
अक्षौहिणीपरिवृतः परिचक्राम मेदिनीम् || १-५१-२१_END
BEGIN_
At one time the great-resplendent king Vishvamitra went round the earth marshalling 
a unit of akshauhini army. [1-51-21]_END

B_1_C_52_14
BEGIN_
फलमूलेन भगवन्विद्यते यत्तवाश्रमे |पाद्येनाचमनीयेन भगवद्दर्शनेन च || १-५२-१६सर्वथा च महाप्राज्ञ 
पूजार्हेण सुपूजितः |नमस्तेऽस्तु गमिष्यामि मैत्रेणेक्षस्व चक्षुषा || १-५२-१७_END
BEGIN_
I am entertained with whatever item that obtains in your hermitage, say fruits, tubers and water 
for feet-wash and to wet mouth. Why those petty items, I regaled just by seeing you, a godly sage like. 
Oh, highly noetic sage, by yourself you are a sage worthy to be reverenced by one and all, such as you 
are you alone have reverenced me. Now I wish to take leave, please accept my obeisance to you, and please 
look upon us with a friendlily regard. [1-52-16, 17]_END

B_1_C_53_3
BEGIN_
सर्वमासीत् सुसंतुष्टं हृष्टपुष्टजनायुतम् |विश्वामित्रबलं राम वसिष्ठेन सुतर्पितम् || 
१-५३-५_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, all of the men in the forces of Vishvamitra, who are already rejoiced and regaled by the 
regular feasts accorded by their king Vishvamitra, are now comparatively well gladdened when feasted 
by Sage Vashishta, in which they rejoiced and regaled, for a good measure. [1-53-5]_END

B_1_C_51_20
BEGIN_
नगराणि च राष्ट्रानि सरितश्च तथा गिरीन् |
आश्रमान् क्रमशो राजा विचरन्नाजगाम ह || १-५१-२२
वसिष्ठस्याश्रमपदं नानापुष्पलताद्रुमम् |
नानामृगगणाकीर्णं सिद्धचारणसेवितम् || १-५१-२३
देवदानवगन्धर्वैः किंनरैरुपशोभितम् |
प्रशान्तहरिणाकिर्णं द्विजसंघनिषेवितम् || १-५१-२४
ब्रह्मर्षिगणसंकीर्णं देवर्षिगणसेवितम् |
तपश्चरणसंसिद्धैरग्निकल्पैर्महात्मभिः || १-५१-२५
सततं संकुलं श्रीमद्ब्रह्मकल्पैर्महात्मभिः |
अब्भक्षैर्वायुभक्षैश्च शिर्णपर्णाशनैस्तथा || १-५१-२६
फलमूलाशनैर्दान्तैर्जितदोषैर्जितेन्द्रियैः - यद्वा -
फलमूलाशनैर्दानैर्जिततोषैर्जितेन्द्रियैः |
ऋषिभिर्वालखिल्यैश्च जपहोमपरायणैः || १-५१-२७
अन्यैर्वैखानसैश्चैव समन्तादुपशोभितम् |_END
BEGIN_
Moving sequentially about the provinces, cities, rivers likewise mountains, king 
Vishvamitra arrived at the threshold of a hermitage which is with numerous flowered 
trees and climbers, overspread with very many herds of animals, adored by the celestials 
like siddha-s and caarana-s, frequented and embellished with gods, demons, gandharva-s, 
and kinnara-s, spread out with equable deer, adored by flights of birds, compacted 
with the assemblages of Brahma-sages, and also with the assemblages of godly-sages 
who are fully accomplished in their ascesis, where the personal resplendence of 
each of the great-souled sage is similar to each of the Ritual-fire available in 
each of the Ritual Fire Altar before which he is sitting, and which hermitage is 
bustling with the activity of great-souled sages who are comparable to Brahma, among 
whom some subsist on water alone, and some on air alone, likewise some more on dry 
leaves, while some on fruits, tubers, and with such of those sages and also with 
particular sages like Vaalakhilyaa-s, also with others like Vaikhaanasa-s, who are 
all self-controlled, who have overcame their peccabilites, who have overpowered 
their senses that hermitage is occupied, and while everyone of the inmates is engaged 
in meditations and oblations into Ritual-fire, and with such sages and their activity 
whole of the perimeter of that hermitage is brightened and rendered splendent, and 
king Vishvamitra arrived at such a magnificent hermitage of Sage Vashishta. [1-51-22, 
23, 24, 2125, 26, 27, 28a]_END

B_1_C_52_15
BEGIN_
एवं ब्रुवन्तं राजानं वसिष्ठः पुनरेव हि |न्यमंत्रयत धर्मात्मा पुनः पुनरुदारधीः || १-५२-१८_END
BEGIN_
Even if the king was speaking in this way obliquely to him, that virtue-souled and magnanimous sage 
Vashishta entreated the king repeatedly. [1-52-18]_END

B_1_C_53_4
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रोऽपि राजर्षिर्हृष्टपुष्टस्तदाभवत् |सान्तःपुरवरो राजा सब्राह्मणपुरोहितः || १-५३-६_END
BEGIN_
