them while fury reddened his eyes. [1-62-15]_END

B_1_C_63_5
BEGIN_
दृष्ट्वा कन्दर्पवशगो मुनिस्तामिदमब्रवीत् |
अप्सरः स्वागतं तेऽस्तु वस चेह ममाश्रमे || १-६३-६
अनुगृह्णीष्व भद्रं ते मदनेन सुमोहितम् |_END
BEGIN_
On seeing her the sage having gone under the sway the Love-god said this to her, 
'oh, apsara, you are welcome, I invite you to bide in my hermitage. Oblige me who 
am bewitched by Love-god for you. You be safe.' [1-63-6, 7a]_END

B_1_C_62_14
BEGIN_
निःसाध्वसमिदं प्रोक्तं धर्मादपि विगर्हितम् |
अतिक्रम्य तु मद्वाक्यं दारुणं रोमहर्षणम् || १-६२-१६_END
BEGIN_
You all have not only transgressed my word, but pertly replied me in an impudent 
manner which is abhorrent and hair-raising, and recriminatory according to probity. 
[1-62-16]_END

B_1_C_63_6
BEGIN_
इत्युक्ता सा वरारोहा तत्र वासमथाकरोत् || १-६३-७
तपसो हि महाविघ्नो विश्वामित्रमुपागतम् |
तस्यां वसन्त्यां वर्षाणि पंच पंच च राघव || १-६३-८
विश्वामित्राश्रमे सौम्य सुखेन व्यतिचक्रमुः |_END
BEGIN_
When he said thus to her, oh, Raghava, then she made a stopover there and ten years 
rolled by comfortably, and oh, gentle Rama, because of her staying Vishvamitra is 
indeed faced with a great hindrance in his ascesis. [1-63-7b, 8, 9a]_END

B_1_C_62_15
BEGIN_
श्वमांसभोजिनः सर्वे वासिष्ठा इव जातिषु |
पूर्णं वर्षसहस्रं तु पृथिव्यामनुवत्स्यथ || १-६२-१७_END
BEGIN_
'You all will be whirling around the earth totally for a thousand years taking 
birth in the race that subsists on dog's meat, like the sons of Vashishta.' Thus 
Vishvamitra cursed his sons. [1-62-17]_END

B_1_C_63_7
BEGIN_
अथ काले गते तस्मिन् विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः || १-६३-९
सव्रीड इव संवृत्तश्चिन्ताशोकपरायणः |
बुद्धिर्मुनेः समुत्पन्ना सामर्षा रघुनंदन || १-६३-१०_END
BEGIN_
Then after the lapse of that ten year period Vishvamitra became doleful with distress 
and he is enwrapped in humiliation, as it were, and, oh, Rama, Raghu's legatee, 
then a resentful thought occurred to him. [1-63-9b, 10]_END

B_1_C_64_0
BEGIN_
सुरकार्यमिदं रंभे कर्तव्यं सुमहत्त्वया |लोभनं कौशिकस्येह काममोहसमन्वितम् || १-६४-१_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rambha, now you have to undertake this very great task of gods in enchanting Vishvamitra with 
a craving caused by lust, for lusting after you.' Thus Indra ordered Rambha..." Thus Sage Shataananda 
continued the legend of Vishvamitra to Rama. [1-64-1]_END

B_1_C_62_16
BEGIN_
कृत्वा शापसमायुक्तान् पुत्रान् मुनिवरस्तदा |
शुनःशेपमुवाचार्थं कृत्वा रक्षां निरामयाम् || १-६२-१८_END
BEGIN_
On making his sons bounden by curse, then that best saint spoke to the pitiable 
Shunashepa, on making unharmed invulnerability to him with sanctifying hymns. [1-62-18]_END

B_1_C_63_8
BEGIN_
सर्वं सुराणां कर्मैतत्तपोऽपहरणं महत् |
अहो रात्रापदेशेन गताः संवत्सरा दश || १-६३-११
काममोहाभिभूतस्य विघ्नोऽयं प्रत्युपस्थितः |_END
BEGIN_
All this is the mischief of gods to defraud me of the great merit of my ascesis. 
Ten years have rolled by as if they are just a day and a night. Furthermore, I who 
am under the influence of lust and lure had to encounter this hindrance in my ascesis. 
[1-63-11, 12a]_END

B_1_C_64_1
BEGIN_
तथोक्ता साप्सरा राम सहस्राक्षेण धीमता |व्रीडिता प्रांजलिर्वाक्यं प्रत्युवाच सुरेश्वरम् || १-६४-२_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, when that celestial wench is spoken thus by the Thousand-eyed Indra, she diffidently said 
to that chief of gods while adjoining her palms suppliantly. [1-64-2]_END

B_1_C_62_17
BEGIN_
पवित्रपाशैर्बद्धो रक्तमाल्यानुलेपनः |
वैष्णवं यूपमासाद्य वाग्भिरग्निमुदाहर || १-६२-१९_END
BEGIN_
When you are fastened with sacred fastener to the sacrificial post of Vishnu, 
smeared with red paste and garlanded with red garlands, you praisefully address 
the Fire-god with the words I going to impart to you in Vedic hymns. [1-62-19]_END

B_1_C_63_9
BEGIN_
विनिःश्वसन् मुनिवरः पश्चात्तापेन दुःखितः || १-६३-१२
भीतामप्सरसं दृष्ट्वा वेपन्तीं प्रांजलिं स्थिताम् |
मेनकां मधुरैर्वाक्यैर्विसृज्य कुशिकात्मजः || १-६३-१३
उत्तरं पर्वतं राम विश्वामित्रो जगाम ह |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, that best saint suspired heavily when he became emotional with reparation. 
But on seeing the scared celestial wench Menaka, who is shivering and waiting with 
suppliantly adjoined palms, he sent her away with pleasant words, and he that Vishvamitra 
indeed went to the northern Himalayan mountain. [1-63-12b, 13, 14a]_END

B_1_C_64_2
BEGIN_
अयं सुरपते घोरो विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः |क्रोधमुत्स्रक्ष्यते घोरं मयि देव न संशयः || १-६४-३
ततो हि मे भयं देव प्रसादं कर्तुमर्हसि |_END
BEGIN_
'Oh, chief of gods, Indra, that great saint Vishvamitra is a dangerous one and undoubtedly he releases 
his deadly anger on me. Oh, god, thereby I am fearful of him. Hence, oh, god, it will be apt of you 
to accord forbearance.' So said Rambha to Indra. [1-64-3, 4a]_END

B_1_C_62_18
BEGIN_
इमे च गाथे द्वे दिव्ये गायेथा मुनिपुत्रक |
अंबरीषस्य यज्ञेऽस्मिंस्ततः सिद्धिमवाप्स्यसि || १-६२-२०_END
BEGIN_
'These two divine hymns, oh, son of saint, shall be chanted in the Vedic-ritual 
of Ambariisha, then you will obtain your aspiration.' Thus Vishvamitra taught two 
Vedic hymns to the boy. [1-62-20]_END

B_1_C_63_10
BEGIN_
स कृत्वा नैष्ठिकीं बुद्धिं जेतुकामो महायशाः || १-६३-१४
कौशिकीतीरमासाद्य तपस्तेपे दुरासदम् |_END
BEGIN_
He that highly celebrated sage who made a resolve to attain a sang-froid temperament 
and to vanquish lust, performed an unsurpassable ascesis on reaching the riverbank 
of River Kaushiki. [1-63-14b, 15a]_END

B_1_C_64_3
BEGIN_
एवमुक्तस्तया राम सभयं भीतया तदा || १-६४-४तामुवाच सहस्राक्षो वेपमानां कृतांजलिम् |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, the Thousand-eyed Indra replied Rambha when she spoke to him in that way while shuddering 
in fear and making palm fold in supplication. [1-64-4b, 5a]_END

B_1_C_62_19
BEGIN_
शुनःशेपो गृहीत्वा ते द्वे गाथे सुसमाहितः |
त्वरया राजसिंहं तमंबरीषमुवाच ह || १-६२-२१_END
BEGIN_
Shunashepa having taken those two hymns from Vishvamitra very attentively has instantly 
gone to that lion-king Ambariisha and indeed spoke to him. [1-62-21]_END

B_1_C_63_11
BEGIN_
तस्य वर्षसहस्राणि घोरं तप उपासतः || १-६३-१५
उत्तरे पर्वते राम देवतानामभूद्भयम् |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, while he reverently performed an unspeakable ascesis for a thousand years 
on the northern mountain, namely Himalayas, then fear occurred to gods. [1-63-15b, 
16a]_END

B_1_C_64_4
BEGIN_
मा भैषि रंभे भद्रं ते कुरुष्व मम शासनम् || १-६४-५कोकिलो हृदयग्राही माधवे रुचिरद्रुमे |अहं 
कंदर्पसहितः स्थास्यामि तव पार्श्वतः || १-६४-६_END
BEGIN_
You need not be fearful, Rambha, carry out my command, safe betides you, I on becoming a heart-stealing 
black-songbird will be at your side along with Love-god in the pleasing trees of springtime. [1-64-5b, 
6]_END

B_1_C_62_20
BEGIN_
राजसिंह महाबुद्धे शीघ्रं गच्छावहे वयम् |
निवर्तयस्व राजेन्द्र दीक्षां च समुदाहर || १-६२-२२_END
BEGIN_
'Oh, the lion-king, let us go promptly to your ritual place, oh, best king, you 
may apply yourself to your pledge in completing the ritual, with me as its sacrificial 
animal,' thus the boy said. [1-62-22]_END

B_1_C_63_12
BEGIN_
आमंत्रयन् समागम्य सर्वे सर्षिगणाः सुराः || १-६३-१६
महर्षिशब्दं लभतां साध्वयं कुशिकात्मजः |_END
BEGIN_
' All gods coming together with assemblages of sages have approached Brahma and conveyed 
that, 'this Vishvamitra, the son of Kushika, may duly be given the epithet of 'Maharshi, 
Exalted Sage.' [1-63-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_64_5
BEGIN_
त्वं हि रूपं बहुगुणं कृत्वा परमभास्वरम् |तमृषिं कौशिकं रंभे भेदयस्व तपस्विनम् || १-६४-७_END
BEGIN_
'Indeed on your assuming a highly sparkling semblance, and multi-multiplexing your savoir faire, with 
bon viveurs and bon vivants, you disengage that ascetical sage Kaushika from his ascesis.' So said Indra 
to Rambha. [1-64-7]_END

B_1_C_62_21
BEGIN_
तद्वाक्यमृषिपुत्रस्य श्रुत्वा हर्षसमन्वितः |
जगाम नृपतिः शीघ्रं यज्ञवाटमतन्द्रितः || १-६२-२३_END
BEGIN_
On listening that sentence of the son of sage, the king Ambariisha is gladdened 
and proceeded to the ritual hall immediately and spiritedly. [1-62-23]_END

B_1_C_63_13
BEGIN_
देवतानां वचः श्रुत्वा सर्वलोकपितामहः || १-६३-१७
अब्रवीन्मधुरं वाक्यं विश्वामित्रं तपोधनम् |_END
BEGIN_
On listening the advice of gods, Brahma, the Grandparent of all the worlds, spoke 
these pleasant words to the ascetically wealthy Vishvamitra. [1-63-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_65_0
BEGIN_
अथ हैमवतीं राम दिशं त्यक्त्वा महामुनिः |
पूर्वां दिशमनुप्राप्य तपस्तेपे सुदारुणम् || १-६५-१_END
BEGIN_
"That great-saint Vishvamitra then leaving off the snowbound Himalayas on north, 
oh, Rama, he reached eastern quarter and undertook rigorous ascesis." Thus Sage 
Shataananda continued the legend of Vishvamitra. [1-65-1]_END

B_1_C_64_6
BEGIN_
सा श्रुत्वा वचनं तस्य कृत्वा रूपमनुत्तमम् |लोभयामास ललिता विश्वामित्रं शुचिस्मिता || १-६४-८_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the sentence of Indra she adopted an unexcelled physique, and on becoming a pulchritudinous 
damsel she started to entice Vishvamitra with giggly grins. [1-64-8]_END

B_1_C_63_14
BEGIN_
महर्षे स्वागतं वत्स तपसोग्रेण तोषितः || १-६३-१८
महत्त्वमृषिमुख्यत्वं ददामि तव कौशिक |_END
BEGIN_
'Oh, exalted sage, I welcome you my dear, as I am gladdened by your stern ascesis, 
oh, Kaushika, I bestow upon you the sublimity and supremacy among sages.' [1-63-18b, 
19a]_END

B_1_C_62_22
BEGIN_
सदस्यानुमते राजा पवित्रकृतलक्षणम् |
पशुं रक्ताम्बरं कृत्वा यूपे तं समबन्धयत् || १-६२-२४_END
BEGIN_
The king with the permission of officiators of ritual got the boy prepared as a 
ritual animal with sanctified bodily features and clad him in red clothes and got 
him securely fastened to the sacrificial post. [1-62-24]_END

B_1_C_65_1
BEGIN_
मौनं वर्षसहस्रस्य कृत्वा व्रतमनुत्तमम् |
चकाराप्रतिमं राम तपः परमदुष्करम् || १-६५-२_END
BEGIN_
Committing himself to a vow of muteness, oh, Rama, he performed an unexcelled and 
unmatched ascesis which is highly impracticable for others to perform. [1-65-2]_END

B_1_C_64_7
BEGIN_
कोकिलस्य तु शुश्राव वल्गु व्याहरतः स्वनम् |संप्रहृष्टेन मनसा स एनामन्वैक्षत || १-६४-९_END
BEGIN_
Vishvamitra has heard melodious trilling tune of songbird, and while his heart is highly gladdening 
about the ambience, he incidentally saw and stared at Rambha. [1-64-9]_END

B_1_C_63_15
BEGIN_
ब्रह्मणः स वचः श्रुत्वा विश्वामित्रस्तपोधनः || १-६३-१९
प्रांजलिः प्रणतो भूत्वा प्रत्युवाच पितामहम् |_END
BEGIN_
And on hearing the words of Brahma he that ascetically wealthy Vishvamitra became 
obeisant and replied the Grandparent adjoining his palms suppliantly. [1-63-19b, 
20a]_END

B_1_C_62_23
BEGIN_
स बद्धो वाग्भिरग्र्याभिरभितुष्टाव वै सुरौ |
इन्द्रमिन्द्रानुजं चैव यथावन्मुनिपुत्रकः || १-६२-२५_END
BEGIN_
When Shunashepa is tied to ritual post he immensely pleased two gods, namely Indra 
and Upendra as well, with those two hymns he got from Vishvamitra. [1-62-25]_END

B_1_C_64_8
BEGIN_
अथ तस्य च शब्देन गीतेनाप्रतिमेन च |दर्शनेन च रंभाया मुनिः संदेहमागतः || १-६४-१०_END
BEGIN_
By the exceptional trilling tune of that songbird and by the unexceptional tableau of Rambha the sage 
is on his qui vive. [1-64-10]_END

B_1_C_65_2
BEGIN_
पूर्णे वर्षसहस्रे तु काष्ठभूतं महामुनिम् |
विघ्नैर्बहुभिराधूतं क्रोधो नान्तरमाविशत् || १-६५-३
स कृत्वा निश्चयं राम तप आतिष्ठदव्ययम् |_END
BEGIN_
Even on completing a thousand years, even when that great-saint became woodenly, 
even many barriers are at full blast, oh, Rama, fury has not entered his heart of 
hearts, for he stood fast in an unmitigated ascesis on making a firm determination. 
[1-65-3, 4a]_END

B_1_C_63_16
BEGIN_
तमुवाच ततो ब्रह्मा न तावत्त्वं जितेन्द्रियः || १-६३-२१
यतस्व मुनिशार्दूल इत्युक्त्वा त्रिदिवं गतः |_END
BEGIN_
Brahma then said to him, 'your senses remain unconquered as such, oh, tigerly sage, 
make an effort for it.' Saying so Brahma went heavenward. [1-63-21b, 22a]_END

B_1_C_62_24
BEGIN_
ततः प्रीतः सहस्राक्षो रहस्यस्तुतितोषितः |
दीर्घमायुस्तदा प्रादाच्छुनःशेपाय राघव || १-६२-२६_END
BEGIN_
Then the Thousand-eyed Indra who is satisfied with esoteric laudation is gladdened, 
and oh, Raghava, then he bestowed longevity to Shunashepa. [1-62-26]_END

B_1_C_65_3
BEGIN_
तस्य वर्षसहस्रस्य व्रते पूर्णे महाव्रतः || १-६५-४
भोक्तुमारब्धवानन्नं तस्मिन् काले रघूत्तम |
इन्द्रो द्विजातिर्भूत्वा तं सिद्धमन्नमयाचत || १-६५-५_END
BEGIN_
On one day when those thousand years of ascesis with the rigorous pledge of Vishvamitra 
are being completed, and when he started to eat his meal, oh, Rama, best of Raghu's 
dynasty, Indra arrived there disguising himself as a Brahman and requested for the 
readily available meal. [1-65-4b, 5]_END

B_1_C_64_9
BEGIN_
सहस्राक्षस्य तत् कर्म विज्ञाय मुनिपुंगवः |रंभां क्रोधसमाविष्टः शशाप कुशिकात्मजः || १-६४-११_END
BEGIN_
On knowing that as an escapade of the Thousand-eyed Indra, Vishvamitra is enwrapped in wrath and he 
cursed Rambha. [1-64-11]_END

B_1_C_63_17
BEGIN_
विप्रस्थितेषु देवेषु विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः || १-६३-२२
ऊर्ध्वबाहुर्निरालंबो वायुभक्षस्तपश्चरन् |_END
BEGIN_
While the gods who came here along with Brahma have returned, that great sage Vishvamitra 
undertook another round of ascesis by standing in levitation, upraising his arms, 
and subsisting on air alone. [1-63-22b, 23a]_END

B_1_C_62_25
BEGIN_
स च राजा नरश्रेष्ठ यज्ञस्य च समाप्तवान् |
फलं बहुगुणं राम सहस्राक्षप्रसादजम् || १-६२-२७_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, the best one among men, he that king Ambariisha also obtained the fruits 
of that Vedic-ritual in manyfold, resulted from the grace of Thousand-eyed Indra. 
[1-62-27]_END

B_1_C_64_10
BEGIN_
यन्मां लोभयसे रंभे कामक्रोधजयैषिणम् |दश वर्षसहस्राणि शैली स्थास्यसि दुर्भगे || १-६४-१२_END
BEGIN_
Whereof you tried to entice me who am wishing to win over the wanton and wroth, you unlucky female 
Rambha, thereof you will become a rocklike statued wastrel. [1-64-12]_END

B_1_C_65_4
BEGIN_
तस्मै दत्त्वा तदा सिद्धं सर्वं विप्राय निश्चितः |
निःषेषितेऽन्ने भगवानभुक्त्वैव महातपाः || १-६५-६
न किंचिदवदद्विप्रं मौनव्रतमुपास्थितः |
तथैवासीत्पुनः मौनमनुच्छ्वासं चकार ह || १-६५-७_END
BEGIN_
Then that godly Vishvamitra willingly gave away all the readied meal to that Brahman, 
and as no meal is leftover by Brahman-Indra, that great-ascetic Vishvamitra starved 
himself. Vishvamitra did not speak a little to the Brahman in dissent as he is abided 
by his pledge of muteness, and he again remained in muteness and breath-control. 
Like that, he indeed carried on his ascesis. [1-65-6, 7]_END

B_1_C_63_18
BEGIN_
धर्मे पंचतपा भूत्वा वर्षास्वाकाशसंश्रयः || १-६३-२३
शिशिरे सलिले शायी रात्र्यहानि तपोधनः |
एवं वर्षसहस्रं हि तपो घोरमुपागमत् || १-६३-२४_END
BEGIN_
In summer he became the Five-Fire Ascetic, in rainy season open sky is his rooftop, 
and in winter water is his reclining bed even by day or by night, and thus that 
ascetically wealthy Vishvamitra indeed undertook a severe ascesis in this way, for 
another thousand years. [1-63-23b, 24]_END

B_1_C_62_26
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रोऽपि धर्मात्मा भूयस्तेपे महातपाः |
पुष्करेषु नरश्रेष्ठ दशवर्षशतानि च || १-६२-२८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, the best among men, even the virtue-souled great ascetic Vishvamitra 
again performed ascesis at the same Holy lakeside for another thousand years." Thus 
Sage Shataananda continued the narration of Vishvamitra's legend. [1-62-28]_END

B_1_C_64_11
BEGIN_
ब्राह्मणः सुमहातेजास्तपोबलसमन्वितः |उद्धरिष्यति रंभे त्वां मत्क्रोधकलुषीकृताम् || १-६४-१३_END
BEGIN_
'A highly resplendent Brahman who is ascetically powerful redeems you, oh, Rambha, who are now blemished 
by my anger.' Vishvamitra cursed Rambha in this way. [1-64-13]_END

B_1_C_65_5
BEGIN_
अथ वर्षसहस्रं च नोच्छ्वसन्मुनिपुंगवः |
तस्यानुच्छ्वसमानस्य मूर्ध्नि धूमो व्यजायत || १-६५-८
त्रैलोक्यं येन संभ्रांतमातापितमिवाभवत् |_END
BEGIN_
That eminent saint remained without respiration for another thousand years, and 
then fumes have started to emit from the head of sage who is controlling his breath, 
by which fumes the triad of worlds looked as if it is searing, and this startled 
all the worlds. [1-65-8, 9a]_END

B_1_C_63_19
BEGIN_
तस्मिन् संतप्यमाने तु विश्वामित्रे महामुनौ |
संतापः सुमहानासीत् सुराणां वासवस्य च || १-६३-२५_END
BEGIN_
While that great saint is undertaking fervent ascesis it has become a very high 
burning problem to gods and even to Indra. [1-63-25]_END

B_1_C_65_6
BEGIN_
ततो देवर्षिगन्धर्वाः पन्नगोरगराक्षसाः || १-६५-९
मोहिता तपसा तस्य तेजसा मंदरश्मयः |
कश्मलोपहताः सर्वे पितामहमथाब्रुवन् || १-६५-१०_END
BEGIN_
Then the gods, sages, gandharva-s, serpents, reptiles, demons are puzzled at the 
ascesis of Vishvamitra, and as their own resplendence is dulled by the ascesis of 
Vishvamitra, thereby they are marred by this blemish of lowered resplendence, then 
all of them addressed the Grandparent, Brahma. [1-65-9b, 10]_END

B_1_C_64_12
BEGIN_
एवमुक्त्वा महातेजा विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः |अशक्नुवन् धारयितुं कोपं संतापमागतः || १-६४-१४_END
BEGIN_
Thus the great-resplendent Vishvamitra became compunctious when that great-saint could not contain 
his anger in uttering an angry curse. [1-64-14]_END

B_1_C_63_20
BEGIN_
रंभामप्सरसं शक्रः सह सर्वैर्मरुद्गणैः |
उवाचात्महितं वाक्यमहितं कौशिकस्य च || १-६३-२६_END
BEGIN_
"Then Indra along with all the assemblages of the Air-gods spoke to Rambha, the 
celestial wench, words that are advantageous to himself, but disadvantageous to 
the son of sage Kushi, namely Vishvamitra." Thus Sage Shataananda continued his 
narration. [1-63-26]_END

B_1_C_66_0
BEGIN_
ततः प्रभाते विमले कृतकर्मा नराधिपः |
विश्वामित्रं महात्मानमाजुहाव सराघवम् || १-६६-१_END
BEGIN_
Then on performing morning time rites in the aurora of next morning, king Janaka 
invited great souled Vishvamitra, along with Raghava-s. [1-66-1]_END

B_1_C_65_7
BEGIN_
बहुभिः कारणैर्देव विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः |
लोभितः क्रोधितश्चैव तपसा चाभिवर्धते || १-६५-११_END
BEGIN_
Even if that great-saint Vishvamitra is angered and allured in order to foil 
his ascetical ascendancy, by all of us and by all means oh, god, he is transcending 
these lures, angers, and passions by his ascesis. [1-65-11]_END

B_1_C_64_13
BEGIN_
तस्य शापेन महता रम्भा शैली तदाभवत् |वचः श्रुत्वा च कन्दर्पो महर्षेः स च निर्गतः || १-६४-१५_END
BEGIN_
Then Rambha has become a rocklike statue by that great curse of Vishvamitra, and having heard the words 
of that great-saint Love-god and Indra also took flight. [1-64-15]_END

B_1_C_66_1
BEGIN_
तमर्चयित्वा धर्मात्मा शास्त्रदृष्टेन कर्मणा |
राघवौ च महात्मानौ तदा वाक्यमुवाच ह || १-६६-२_END
BEGIN_
On reverencing Vishvamitra and the noble souled Raghava-s according to the formalities 
envisaged by scriptures, then the virtue souled Janaka spoke these words, indeed. 
[1-66-2]_END

B_1_C_65_8
BEGIN_
न ह्यस्य वृजिनं किंचिद् दृश्यते सूक्ष्ममप्यथ |
न दीयते यदि त्वस्य मनसा यदभीप्सितम् || १-६५-१२
विनाशयति त्रैलोक्यं तपसा स चराचरम् |_END
BEGIN_
Now, even an imperceptible imperfection does not really appear in him, but if 
his heartfelt desire is not meted out, he will devastate the triad of worlds with 
his ascetic power. [1-65-12, 13a]_END

B_1_C_64_14
BEGIN_
कोपेन स महातेजास्तपोऽपहरणे कृते |इन्द्रियैरजितै राम न लेभे शान्तिमात्मनः || १-६४-१६_END
BEGIN_
Owing to his angering that great-resplendent Vishvamitra is now divested of his ascetical merit, and 
he has no peace of mind owing to ungovernable senses. [1-64-16]_END

B_1_C_66_2
BEGIN_
भगवन् स्वागतं तेऽस्तु किं करोमि तवानघ |
भवानाज्ञापयतु मामाज्ञाप्यो भवताह्यहम् || १-६६-३_END
BEGIN_
Oh, god, you are welcome, oh, holy sage, bid me as to what I should for you, for 
I am biddable by you, indeed... [1-66-3]_END

B_1_C_65_9
BEGIN_
व्याकुलाश्च दिशः सर्वा न च किंचित् प्रकाशते || १-६५-१३
सागराः क्षुभिताः सर्वे विशीर्यन्ते च पर्वताः |_END
BEGIN_
All the directions are all tumultuous, all the oceans are tempestuous, and all 
the mountains are eruptive, and nothing is bright. [1-65-13b, 14a]_END

B_1_C_64_15
BEGIN_
बभूवास्य मनश्चिंता तपोऽपहरणे कृते |नैव क्रोधं गमिष्यामि न च वक्ष्ये कथंचन || १-६४-१७_END
BEGIN_
His conscience became sentimental owing to the divesture of his ascetical merit, and he soliloquised, 
'I shall not succumb to wrath in anyway, nor I put my presentiment into words.' [1-64-17]_END

B_1_C_66_3
BEGIN_
एवमुक्तः स धर्मात्मा जनकेन महात्मना |
प्रत्युवाच मुनिर्वीरं वाक्यं वाक्यविशारदः || १-६६-४_END
BEGIN_
When said thus by the foreseer Janaka, [who can foresee as to why Vishvamitra came 
with Raghava-s this far, and thus asked him as to what next is to be done,] that 
sage Vishvamitra, for he is presager and wordsmith, [and who knows what is to be 
done next,] said these words in reply to that valiant king Janaka. [1-66-4]_END

B_1_C_65_10
BEGIN_
प्रकंपते च वसुधा वायुर्वातीह संकुलः || १-६५-१४
ब्रह्मन्न प्रतिजानीमो नास्तिको जायते जनः |_END
BEGIN_
The earth is highly tremulous, air is gusting turbulently, oh, Brahma, people 
tend to become non-theistic and we do not know what to do. [1-65-14b, 15a]_END

B_1_C_64_16
BEGIN_
अथवा नोच्छ्वसिष्यामि संवत्सरशतान्यपि |अहं हि शोषयिष्यामि आत्मानं विजितेन्द्रियः || १-६४-१८_END
BEGIN_
Otherwise, I do not even respire for a hundred years for the respiratory gestures will also exhibit 
moods, and I indeed emaciate myself until I become a real conqueror of my own senses. [1-64-18]_END

B_1_C_66_4
BEGIN_
पुत्रौ दशरथस्येमौ क्षत्रियौ लोकविश्रुतौ |
द्रष्टुकामौ धनुः श्रेष्ठं यदेतत्त्वयि तिष्ठति || १-६६-५_END
BEGIN_
These two are the sons of Dasharatha, well-renowned Kshatriya-s in world, and they 
are desirous to see that marvellous bow which has a place with you... [1-66-5]_END

B_1_C_65_11
BEGIN_
सम्मूढमिव त्रैलोक्यं संप्रक्षुभितमानसम् || १-६५-१५
भास्करो निष्प्रभश्चैव महर्षेस्तस्य तेजसा |_END
BEGIN_
All the beings in the triad of the worlds are very highly perturbed at their 
senses and they are as though stupefied, and when juxtaposed the sun is lustreless 
before the resplendence of that great sage. [1-65-15b, 16a]_END

B_1_C_64_17
BEGIN_
तावद्यावद्धि मे प्राप्तं ब्राह्मण्यं तपसार्जितम् |अनुच्छ्वसन्नभुंजास्तिष्ठेयं शाश्वतीः समाः 
|| १-६४-१९न हि मे तप्यमानस्य क्षयं यास्यन्ति मूर्तयः |_END
BEGIN_
'Till such time as I acquire Brahman-hood with the merit of my own ascesis I will be breathless and 
foodless, even if it is going to take endless years, and while I am in ascesis my bodily organs indeed 
will not undergo any deterioration.' So said Vishvamitra to himself. [1-64-19]_END

B_1_C_65_12
BEGIN_
बुद्धिं न कुरुते यावन्नाशे देव महामुनिः || १-६५-१६
तावत्प्रसादो भगवानग्निरूपो महाद्युतिः |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, God, great saint Vishvamitra turned out to be the embodiment of Fire-god, 
and before that great-resplendent and most reverential sage makes up his mind for 
total destruction of all worlds he is to be placated. [1-65-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_66_5
BEGIN_
एतद्दर्शय भद्रं ते कृतकामौ नृपात्मजौ |
दर्शनादस्य धनुषो यथेष्टं प्रतियास्यतः || १-६६-६_END
BEGIN_
You may show that bow, well bodes you, and on beholding that bow the desire of 
these two princes will come true, and they will go back as they like... [1-66-6]_END

B_1_C_64_18
BEGIN_
एवं वर्षसहस्रस्य दीक्षां स मुनिपुंगवः |चकार प्रतिमां लोके प्रतिज्ञां रघुन्ंदन || १-६४-२०_END
BEGIN_
"Thus that eminent sage abided by the commitment to the vow for a thousand years, oh, Rama, the legatee 
of Ragu, which is a nonpareil vow in the world." Thus Shataananda continued. [1-64-20]_END

B_1_C_65_13
BEGIN_
कालाग्निना यथा पूर्वं त्रैलोक्यं दह्यतेऽखिलम् || १-६५-१७
देवराज्यं चिकीर्षेत दीयतामस्य यन्मतम् |_END
BEGIN_
'As to how the End-Time Fire entirely blazed away the triad of worlds previously, 
now this sage may do likewise, hence whatever is his predilection that may be given 
to him, even if he wants to become the potentate on the realm of gods.' Thus, all 
gods appealed to Brahma [1-65-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_66_6
BEGIN_
एवमुक्तस्तु जनकः प्रत्युवाच महामुनिम् |
श्रूयतामस्य धनुषो यदर्थमिह तिष्ठति || १-६६-७_END
BEGIN_
But Janaka replied the great sage Vishvamitra when he was addressed thus, "I shall 
[firstly] tell by which reason that bow has its place here... [1-66-7]_END

B_1_C_65_14
BEGIN_
ततः सुरगणाः सर्वे पितामहपुरोगमाः || १-६५-१८
विश्वामित्रं महात्मानं वाक्यं मधुरमब्रुवन् |_END
BEGIN_
Then all the assemblages of gods keeping the Grandparent Brahma in their forefront 
appeared before that great souled Vishvamitra and said this harmonious word. [1-65-18b, 
19a]_END

B_1_C_66_7
BEGIN_
देवरात इति ख्यातो निमेः षष्ठो महीपतिः |
न्यासोऽयं तस्य भगवन् हस्ते दत्तो महात्मना || १-६६-८_END
BEGIN_
Oh, godly sage, there was a king renowned as Devaraata, sixth one from Nimi, [the 
originator of our lineage,] and this bow was handed down to him for custodial care 
by the Sublime Soul, Shiva... [1-66-8]_END

B_1_C_65_15
BEGIN_
ब्रह्मर्षे स्वागतं तेऽस्तु तपसा स्म सुतोषिताः || १-६५-१९
ब्राह्मण्यं तपसोग्रेण प्राप्तवानसि कौशिक |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Brahma-sage, you are welcome. We are much contented with your ascesis. Oh, 
Kaushika, you have achieved Bahaman-hood by your rigorous ascesis. [1-65-19b, 20a]_END

B_1_C_66_8
BEGIN_
दक्षयज्ञवधे पूर्वं धनुरायम्य वीर्यवान् |
रुद्रस्तु त्रिदशान् रोषात् सलीलमिदमब्रवीत् || १-६६-९_END
BEGIN_
Once, during the devastation of the Vedic-ritual of Daksha Prajapati, the mettlesome 
god Rudra, rancorously outstretching the bowstring of this bow, said this to all 
gods, superciliously... [1-66-9]_END

B_1_C_65_16
BEGIN_
दीर्घमायुश्च ते ब्रह्मन् ददामि समरुद्गणः || १-६५-२०
स्वस्ति प्राप्नुहि भद्रं ते गच्छ सौम्य यथासुखम् |_END
BEGIN_
'Along with the assemblages of Marut-Wind-gods, I bestow upon you a long life. 
Let blissfulness betide you. You be safe. Oh, gentle sage, you may take leave as 
you please.' Thus, Brahma said to Vishvamitra. [1-65-20b, 21a]_END

B_1_C_66_9
BEGIN_
यस्माद्भागार्थिनो भागं नाकल्पयत मे सुराः |
वरांगाणि महार्हाणि धनुषा शातयामि वः || १-६६-१०_END
BEGIN_
'Oh, gods, whereby you have not apportioned my portion [of oblations in Vedic-ritual 
s, as I am also the] desirer of such portion, [thereby] I will shred the highly 
revered heads of yours with this bow...' [So said Shiva to gods.] [1-66-10]_END

B_1_C_65_17
BEGIN_
पितामहवचः श्रुत्वा सर्वेषां त्रिदिवौकसाम् || १-६५-२१
कृत्वा प्रणामं मुदितो व्याजहार महामुनिः |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the word of Grandparent Brahma and the other residents of heaven, and 
on paying good devoirs to all of them that great saint cheerfully said. [1-65-21b, 
22a]_END

B_1_C_66_10
BEGIN_
ततो विमनसः सर्वे देवा वै मुनिपुंगव |
प्रसादयन्ति देवेशं तेषां प्रीतोऽभवद्भवः || १-६६-११_END
BEGIN_
Then, oh, best saint Vishvamitra, all gods are truly dismayed, and on their supplicating, 
Bhava, namely Shiva, the God of Gods is gladdened... [1-66-11]_END

B_1_C_65_18
BEGIN_
ब्राह्मण्यं यदि मे प्राप्तं दीर्घमायुस्तथैव च || १-६५-२२
ओंकारोऽथ वषट्कारो वेदाश्च वरयन्तु माम् |_END
BEGIN_
If Brahman-hood and eternality have befallen on me, let the quintessence of AUM 
and vaSat syllables, and even all Veda-s patronise me. [1-65-22b, 23a]_END

B_1_C_66_11
BEGIN_
प्रीतियुक्तस्तु सर्वेषां ददौ तेषां महात्मनाम् |
तदेतद्देवदेवस्य धनूरत्नं महात्मनः || १-६६-१२
न्यासभूतं तदा न्यस्तमस्माकं पूर्वजे विभो |_END
BEGIN_
And that Sublime Soul Shiva gladly gave that bow to all of the great souled gods, 
and oh, godly saint, then those great souled gods gave this gem of a bow of Shiva, 
the God of Gods, to our ancestor [Devaraata,] for custodial care... [1-66-12, 13a]_END

B_1_C_65_19
BEGIN_
क्षत्र वेदविदां श्रेष्ठो ब्रह्मवेदविदामपि || १-६५-२३
ब्रह्मपुत्रो वसिष्ठो मामेवं वदतु देवताः |
यद्ययं परमः कामः कृतो यान्तु सुरर्षभाः || १-६५-२४_END
BEGIN_
'Oh, gods, he who is the outstanding one among the geniuses of kingcraft, and 
among the scholars of Veda-s as well, even that Vashishta, the brainchild of Brahma, 
shall acknowledge me in this way as Brahma-sage. Oh, the best gods, you may take 
leave if you can effectuate this ultimate yearning of mine.' Thus Vishvamitra requested 
the gods. [1-65-23b, 24]_END

B_1_C_66_12
BEGIN_
अथ मे कृषतः क्षेत्रं लांगलादुत्थिता मम || १-६६-१३
क्षेत्रं शोधयता लब्धा नाम्ना सीतेति विश्रुता |_END
BEGIN_
Later, when I was ploughing the ritual field then raised by the plough [from the 
furrow is a baby girl... since she is] gained while consecrating the ritual-field, 
she is named as Seetha, and thus she is renowned... [1-66-13b, 14a]_END

B_1_C_66_13
BEGIN_
भूतलादुत्थिता सा तु व्यवर्धत ममात्मजा || १-६६-१४
वीर्यशुल्केति मे कन्या स्थापितेयमयोनिजा |_END
BEGIN_
Hers is a non-uterine birth as she surfaced from the surface of the earth, but 
fostered as my own soul-born girl and I determined [to give her in marriage to 
a bridegroom where his] boldness is the only bounty, [I receive in that marriage...] 
[1-66-14b, 15a]_END

B_1_C_65_20
BEGIN_
ततः प्रसादितो देवैर्वसिष्ठो जपतां वरः |
सख्यं चकार ब्रह्मर्षिरेवमस्त्विति चाब्रवीत् || १-६५-२५_END
BEGIN_
Then the best one among meditators Vashishta has come over there when the gods 
besought him to come, and he made friendship with Vishvamitra. He also said in this 
way to Vishvamitra, 'you are a Brahma-sage.' [1-65-25]_END

B_1_C_65_21
BEGIN_
ब्रह्मर्षिस्त्वं न संदेहः सर्वं संपद्यते तव |
इत्युक्त्वा देवताश्चापि सर्वा जग्मुर्यथागतम् || १-६५-२६_END
BEGIN_
'No doubt, you are a Brahma-sage and everything will accrue to you in accordance 
with the sublimity of this sageship,' and when Vashishta said so to Vishvamitra, 
all the gods have gone away as they have come. [1-65-26]_END

B_1_C_66_14
BEGIN_
भूतलादुत्थितां तां तु वर्धमानां ममात्मजाम् || १-६६-१५
वरयामासुरागम्य राजानो मुनिपुंगव |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, eminent sage, as my daughter has surfaced from the surface of earth and has 
come of age, the kings, [having heard my declaration that the bounty for Seetha 
is boldness alone,] have come and besought for her... [1-66-15b, 16a]_END

B_1_C_65_22
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रोऽपि धर्मात्मा लब्ध्वा ब्राह्मण्यमुत्तमम् |
पूजयामास ब्रह्मर्षिं वसिष्ठं जपतां वरम् || १-६५-२७_END
BEGIN_
On getting his Brahman-hood even the virtue-souled Vishvamitra started to reverence 
the supreme among meditators and his counterpart Brahma-sage, namely Vashishta. 
[1-65-27]_END

B_1_C_66_15
BEGIN_
तेषां वरयतां कन्यां सर्वेषां पृथिवीक्षिताम् || १-६६-१६
वीर्यशुल्केति भगवन्न ददामि सुतामहम् |_END
BEGIN_
To all of those kings who are beseeching for the girl, I have not given my daughter, 
saying that she will be given for a bounty of boldness... [1-6-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_65_23
BEGIN_
कृतकामो महीं सर्वां चचार तपसि स्थितः |
एवं त्वनेन ब्राह्मण्यं प्राप्तं राम महात्मना || १-६५-२८_END
BEGIN_
When his aim is effectuated Vishvamitra ambled all over the earth abiding in ascesis, 
and oh, Rama, this great souled sage Vishvamitra achieved Brahman-hood in this way. 
[1-65-28]_END

B_1_C_66_16
BEGIN_
ततः सर्वे नृपतयः समेत्य मुनिपुंगव || १-६६-१७
मिथिलामभ्युपागम्य वीर्यं जिज्ञासवस्तदा |_END
BEGIN_
Then all the kings convoked and on arriving at Mithila, then they wanted to ascertain 
the calibre [of the bow, vis-a-vis their own...] [1-66-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_65_24
BEGIN_
एष राम मुनिश्रेष्ठ एष विग्रहवान् तपः |
एष धर्मः परो नित्यं वीर्यस्यैष परायणम् || १-६५-२९_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, he is the best saint, he is the embodiment of ascesis, he is always obliged 
with righteousness, and he is the stronghold for fortitude." [1-65-29]_END

B_1_C_66_17
BEGIN_
तेषां जिज्ञासमानानां शैवं धनुरुपाहृतम् || १-६६-१८
न शेकुर्ग्रहणे तस्य धनुषस्तोलनेऽपि वा |_END
BEGIN_
For them, those who wanted to ascertain the calibre of the bow, that bow of Shiva 
is fetched to their proximity, but they are incapable to joggle it, or even to catch 
hold of it... [1-66-18b, 19a]_END

B_1_C_66_18
BEGIN_
तेषां वीर्यवतां वीर्यमल्पं ज्ञात्वा महामुने || १-६६-१९
प्रत्याख्याता नृपतयस्तन्निबोध तपोधन |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, great saint, on knowing the valour of those valorous ones as valueless, I countermanded 
them... oh, ascetically wealthy Vishvamitra, by that you may know [the sequel of 
it...] [1-66-19b, 20a]_END

B_1_C_65_25
BEGIN_
एवमुक्त्वा महातेजा विरराम द्विजोत्तमः |
शतानंदवचः श्रुत्वा रामलक्ष्मणसंनिधौ ||१-६५-३०
जनकः प्रांजलिर्वाक्यमुवाच कुशिकात्मजम् |_END
BEGIN_
On narrating the legend of Vishvamitra in this way that best Brahman and great-resplendent 
Sage Shataananda took respite. And on listening the narration of Sage Shataananda 
said in the presence of Rama and Lakshmana, king Janaka said this sentence to Kushika's 
son, Vishvamitra, with suppliantly adjoined palms. [1-65-30b, 31a]_END

B_1_C_67_0
BEGIN_
 जनकस्य वचः श्रुत्वा विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः |
 
  धनुर्दर्शय रामाय इति होवाच पार्थिवम् || १-६७-१_END
BEGIN_
 On listening to the words of Janaka, the eminent-saint Vishvamitra indeed said to
  the king Janaka thus as, "let the bow be displayed to Rama..." [1-67-1]_END

B_1_C_66_19
BEGIN_
ततः परमकोपेन राजानो मुनिपुंगव || १-६६-२०
अरुन्धन् मिथिलां सर्वे वीर्यसंदेहमागताः |_END
BEGIN_
Then, oh, eminent sage, those kings beleaguered Mithila in a blind fury, since 
a self-mistrust bechanced among them all, about their own valour... [1-66-20b, 21a]_END

B_1_C_65_26
BEGIN_
धन्योऽस्म्यनुगृहीतोऽस्मि यस्य मे मुनिपुंगव || १-६५-३१
यज्ञं काकुत्स्थसहितः प्राप्तवानसि कौशिक |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, eminent sage Vishvamitra, you happened to be here at this Vedic-ritual which 
is conducted by me, oh, Kaushika, that too, along with Rama and Lakshmana, the legatees 
of Kakutstha, thereby I am fortunate, I am much obliged. [31b, 32a]_END

B_1_C_67_1
BEGIN_
 ततः स राजा जनकः सचिवान् व्यादिदेश ह |
 
  धनुरानीयतां दिव्यं गन्धमाल्यानुलेपितम् || १-६७-२_END
BEGIN_
 Then king Janaka indeed ordered his ministers, "bring the divine bow which is
  decorated with sandalwood paste and garlands... [1-67-2]_END

B_1_C_65_27
BEGIN_
पावितोऽहं त्वया ब्रह्मन् दर्शनेन महामुने || १-६५-३२
गुणा बहुविधाः प्राप्तास्तव संदर्शनान्मया |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Brahman, I stand consecrated just by your graceful glance, and oh, great saint, 
I reckon that I have achieved many boons just glancing at you. [1-65-32b, 33a]_END

B_1_C_66_20
BEGIN_
आत्मानमवधूतं ते विज्ञाय मुनिपुंगव || १-६६-२१
रोषेण महताविष्टाः पीडयन् मिथिलां पुरीम् |_END
BEGIN_
They surmised for themselves that they are brushed off by me, and they possessed 
by a high rancour, they strangled the City of Mithila... [1-66-21b, 22a]_END

B_1_C_67_2
BEGIN_
 जनकेन समादिष्ठाः सचिवाः प्राविशन् पुरम् |
 
  तद्धनुः पुरतः कृत्वा निर्जग्मुरमितौजसः || १-६७-३
  नृणां शतानि पंचाशद्व्यायतानां महात्मनाम् |
  मंजूषामष्टचक्रां तां समूहुस्ते कथंचन || १-६७-४_END
BEGIN_
 Thus clearly instructed by Janaka those high souled ministers have gone out from
  there and entered the palace-chambers, and they came out with an eight-wheeled coffer in which
  the bow of Shiva is ensconced, and those ministers got it tugged by five thousand tall men of
  illimitable energy who somehow tugged it very difficultly, and thus the ministers have re-entered
  there keeping that bow afore of them. [1-67-3, 4]_END

B_1_C_66_21
BEGIN_
ततः संवत्सरे पूर्णे क्षयं यातानि सर्वशः || १-६६-२२
साधनानि मुनिश्रेष्ठ ततोऽहं भृशदुःखितः |_END
BEGIN_
Then elapsed is an year and in anyway the possessions for livelihood went into 
a decline, oh, eminent sage, thereby I am highly anguished [1-66-22b, 23a]_END

B_1_C_65_28
BEGIN_
विस्तरेण च वै ब्रह्मन् कीर्त्यमानं महत्तपः || १-६५-३३
श्रुतं मया महातेजो रामेण च महात्मना |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, great-resplendent Brahman, myself and the noble souled Rama have heard about 
your great ascesis when Sage Shataananda extolled it comprehensively. [1-65-33b, 
34a]_END

B_1_C_67_3
BEGIN_
 तामादाय तु मंजूषामायसीं यत्र तद्धनुः |
 
  सुरोपमं ते जनकमूचुर्नृपतिमन्त्रिणः || १-६७-५_END
BEGIN_
 On fetching that iron coffer wherein that bow is there, those ministers of the
  king have reported to their godlike King Janaka. [1-67-5]_END

B_1_C_65_29
BEGIN_
सदस्यैः प्राप्य च सदः श्रुतास्ते बहवो गुणाः || १-६५-३४
अप्रमेया तपस्तुभ्यमप्रमेयं च ते बलम् |
अप्रमेया गुणाश्चैव नित्यं ते कुशिकात्मज || १-६५-३५_END
BEGIN_
The congregationalists available in this Vedic-ritual congregation have also heard 
about your numerous endowments. Inestimable is your ascesis, infinite is your power, 
and oh, son of Kushika, your talents are everlastingly invaluable. [1-65-34b, 35]_END

B_1_C_66_22
BEGIN_
ततो देवगणान् सर्वांस्तपसाहं प्रसादयम् || १-६६-२३
ददुश्च परमप्रीताश्चतुरंगबलं सुराः |_END
BEGIN_
Then I have assuaged the assemblages of gods by my ascesis and gods are also highly 
gladdened and gave me fourfold forces... [1-66-23b, 24a]_END

B_1_C_67_4
BEGIN_
 इदं धनुर्वरं राजन् पूजितं सर्वराजभिः |
 
  मिथिलाधिप राजेन्द्र दर्शनीयं यदिच्छसि || १-६७-६_END
BEGIN_
 Oh king and sovereign of Mithila, here is the select bow that is reverenced by
  all kings, oh, best king, which you wished to be evincible to the boys, to evince their
  capabilities... [1-67-6]_END

B_1_C_66_23
BEGIN_
ततो भग्ना नृपतयो हन्यमाना दिशो ययुः || १-६६-२४
अवीर्या वीर्यसंदिग्धाः सामात्याः पापकारिणः |_END
BEGIN_
Then those evildoers and self-mistrustful kings while being drubbed [by the heaven-sent 
army, they have become] vigourless and broken, and they beat a hasty retreat... 
[1-66-24b, 25a]_END

B_1_C_65_30
BEGIN_
तृप्तिराश्चर्यभूतानां कथानां नास्ति मे विभो |
कर्मकालो मुनिश्रेष्ठ लम्बते रविमण्डलम् || १-६५-३६_END
BEGIN_
Oh, lord, there is no contentment to me while listening to your wondrous narratives, 
but oh nobleman, time for vespertine ritual is fast approaching as sun's sphere 
is dangling westward. [1-65-36]_END

B_1_C_67_5
BEGIN_
 तेषां नृपो वचः श्रुत्वा कृताञ्जलिरभाषत |
 
  विश्वामित्रं महात्मानं तावुभौ रामलक्ष्मणौ || १-६७-७_END
BEGIN_
 On listening the announcement of his ministers the king spoke to the noble souled
  Vishvamitra and to both Rama and Lakshmana too duly making palm-fold. [1-67-7]_END

B_1_C_66_24
BEGIN_
तदेतन्मुनिशार्दूल धनुः परमभास्वरम् || १-६६-२५
रामलक्ष्मणयोश्चापि दर्शयिष्यामि सुव्रत |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, tigerly sage this is that supremely radiant bow, and oh, saint of sacred vows, 
I will show it, even to Rama and Lakshmana... [1-66-25b, 26a]_END

B_1_C_65_31
BEGIN_
श्वः प्रभाते महातेजो द्रष्टुमर्हसि मां पुनः |
स्वागतं जपतां श्रेष्ठ मामनुज्ञातुमर्हसि || १-६५-३७_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, great-resplendent sage, it will be apt of you to see me tomorrow. Oh, best 
meditator, it will be apt of you to permit me to leave for now." Thus Janaka sought 
leave from Vishvamitra. [1-65-37]_END

B_1_C_67_6
BEGIN_
 इदं धनुर्वरं ब्रह्मन् जनकैरभिपूजितम् |
 
  राजभिश्च महावीर्यैरशक्तैः पूरितं तदा || १-६७-८_END
BEGIN_
 Here is that exquisite bow, oh, Brahman, which is held as a time-honoured bow by
  the lineage of Janaka kings, and with which even the highly forceful kings are rendered
  inefficient to take aim with it, previously... [1-67-8]_END

B_1_C_66_25
BEGIN_
यद्यस्य धनुषो रामः कुर्यादारोपणं मुने |
सुतामयोनिजां सीतां दद्यां दाशरथेरहम् || १-६६-२६_END
BEGIN_
"If Rama strings the bowstring of that bow, oh, sage, I will offer my daughter, 
whose birth is non-uterine, to Dasharatha's Rama..." [So said Janaka to Vishvamitra.] 
[1-66-26b, c]_END

B_1_C_65_32
BEGIN_
एवमुक्तो मुनिवरः प्रशस्य पुरुषर्षभम् |
विससर्जाशु जनकं प्रीतं प्रीतिमांस्तदा || १-६५-३८_END
BEGIN_
When he is spoken in that way, the best saint Vishvamitra is pleased at heart, and 
praising Janaka, who too is pleased to meet the sage, immediately bid farewell to 
the best one among men, namely Janaka. [1-65-38]_END

B_1_C_67_7
BEGIN_
नैतत् सुरगणाः सर्वे सासुरा न च राक्षसाः |
 
  गंधर्वयक्षप्रवराः सकिन्नरमहोरगाः || १-६७-९
  क्व गतिर्मानुषाणां च धनुषोऽस्य प्रपूरणे |
  आरोपणे समायोगे वेपने तोलनेऽपि वा || १-६७-१०_END
BEGIN_
 None in all the assemblages of gods, inclusive of demigods, demons, gandharva-s,
  yaksha-s, kinnaraa-s, or reptilian demigods, is capable enough to take aim with this bow and all
  are rendered incapable... and then, in brandishing this bow for a proper grip, or in bracing its
  bowstring to the other end, or in twitching the bowstring for its tautness, or in placing the
  arrow on bowstring at a proper place for a proper stretchability, or even in taking a good aim
  with it... what will be that capability of one from among humans... [1-1-9, 10]_END

B_1_C_65_33
BEGIN_
एवमुक्त्वा मुनिश्रेष्ठं वैदेहो मिथिलाधिपः |
प्रदक्षिणं चकाराशु सोपाध्यायः सबांधवः || १-६५-३९_END
BEGIN_
This way on saying to the best saint, the king of Mithila and the legatee of Videha 
lineage, immediately performed circumambulations along with his teachers and relatives 
to Vishvamitra in veneration. [1-65-39]_END

B_1_C_67_8
BEGIN_
 तदेतद्धनुषां श्रेष्ठमानीतं मुनिपुंगव |
 
  दर्शयैतन्महाभाग अनयो राजपुत्रयोः || १-६७-११_END
BEGIN_
 "Oh, eminent-saint, such as it is, this nonpareil bow among all bows is brought
  in, and oh, highly fortunate sage Vishvamitra, let this be displayed to those two princes..."
  Thus Janaka said to Vishvamitra. [1-67-11]_END

B_1_C_65_34
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रोऽपि धर्मात्मा सहरामः सलक्ष्मणः |
स्वं वासमभिचक्राम पूज्यमानो महर्षिभिः || १-६५-४०_END
BEGIN_
Even that virtue souled Vishvamitra started towards his own camp along with Rama 
and Lakshmana, while being venerated by great sages who are available in the ritual-hall. 
[1-65-40]_END

B_1_C_67_9
BEGIN_
 विश्वामित्रः सरामस्तु श्रुत्वा जनकभाषितम् |
 
  वत्स राम धनुः पश्य इति राघवमब्रवीत् || १-६७-१२_END
BEGIN_
 Vishvamitra on listening the sentence of Janaka along with Rama, on his part said
  to Raghava, "oh, boy Rama... you may see the bow..." [1-67-12]_END

B_1_C_68_0
BEGIN_
जनकेन समादिष्टा दूतास्ते क्लान्तवाहनाः |
त्रिरात्रमुषिताः मार्गे तेऽयोध्यां प्राविशन् पुरीम् || १-६८-१_END
BEGIN_
Those envoys who are clearly ordered by Janaka entered the city of Ayodhya on sojourning 
for three nights en route, and whose horses are overtired for they are galloped 
so fast to loose no time. [1-68-1]_END

B_1_C_67_10
BEGIN_
 महर्षेर्वचनाद्रामो यत्र तिष्ठति तद्धनुः |
 
  मंजूषां तामपावृत्य दृष्ट्वा धनुरथाब्रवीत् || १-६७-१३_END
BEGIN_
 Upon the word of the great sage Vishvamitra, Rama on unclosing the lid of that
  strongbox, wherein that bow is ensconced, saw the bow and said. [1-67-13]_END

B_1_C_68_1
BEGIN_
ते राजवचनाद्गत्वा राजवेश्म प्रवेशिताः |
ददृशुर्देवसंकाशं वृद्धं दशरथं नृपम् || १-६८-२_END
BEGIN_
On going to the palace those envoys are given an audience with the consent of Dasharatha, 
and when they are conducted into the palace-chambers they have seen the elderly 
king Dasharatha gleaming like a god. [1-68-2]_END

B_1_C_67_11
BEGIN_
 इदं धनुर्वरं ब्रह्मन् संस्पृशामीह पाणिना |
 
  यत्नवांश्च भविष्यामि तोलने पूरणेऽपि वा || १-६७-१४_END
BEGIN_
 Now I wish to get the feel of this supreme bow, oh, Brahman, and I shall try to
  brandish it, or even try to take aim with it... [1-67-14]_END

B_1_C_68_2
BEGIN_
बद्धाञ्जलिपुटाः सर्वे दूता विगतसाध्वसाः |
राजानं प्रश्रितं वाक्यमब्रुवन्मधुराक्षरम् || १-६८-३_END
BEGIN_
Completely gone is the angst of all the legates on seeing godly Dasharatha, and 
all of them adjoing palms in reverence said this compliant and mellowly worded sentence 
to the king. [1-68-3]_END

B_1_C_67_12
BEGIN_
 बाढमित्येव तं राजा मुनिश्च समभाषत |
 
  लीलया स धनुर्मध्ये जग्राह वचनान्मुनेः || १-६७-१५_END
BEGIN_
 "All Right!" said the saint and king to Rama in chorus, and Rama upon the word of
  the sage grasping it at the middle handgrip playfully grabbed the bow. [1-67-15]_END

B_1_C_68_3
BEGIN_
मैथिलो जनको राजा साग्निहोत्रपुरस्कृतः |
मुहुर्मुहुर्मधुरया स्नेहसंरक्तया गिरा || १-६८-४
कुशलं चाव्ययं चैव सोपाध्यायपुरोहितम् |
जनकस्त्वां महाराज पृच्छते सपुरःसरम् || १-६८-५_END
BEGIN_
Oh, exalted emperor Dasharatha! Janaka, the lineal king of Janaka-s and the present 
sovereign of Mithila is asking time and time again with mellowly words instilled 
with friendliness, after the wellbeing and after the unmitigated prosperity of your 
highness, along with that of your highness' priests and teachers, also that of your 
highness' subjects, who always precede your highness in convoys in any event, as 
your highness are the one who ingratiates himself with the Ritual-fires, ever and 
anon... [1-68-4, 5]_END

B_1_C_67_13
BEGIN_
 पश्यतां नृसहस्राणां बहूनां रघुनंदनः |
 
  आरोपयत्स धर्मात्मा सलीलमिव तद्धनुः || १-६७-१६_END
BEGIN_
 While many thousands of men are witnessing that right-minded Rama the legatee of
  Raghu stringed the bow effortlessly. [1-67-16]_END

B_1_C_68_4
BEGIN_
पृष्ट्वा कुशलमव्यग्रं वैदेहो मिथिलाधिपः |
कौशिकानुमते वाक्यं भवन्तमिदमब्रवीत् || १-६८-६_END
BEGIN_
His highness Janaka of Videha, and the sovereign of Mithila, having asked after 
your highness' wellbeing is sensibly saying this word to your highness, with the 
indorse of Kaushika... [1-68-6]_END

B_1_C_67_14
BEGIN_
 आरोपयित्वा मौर्वीं च पूरयामास वीर्यवान् |
 
  तद्बभंज धनुर्मध्ये नरश्रेष्ठो महायशाः || १-६७-१७_END
BEGIN_
 Further, that dextrous one has stringed that bow with bowstring and started to
  stretch it up to his ear to examine its tautness, but that glorious one who is foremost among
  men, Rama, broke that bow medially. [1-67-17]_END

B_1_C_68_5
BEGIN_
पूर्वं प्रतिज्ञा विदिता वीर्यशुल्का ममात्मजा |
राजानश्च कृतामर्षा निर्वीर्या विमुखीकृताः || १-६८-७_END
BEGIN_
Well-known is the solemn promise of mine that my daughter Seetha is a bounty 
for bravery... also well-know is that the kings who came to lift the bow turned 
out as gutless kings, and then they turned out as rancorous kings at me, and it 
is also well-known that I turned them back with my guts... [1-68-7]_END

B_1_C_67_15
BEGIN_
 तस्य शब्दो महानासीन्निर्घातसमनिःस्वनः |
 
  भूमिकंपश्च सुमहान् पर्वतस्येव दीर्यतः || १-६७-१८_END
BEGIN_
 Then there bechanced an explosive explosion when the bow is broken, like the
  explosiveness of down plunging thunder, and the earth is tremulously tremulous, as it happens
  when a mountain is exploding. [1-67-18]_END

B_1_C_68_6
BEGIN_
सेयं मम सुता राजन् विश्वामित्रपुरस्कृतैः |
यदृच्छयागतैर्वीरैर्निर्जिता तव पुत्रकैः || १-६८-८_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Emperor Dasharatha, your young and valorous son who serendipitously arrived 
at Mithila along with his younger brother Lakshmana, keeping Vishvamitra at his 
fore, finally carries off this girl, the well-known daughter of mine... [1-68-8]_END

B_1_C_67_16
BEGIN_
 निपेतुश्च नराः सर्वे तेन शब्देन मोहिताः |
 
  व्रजयित्वा मुनिवरं राजानं तौ च राघवौ || १-६७-१९_END
BEGIN_
 Bewildered by that raucous caused by the breakage of bow, all the people swooned,
  except for that eminent-saint Vishvamitra, king Janaka, and those two Raghava-s, namely Rama and
  Lakshmana. [1-67-19]_END

B_1_C_67_17
BEGIN_
 प्रत्याश्वस्तो जने तस्मिन् राजा विगतसाध्वसः |
 
  उवाच प्रांजलिर्वाक्यं वाक्यज्ञो मुनिपुंगवम् || १-६७-२०_END
BEGIN_
 While the people are being reaccustomed after their undergoing the shock, at that
  moment that sententious king Janaka, whose discomfiture has completely departed by now has said
  this to the eminent-saint Vishvamitra with a reverent palm-fold. [1-67-20]_END

B_1_C_68_7
BEGIN_
तच्च रत्नं धनुर्दिव्यं मध्ये भग्नं महात्मना |
रामेण हि महाबाहो महत्यां जनसंसदि || १-६८-९_END
BEGIN_
Also, oh, highly dextrous king Dasharatha, noble souled Rama wrecked that divine 
bow, which is a gem of a bow among bows, at its central point before a grand assembly 
of people... [1-68-9]_END

B_1_C_69_0
BEGIN_
ततो रात्र्यां व्यतीतायां सोपाध्यायः सबान्धवः |
राजा दशरथो हृष्टः सुमंत्रमिदमब्रवीत् || १-६९-१_END
BEGIN_
On the next dawn that heartened king Dasharatha who is with his teachers and his 
relatives then said this to his minister Sumantra. [1-69-1]_END

B_1_C_67_18
BEGIN_
 भगवन् दृष्टवीर्यो मे रामो दशरथात्मजः |
 
  अत्यद्भुतमचिन्त्यं चातर्कितमिदं मया || १-६७-२१_END
BEGIN_
 Oh, godly sage, the gallantry of Dasharatha's Rama is evidently seen... and the
  whys of this boy and wherefores of his stringing that massive bow are unimaginable to me! More
  so, humans lifting it! How so? This is an unhoped-for incident for me, besides, breaking it! This
  a is highly wondrous experience for me... [1-67-21]_END

B_1_C_68_8
BEGIN_
अस्मै देया मया सीता वीर्यशुल्का महात्मने |
प्रतिज्ञां तर्तुमिच्छामि तदनुज्ञातुमर्हसि || १-६८-१०_END
BEGIN_
Seetha is the bounty for bravery and I shall have to afford her to the noble-souled 
Rama, as such it will be apt of you to give your consent as I wish to keep up my 
solemn promise... [1-68-10]_END

B_1_C_69_1
BEGIN_
अद्य सर्वे धनाध्यक्षा धनमादाय पुष्कलम् |
व्रजंत्वग्रे सुविहिता नानारत्नसमन्विताः || १-६९-२_END
BEGIN_
Now let the chancellors of exchequers draw ample riches, gems and numerous other 
items that are used in the marriage from bridegroom's side, all-inclusively, and 
let them travel in advance and let them be well-prepared for any exigency... [1-69-2]_END

B_1_C_67_19
BEGIN_
 जनकानां कुले कीर्तिमाहरिष्यति मे सुता |
 
  सीता भर्तारमासाद्य रामं दशरथात्मजम् || १-६७-२२_END
BEGIN_
 My daughter Seetha on getting Dasharatha's Rama as her husband, she will bring
  celebrity to the lineage of Janaka-s... [1-67-22]_END

B_1_C_68_9
BEGIN_
सोपाध्यायो महाराज पुरोहितपुरस्कृतः |
शीघ्रमागच्छ भद्रं ते द्रष्टुमर्हसि राघवौ || १-६८-११_END
BEGIN_
Keeping your royal priest Vashishta and other teachers ahead of you, oh, great 
emperor, I wish you to come apace, let safe betide you, for it will be apt of you 
to take a look at your ennobled son Rama, and Lakshmana, too... [1-68-11]_END

B_1_C_69_2
BEGIN_
चतुरंगबलं चापि शीघ्रं निर्यातु सर्वशः |
ममाज्ञा समकालं च यानं युग्ममनुत्तमम् || १-६९-३_END
BEGIN_
Let the quadruple forces start off in a trice from everywhere at my order, and 
others shall start with unexcelled vehicles like palanquins, sedan chairs, litters 
etc., and with those that can be yoked with horses, like cabined-coaches and horse-carriages... 
[1-69-3]_END

B_1_C_67_20
BEGIN_
 मम सत्या प्रतिज्ञा सा वीर्यशुल्केति कौशिक |
 
  सीता प्राणैर्बहुमता देया रामाय मे सुता || १-६७-२३_END
BEGIN_
 Oh, Kaushika, my commitment that she is the bounty of bravery has also come
  true... and my daughter Seetha who is nurtured well than my own lives is a worthy bride for
  Rama... [1-67-23]_END

B_1_C_68_10
BEGIN_
प्रतिज्ञां मम राजेन्द्र निर्वर्तयितुमर्हसि |
पुत्रयोरुभयोरेव प्रीतिं त्वमपि लप्स्यसे || १-६८-१२_END
BEGIN_
'It will be apt of you to make my solemn promise maintainable, and that way you 
will derive delight on seeing both of your sons...' [1-68-12]_END

B_1_C_69_3
BEGIN_
वसिष्ठो वामदेवश्च जाबालिरथ काश्यपः |
मार्कण्डेयश्च दीर्घायुर्ऋषिः कात्यायनस्तथा || १-६९-४
एते द्विजाः प्रयान्त्वग्रे स्यंदनं योजयस्व मे |
यथा कालात्ययो न स्याद्दूता हि त्वरयन्ति माम् || १-६९-५_END
BEGIN_
"Vashishta, Vaamadeva, Jaabaali and Kaashyapa, and the long-lived Maarkandeya, and 
Sage Kaatyaayana... let these Brahmans travel in forefront... and let horses be 
yoked to my royal-cariole, and as the messengers of Janaka are hastening me arrange 
for the travel without time lapse..." Thus Dasharatha ordered. [1-69-4, 5]_END

B_1_C_67_21
BEGIN_
 भवतोऽनुमते ब्रह्मन् शीघ्रं गच्छंतु मंत्रिणः |
 
  मम कौशिक भद्रं ते अयोध्यां त्वरिता रथैः || १-६७-२४_END
BEGIN_
 Should you give consent, oh, Brahman, my ministers will be hastened to speedily
  go to Ayodhya in chariots, oh, Kaushika, let safeness betide you, and one and all by this
  matrimony... [1-67-24]_END

B_1_C_68_11
BEGIN_
एवं विदेहाधिपतिर्मधुरं वाक्यमब्रवीत् |
विश्वामित्राभ्यनुज्ञातः शतानन्दमते स्थितः || १-६८-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Thus the sovereign of Videha kingdom said these endearing words, abiding by the 
counsel of Sage Shataananda, and Sage Vishvamitra is also consentient to the proposal..." 
Thus the envoys conveyed the proposal and paused. [1-68-13]_END

B_1_C_69_4
BEGIN_
वचनाच्च नरेन्द्रस्य सेना च चतुरंगिणी |
राजानमृषिभिः सार्धं व्रजंतं पृष्ठतोऽन्वगात् || १-६९-६_END
BEGIN_
On the word of that best king the fourfold opulence, and even the fourfold forces 
up to some extent followed rearward of the king who is going after the sages who 
are going afore of him. [1-69-6]_END

B_1_C_67_22
BEGIN_
 राजानं प्रश्रितैर्वाक्यैरानयंतु पुरं मम |
 
  प्रदानं वीर्यशुक्लायाः कथयंतु च सर्वशः || १-६७-२५_END
BEGIN_
 With their observant submissions those ministers will narrate in detail about the
  sincere endowment of Seetha as bravery's bounty to Rama, and they will lead king Dasharatha into
  my city that observantly... [1-67-25]_END

B_1_C_68_12
BEGIN_
दूतवाक्यं तु तच्छ्रुत्वा राजा परमहर्षितः |
वसिष्ठं वामदेवं च मंत्रिणश्चैवमब्रवीत् || १-६८-१४_END
BEGIN_
King Dasharatha is highly gladdened on hearing that message from the delegates, 
and said this way to Vashishta, Vaamadeva, and to his other ministers, as well. 
[1-68-14]_END

B_1_C_69_5
BEGIN_
गत्वा चतुरहं मार्गं विदेहानभ्युपेयिवान् |
राजा तु जनकः श्रीमान् श्रुत्वा पूजामकल्पयत् || १-६९-७_END
BEGIN_
Travelling on a four-day-route Dasharatha reached the fringes of Videha kingdom, 
and on hearing this, the illustrious king Janaka arranged for welcome ceremonies 
at the outskirts of the city. [1-69-7]_END

B_1_C_67_23
BEGIN_
 मुनिगुप्तौ च काकुत्स्थौ कथयंतु नृपाय वै |
 
  प्रीतियुक्तं तु राजानमानयंतु सुशीघ्रगाः || १-६७-२६_END


B_1_C_68_13
BEGIN_
गुप्तः कुशिकपुत्रेण कौसल्यानन्दवर्धनः |
लक्ष्मणेन सह भ्रात्रा विदेहेषु वसत्यसौ || १-६८-१५_END
BEGIN_
This one Rama, the enhancer of Kausalya's rejoice, is stopping over at Videha kingdom 
along with his brother Lakshmana, and Vishvamitra is taking care of both these boys... 
[1-68-15]_END

B_1_C_69_6
BEGIN_
ततो राजानमासाद्य वृद्धं दशरथं नृपम् |
जनको मुदितो राजा हर्षं च परमं ययौ || १-६९-८_END
BEGIN_
Then the king Janaka who is by far gladdened went into a state of ecstatic elation 
when he met the senescent king and paladin of people, namely Dasharatha, as the 
pace for the marriage celebrations is quickened because of the immediate arrival 
of Dasharatha. [1-69-8]_END

B_1_C_67_24
BEGIN_
 कौशिकश्च तथेत्याह राजा चाभाष्य मंत्रिणः |
 
  अयोध्यां प्रेषयामास धर्मात्मा कृतशासनान् |
  यथावृत्तं समाख्यातुमानेतुं च नृपं तथा || १-६७-२७_END
BEGIN_
 Vishvamitra said, "so be it," and then that right-minded king Janaka on consulting
  with his ministers started to send his ministers, plenipotentiaries, to Ayodhya to inform
  Dasharatha in detail as to what has happened, and likewise to bring him to Mithila. [1-67-27]_END

B_1_C_68_14
BEGIN_
दृष्टवीर्यस्तु काकुत्स्थो जनकेन महात्मना |
संप्रदानं सुतायास्तु राघवे कर्तुमिच्छति || १-६८-१६_END
BEGIN_
On observing the valour of Kakutstha Rama, noble souled Janaka wishes to gift his 
daughter as bride to Raghava Rama... [1-68-16]_END

B_1_C_69_7
BEGIN_
उवाच वचनं श्रेष्ठो नरश्रेष्ठं मुदान्वितम् |
स्वागतं ते नरश्रेष्ठः दिष्ट्या प्राप्तोऽसि राघव || १-६९-९
पुत्रयोरुभयोः प्रीतिं लप्स्यसे वीर्यनिर्जिताम् |_END
BEGIN_
And the best one among men, king Janaka, gleefully said this commendable sentence 
to Dasharatha, the best legatee of Raghu, "oh, king, a hearty welcome to you. Oh, 
legatee of Raghu, your arrival to my city is just by my providence... you will now 
get delectation on seeing your sons who won accolades just by their valorousness 
in the act of raising and breaking Shiva's bow..." [1-69-9, 10a]_END

B_1_C_68_15
BEGIN_
यदि वो रोचते वृत्तं जनकस्य महात्मनः |
पुरीं गच्छामहे शीघ्रं मा भूत्कालस्य पर्ययः || १-६८-१७_END
BEGIN_
"If you all favour the tidings from the noble-souled Janaka as to what has happened 
in Mithila, we quickly proceed to that city, let not the time lapse..." Thus Dasharatha 
informed his counsel. [1-68-17]_END

B_1_C_69_8
BEGIN_
दिष्ट्या प्राप्तो महातेजा वसिष्ठो भगवानृषिः || १-६९-१०
सह सर्वैर्द्विजश्रेष्ठैर्देवैरिव शतक्रतुः |_END
BEGIN_
Providentially bechanced is the arrival of this great-resplendent and godly sage 
Vashishta, who arrived here with all of these eminent Brahmans, like Indra himself 
with all gods... [1-69-10b, 11a]_END

B_1_C_68_16
BEGIN_
मंत्रिणो बाढमित्याहुः सह सर्वैर्महर्षिभिः |
सुप्रीतश्चाब्रवीद्राजा श्वो यात्रेति च मंत्रिणः || १-६८-१८_END
BEGIN_
The ministers along with all of the great sages said in consonance, "Most Welcome..." 
and then that highly pleased king Dasharatha said to the ministers, "we travel tomorrow..." 
[1-68-18]_END

B_1_C_69_9
BEGIN_
दिष्ट्या मे निर्जिता विघ्ना दिष्ट्या मे पूजितं कुलम् || १-६९-११
राघवैः सह संबंधाद्वीर्यश्रेष्ठैर्महात्मभिः |_END
BEGIN_
Providentially my hindrances are overcome by the arrival of godlike sages, and 
providentially my lineage too is gloried owing to this hymeneal engagement with 
noble-souled Raghava-s, who are the most valorous among all the valorous people... 
[1-69-11b, 12a]_END

B_1_C_68_17
BEGIN_
मंत्रिणस्तु नरेन्द्रस्य रात्रिं परमसत्कृताः |
ऊषुः प्रमुदिताः सर्वे गुणैः सर्वैः समन्विताः || १-६८-१९_END
BEGIN_
The ministers of king Janaka who are gifted with all talents are given grateful 
hospitality by Dasharatha, and they all dwelt that night in Ayodhya, overjoyed at 
the successful completion of their august legatine, called 
sIta kalyANam...  [1-68-19]_END

B_1_C_69_10
BEGIN_
श्वः प्रभाते नरेन्द्र त्वम् सम्वर्तयितुमर्हसि || १-६९-१२
यज्ञस्यान्ते नरश्रेष्ठ विवाहमृषिसत्तमैः |_END
BEGIN_
Because you are born in first and foremost Ikshvaku dynasty, hence you are the 
Indra of Indra-like kings on earth... and hence, it will be apt of you to initiate 
the celebrations of marriage tomorrow, and the marriage itself after the culmination 
of the Vedic-ritual in three or four days, and the date and time for the marriage, 
that which is agreeable to the best sages can be decided, and you can get it performed 
on that date, through those great sages... [1-69-12b, 13a]_END

B_1_C_70_0
BEGIN_
ततः प्रभाते जनकः कृतकर्मा महर्षिभिः |
उवाच वाक्यं वाक्यज्ञः शतानंदं पुरोहितम् || १-७०-१_END
BEGIN_
Then on the next day morning after getting the ritual liturgies performed through sages, he that articulator Janaka articulated 
this to sage Shataananda, the royal priest. [1-70-1]_END

B_1_C_69_11
BEGIN_
तस्य तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा ऋषिमध्ये नराधिपः || १-६९-१३
वाक्यं वाक्यविदां श्रेष्ठः प्रत्युवाच महीपतिम् |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that sentence of king Janaka the sententious king Dasharatha replied 
the king Janaka from amongst the sages. [1-69-13b, 14a]_END

B_1_C_70_1
BEGIN_
भ्राता मम महातेजा यवीयानतिधार्मिकः |
कुशध्वज इति ख्यातः पुरीमध्यवसच्छुभाम् || १-७०-२
वार्या फलकपर्यन्तां पिबन्निक्षुमतीं नदीम् |
सांकाश्यां पुण्यसंकाशां विमानमिव पुष्पकम् || १-७०-३_END
BEGIN_
My younger brother renowned thus as Kushadhvaja, a highly self-righteous one and a highly brilliant one is ruling from 
the auspicious and holy city named Saankaasya, which city is surrounded by River Ikshumati as a natural moat, in which moat 
bastions of tridents are staked all around... and my brother presides over that city as if he is sitting in the Pushpaka 
aircraft of richly-rich god Kubera, and as though supping the sugarcane juice-like waters of River Ikshumati... [1-70-2, 
3]_END

B_1_C_70_2
BEGIN_
तमहं द्रष्टुमिच्छामि यज्ञगोप्ता स मे मतः |
प्रीतिं सोऽपि महातेजा इमां भोक्ता मया सह || १-७०-४_END
BEGIN_
"And I wish to see him, as he is the nominated benefactor of this Vedic-ritual of mine, and he too shall become a rejoicer 
in partaking the joyousness of this marriage... " So said Janaka to Shataananda. [1-70-4]_END

B_1_C_69_12
BEGIN_
प्रतिग्रहो दातृवशः श्रुतमेतन्मया पुरा || १-६९-१४
यथा वक्ष्यसि धर्मज्ञ तत् करिष्यामहे वयम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Recipiency rests with the restitutor..." so I have heard earlier. Hence, whatever 
you say, for you are the knower of probity and nothing goes amiss in your astute 
thinking, that we will do... [1-69-14b, 15a]_END

B_1_C_70_3
BEGIN_
एवमुक्ते तु वचने शतानंदस्य संनिधौ |
आगताः केचिदव्यग्रा जनकस्तान् समादिशत् || १-७०-५_END
BEGIN_
That way when Janaka asseverated that enunciation in the presence of Shataananda, Shataananda in turn ordered and summoned 
envoys, and then some alacritous envoys have come, whom Janaka ordered to proceed to his brother. [1-70-5]_END

B_1_C_69_13
BEGIN_
तद्धर्मिष्ठं यशस्यं च वचनं सत्यवादिनः || १-६९-१५
श्रुत्वा विदेहाधिपतिः परं विस्मयमागतः |_END
BEGIN_
On listening that sentence of that affirmer of principles, namely Dasharatha, that 
which is conformable to the principles of marriages and familial glory, a thrill 
of joy came over the king of Videha. [1-69-15b. 16a]_END

B_1_C_69_14
BEGIN_
ततः सर्वे मुनिगणाः परस्परसमागमे || १-६९-१६
हर्षेण महता युक्तास्तां निशामवसन् सुखम् |_END
BEGIN_
Then, on the foregathering of sages from Vashishta's side with the sages of Mithila 
all the sages have attained extreme joy and they spent that night happily. [1-69-16b, 
17a]_END

B_1_C_70_4
BEGIN_
शासनात्तु नरेन्द्रस्य प्रययुः शीघ्रवाजिभिः |
समानेतुं नरव्याघ्रं विष्णुमिन्द्राज्ञया यथा || १-७०-६_END
BEGIN_
By the order of the king those envoys who have speedy horses have travelled on to city Saankaasya speedily, to lead forth 
that tigerly man Kushadhvaja that speedily, which is as good as fetching Vishnu by order of Indra. [1-70-6]_END

B_1_C_69_15
BEGIN_
अथ रामो महातेजा लक्ष्मणेन समं ययौ || १-६९-१७
विश्वामित्रं पुरस्कृत्य पितुः पादावुपस्पृशन् |_END
BEGIN_
Then that most brilliant Rama, keeping Vishvamitra ahead, and strutting in step 
with Lakshmana, strutted to touch the feet of his father Dasharatha. [1-69-17]_END

B_1_C_70_5
BEGIN_
सांकाश्यां ते समागम्य ददृशुश्च कुशध्वजम् |
न्यवेदयन् यथावृत्तं जनकस्य च चिन्तितम् || १-७०-७_END
BEGIN_
On arriving in city Saankaasya those envoys have seen king Kushadhvaja and on submitting what has happened to the king about 
Rama's breaking of Shiva's bow, and they have also submitted the point of view of Janaka regarding marriages of four daughters. 
[1-70-7]_END

B_1_C_69_16
BEGIN_
राजा च राघवौ पुत्रौ निशाम्य परिहर्षितः || १-६९-१८
उवास परमप्रीतो जनकेन सुपूजितः |_END
BEGIN_
On seeing his two sons, the super medallists in Raghu's dynasty, King Dasharatha 
is highly rejoiced and he resided in Mithila with a high contentment, for the reverence 
of Janaka is that high. [1-69-18]_END

B_1_C_70_6
BEGIN_
तद्वृत्तं नृपतिः श्रुत्वा दूतश्रेष्ठैर्महाजवैः |
आज्ञया तु नरेन्द्रस्य आजगाम कुशध्वजः || १-७०-८_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that event from the worthy envoys whose speed is praiseworthy, king Kushadhvaja came right away to Mithila by 
the order of king Janaka. [1-70-8]_END

B_1_C_69_17
BEGIN_
जनकोऽपि महातेजाः क्रियां धर्मेण तत्त्ववित् |
यज्ञस्य च सुताभ्यां च कृत्वा रात्रिमुवास ह || १-६९-१९_END
BEGIN_
Even the great-resplendent Janaka on performing ritual acts according to scriptures 
for the Vedic-ritual on hand, and the preparatory rituals for handing out both of 
his daughters in marriage, went into the sleep of the just, with his palm on his 
chest. [1-69-19]_END

B_1_C_70_7
BEGIN_
स ददर्श महात्मानं जनकं धर्मवत्सलम् |
सोऽभिवाद्य शतानंदं जनकं चातिधार्मिकम् || १-७०-९
राजार्हं परमं दिव्यमासनं चाध्यरोहत |_END
BEGIN_
Kushadhvaja addressed himself to the insightful one and a compassionate person in the duty of an elder brother, namely Janaka, 
and on reverencing sage Shataananda firstly, next he has reverenced his fondly affectionate brother Janaka, and then he 
sat upon a majestic seat, that which is befitting to kings. [1-70-9, 10a]_END

B_1_C_70_8
BEGIN_
उपविष्टावुभौ तौ तु भ्रातरावमितौजसौ || १-७०-१०
प्रेषयामासतुर्वीरौ मन्त्रिश्रेष्ठं सुदामनम् |_END
BEGIN_
Both the brothers of unlimited self-refulgence having assumed their high seats, they who are distinguished for their righteous 
acts have started to send Sudaamana, the distinguished minister. [1-70-10b, 11a]_END

B_1_C_71_0
BEGIN_
एवं ब्रुवाणं जनकः प्रत्युवाच कृतांजलिः |
श्रोतुमर्हसि भद्रं ते कुलं नः परिकीर्तितम् || १-७१-१_END
BEGIN_
When sage Vashishta said that way, Janaka reverentially made palm fold and said this in reply, "oh, sage, let safeness betide 
you all... now, it will be apt of you all to listen to our distinguished lineage..." [1-71-1]_END

B_1_C_70_9
BEGIN_
गच्छ मंत्रिपते शीघ्रमैक्ष्वाकममितप्रभम् || १-७०-११
आत्मजैः सह दुर्धर्षमानयस्व समंत्रिणम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, minister plenipotentiary, Sudaamana, you please proceed immediately to king Dasharatha, the legatee of Ikshvaku-s with 
illimitable resplendence, and let that invincible king Dasharatha be led hither along with his sons and along with his Vedic-celebrants..." 
Thus Janaka ordered Sudaamana, the minister. [1-70-11b, 12a]_END

B_1_C_71_1
BEGIN_
प्रदाने हि मुनिश्रेष्ठ कुलं निरवशेषतः |
वक्तव्यं कुलजातेन तन्निबोध महामुने || १-७१-२_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, eminent sage Vashishta, he who is born in a particular noble gens has to inform about his parentage in its entirety, 
especially when he offers a bride... thereby oh, great sage, let all be informed of about our lineage..." [1-71-2]_END

B_1_C_70_10
BEGIN_
औपकार्यां स गत्वा तु रघूणां कुलवर्धनम् || १-७०-१२
ददर्श शिरसा चैनमभिवाद्येदमब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
Accordingly Sudaamana has gone to the visitatorial-palace of the promoter of Raghu's heritage, namely Dasharatha, and he 
said this on appearing before that king duly bowing down and hailing the king. [1-70-12b, 13a]_END

B_1_C_71_2
BEGIN_
राजाभूत् त्रिषु लोकेषु विश्रुतः स्वेन कर्मणा |
निमिः परमधर्मात्मा सर्वसत्त्ववतां वरः || १-७१-३_END
BEGIN_
Once there was an emperor Nimi, who was renowned in the triad of worlds by his own accomplishments, and who was uniquely 
seraphic-souled and a best one among all stalwart emperors... [1-71-3]_END

B_1_C_70_11
BEGIN_
अयोध्याधिपते वीर वैदेहो मिथिलाधिपः || १-७०-१३
स त्वां द्रष्टुं व्यवसितः सोपाध्यायपुरोहितम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, valiant king, oh, sovereign of Ayodhya, his highness the sovereign of Mithila from the heritage of Videha kings is 
poised for seeking an audience with your highness, along with your highness' royal-priest Vashishta and other mentors..." 
The minister Sudaamana said so to Dasharatha. [1-70-13b, 14a]_END

B_1_C_71_3
BEGIN_
तस्य पुत्रो मिथिर्नाम जनको मिथिपुत्रकः |
प्रथमो जनको नाम जनकादप्युदावसुः || १-७१-४_END
BEGIN_
And his son was named as Mithi, and Janaka was Mithi's son... the first one to be designated as Janaka... and even from 
that Janaka it is Udaavasu who took birth... [1-71-4]_END

B_1_C_70_12
BEGIN_
मंत्रिश्रेष्ठवचः श्रुत्वा राजा सर्षिगणस्तदा || १-७०-१४
सबन्धुरगमत्तत्र जनको यत्र वर्तते |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that best minister's words, then king Dasharatha came to the place where Janaka is available, along with his 
kinsmen and the assemblages of sages. [1-70-14b, 15a]_END

B_1_C_71_4
BEGIN_
उदावसोस्तु धर्मात्मा जातो वै नन्दिवर्धनः |
नन्दिवर्धनपुत्रस्तु सुकेतुर्नाम नामतः || १-७१-५_END
BEGIN_
From Udaavasu it is noble souled Nandivardhana took birth, and Nandivardhana's son is named as Suketu, by his name... [1-71-5]_END

B_1_C_70_13
BEGIN_
राजा च मंत्रिसहितः सोपाध्यायः सबांधवः || १-७०-१५
वाक्यं वाक्यविदां श्रेष्ठो वैदेहमिदमब्रवीत् |_END
BEGIN_
That sententious king Dasharatha said this to the king from the lineage of Videha kings, Janaka, who is with his mentors, 
kinsfolk, and ministers. [1-70-15b, 16a]_END

B_1_C_71_5
BEGIN_
सुकेतोरपि धर्मात्मा देवरातो महाबलः |
देवरातस्य राजर्षेर्बृहद्रथ इति स्मृतः || १-७१-६_END
BEGIN_
From Suketu the highly powerful and virtue-souled Devaraata is born, and from that kingly sage Devaraata, it is Brihadratha 
who took birth, thus we have heard... [1-71-6]_END

B_1_C_70_14
BEGIN_
विदितं ते महाराज इक्ष्वाकुकुलदैवतम् || १-७०-१६
वक्ता सर्वेषु कृत्येषु वसिष्ठो भगवानृषिः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, exalted king Janaka, you already appreciate that this godly sage Vashishta is godlike to the bloodline of Ikshvaku-s, 
and in all affairs he is our internuncio... [1-70-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_71_6
BEGIN_
बृहद्रथस्य शूरोऽभून्महावीरः प्रतापवान् |
महावीरस्य धृतिमान् सुधृतिः सत्यविक्रमः || १-७१-७_END
BEGIN_
From Brihadratha it is the highly braving, courageous and valiant Mahaaviira has come, and the bold and truth-valiant Sudhriti 
from Mahaaviira... [1-71-7]_END

B_1_C_70_15
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्राभ्यनुज्ञातः सह सर्वैर्महर्षिभिः || १-७०-१७
एष वक्ष्यति धर्मात्मा वसिष्ठो मे यथाक्रमम् |
तूष्णींभूते दशरथे वसिष्ठो भगवानृषिः || १-७०-१८
उवाच वाक्यं वाक्यज्ञो वैदेहं सपुरोधसाम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Should an assent be given by Sage Vishvamitra, along with all the great sages present here, this equanimous Vashishta will 
narrate about my bloodline, lineally..." And, to the nod of Vishvamitra Dasharatha become reticent, and then the godly and 
sententious sage Vashishta who is along with his men of the cloth said these sentences to the king of Videha, namely Janaka. 
[1-70-17b, 18, 19a]_END

B_1_C_71_7
BEGIN_
सुधृतेरपि धर्मात्मा धृष्टकेतुः सुधार्मिकः |
धृष्टकेतोश्च राजर्षेर्हर्यश्व इति विश्रुतः || १-७१-८_END
BEGIN_
Form Sudhriti, the right-minded and highly generous Dhristaketu took birth, and from the kingly sage Dhristaketu it is 
highly renowned Haryashva is the son... [1-71-8]_END

B_1_C_70_16
BEGIN_
अव्यक्तप्रभवो ब्रह्मा शाश्वतो नित्य अव्ययः || १-७०-१९
तस्मान्मरीचिः संजज्ञे मरीचेः कश्यपः सुतः |
विवस्वान् कश्यपाज्जज्ञे मनुर्वैवस्वतः स्मृतः || १-७०-२०_END
BEGIN_
The Unprovable emanated the timeless, changeless and perishless Brahma, and from that Being, namely Brahma, Mariichi is 
begotten, and Kaashyapa is the son of Mariichi, and the Sun is begotten from Kaashyapa, and Manu is said to be the son of 
the Sun... [1-70-19b, 20]_END

B_1_C_71_8
BEGIN_
हर्यश्वस्य मरुः पुत्रो मरोः पुत्रः प्रतीन्धकः |
प्रतीन्धकस्य धर्मात्मा राजा कीर्तिरथः सुतः || १-७१-९_END
BEGIN_
Haryashva's son is Maru, and Maru's, son is Pratiindhaka, and the son of Pratiindhaka's is noble-souled king Kiirtiratha... 
[1-71-9]_END

B_1_C_70_17
BEGIN_
मनुः प्रजापतिः पूर्वमिक्ष्वाकुश्च मनोः सुतः |
तमिक्ष्वाकुमयोध्यायां राजानं विद्धि पूर्वकम् || १-७०-२१_END
BEGIN_
Manu is the earliest Prajaapati and Ikshvaaku is the son of Manu, and that Ikshvaaku is the first king of Ayodhya... know 
thus... [1-70-21]_END

B_1_C_71_9
BEGIN_
पुत्रः कीर्तिरथस्यापि देवमीढ इति स्मृतः |
देवमीढस्य विबुधो विबुधस्य महीध्रकः || १-७१-१०_END
BEGIN_
The son of Kiirtiratha is remembered as Devamiidha, and the son of Devamiidha is Vibudha, and Vibudha's son is Mahiidraka... 
[1-71-10]_END

B_1_C_70_18
BEGIN_
इक्ष्वाकोस्तु सुतः श्रीमान् कुक्षिरित्येव विश्रुतः |
कुक्षेरथात्मजः श्रीमान् विकुक्षिरुपपद्यत || १-७०-२२_END
BEGIN_
The son of Ikshvaaku is the legendary Kukshi, thus he is renowned, and the famous Vikukshi is the son of Kukshi... 
[1-70-22]_END

B_1_C_71_10
BEGIN_
महीध्रकसुतो राजा कीर्तिरातो महाबलः |
कीर्तिरातस्य राजर्षेर्महारोमा व्यजायत || १-७१-११_END
BEGIN_
Mahiidraka's son is the great mighty king Kiirtiraata, and the son born to sagely king Kiirtiraata is Mahaaroma... [1-71-11]_END

B_1_C_70_19
BEGIN_
विकुक्षेस्तु महातेजा बाणः पुत्रः प्रतापवान् |
बाणस्य तु महातेजा अनरण्यः प्रतापवान् || १-७०-२३_END
BEGIN_
From that most brilliant and courageous Vikukshi, Baana emerged as son, and the highly refulgent and valinat Anaranya is 
the son of Baana... [1-70-23]_END

B_1_C_71_11
BEGIN_
महारोम्णस्तु धर्मात्मा स्वर्णरोमा व्यजायत |
स्वर्णरोम्णस्तु राजर्षेर्ह्रस्वरोमा व्यजायत || १-७१-१२_END
BEGIN_
From Mahaaroma it is the virtue-souled Swarnaroma, and from kingly sage Swarnaroma it is Hrasvaroma... [1-71-12]_END

B_1_C_70_20
BEGIN_
अनरण्यात्पृथुर्जज्ञे त्रिशंकुस्तु पृथोः सुतः |
त्रिशंकोरभवत्पुत्रो धुन्धुमारो महायशाः || १-७०-२४_END
BEGIN_
Pruthu is the son of Anaranya, and Trishanku is Pruthu's son, and the highly renowned Dhundumaara happened to be the son 
of Trishanku... [1-70-24]_END

B_1_C_71_12
BEGIN_
तस्य पुत्रद्वयं जज्ञे धर्मज्ञस्य महात्मनः |
ज्येष्ठोऽहमनुजो भ्राता मम वीरः कुशध्वजः || १-७१-१३_END
BEGIN_
Two sons are born to that knower of virtue and noble souled Hrasvaroma, I am the elder, and my younger brother is this 
brave Kushadhvaja... [1-71-13]_END

B_1_C_70_21
BEGIN_
धुन्धुमारान्महातेजा युवनाश्वो महारथः |
युवनाश्वसुतस्त्वासीन्मान्धाता पृथिवीपतिः || १-७०-२५_END
BEGIN_
Dhundumaara begot a highly glorious and a speediest charioteer Yuvanaashva as son, and Mandhaata emerged as the son of 
Yuvanaashva... [1-70-25]_END

B_1_C_71_13
BEGIN_
मां तु ज्येष्ठं पिता राज्ये सोऽभिषिच्य नराधिपः |
कुशध्वजं समावेश्य भारं मयि वनं गतः|| १-७१-१४_END
BEGIN_
He that king and father of ours, Hrasvaroma, anointing me in kingdom as I am the elder, and vesting the duty of looking 
after Kushadhvaja in me, he departed to forests... [1-71-14]_END

B_1_C_70_22
BEGIN_
मान्धातुस्तु सुतः श्रीमान् सुसन्धिरुदपद्यत |
सुसंधेरपि पुत्रौ द्वौ ध्रुवसंधिः प्रसेनजित् || १-७०-२६_END
BEGIN_

Maandhaata engendered the highly noble Susandhi as son, and even Susandhi engendered two sons, namely Dhruvasandhi and 
Prasenajit... [1-70-26]_END

B_1_C_71_14
BEGIN_
वृद्धे पितरि स्वर्याते धर्मेण धुरमावहम् |
भ्रातरं देवसंकाशं स्नेहात् पश्यन् कुशध्वजम् || १-७१-१५_END
BEGIN_
On the departure of our aged father to heaven, I am looking after this godlike Kushadhvaja with brotherliness and lugging 
around the burden of this kingship... [1-71-15]_END

B_1_C_70_23
BEGIN_
यशस्वी ध्रुवसंधेस्तु भरतो नाम नामतः |
भरतात्तु महातेजा असितो नाम जायत || १-७०-२७_END
BEGIN_
From Dhruvasandhi, an illustrious one named as Bharata is begotten, and Bharata begot a highly effulgent son named as Asita... 
[1-70-27]_END

B_1_C_71_15
BEGIN_
कस्यचित्त्वथ कालस्य सांकाश्यादगमत्पुरात् |
सुधन्वा वीर्यवान् राजा मिथिलामवरोधकः || १-७१-१६_END
BEGIN_
Then after sometime, a valorous king named Sudhanva came beleaguering Mithila, from his city Saamkaasha... [1-71-16]_END

B_1_C_70_24
BEGIN_
यस्यैते प्रतिराजान उदपद्यन्त शात्रवः |
हैहयास्तालजंघाश्च शूराश्च शशबिंदवः || १-७०-२८_END
BEGIN_
To which Asita, kings like Haihaya-s, Taalajanghaa-s, and the valiant Shashabindu-s have become adversaries and kings in 
hostility, he had to wage war with them... [1-70-28]_END

B_1_C_71_16
BEGIN_
स च मे प्रेषयामास शैवं धनुरनुत्तमम् |
सीता कन्या च पद्माक्षी मह्यं वै दीयतामिति || १-७१-१७_END
BEGIN_
'The unexcelled bow of Shiva shall be given to me, along with the lotus-eyed virgin, Seetha...' thus he started to urge 
me... [1-71-17]_END

B_1_C_70_25
BEGIN_
तांस्तु स प्रतियुद्ध्यन् वै युद्धे राजा प्रवासितः |
हिमवन्तमुपागम्य भार्याभ्यां सहितस्तदा || १-७०-२९_END
BEGIN_
While counterattacking those kings, Asita is dethroned in war and then he reached Himalayas along with his two wives... 
[1-70-29]_END

B_1_C_71_17
BEGIN_
तस्याप्रदानाद्ब्रह्मर्षे युद्धमासीन्मया सह |
स हतोऽभिमुखो राजा सुधन्वा तु मया रणे || १-७१-१८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Brahma sage Vashishta, for the reason of my non-bestowal of bow or bride he warred with me, and when he affronted me 
in that war I have put that Sudhanva to the sword..." [1-71-18]_END

B_1_C_70_26
BEGIN_
असितोऽल्पबलो राजा कालधर्ममुपेयिवान् |
द्वे चास्य भार्ये गर्भिण्यौ बभूवतुरिति श्रुतम् || १-७०-३०
एका गर्भविनाशार्थं सपत्न्यै सगरं ददौ |_END
BEGIN_
Asita was with his meagre forces when he was in Himalayas, and there he drew nigh of his Time. At the time of his demise 
two of his wives were pregnant, and one of two wives gave toxic food to the co-wife for abortion... thus we heard... [1-70-30-31a]_END

B_1_C_71_18
BEGIN_
निहत्य तं मुनिश्रेष्ठ सुधन्वानं नराधिपम् |
सांकाश्ये भ्रातरं शूरमभ्यषिंचं कुशध्वजम् || १-७१-१९_END
BEGIN_
Oh, best sage Vashishta, on eliminating king Sudhanva, I have anointed my valiant brother Kushadhvaja in the kingdom of 
Saamkaasha... [1-71-19]_END

B_1_C_70_27
BEGIN_
ततः शैलवरे रम्ये बभूवाभिरतो मुनिः || १-७०-३१
भार्गवश्च्यवनो नाम हिमवंतमुपाश्रितः |_END
BEGIN_
There was a saint named Cyavana, the heir of Sage Bhrigu, who in fascination with best and beautiful mountains then taking 
shelter on Himalayas. [1-70-31b, 32a]_END

B_1_C_71_19
BEGIN_
कनीयानेष मे भ्राता अहं ज्येष्ठो महामुने |
ददामि परमप्रीतो वध्वौ ते मुनिपुंगव || १-७१-२०
सीतां रामाय भद्रं ते ऊर्मिलां लक्ष्मणाय वै |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, best saint Vashishta, this is that younger brother of mine, and I am the elder. Oh, eminent-saint, I am bestowing those 
brides with a highly gladdened heart... Seetha for Rama, and Urmila for Lakshmana, let there be felicity for all... [1-71-20, 
21a]_END

B_1_C_70_28
BEGIN_
तत्र चैका महाभागा भार्गवं देववर्चसम् || १-७०-३२
ववन्दे पद्मपत्राक्षी कांक्षन्ती सुतमुत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_
One of the two wives of Asita, the lotus-petal eyed and highly fortunate one queen came there desirous of a best son, and 
reverenced the sage who is godly in his glow... [1-70-32b-33a]_END

B_1_C_71_20
BEGIN_
वीर्यशुल्कां मम सुतां सीतां सुरसुतोपमाम् || १-७१-२१
द्वितीयामूर्मिलां चैव त्रिर्वदामि न संशयः |
ददामि परमप्रीतो वध्वौ ते मुनिपुंगव || १-७१-२२_END
BEGIN_
My daughter Seetha is the bounty for bravery and in simile she is the daughter of the divine Providence, and thus the second 
one Urmila too... oh, eminent-saint, with a highly gladdened heart I reiterate thrice while I bestow those brides, there 
is no doubt about it... [1-71-21b, 22a]_END

B_1_C_71_21
BEGIN_
रामलक्ष्मणयो राजन् गोदानं कारयस्व ह |
पितृकार्यं च भद्रं ते ततो वैवाहिकं कुरु || १-७१-२३_END
BEGIN_
Oh, king Dasharatha, let the preceding ritual of samaavartana, be undertaken, and let manes 
be propitiated by the ritual, naandi-shraadha, and afterwards you make happen the wedding celebrations 
... thus, all will be blest... [1-71-22b, 23]_END

B_1_C_70_29
BEGIN_
तमृषिं साभ्युपागम्य कालिन्दी चाभ्यवादयत् || १-७०-३३
स तामभ्यवदद्विप्रः पुत्रेप्सुं पुत्रजन्मनि |_END
BEGIN_
Another queen Kaalindi who administer food poison to her co-wife has also come to the sage, and she too reverenced him. 
That sage spoke to her who received poison from her co-wife regarding the birth of her son. [1-70-34]_END

B_1_C_71_22
BEGIN_
मघा ह्यद्य महाबाहो तृतीये दिवसे प्रभो |
फल्गुन्यामुत्तरे राजंस्तस्मिन् वैवाहिकं कुरु |
रामलक्ष्मणयोरर्थे दानं कार्यं सुखोदयम् || १-७१-२४_END
BEGIN_
Oh, great dextrous Dasharatha, the star ruling today is magha, isn't it... oh, lord, on the 
third from now, say day after tomorrow, when the star phaalguNi comes, in its later part, namely
uttara-phalugNi, you may make happen this wedding, and the bounties like
go-bhuu-tila-hiraNyaadi i.e., ' cows, lands, grains, gold etc., that ensue the wellbeing 
of Rama and Lakshmana, may be accorded to the eligible generously... [1-71-24]_END

B_1_C_70_30
BEGIN_
तव कुक्षौ महाभागे सुपुत्रः सुमहाबलः || १-७०-३४
महावीर्यो महातेजा अचिरात् संजनिष्यति |
गरेण सहितः श्रीमान् मा शुचः कमलेक्षणे || १-७०-३५_END
BEGIN_
'Oh, highly fortunate lady, a very good son and a very mighty son is there in your womb. Soon you will give birth to a 
highly vigorous, highly refulgent son and that illustrious one will take birth with toxicity, but there is no need to worry...' 
So said Sage Cyavana to the queen of Asita who received the poison. [1-70-35]_END

B_1_C_70_31
BEGIN_
च्यवनं च नमस्कृत्य राजपुत्री पतिव्रता |
पत्या विरहिता तस्मात् पुत्रं देवी व्यजायत || १-७०-३६_END
BEGIN_
On reverencing Sage Cyavana that husband devout princess whose husband is no more that lady gave birth to a son... [1-70-36]_END

B_1_C_70_32
BEGIN_
सपत्न्या तु गरस्तस्यै दत्तो गर्भजिघांसया |
सह तेन गरेणैव संजातः सगरोऽभवत् || १-७०-३७_END
BEGIN_
"Because he took birth along with the poison administered to his mother by her co-wife, he became Sagara, the emperor..." 
[1-70-37]_END

B_1_C_70_33
BEGIN_
सगरस्यासमंजस्तु असमंजादथांशुमान् |
दिलीपोंऽशुमतः पुत्रो दिलीपस्य भगीरथः || १-७०-३८_END
BEGIN_
From Sagara it is Asamanja and from Asamanja it is Amshuman, and from Amshuman it is Diliipa, and the son of Diliipa is 
Bhageeratha... [1-70-38]_END

B_1_C_70_34
BEGIN_
भगीरथात्ककुत्स्थश्च ककुत्स्थस्य रघुस्तथा |
रघोस्तु पुत्रस्तेजस्वी प्रवृद्धः पुरुषादकः || १-७०-३९
कल्माषपादो ह्यभवत्तस्माज्जातस्तु शङ्खणः |_END
BEGIN_
From Bhageeratha it is Kakutstha, from Kakutstha it is Raghu, and Raghu's son is the great resplendent Pravriddha, who 
is reduced to a human flesh eater, and he is also known as Kalmaashapaada... and from him, that Pravriddha, Shankana is born... 
[1-70-39, 40a]_END

B_1_C_70_35
BEGIN_
सुदर्शनः शंखणस्य अग्निवर्णः सुदर्शनात् || १-७०-४०
शीघ्रगस्त्वग्निवर्णस्य शीघ्रगस्य मरुः सुतः |
मरोः प्रशुश्रुकस्त्वासीदंबरीषः प्रशुश्रुकात् || १-७०-४१_END
BEGIN_
Shankana's son is Sudarshana, and from Sudarshana it is Agnivarsna... And Shiigraga is the son of Agnivarsna, and Shiighraga's 
son is Maru and from Maru it is Prashushruka, and Ambariisha is the son of Prashushruka... [1-70-41]_END

B_1_C_70_36
BEGIN_
अंबरीषस्य पुत्रोऽभून्नहुषश्च महीपतिः |
नहुषस्य ययातिस्तु नाभागस्तु ययातिजः || १-७०-४२_END
BEGIN_
Ambariisha's son was Nahusha, the emperor and Yayaati is the son of Nahusha, but Naabhaaga is born to Yayaati... [1-70-42]_END

B_1_C_70_37
BEGIN_
नाभागस्य बभूवाजः अजाद्दशरथोऽभवत् |
अस्माद्दशरथाज्जातौ भ्रातरौ रामलक्ष्मणौ || १-७०-४३_END
BEGIN_
Aja was Naabhaaga's son and from Aja, this Dasharatha is manifest, and from him, from this Dasharatha, these brothers, 
Rama and Lakshmana are born... [1-70-43]_END

B_1_C_70_38
BEGIN_
आदिवंशविशुद्धानां राज्ञां परमधर्मिणाम् |
इक्ष्वाकुकुलजातानां वीराणां सत्यवादिनाम् || १-७०-४४
रामलक्ष्मणयोरर्थे त्वत्सुते वरये नृप |
सदृशाभ्यां नरश्रेष्ठ सदृशे दातुमर्हसि || १-७०-४५_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best one among men, Janaka, from the beginning this bloodline of Ikshvaaku-s is spotlessly immaculate, immensely impeccable, 
indomitable, and irreproachable, and in respect of these kings born in this line of blood, oh, king Janaka, I espouse that 
it will be meetly of you to offer your seemly daughters to this seemly pair of Rama and Lakshmana..." So said Vashishta
