to king Janaka. [1-70-44, 45]_END

B_1_C_72_0
BEGIN_
तमुक्तवंतं वैदेहं विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः |
उवाच वचनं वीरं वसिष्ठसहितो नृपम् || १-७२-१_END
BEGIN_
Then the eminent-saint Vishvamitra together with Vashishta said these words to Janaka, the valiant king of Videha, who has 
just said about his lineage. [1-72-1]_END

B_1_C_72_1
BEGIN_
अचिंत्यान्यप्रमेयाणि कुलानि नरपुंगव |
इक्ष्वाकूणां विदेहानां नैषां तुल्योऽस्ति कश्चन || १-७२-२_END
BEGIN_
The Ikshvaku-s and Videha-s are unimaginably admirable and immeasurably distinguished dynasties, oh, Janaka, the best one 
among all men, there is no single king comparable to one from these dynasties... [1-72-2]_END

B_1_C_72_2
BEGIN_
सदृशो धर्मसंबन्धः सदृशो रूपसंपदा |
रामलक्ष्मणयो राजन् सीता चोर्मिलया सह || १-७२-३_END
BEGIN_
Oh, king Janaka, these espousals of Seetha with Rama and Urmila with Lakshmana is behovely to each other's dynastical prestige 
and even it is befitting to the winsome charms of the brides and bridegrooms, but that being so... [1-72-3]_END

B_1_C_72_3
BEGIN_
वक्तव्यं च नरश्रेष्ठ श्रूयतां वचनं मम |
भ्राता यवीयान् धर्मज्ञ एष राजा कुशध्वजः || १-७२-४_END
BEGIN_
Oh, grand sire, you may listen to my words of advise... this younger brother of yours, king Kushadhvaja, is at home in 
every kind of probity... [1-72-4]_END

B_1_C_72_4
BEGIN_
अस्य धर्मात्मनो राजन् रूपेणाप्रतिमं भुवि |
सुताद्वयं नरश्रेष्ठ पत्न्यर्थं वरयामहे || १-७२-५_END
BEGIN_
Oh, king, the pair of daughters of this right-minded Kushadhvaja is nonpareil in comeliness in this world, hence, oh, grand 
sire, we choose to pair them off with Bharata and Shatrughna... [1-72-5]_END

B_1_C_72_5
BEGIN_
भरतस्य कुमारस्य शत्रुघ्नस्य च धीमतः |
वरयेम सुते राजंस्तयोरर्थे महात्मनोः || १-७२-६_END
BEGIN_
Oh, king, for the sake of those two honourable boys, for that young man Bharata and for that smart man Shatrughna, we opt 
your brother's daughters... [1-72-6]_END

B_1_C_72_6
BEGIN_
पुत्रा दशरथस्येमे रूपयौवनशालिनः |
लोकपालसमाः सर्वे देवतुल्यपराक्रमाः || १-७२-७_END
BEGIN_
All these four sons of Dasharatha have handsomeness and youthfulness, and they are equal to the four rulers of the world 
from four quarters, and their valour vies with the valour of God Vishnu... [1-72-7]_END

B_1_C_72_7
BEGIN_
उभयोरपि राजेन्द्र संबन्धेनानुबध्यताम् |
इक्ष्वाकोः कुलमव्यग्रं भवतः पुण्यकर्मणः || १-७२-८_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, best king, let both these dynasties of yours, the impeccable dynasty of Ikshvaku-s and the immaculate dynasty of yours 
as well, be interlocked by these wedlock-s..." Thus Vishvamitra advised Janaka. [1-72-8]_END

B_1_C_72_8
BEGIN_
विश्वामित्रवचः श्रुत्वा वसिष्ठस्य मते तदा |
जनकः प्रांजलिर्वाक्यमुवाच मुनिपुंगवौ || १-७२-९_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Vishvamitra that have the concurrence of Vashishta then Janaka reverently said this to those two 
eminent-saints. [1-72-9]_END

B_1_C_72_9
BEGIN_
कुलं धन्यमिदं मन्ये येषां तौ मुनिपुंगवौ |
सदृशं कुलसंबन्धं यदाज्ञापयथः स्वयम् || १-७२-१०_END
BEGIN_
By which reason you two eminent-saints personally bid fair to this befitting proposal, thereby I opine that my dynasty 
is highly honoured... [1-72-10]_END

B_1_C_72_10
BEGIN_
एवं भवतु भद्रं वः कुशध्वजसुते इमे |
पत्न्यौ भजेतां सहितौ शत्रुघ्नभरतावुभौ || १-७२-११_END
BEGIN_
So be it! Safe betides you all! Let the pair of Kushdhvaja's daughters, namely Maandavi, Shrutakiirti, devout themselves 
as a pair of wives to the paired brothers, namely Bharata and Shatrughna, respectively... [1-72-11]_END

B_1_C_72_11
BEGIN_
एकाह्ना राजपुत्रीणां चतसॄणां महामुने |
पाणीन् गृह्णन्तु चत्वारो राजपुत्रा महाबलाः || १-७२-१२_END
BEGIN_
Oh, eminent-saint Vishvamitra, let the palms of four princesses be taken in the palms of these four mettlesome princes 
in marriage, in the light of one day... [1-72-12]_END

B_1_C_72_12
BEGIN_
उत्तरे दिवसे ब्रह्मन् फल्गुनीभ्यां मनीषिणः |
वैवाहिकं प्रशंसन्ति भगो यत्र प्रजापतिः || १-७२-१३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Brahman, the savants acclaim that part of the day as the best for wedding ceremonies when both of the pre-Phalguni 
and post-Phalguni stars are available, and on such a time where post-Phalguni is ruling, for which Bhaga is the presiding 
deity for progeny..." So said Janaka to the marriage party. [1-72-13]_END

B_1_C_72_13
BEGIN_
एवमुक्त्वा वचः सौम्यं प्रत्युत्थाय कृतांजलिः |
उभौ मुनिवरौ राजा जनको वाक्यमब्रवीत् || १-७२-१४_END
BEGIN_
On saying those gracious words thus, king Janaka got up from his throne and coming nigh of both of the eminent-saints, Vishvamitra 
and Vashishta, reverently said this sentence. [1-72-14]_END

B_1_C_72_14
BEGIN_
परो धर्मः कृतो मह्यं शिष्योऽस्मि भवतोः सदा |
इमान्यासनमुख्यानि आस्यतां मुनिपुंगवौ || १-७२-१५_END
BEGIN_
You two, oh, eminent-saints, have done an excellent generous act in my respect, thus I will ever remain your proselyte... 
you may please preside over these thrones, that of mine, my brother's, and that of Dasharatha... [1-72-15]_END

B_1_C_72_15
BEGIN_
यथा दशरथस्येयं तथाऽयोध्या पुरी मम |
प्रभुत्वे नास्ति सन्देहो यथार्हं कर्तुमर्हथ || १-७२-१६_END
BEGIN_
"As to how this city Mithila appertains to Dasharatha, in the same way city of Ayodhya is mine... and there shall be no 
hesitancy for you two sages in governance on these three kingdoms, thus it will be apt of you to make the marriages happen 
as aptly as you can..." So said Janaka to the sages. [1-72-16]_END

B_1_C_72_16
BEGIN_
तथा ब्रुवति वैदेहे जनके रघुनंदनः |
राजा दशरथो हृष्टः प्रत्युवाच महीपतिम् || १-७२-१७_END
BEGIN_
The legatee of Raghu-s king Dasharatha is gladdened while the legatee of Videha is talking in such a hobnobbing way, and 
he replied king Janaka in this way. [1-72-17]_END

B_1_C_72_17
BEGIN_
युवामसंख्येयगुणौ भ्रातरौ मिथिलेश्वरौ |
ऋषयो राजसंघाश्च भवद्भ्यामभिपूजिताः || १-७२-१८_END
BEGIN_
Oh, kings of Mithila, Janaka and Kushadhvaja, you two brothers have reverenced inestimable sages and coteries of kings, 
as such inestimable good manners are treasured in both of you... [1-72-18]_END

B_1_C_72_18
BEGIN_
स्वस्ति प्राप्नुहि भद्रं ते गमिष्यामः स्वमालयम् |
श्राद्धकर्माणि विधिवत् विधास्येति चाब्रवीत् || १-७२-१९_END
BEGIN_
"Enjoy that blessedness! Let safe betide you! We now depart to our visitatorial-palace, and we shall customarily carry out 
the tributary rituals..." Dasharatha said thus. [1-72-19]_END

B_1_C_72_19
BEGIN_
तमापृष्ट्वा नरपतिं राजा दशरथस्तदा |
मुनीन्द्रौ तौ पुरस्कृत्य जगामाशु महायशाः || १-७२-२०_END
BEGIN_
On seeking leave of absence from the sovereign of people, Janaka, that highly renowned king Dasharatha promptly departed 
from there, keeping both of the eminent-saints afore, namely Vishvamitra and Vashishta. [1-72-20]_END

B_1_C_72_20
BEGIN_
स गत्वा निलयं राजा श्राद्धं कृत्वा विधानतः |
प्रभाते काल्यमुत्थाय चक्रे गोदानमुत्तमम् || १-७२-२१_END
BEGIN_
King Dasharatha on going to his visitatorial-palace has procedurally undertaken the tributary rituals, and on getting up 
in the next morning, he carried out the initiatory rituals of marriages, in a grand way, in which donation of cows is a 
part. [1-72-21]_END

B_1_C_72_21
BEGIN_
गवां शतसहस्रं च ब्राह्मणेभ्यो नराधिपः |
एकैकशो ददौ राजा पुत्रानुद्दिश्य धर्मतः || १-७२-२२_END
BEGIN_
That lord of people king Dasharatha has righteously donated hundred thousand cows to Brahman-s, in the name of each of his 
four sons. [1-72-22]_END

B_1_C_72_22
BEGIN_
सुवर्णशृंगाः संपन्नाः सवत्साः कांस्यदोहनाः |
गवां शतसहस्राणि चत्वारि पुरुषर्षभः || १-७२-२३
वित्तमन्यच्च सुबहु द्विजेभ्यो रघुनंदनः |
ददौ गोदानमुद्दिश्य पुत्रा पुत्रवत्सलः || १-७२-२४_END
BEGIN_
In that cow donation ceremony intended for his sons, he that best one among men and the one who is affectionate towards 
his sons, Dasharatha, the legatee of Raghu-s, has donated on behalf of each of his sons, four hundred thousand cows, that 
are abundant milkers, and that have golden casings on their horns, and that are with their calves, and along with milking 
jugs made with bell metal, and he even donated very many other kinds of assets to Brahmans. [1-72-23, 24]_END

B_1_C_72_23
BEGIN_
सु सुतैः कृतगोदानैर्वृतः सः नृपतिस्तदा |
लोकपालैरिवाभाति वृतः सौम्यः प्रजापतिः || १-७२-२५_END
BEGIN_
On performing the cow donations and samaavartana, snaataka, the initiatory ceremonies of his 
sons, as well, he that serene king Dasharatha who is amidst the quartet of his sons, shone forth like serene Brahma, who 
is quartet-faced, with the quartet of Veda-s, and who is the overlord of mankind, amidst the quartet of presiding deities 
in the quartet of the world. [1-72-25]_END

B_1_C_73_0
BEGIN_
यस्मिंस्तु दिवसे राजा चक्रे गोदानमुत्तमम् |
तस्मिंस्तु दिवसे शूरो युधाजित् समुपेयिवान् || १-७३-१_END
BEGIN_
On which day the king Dasharatha made the impressive cow donations or, initiatory rites, on that day alone the valiant Yudhaajit 
turned up. [1-73-1]_END

B_1_C_73_1
BEGIN_
पुत्रः केकयराजस्य साक्षाद्भरतमातुलः |
दृष्ट्वा पृष्ट्वा च कुशलं राजानमिदमब्रवीत् || १-७३-२_END
BEGIN_
Yudhaajit, the son of Kekaya king and the brother of Kaikeyi, thus the direct maternal uncle of Bharata, having seen and 
asked after the wellbeing of Dasharatha said this to him. [1-73-2]_END

B_1_C_73_2
BEGIN_
केकयाधिपती राजा स्नेहात् कुशलमब्रवीत् |
येषां कुशलकामोऽसि तेषां संप्रत्यनामयम् || १-७३-३_END
BEGIN_
The ruler and king of Kekaya, viz., my father and your father-in-law, has affectionately asked after the wellbeing of all, 
and in whose wellbeing you are interested at my place, they are all hale and healthy as of now... [1-73-3]_END

B_1_C_73_3
BEGIN_
स्वस्रीयं मम राजेन्द्र द्रष्टुकामो महीपतिः |
तदर्थमुपयातोऽहमयोध्यां रघुनंदन || १-७३-४_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Raghu's legatee, oh, best king, my father and the king of Kekaya is interested to see my sister Kaikeyi's son, Bharata, 
and for that reason I am sent to Ayodhya... [1-73-4]_END

B_1_C_73_4
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा त्वहमयोध्यायां विवाहार्थं तवात्मजान् |
मिथिलामुपयातांस्तु त्वया सह महीपते || १-७३-५
त्वरयाभ्युपयातोऽहं द्रष्टुकामः स्वसुः सुतम् |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, lord of the land, in Ayodhya I have heard that you went to Mithila along with your sons for their marriages, and wishing 
to see my sister's son Bharata I promptly travelled here..." Thus Yudhaajit told Dasharatha. [1-73-5, 6a]_END

B_1_C_73_5
BEGIN_
अथ राजा दशरथः प्रियातिथिमुपस्थितम् || १-७३-६
दृष्ट्वा परमसत्कारैः पूजार्हं समपूजयत् |_END
BEGIN_
Then king Dasharatha on seeing the adorable guest who arrived in his presence, and who is a merited one for adoration, Dasharatha 
adored Yudhaajit well, with full observances. [1-73-6b, 7a]_END

B_1_C_73_6
BEGIN_
ततस्तामुषितो रात्रिं सह पुत्रैर्महात्मभिः || १-७३-७
प्रभाते पुनरुत्थाय कृत्वा कर्माणि तत्त्ववित् |
ऋषींस्तदा पुरस्कृत्य यज्ञवाटमुपागमत् || १-७३-८_END
BEGIN_
Then on taking rest for that night along with his noble-minded sons, and again on getting up in the next morning, and on 
performing morning-observances as a duty-bound king, Dasharatha arrived at the hall of Vedic-ritual, keeping the sages in 
his forefront. [1-73-7b-8]_END

B_1_C_73_7
BEGIN_
युक्ते मुहूर्ते विजये सर्वाभरणभूषितैः |
भ्रातृभिः सहितो रामः कृतकौतुकमंगलः || १-७३-९
वसिष्ठं पुरतः कृत्वा महर्षीनपरानपि |_END
BEGIN_
Rama arrived at his father together with all of his brothers, keeping sage Vashishta and other eminent-saint ahead of them, 
on an opportune and appropriate hour called 'Victory...' and all the bridegrooms are adorned with all kinds of jewellery 
appropriate for the wedding time, and all have performed the auspicious ceremony for marriage-thread, conducted prior to 
the marriage and, all have thread-bands tied around their wrists, as they all have performed an auspicious ceremony antecedent 
to marriage ceremony. [1-73-9, 10a]_END

B_1_C_73_8
BEGIN_
वशिष्ठो भगवानेत्य वैदेहमिदमब्रवीत् || १-७३-१०
राजा दशरथो राजन् कृतकौतुकमङ्गलैः |
पुत्रैर्नरवरश्रेष्ठ दातारमभिकांक्षते || १-७३-११_END
BEGIN_
Then that godly sage Vashishta on going from Vedic-ritual hall to marriage hall said this to Janaka, "Oh, best one among 
best people, oh, king Janaka, having performed the auspicious marriage-thread ceremony, Dasharatha along with his sons is 
looking forward for the donor... [1-73-10b, 11]_END

B_1_C_73_9
BEGIN_
दातृप्रतिग्रहीतृभ्यां सर्वार्थाः संभवन्ति हि |
स्वधर्मं प्रतिपद्यस्व कृत्वा वैवाह्यमुत्तमम् || १-७३-१२_END
BEGIN_
"In marriages all the puruSaartha-s , the component values of life, namely rightness, riches, 
revelries, and results of final release will be occurring only if the benefactor and beneficiary meet, isn't it. Hence let 
king Dasharatha come, and then on actualising this best marriage you too will be doing your best devoir as royal priest... 
[1-73-12]_END

B_1_C_73_10
BEGIN_
इत्युक्तः परमोदारो वसिष्ठेन महात्मना |
प्रत्युवाच महातेजा वाक्यं परमधर्मवित् || १-७३-१३_END
BEGIN_
Janaka is not just a decidedly valiant king but he is the profound knower of probity also, besides being an unreservedly 
generous king, hence he has already made all arrangements, and when he is spoken in this way by Vashishta that king replied 
this sentence to that right honourable Vashishta. [1-73-13]_END

B_1_C_73_11
BEGIN_
कः स्थितः प्रतिहारो मे कस्याज्ञा संप्रतीक्ष्यते |
स्वगृहे को विचारोऽस्ति यथा राज्यमिदं तव || १-७३-१४_END
BEGIN_
Who is that doorman that prevents your entry? Or, for whose orders you all await with a bated breath? Do you hesitate in 
your own house, or what? This kingdom is as good as yours... isn't so... [1-73-14]_END

B_1_C_73_12
BEGIN_
कृतकौतुकसर्वस्वा वेदिमूलमुपागताः |
मम कन्या मुनिश्रेष्ठ दीप्ता वह्नेरिवार्चिषः || १-७३-१५_END
BEGIN_
Oh, eminent-saint Vashishta, on absolutely performing the auspicious ceremony for the marriage-thread, and thereby tying 
thread-band at wrists my daughters have already arrived, and they are at the base of the Altar of Fire, like the irradiant 
jets of flames of radiant fire... [1-73-15]_END

B_1_C_73_13
BEGIN_
सद्योऽहं त्वत्प्रतीक्षोऽस्मि वेद्यामस्यां प्रतिष्ठितः |
अविघ्नं कुरुतां राजा किमर्थं हि विलम्ब्यते || १-७३-१६_END
BEGIN_
"I am already ready and awaiting for you remaining at this Altar of Fire. Let everything be done indeed without any deterrents. 
What for the king Dasharatha is dawdling..." So said Janaka to Vashishta. [1-73-16]_END

B_1_C_73_14
BEGIN_
तद्वाक्यं जनकेनोक्तं श्रुत्वा दशरथस्तदा |
प्रवेशयामास सुतान् सर्वानृषिगणानपि || १-७३-१७_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that sentence of Janaka, then Dasharatha started towards marriage hall, and then he started to enter his sons 
one by one, four in all, into marriage hall along with all of the assemblages of sages. [1-73-17]_END

B_1_C_73_15
BEGIN_
ततो राजा विदेहानां वशिष्ठमिदमब्रवीत् |
कारयस्व ऋषे सर्वानृषिभिः सह धार्मिक || १-७३-१८
रामस्य लोकरामस्य क्रियां वैवाहिकीं प्रभो |_END
BEGIN_
Then that king from Videha bloodline, Janaka, said in this way to Vashishta, "Oh, the knower of punctilios, oh, Brahma-sage, 
oh, masterly sage, along with other sages you make happen all of the marriage ceremonies of Rama, the rejoicer of the world..." 
Thus Janaka spoke to Vashishta. [1-73-18, 19a]_END

B_1_C_73_16
BEGIN_
तथेत्युक्त्वा तु जनकं वशिष्ठो भगवानृषिः || १-७३-१९
विश्वामित्रं पुरस्कृत्य शतानंदं च धार्मिकम् |
प्रपामध्ये तु विधिवद्वेदीं कृत्वा महातपाः || १-७३-२०
अलञ्चकार तां वेदीं गन्धपुष्पैः समंततः |
सुवर्णपालिकाभिश्च चित्रकुम्भैश्च साङ्कुरैः || १-७३-२१
अंकुराढ्यैः शरावैश्च धूपपात्रैः सधूपकैः |
शंखपात्रैः श्रुवैः स्रुग्भिः पात्रैरर्घ्यादिपूजितैः || १-७३-२२
लाजपूर्णैश्च पात्रीभिरक्षितैरपि संस्कृतैः |_END


B_1_C_73_17
BEGIN_
दर्भैः समैः समास्तीर्य विधिवन्मंत्रपूर्वकम् || १-७३-२३
अग्निमाधाय तं वेद्यां विधिमंत्रपुरस्कृतम् |
जुहावाग्नौ महातेजा वशिष्ठो मुनिपुंगव || १-७३-२४_END
BEGIN_
Then that great resplendent and eminent-saint Vashishta neatly overlaid even-sized sacred grass on that Altar of Fire synchronising 
with Vedic-chants, and on preparing Ritual-fire by rubbing two wooden sticks, called araNi 
, he placed that fire in the pit of Altar, which is aflame now, and then reverently and in tune with the Vedic-hymns he 
effused oblational liquids into that Altar of Fire, with short-handled and long-handled wooden scoops. [1-73-23b, 24]_END

B_1_C_73_18
BEGIN_
ततः सीतां समानीय सर्वाभरणभूषिताम् |
समक्षमग्नेः संस्थाप्य राघवाभिमुखे तदा || १-७३-२५
अब्रवीज्जनको राजा कौसल्यानंदवर्धनम् |_END
BEGIN_
Then that king Janaka led forth Seetha, who by now is decorated with every variety of bridal jewellery, and on positioning 
her en face Raghava in the presence of Altar of Fire, then Janaka addressed Rama who is the enhancer of his mother Kausalya's 
rejoice. [1-73-25, 26a]_END

B_1_C_73_19
BEGIN_
इयं सीता मम सुता सहधर्मचरी तव || १-७३-२६
प्रतीच्छ चैनां भद्रं ते पाणिं गृह्णीष्व पाणिना |_END
BEGIN_
"This is Seetha, my daughter, she acquits herself in whatever duty you undertake. Take her wishfully, let safeness betide 
you, take her palm into your palm..." [1-73-26b, 27a]_END

B_1_C_73_20
BEGIN_
Or_END
BEGIN_
Here Sita stands, my daughter fair, / The duties of thy life to share. / Take from her father, take thy bride, / Join hand 
to hand, and bliss betide! / - Ralph T. H. Griffith_END

B_1_C_73_21
BEGIN_
पतिव्रता महभागा छायेवानुगता सदा || १-७३-२७
इत्युक्त्वा प्राक्षिपद्राजा मंत्रपूतं जलं तदा |_END
BEGIN_
"She who is prosperous and husband-devout, will always be abiding you like your own shadow..." So saying that king Janaka 
then poured forth water into the palms of Rama, which is sanctified with hymns. [1-73-27b, 28a]_END

B_1_C_73_22
BEGIN_
साधु साध्विति देवानामृषीणां वदतां तदा || १-७३-२८
देवदुंदुभिनिर्घोषः पुष्पवर्षो महानभूत् |_END
BEGIN_
Then there occurred great flower-showers from firmament, while sages and gods staying in firmament have exclaimed, "nice... 
fine..." to the drumbeats of heavenly drums. [1-3-28b, 29a]_END

B_1_C_73_23
BEGIN_
एवं दत्त्वा सुतां सीतां मंत्रोदकपुरस्कृताम् || १-७३-२९
अब्रवीज्जनको राजा हर्षेणाभिपरिप्लुतः |_END
BEGIN_
On handing over his daughter Seetha who is duly sanctified with sanctified waters, King Janaka is completely overwhelmed 
with exhilaration for the successful performance of his bit as a father and he said this. [1-73-29b, 30a]_END

B_1_C_73_24
BEGIN_
लक्ष्मणागच्छ भद्रं ते ऊर्मिलामुद्यतां मया || १-७३-३०
प्रतीच्छ पाणिं गृह्णीष्व मा भूत् कालस्य पर्ययः |_END
BEGIN_
Come on, Lakshmana, safe betides you... say yes to Urmila, the one who is decided by me to be given to you... take her 
palm into yours... lapse not the time... [1-73-30b, 31a]_END

B_1_C_73_25
BEGIN_
तमेवमुक्त्वा जनको भरतं चाभ्यभाषत || १-७३-३१
गृहाण पाणिं माण्डव्याः पाणिना रघुनंदन |_END
BEGIN_
Janaka having said to Lakshmana that way, he also addressed Bharata, "Oh, Bharata, the delight of Raghu-s, take Maandavi's 
palm into your palm... [1-73-31b-32a]_END

B_1_C_73_26
BEGIN_
शत्रुघ्नं चापि धर्मात्मा अब्रवीन्मिथिलेश्वरः || १-७३-३२
श्रुतकीर्तेर्महाबाहो पाणिं गृह्णीष्व पाणिना |_END
BEGIN_
That honourable king of Mithila even said to Shatrughna, "oh, dextrous Shatrughna, take the palm of Shrutakiirti into yours... 
[1-73-32b, 33a]_END

B_1_C_73_27
BEGIN_
सर्वे भवन्तः सौम्याश्च सर्वे सुचरितव्रताः || १-७३-३३
पत्नीभिः सन्तु काकुत्स्था मा भूत्कालस्य पर्ययः |_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Rama, Lakshmana, Bharata, Shatrughna ... you all are tender-hearted, well-behaved and well-intentioned brothers from 
Kakutstha lineage... without lapse of time take up other ceremonies..." So said Janaka to bridegrooms. [1-73-33b, 34a]_END

B_1_C_73_28
BEGIN_
जनकस्य वचः श्रुत्वा पाणीन् पाणिभिरस्पृशन् || १-७३-३४
चत्वारस्ते चतसॄणां वसिष्ठस्य मते स्थिताः |_END
BEGIN_
All the four bridegrooms are palminpalmed with all the four brides, paying heed to Janaka's words, and abiding in Vashishta's 
orchestration of Vedic hymns and procedures. [1-73-34b, 35a]_END

B_1_C_73_29
BEGIN_
अग्निं प्रदक्षिणं कृत्वा वेदिं राजानमेव च || १-७३-३५
ऋषींश्चैव महात्मानः सहभार्या रघूद्वहाः |
यथोक्तेन तथा चक्रुर्विवाहं विधिपूर्वकम् || १-७३-३६_END
BEGIN_
On performing circumambulations along with their wives around the Ritual-fire, and around the Altar of Fire, and that way, 
around king Janaka, the awarder of wives, and around sages as well for they conducted the marriages well, those great-souled 
bridegrooms that have emerged from Raghu's dynasty on performing further deeds of ritual consistent with custom as directed 
by Vashishta, they are all wed. [1-73-35b, 36]_END

B_1_C_73_30
BEGIN_
पुष्पवृष्टिर्महत्यासीदन्तरिक्षात्सुभास्वरा |
दिव्यदुन्दुभिनिर्घोषैर्गीतवादित्रनिःस्वनैः || १-७३-३७
ननृतुश्चाप्सरःसंघा गन्धर्वाश्च जगुः कलम् |
विवाहे रघुमुख्यानां तदद्भुतमदृश्यत || १-७३-३८_END
BEGIN_
There occurred rich and highly dazzling flower showers from firmament, and that ambience is filled with the drumbeats of 
divine drums and with vocal and instrumental music, and promenades of apsara-s danced, and even the gandharva-s sang tunefully, 
and because it is the marriage of celebrated bridegrooms from Raghu's dynasty, such a charming spectacle is envisioned.. 
[1-73-37, 38]_END

B_1_C_73_31
BEGIN_
ईदृशे वर्तमाने तु तूर्योद्घुष्टनिनादिते |
त्रिरग्निं ते परिक्रम्य ऊहुर्भार्या महौजसः || १-७३-३९_END
BEGIN_
In this kind of ongoingness of harmonious music of vocal, instrumental and that of dancers, those great resplendent brothers 
married their wives on circumabulating the Ritual-fire fire thrice. [1-73-39]_END

B_1_C_73_32
BEGIN_
अथोपकार्यां जग्मुस्ते स दारा रघुनंदनाः |
राजाप्यनुययौ पश्यन् सर्षिसंघः सबान्धवः || १-७३-४०_END
BEGIN_
Then those legatees of Raghu went to their visitatorial-palace with their wives, followed by king Dasharatha along with 
the assemblages of sages, kinfolks, queens and wives included, and Dasharatha feasted his eyes on sons and daughter-in-laws. 
[1-73-40]_END

B_1_C_74_0
BEGIN_
 अथ रात्र्यां व्यतीतायां विश्वामित्रो महामुनिः |
 
  आपृच्छ्य तौ च राजानौ जगामोत्तरपर्वतम् || १-७४-१_END
BEGIN_
 When that night is elapsing into the wee hours of next day, then the eminent-saint
  Vishvamitra on asking for the leave of absence from those kings, Dasharatha and Janaka, and from
  both Rama and Lakshmana, he set out to northern mountains, namely Himalayas. [1-74-1]_END

B_1_C_74_1
BEGIN_
 विश्वामित्रो गते राजा वैदेहं मिथिलाधिपम् |
 
  आपृष्ट्वैव जगामाशु राजा दशरथः पुरीम् || १-७४-२_END
BEGIN_
 When Vishvamitra departed that ruler to the delight of people, namely Dasharatha,
  on asking leave of absence with king Janaka who outvies bodily affairs, promptly set forth for
  the city of Ayodhya. [1-74-2]_END

B_1_C_74_2
BEGIN_
 अथ राजा विदेहानां ददौ कन्याधनं बहु |
 गवां शतसहस्राणि बहूनि मिथिलेश्वरः || १-७४-३
  कंबलानां च मुख्यानां क्षौमान् कोट्यंबराणि च |
  हस्त्यश्वरथपादातं दिव्यरूपं स्वलंकृतम् || १-७४-४
  ददौ कन्याशतं तासां दासीदासमनुत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_
 Then that king Janaka of Mithila, the one from Videha lineage, gave innumerable
  patrimonial riches. He has also given umpteen number of cows, millions of excellent shawls and
  silk dresses, and elephants, horses, chariots, foot soldiers, besides hundreds of highly
  decorated girls, divine in their mien, as unexcelled chambermaids and handmaidens to the brides.
  [1-74-3, 4, 5a]_END

B_1_C_74_3
BEGIN_
 हिरण्यस्य सुवर्णस्य मुक्तानां विद्रुमस्य च || १-७४-५
 
  ददौ राजा सुसंहृष्टः कन्याधनमनुत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_
 King Janaka gave beau idéal bridal riches in gold, silver, pearls and corals even,
  for he is very highly gladdened as Seetha's marriage came true. [1-74-5b, 6a]_END

B_1_C_74_4
BEGIN_
 दत्त्वा बहुविधं राजा समनुज्ञाप्य पार्थिवम् || १-७४-६
 
  प्रविवेश स्वनिलयं मिथिलां मिथिलेश्वरः |_END
BEGIN_
 Having given many kinds of bridal gifts and having accompanied his daughters for a
  distance, then having received a bid adieu from Dasharatha, that sovereign of Mithila, Janaka,
  re-entered is own palace in Mithila. [1-74-6, 7a]_END

B_1_C_74_5
BEGIN_
 राजाप्ययोध्याधिपतिः सह पुत्रैर्महात्मभिः || १-७४-७
 
  ऋषीन् सर्वान् पुरस्कृत्य जगाम सबलानुगः |_END
BEGIN_
 Even the king Dasharatha, the sovereign of Ayodhya proceeded with his noble-souled
  sons, keeping all the sages in the fore, while his forces followed him. [1-74-7b, 8a]_END

B_1_C_74_6
BEGIN_
 गच्छन्तं तु नरव्याघ्रं सर्षिसंघं सराघवम् || १-७४-८
 
  घोरास्तु पक्षिणो वाचो व्याहरन्ति समंततः |_END
BEGIN_
 But while going with the assemblages of sages and with young Raghava-s, namely
  Rama, Lakshmana, Bharata, Shatrughna, the sky-bound birds started to screech with startling voice
  from all around facing that tigerly-man Dasharatha. [1-74-8b, 9a]_END

B_1_C_74_7
BEGIN_
 भौमाश्चैव मृगाः सर्वे गच्छन्ति स्म प्रदक्षिणम् || १-७४-९
 
  तान् दृष्ट्वा राजशार्दूलो वसिष्ठं पर्यपृच्छत |_END
BEGIN_
 Also thus, all of the earth bound animals are going his leftward, and on seeing
  this, albeit he is a tigerly king he is perplexed, and particularly asked Vashishta. [1-74-9b,
  10a]_END

B_1_C_74_8
BEGIN_
 असौम्याः पक्षिणो घोरा मृगाश्चापि प्रदक्षिणाः || १-७४-१०
 
  किमिदं हृदयोत्कंपि मनो मम विषीदति |_END
BEGIN_
 "Unpropitious is the starling voicing of birds, whereby my heart is throbbing
  down... and propitious is the leftward going of the animals, thereby my heart is throbbing up...
  why so?" [1-74-10b, 11a]_END

B_1_C_74_9
BEGIN_
 राज्ञो दशरथस्यैतत् श्रुत्वा वाक्यं महानृषिः || १-७४-११
 
  उवाच मधुरां वाणीं श्रूयतामस्य यत्फलम् |_END
BEGIN_
 On hearing all that is said by king Dasharatha, the instinctual sage Vashishta
  said this sentence in a soothing voice, "I will tell apart the result of these auguries...
  [1-74-11b, 12a]_END

B_1_C_74_10
BEGIN_
 उपस्थितं भयं घोरं दिव्यं पक्षिमुखाच्च्युतम् || १-७४-१२
 
  मृगाः प्रशमयन्त्येते संतापः त्यज्यतामयम् |_END
BEGIN_
 "The shrieks voiced by the birds are foretokening the forthcoming providential and
  perilous trepidation, but the behaviour of these animals is betokening it as mitigable... hence,
  let this consternation be forsaken... [1-74-12b, 13a]_END

B_1_C_74_11
BEGIN_
 तेषां संवदतां तत्र वायुः प्रादुर्बभूव ह || १-७४-१३
 
  कंपयन् मेदिनीं सर्वां पातयंश्च महाद्रुमान् |_END
BEGIN_
 While they are discussing among themselves, a whirlwind started to whirligig
  there, as though to shake the earth and shatter all gigantic trees. [1-74-13b, 14a]_END

B_1_C_74_12
BEGIN_
 तमसा संवृतः सूर्यः सर्वे न वेदिषुर्दिशः || १-७४-१४
 
  भस्मना चावृतं सर्वं सम्मूढमिव तद्बलम् |_END
BEGIN_
 Murkiness enshrouded the sun, thus everyone is unaware of quarters, a sandstorm
  enwrapped that army, by which it has become as though ensorcelled. [1-74-14b, 15a]_END

B_1_C_74_13
BEGIN_
 वसिष्ठ ऋषयचान्ये राजा च ससुतस्तदा || १-७४-१५
 
  ससंज्ञा इव तत्रासन् सर्वमन्यद्विचेतनम् |_END
BEGIN_
 Then Vashishta and the other sages, the king Dasharatha along with his sons
  remained there with animation, and everything and every other one available there has become
  inanimate. [1-74-15b, 16a]_END

B_1_C_74_14
BEGIN_
 तस्मिंस्तमसि घोरे तु भस्मच्छन्नेव सा चमूः || १-७४-१६
 
  ददर्श भीमसंकाशं जटामण्डलधारिणम् |
  भार्गवं जामदग्न्यं तं राजा राजविमर्दनम् || १-७४-१७
  कैलासमिव दुर्धर्षं कालाग्निमिव दुःसहम् |
  ज्वलंतमिव तेजोभिः दुर्निरीक्ष्यं पृथग्जनैः || १-७४-१८
  स्कन्धे चासज्य परशुं धनुर्विद्युद्गणोपमम् |
  प्रगृह्य शरमुग्रं च त्रिपुरघ्नं यथा शिवम् || १-७४-१९_END
BEGIN_
 In that catastrophic darkness, that sand-muffled military of king Dasharatha has
  seen the son of Sage Jamadagni, namely Bhaargava Rama, the subjugator of kings of kings. He
  appeared calamitous in his look by wearing tufty matted and unruly head-hair, an unassailable one
  like Mt. Kailash, an unbearable one like the Epoch-End-Fire, irradiant with his own radiance,
  hence imperceivable for commoners, and such as he is, he clinched an axe on his right shoulder
  and clasped a bow in his left hand, that in simile is like a congeries of electroluminescence,
  and handling an arrow which is as if ready to electrocute, and he vied in his overall look with
  the devastator of triple cities, namely God Shiva. [1-74-16b, 17, 18, 19]_END

B_1_C_74_15
BEGIN_
तं दृष्ट्वा भीमसंकाशं ज्वलंतमिव पावकम् |
 
  वसिष्ठप्रमुखा विप्रा जपहोमपरायणाः || १-७४-२०
  संगता मुनयः सर्वे संजजल्पुरथो मिथः |_END
BEGIN_
 On seeing him who is perilous in his propensity and flaming like the Ritual-fire,
  Vashishta and the other prominent Brahman-s who are the practisers of meditation and
  fire-oblations have come together and started to susurrate, up and down. [1-74-20, 21a]_END

B_1_C_74_16
BEGIN_
 कच्चित् पितृवधामर्षी क्षत्र ं नोत्सादयिष्यति || १-७४-२१
 
  पूर्वं क्षत्रवधं कृत्वा गतमन्युर्गतज्वरः |
  क्षत्रस्योत्सादनं भूयो न खल्वस्य चिकीर्षितम् || १-७४-२२_END
BEGIN_
 "Will he eradicate the race of Kshatriya-s even now as he was once envenomed by
  the murder of his father, or what... abated is his anger and alleviated is his frenzy previously
  when he eliminated Kshatriya-s... but is he really intending to eliminate Kshatriya-s once again,
  or what?" Thus, those Brahmans talked among themselves. [1-74-21b, 22]_END

B_1_C_74_17
BEGIN_
 एवमुक्त्वार्घ्यमादाय भार्गवं भीमदर्शनम् |
 
  ऋषयो राम रामेति मधुरं वाक्यमब्रुवन् || १-७४-२३_END
BEGIN_
 After their susurrus the sages have approached him, who in his very look is like a
  visitation, with oblational water and addressed him with benign words of greeting like, "oh,
  Rama, oh, Bhaargava Rama..." [1-74-23]_END

B_1_C_74_18
BEGIN_
 प्रतिगृह्य तु तां पूजामृषिदत्तां प्रतापवान् |
 
  रामं दाशरथिं रामो जामदग्न्योऽभ्यभाषत || १-७४-२४_END
BEGIN_
 On receiving the deference paid by the sage Vashishta, that inexorable Rama of
  Jamadagni started to talk to Rama of Dasharatha. [1-74-24]_END

B_1_C_75_0
BEGIN_
राम दाशरथे वीर वीर्यं ते श्रूयतेऽद्भुतम् |
धनुषो भेदनं चैव निखिलेन मया श्रुतम् || १-७५-१_END
BEGIN_
Oh, valiant Rama of Dasharatha, your valour is bruited as a sensational valour, and sensational is your smashing of Shiva's 
bow, also thus I have thoroughly heard about your others deeds like elimination of Tataka et cetera... [1-75-1]_END

B_1_C_75_1
BEGIN_
तदद्भुतमचिंत्यं च भेदनं धनुषस्तथा |
तच्छ्रुत्वाहमनुप्राप्तो धनुर्गृह्यापरं शुभम् || १-७५-२_END
BEGIN_
That way, smashing of that particular bow of Shiva is wondrous and even unimaginable... on hearing that alone I happened 
upon you, bringing another outranking bow... [1-75-2]_END

B_1_C_75_2
BEGIN_
तदिदं घोरसंकाशं जामदग्न्यं महद्धनुः |
पूरयस्व शरेणैव स्वबलं दर्शयस्व च || १-७५-३_END
BEGIN_
This alone is that catastrophic bow received through Sage Jamadagni... flex it with an arrow on bowstring stretching up 
to your ear, and in that way show your capability... [1-75-3]_END

B_1_C_75_3
BEGIN_
तदहं ते बलं दृष्ट्वा धनुषोऽस्य प्रपूरणे |
द्वंद्वयुद्धं प्रदास्यामि वीर्यश्लाघ्यमहं तव || १-७५-४_END
BEGIN_
"Thereby, on examining your strength in your taking aim with this bow, and should you be deservedly valorous, I will give 
you a combative duel..." So said Parashu Rama to Dasharatha Rama. [1-75-4]_END

B_1_C_75_4
BEGIN_
तस्य तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा राजा दशरथस्तदा |
विषण्णवदनो दीनः प्रांजलिर्वाक्यमब्रवीत् || १-७५-५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that sentence of Bhaargava Rama, then king Dasharatha became a pitiable one, and with a downcast face and adjoined 
palms said this. [1-75-5]_END

B_1_C_75_5
BEGIN_
क्षत्ररोषात् प्रशांतस्त्वं ब्राह्मणश्च महातपाः |
बालानां मम पुत्राणामभयं दातुमर्हसि || १-७५-६_END
BEGIN_
Aren't you a Brahman with inviolable ascesis, and whose rancour on Kshatriya-s has calmed down long back. Why this hostility 
again. It'll be apt of you to award aegis to my sons, for they are yet youngsters... [1-75-6]_END

B_1_C_75_6
BEGIN_
भार्गवाणां कुले जातः स्वाध्यायव्रतशालिनाम् |
सहस्राक्षे प्रतिज्ञाय शस्त्रं प्रक्षिप्तवानसि || १-७५-७_END
BEGIN_
Aren't you from the bloodline of Bhaargava-s who always conduct themselves in self-study of Vedas and self-principled ways... 
haven't you readily discarded weapon-wielding on your promise to Thousand-eyed Indra... [1-75-7]_END

B_1_C_75_7
BEGIN_
स त्वं धर्मपरो भूत्वा काश्यपाय वसुंधराम् |
दत्त्वा वनमुपागम्य महेन्द्रकृतकेतनः || १-७५-८_END
BEGIN_
Such as you were, you on becoming a dedicatee to probity, haven't you given the planet earth to Kashyapa and haven't you 
repaired to forests, and haven't you flagged yourself on Mt. Mahendra... [1-75-8]_END

B_1_C_75_8
BEGIN_
मम सर्वविनाशाय संप्राप्तस्त्वं महामुने |
न चैकस्मिन् हते रामे सर्वे जीवामहे वयम् || १-७५-९_END
BEGIN_
"Or, oh, insurmountable sage, have you chanced upon us for a total annihilation of ours... when Rama is singularised and 
eliminated, nay-said that we all will be living..." Thus Dasharatha had gone on appealing in his love for his sons. [1-75-9]_END

B_1_C_75_9
BEGIN_
ब्रुवत्येवं दशरथे जामदग्न्यः प्रतापवान् |
अनादृत्य तु तद्वाक्यं राममेवाभ्यभाषत || १-७५-१०_END
BEGIN_
While Dasharatha is speaking in that way that intransigent Bhaargava Rama of Sage Jamadagni uncaring for those merciful 
words of Dasharatha addressed Rama of Dasharatha alone. [1-75-10]_END

B_1_C_75_10
BEGIN_
इमे द्वे धनुषी श्रेष्ठे दिव्ये लोकाभिपूजिते |
दृढे बलवती मुख्ये सुकृते विश्वकर्मणा || १-७५-११_END
BEGIN_
These are the two strong and sturdy unsurpassed longbows, well-designed by gods and well-crafted by Vishvakarma, the Divine 
Architect, and these are very important among all bows and well-worshipped by all worlds... one broken in your, and the 
other in my hand... [1-75-11]_END

B_1_C_75_11
BEGIN_
अनिसृष्टं सुरैरेकं त्र्यम्बकाय युयुत्सवे |
त्रिपुरघ्नं नरश्रेष्ठ भग्नं काकुत्स्थ यत्त्वया || १-७५-१२_END
BEGIN_
Oh, best one among men, out of the two longbows gods gave one to restive Trymbaka, God Shiva for a combat with demon Tripura, 
and oh, Kakutstha, that bow alone is the annihilator of Tripura, the demon... and you have broken that alone... [1-75-12]_END

B_1_C_75_12
BEGIN_
इदं द्वितीयं दुर्धर्षं विष्णोर्दत्तं सुरोत्तमैः |
तदिदं वैष्णवं राम धनुः परपुरञ्जयम् || १-७५-१३
समानसारं काकुत्स्थ रौद्रेण धनुषा त्विदम् |_END
BEGIN_
This is the second one and the choicest gods gave this to Vishnu, thereby this is named after Him as 'Vishnu's bow...' 
this is an indestructible and enemy-citadel conquering longbow... and this is identical in its efficacy with Rudra's longbow... 
[1-75-13, 14a]_END

B_1_C_75_13
BEGIN_
तदा तु देवताः सर्वाः पृच्छन्ति स्म पितामहम् || १-७५-१४
शितिकण्ठस्य विष्णोश्च बलाबलनिरीक्षया |
अभिप्रायं तु विज्ञाय देवतानां पितामहः || १-७५-१५
विरोधं जनयामास तयोः सत्यवतां वरः |_END
BEGIN_
Once, all the gods were asking the Grandparent, Brahma, as to who is powerful and who is less powerful among the blue-throated 
Shiva and Vishnu... but the Grandparent Brahma on inferring the intent of gods started to create adversity among those two, 
Shiva and Vishnu, for the Grandparent is the best adherer of truthfulness, as truth cannot be demonstrated on hearsay evidence... 
[1-75-14b, 15, 16a]_END

B_1_C_75_14
BEGIN_
विरोधे तु महद्युद्धमभवद्रोमहर्षणम् || १-७५-१६
शितिकण्ठस्य विष्णोश्च परस्परजयैषिणोः |_END
BEGIN_
Owing to their animosity then occurred a fierce and hair-raising war among Shiva and Vishnu, as each aspired victory for 
himself... [1-75-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_75_15
BEGIN_
तदा तु जृम्भितं शैवं धनुर्भीमपराक्रमम् || १-७५-१७
हुंकारेण महादेवः स्तम्भितोऽथ त्रिलोचनः |_END
BEGIN_
By the 'hum' sound of Vishnu that ruinously overpowering longbow of Shiva is broken, and the triple-eyed God, Mahadeva, 
is frozen... [1-75-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_75_16
BEGIN_
देवैस्तदा समागम्य सर्षिसन्घैः सचारणैः || १-७५-१८
याचितौ प्रशमं तत्र जग्मतुस्तौ सुरोत्तमौ |_END
BEGIN_
Then gods along with the assemblages of sages and celestial carana-s have come together and appealed to those two for appeasement 
in the matter of wielding authority, and then those two superior gods, Shiva and Vishnu, went into a state of amity... [1-75-18b, 
19a]_END

B_1_C_75_17
BEGIN_
जृम्भितं तद्धनुर्दृष्ट्वा शैवं विष्णुपराक्रमैः || १-७५-१९
अधिकं मेनिरे विष्णुं देवाः सर्षिगणास्तदा |_END
BEGIN_
"On seeing the bow of Shiva rendered inert by the mettlesomeness of Vishnu, from then on the gods along with the assemblages 
of sages deemed Vishnu to be the paramount... [1-75-19b, 20a]_END

B_1_C_75_18
BEGIN_
धनू रुद्रस्तु संक्रुद्धो विदेहेषु महायशाः || १-७५-२०
देवरातस्य राजर्षेर्ददौ हस्ते ससायकम् |_END
BEGIN_
That celebrated Rudra on his part with indignation has handed over that longbow, which is already fitted with unloosened 
arrow, to the sagely king among Videha kings, namely Devaraata... [1-75-20b, 21a]_END

B_1_C_75_19
BEGIN_
इदं च वैष्णवं राम धनुः परपुरञ्जयम् || १-७५-२१
ऋचीके भार्गवे प्रादाद्विष्णुः सन्यासमुत्तमम् |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, this alone is that enemy-citadel conquering longbow of Vishnu, and Vishnu handed over this to Sage Riciika, the 
son of Bhrigu, as a trustworthy trust... [1-75-21b, 22a]_END

B_1_C_75_20
BEGIN_
ऋचीकस्तु महातेजाः पुत्रस्याप्रतिकर्मणः || १-७५-२२
पितुर्मम ददौ दिव्यं जमदग्नेर्महात्मनः |_END
BEGIN_
That great-resplendent Sage Riciika on his part has handed over this divine bow to his son with unmatchable deeds of religious 
merit, who is my father Sage Jamadagni... [1-75-22b, 23a]_END

B_1_C_75_21
BEGIN_
न्यस्तशस्त्रे पितरि मे तपोबलसमन्विते || १-७५-२३
अर्जुनो विदधे मृत्युं प्राकृतां बुद्धिमास्थितः |_END
BEGIN_
Adhering to a barbarous mentality Kaartaviirya Arjuna put my father to death, when the ascetically powerful father of 
mine has isolated himself from arsenal... [1-75-23b, 24a]_END

B_1_C_75_22
BEGIN_
वधमप्रतिरूपं तु पितुः श्रुत्वा सुदारुणम् |
क्षत्रमुत्सादयन् रोषाज्जातं जातमनेकशः || १-७५-२४
पृथिवीं चाखिलां प्राप्य काश्यपाय महात्मने |
यज्ञस्यान्ते तदा राम दक्षिणां पुण्यकर्मणे || १-७५-२५
दत्त्वा महेन्द्रनिलयः तपोबलसमन्वितः |_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Rama, on hearing the unregenerate and highly perfidious murdering of my father, I rancorously extirpated Kshatriya-s 
as and when they are born, that too not for one time, but I did so for thirty-seven times going around the earth... and 
on getting the entire earth under my control I performed Vedic-ritual, and at the end of that Vedic-ritual, I gave all that 
earth to sage Kashyapa, a sage with divine soul and with pious observances, as a ritualistic-generosity... and I am at present 
on Mt. Mahendra practising ascesis and thus conjoined are the powers of ascesis in me... [1-75-24b, c, 25, 26a]_END

B_1_C_75_23
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा तु धनुषो भेदं ततोऽहं द्रुतमागतः || १-७५-२६
तदेवं वैष्णवं राम पितृपैतामहं महत् |
क्षत्रधर्मं पुरस्कृत्य गृह्णीष्व धनुरुत्तमम् || १-७५-२७_END
BEGIN_
On hearing about the breakage of Shiva's longbow, then I promptly came here. Thereby, oh, Rama, wield this supernatural 
and superlative longbow of Vishnu, which is passed on to me from my forefathers and my father. Keep your fealty to Kshatriya-hood 
in view, and wield this as you have wielded Shiva's longbow... [1-75-26b, 27]_END

B_1_C_75_24
BEGIN_
योजयस्व धनुःश्रेष्ठे शरं परपुरञ्जयम् |
यदि शक्तोऽसि काकुत्स्थ द्वन्द्वं दास्यामि ते ततः || १-७५-२८_END
BEGIN_
Take an aim with an arrow that conquers enemy's citadels fixing it on this supramundane longbow... and oh, Kakutstha, should 
you be capable of it, thereafter I will give you a duel... [1-75-27]_END

B_1_C_76_0
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा तज्जामदग्न्यस्य वाक्यं दाशरथिस्तदा |
गौरवाद्यंत्रितकथः पितू राममथाब्रवीत् || १-७६-१_END
BEGIN_
On hearing that sentence of Rama of Jamadagni, then Rama of Dasharatha said this to him in a courtly owing to the presence 
of his father Dasharatha. [1-76-1]_END

B_1_C_76_1
BEGIN_
कृतवानस्मि यत् कर्म श्रुतवानसि भार्गव |
अनुरुन्ध्यामहे ब्रह्मन् पितुरानृण्यमास्थितः || १-७६-२_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Bhaargava Rama, whatsoever endeavour you have strived for freeing yourself from the indebtedness towards your father, 
I have heard of them, and oh, Brahman, we appreciate for your achieving that freeness from your paternal debt, but... [1-76-2]_END

B_1_C_76_2
BEGIN_
वीर्यहीनमिवाशक्तं क्षत्रधर्मेण भार्गव |
अवजानासि मे तेजः पश्य मेऽद्य पराक्रमम् || १-७६-३_END
BEGIN_
"Oh, Bhaargava Rama, demeaning me as though I am timorous, hence incapable to handle the bow, and hence I am an ignoble 
one for Kshatriya-hood, is meaningless... come on, now you may see my spiritedness and sprightliness..." So said Rama to 
Bhaargava. [1-76-3]_END

B_1_C_76_3
BEGIN_
इत्युक्त्वा राघवः क्रुद्धो भार्गवस्य वरायुधम् |
शरं च प्रतिजग्राह हस्ताल्लघुपराक्रमः || १-७६-४_END
BEGIN_
Raghava, the nimble-handed vanquisher of his opponents, speaking thus in high dudgeon expropriated that estimable weapon, 
namely the longbow of Vishnu, from the hand of Bhaargava Rama, along with the long-arrow that is already fitted on it... 
[1-76-4]_END

B_1_C_76_4
BEGIN_
आरोप्य स धनू रामः शरं सज्यं चकार ह |
जामदग्न्यं ततो रामं रामः क्रुद्धोऽब्रवीदिदम् || १-७६-५_END
BEGIN_
On lifting up the bow that is already fitted with an arrow on bowstring, then Rama started to take aim with it, but being 
indecisive about the target, then Rama of Dasharatha irefully said this to Rama of Jamagadni. [1-76-5]_END

B_1_C_76_5
BEGIN_
ब्राह्मणोऽसीति पूज्यो मे विश्वामित्रकृतेन च |
तस्माच्छक्तो न ते राम मोक्तुं प्राणहरं शरम् || १-७६-६_END
BEGIN_
Oh Rama of Bhaargava, even if you are a Brahman you are eliminable, but because of your relationship with Vishvamitra, 
and because you are a venerable one for me, I am disinclined to release this arrow that exterminates your life... [1-76-6]_END

B_1_C_76_6
BEGIN_
इमां वा त्वद्गतिं राम तपोबलसमार्जितान् |
लोकानप्रतिमान्वापि हनिष्यामि यदिच्छसि || १-७६-७_END
BEGIN_
Oh Bhaargava Rama, either this motility of yours at the speed of your mind, or even those unparalleled realms of heavens 
which you have earned by the power of your ascesis, I will eliminate whichever you wish... [1-76-7]_END

B_1_C_76_7
BEGIN_
न ह्ययं वैष्णवो दिव्यः शरः परपुरंजयः |
मोघः पतति वीर्येण बलदर्पविनाशनः || १-७६-८_END
BEGIN_
"This Vishnu's divine arrow is the conqueror of opponents' citadels, and a vanquisher of their vigour and vainglory, and 
it will not fall through wastefully... isn't it!" So said archer Rama to axeman Rama. [1-76-8]_END

B_1_C_76_8
BEGIN_
वरायुधधरं रामं द्रष्टुं सर्षिगणाः सुराः |
पितामहं पुरस्कृत्य समेतास्तत्र सर्वशः || १-७६-९
गंधर्वाप्सरसश्चैव सिद्धचारणकिन्नराः |
यक्षराक्षसनागाश्च तद्द्रष्टुं महदद्भुतम् || १-७६-१०_END
BEGIN_
Gods together with the assemblages of sages have come keeping the Grandparent Brahma at their fore, likewise the gandharva-s, 
apsara-s, siddha-s, caarana-s, kinnaraa-s, yaksha-s, sprites and reptilian beings have also come to see Rama who is now 
wielding the extraordinary longbow of Vishnu, and extremely amazing event that is going to ensue. [1-76-9, 10]_END

B_1_C_76_9
BEGIN_
जडीकृते तदा लोके रामे वरधनुर्धरे |
निर्वीर्यो जामदग्न्योऽसौ रमो राममुदैक्षत || १-७६-११_END
BEGIN_
Then, when Rama is ready to take aim with the arrow on that inscrutable longbow, and when the worlds are being rendered 
as insentient, then that Rama of Jamadagni is rendered vigourless and he stared up at Rama of Dasharatha. [1-76-11]_END

B_1_C_76_10
BEGIN_
तेजोभिर्हतवीर्यत्वाज्जामदग्न्यो जडीकृतः |
रामं कमलपत्राक्षं मन्दं मन्दमुवाच ह || १-७६-१२_END
BEGIN_
Rama of Jamadagni is calloused as his vitality is subdued by the radiance of that lotus-petal eyed Rama of Dasharatha, and 
he spoke to Rama of Dasharatha, slowly and softly. [1-76-12]_END

B_1_C_76_11
BEGIN_
काश्यपाय मया दत्ता यदा पूर्वं वसुंधरा |
विषये मे न वस्तव्यमिति मां काश्यपोऽब्रवीत् || १-७६-१३_END
BEGIN_
Once, when I donated entire earth to Sage Kashyapa, Kashyapa told me 'uninhabitable is my domain, viz., this earth for 
you...' thus... [1-76-13]_END

B_1_C_76_12
BEGIN_
सोऽहं गुरुवचः कुर्वन् पृथिव्यां न वसे निशाम् |
तदा प्रभृति काकुत्स्थ कृता मे काश्यपस्य ह || १-७६-१४_END
BEGIN_
Such as I was, in my observance of my mentor Kashyapa's order I do not spend nights on this earth from then afterwards, 
oh, Kakutstha Rama, as I made over this earth for Kashyapa, indeed... [1-76-14]_END

B_1_C_76_13
BEGIN_
तमिमां मद्गतिं वीर हन्तुं नार्हसि राघव |
मनोजवं गमिष्यामि महेन्द्रं पर्वतोत्तमम् || १-७६-१५_END
BEGIN_
Thereby oh, valiant one, it will be inapt of you to impair this motility of mine, oh, Raghava, I will depart with the speed 
of cerebration to Mt. Mahendra, a par excellent mountain... [1-76-15]_END

B_1_C_76_14
BEGIN_
लोकास्त्वप्रतिमा राम निर्जितास्तपसा मया |
जहि तान् शरमुख्येन मा भूत् कालस्य पर्ययः || १-७६-१६_END
BEGIN_
But I triumphed over matchless realms of heavens with my ascesis, oh, Rama, you may hash them up with that irreversible 
arrow... let there be no time-lag... [1-76-16]_END

B_1_C_76_15
BEGIN_
अक्षय्यं मधुहन्तारं जानामि त्वां सुरेश्वरम् |
धनुषोऽस्य परामर्शात् स्वस्ति तेऽस्तु परंतप || १-७६-१७_END
BEGIN_
I have realized your touch of nature as that of the Immutable Supreme Being, God of Gods, the Exterminator of the demon 
Madhu, namely Vishnu, by the touch of your handling that bow... oh, enemy-inflamer, blessedness alone betides you... [1-76-17]_END

B_1_C_76_16
BEGIN_
एते सुरगणाः सर्वे निरीक्षन्ते समागताः |
त्वामप्रतिमकर्माणमप्रतिद्वन्द्वमाहवे || १-७६-१८_END
BEGIN_
All of these gods who have come collectively are beholding you and your next move, for you are an unequalled one in your 
achievements and to whom there is no counter-dueller in conflicts... [1-76-18]_END

B_1_C_76_17
BEGIN_
न चेयं तव काकुत्स्थ व्रीडा भवितुमर्हति |
त्वया त्रैलोक्यनाथेन यदहं विमुखीकृतः || १-७६-१९_END
BEGIN_
Oh, Kakutstha Rama, you are the lord of the triad of worlds, such as you are, you faced me down, and it is malapropos to 
say that this is a disgrace to me... [1-76-19]_END

B_1_C_76_18
BEGIN_
शरमप्रतिमं राम मोक्तुमर्हसि सुव्रत |
शरमोक्षे गमिष्यामि महेन्द्रं पर्वतोत्तमम् || १-७६-२०_END
BEGIN_
"It will be apt of you to unloose that unsurpassed arrow, oh, Rama, as you have ethical commitment to wipe out demons as 
I wiped out menacing kings, and should you unloosen that arrow now I wish to depart to the ethereal mountain Mt. Mahendra, 
a point of no return for me..." So said Parashu Rama to Dasharatha Rama. [1-76-20]_END

B_1_C_76_19
BEGIN_
तथा ब्रुवति रामे तु जामदग्न्ये प्रतापवान् |
रामो दाशरथिः श्रीमान् चिक्षेप शरमुत्तमम् || १-७६-२१_END
BEGIN_
While Rama of Jamadagni is speaking that way, that venturesome and blessed Rama of Dasharatha shot off that nonpareil arrow 
from that longbow of Vishnu. [1-76-21]_END

B_1_C_76_20
BEGIN_
स हतान् दृश्य रामेण स्वान् लोकांस्तपसार्जितान् |
जामदग्न्यो जगामाशु महेन्द्रं पर्वतोत्तमम् || १-७६-२२_END
BEGIN_
On seeing all of his realms of heavens are shot-blasted by Rama of Dasharatha, Rama of Jamadagni vanished in a trice to 
Mt. Mahendra, the heavenly mountain. [1-76-22]_END

B_1_C_76_21
BEGIN_
ततो वितिमिराः सर्वा दिशा चोपदिशस्तथा |
सुराः सर्षिगणाः रामं प्रशशंसुरुदायुधम् || १-७६-२३_END
BEGIN_
Then dissipated is the darkness in all the divisions and likewise in all the subdivisions of compass, and the gods with 
the assemblages of sages extolled Rama, in whose hands the longbow is upraised. [1-76-23]_END

B_1_C_76_22
BEGIN_
रामं दाशरथिं रामो जामदग्न्यः प्रशस्य च |
ततः प्रदक्षिणीकृत्य जगामात्मगतिं प्रभुः || १-७६-२४_END
BEGIN_
Then that dab hand at axe, Rama of Jamadagni, on acclaiming, and even on making circumambulations to Rama of Dasharatha, 
went on his own way into oblivion. [1-76-24]_END

B_1_C_77_0
BEGIN_
गते रामे प्रशांतात्मा रामो दाशरथिर्धनुः |
वरुणायाप्रमेयाय ददौ हस्ते महायशाः || १-७७-१_END
BEGIN_
On the departure of Rama of Jamadagni, that most glorious Rama of Dasharatha is quietened at heart, and he gave away that 
longbow of Vishnu into the hand of inimitable Rain-god. [1-77-1]_END

B_1_C_77_1
BEGIN_
अभिवाद्य ततो रामो वसिष्ठ प्रमुखानृषीन् |
पितरं विह्वलं दृष्ट्वा प्रोवाच रघुनंदनः || १-७७-२_END
BEGIN_
On paying respects to sage Vashishta and to the other important sages, Rama, the delight of Raghu's lineage, placatingly 
addressed his agitated father Dasharatha. [1-77-2]_END

B_1_C_77_2
BEGIN_
जामदग्न्यो गतो रामः प्रयातु चतुरङ्गिगिणी |
अयोध्याभिमुखी सेना त्वया नाथेन पालिता || १-७७-३_END
BEGIN_
"Rama of Jamadagni has gone on his way, you may now order the army under your wardship, for which you are the lord, 
to move on towards Ayodhya..." So said Rama to his father. [1-77-3]_END

B_1_C_77_3
BEGIN_4,5
रामस्य वचनं श्रुत्वा राजा दशरथः सुतम् |
बाहुभ्यां संपरिष्वज्य मूर्ध्नि चाघ्राय राघवम् || १-७७-४
गतो राम इति श्रुत्वा हृष्टः प्रमुदितो नृपः |
पुनर्जातं तदा मेने पुत्रमात्मानमेव च || १-७७-५_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the words of Rama king Dasharatha hugged his son with both of his arms, and kissed on the forehead of Raghava, 
and king Dasharatha is gladdened to listen about the departure of Parashu Rama, and then he is further gladdened in deeming 
that he and his sons took a rebirth. [1-77-4, 5]_END

B_1_C_77_4
BEGIN_
चोदयामास तां सेनां जगामाशु ततः पुरीम् |
पताकाध्वजिनीं रम्यां तूर्योद्घुष्टनिनादिताम् || १-७७-६
सिक्तराजपथां रम्यां प्रकीर्णकुसुमोत्कराम् |
राजप्रवेशसुमुखैः पौरैर्मंगलपाणिभिः || १-७७-७
संपूर्णां प्राविशद्राजा जनौघैः समलंकृताम् |_END
BEGIN_
Then the King Dasharatha ordered that legion to move ahead, and then they all went towards delightful city Ayodhya, whose 
royal highways are wetted with water, sprinkled with bunches of flowers, decorated with banners and bannerettes up above 
them, and reverberating with high sounding bugle-horns. Further, those highways are replete with urbanites welcomers who 
are handling welcoming kits which are golden handy-crates or plates in which lit camphor, fragrant incenses, vermilion powder, 
flowers to shower on the incomers are arranged, and those highways are well-decorated with throngs of people who are glee-faced 
at their king's re-entry, and into such an exhilarating city Ayodhya king Dasharatha and his retinue entered. [1-77-7, 8a]_END

B_1_C_77_5
BEGIN_
पौरैः प्रत्युद्गतो दूरं द्विजैश्च पुरवासिभिः || १-७७-८
पुत्रैरनुगतः श्रीमान् श्रीमद्भिश्च महायशाः |
प्रविवेश गृहं राजा हिमवत्सदृशं प्रियम् || १-७७-९_END
BEGIN_
When the citizenry and city-dwelling Brahman-s have received him from a distance, that illustrious king Dasharatha followed 
by his phenomenal and praiseworthy sons then entered his happy house and home, which is like the lofty and lordly Himalayan 
palazzo. [1-77-8b, 9]_END

B_1_C_77_6
BEGIN_
ननन्द स्वजनै राजा गृहे कामैः सुपूजितः |
कौसल्या च सुमित्रा च कैकेयी च सुमध्यमा || १-७७-१०
वधूप्रतिग्रहे युक्ता याश्चान्या राजयोषितः |_END
BEGIN_
In palace king Dasharatha is overjoyed when he is surrounded with his own inmates of palace-chambers, and when his long 
cherished ambitions have come true, while his queens, Kausalya, Sumitra, and slender waisted Kaikeyi and other wives are 
overjoyed in the functions of receiving the four brides. [1-77-10]_END

B_1_C_77_7
BEGIN_
ततः सीतां महाभागामूर्मिलां च यशस्विनीम् || १-७७-११
कुशध्वजसुते चोभे जगृहुर्नृपयोषितः |_END
BEGIN_
Then the womenfolk of the king welcomed the highly propitious Seetha and the highly fortunate Urmila too, along with both 
the daughters of Kushadhvaja, namely Maandavi and Shrutakiirti, with pageantry and festivity. [1-77-11b, 12a]_END

B_1_C_77_8
BEGIN_
मंगलालापनैर्होमैः शोभिताः क्षौमवाससः || १-७७-१२
देवतायतनान्याशु सर्वास्ताः प्रत्यपूजयन् |_END
BEGIN_
All of the brides and bridegrooms clad in silks promptly worshipped the gods in sanctums to the benedictory chanting of 
Vedic hymns and Ritual-fires, thus they shone forth like the tongues of Holy Fires of Vedic Altars. [1-77-12b, 13a]_END

B_1_C_77_9
BEGIN_
अभिवाद्याभिवाद्यांश्च सर्वा राजसुतास्तदा || १-७७-१३
रेमिरे मुदिताः सर्वा भर्तृभिः सहिता रहः |_END
BEGIN_
Then all the princesses paid respects to all of the respectable ones, and they luxuriated in sequestered palace-chambers 
along with their husbands. [1-77-13b, 14a]_END

B_1_C_77_10
BEGIN_
कृतदाराः कृतास्त्राश्च सधनाः ससुहृज्जनाः || १-७७-१४
शुश्रूषमाणाः पितरं वर्तयन्ति नरर्षभाः |_END
BEGIN_
And those best men among men, Rama, Lakshmana, Bharata, Shatrughna, who are by now accomplished persons in weaponry and 
whose marriages have also come to pass, occupied themselves in the welfare of kingdom while assisting their father and moving 
around with good hearted people. [1-77-14b, 15a]_END

B_1_C_77_11
BEGIN_
कस्यचित्त्वथ कालस्य राजा दशरधः सुतम् || १-७७-१५
भरतं कैकेयीपुत्रमब्रवीद्रघुनन्दनः |_END
BEGIN_
Then after sometime that king Dasharatha, the legatee of Raghu-s, spoke to his and Kaikeyi's son, Bharata. [1-77-15b, 16a]_END

B_1_C_77_12
BEGIN_
अयं केकयराजस्य पुत्रो वसति पुत्रक || १-७७-१६
त्वां नेतुमागतो वीरो युधाजिन्मातुलस्तव |_END
BEGIN_
"This is your maternal uncle and the son of king of Kekaya, and this valiant Yudhaajit came here to take you to Kekaya province, 
and he is staying behind because of your marriage..." thus Dasharatha bade farewell to Bharata suggesting that Bharata may 
now go with Yudhaajit. [1-77-16b, 17a]_END

B_1_C_77_13
BEGIN_
श्रुत्वा दशरथस्यैतद्भरतः कैकेयीसुतः || १-७७-१७
गमनायाभिचक्राम शत्रुघ्नसहितस्तदा |_END
BEGIN_
On hearing the opinion of Dasharatha, Bharata, the son of Kaikeyi, then readied himself to travel along with Shatrughna 
to Kekaya province. [1-77-17b, 18a]_END

B_1_C_77_14
BEGIN_
आपृच्छ्य पितरं शूरो रामं चाक्लिष्टकर्मणम् || १-७७-१८
मातृश्चापि नरश्रेष्टः शत्रुघ्नसहितो ययौ |_END
BEGIN_
That valiant and best one among men Bharata on asking leave from his father, from Rama, an uncomplicatedly dextrous one 
in undertaking deeds, and even from his mothers, Kaikeyi, Sumitra, and Kausalya, travelled on along with Shatrughna. [1-77-18b, 
19a]_END

B_1_C_77_15
BEGIN_
युधाजित् प्राप्य भरतं सशत्रुघ्नं प्रहर्षितः || १-७७-१९
स्वपुरं प्राविशद्वीरः पिता तस्य तुतोष ह |_END
BEGIN_
Yudhaajit on clinching not only Bharata, but Shatrughna also, that valiant one is highly gladdened and entered his own city, 
indeed to the high rejoice of his father, King of Kekaya. [1-77-19b, 20a]_END

B_1_C_77_16
BEGIN_
गते च भरते रामो लक्ष्मणश्च महाबलः || १-७७-२०
पितरं देवसंकाशं पूजयामासतुस्तदा |_END
BEGIN_
After the departure of Bharata, then the masterly proficient Rama along with Lakshmana started to square with the plans 
and programs of his godly father for an ideal-sovereignty. [1-77-20b, 21a]_END

B_1_C_77_17
BEGIN_
पितुराज्ञां पुरस्कृत्य पौरकार्याणि सर्वशः || १-७७-२१
चकार रामः सर्वाणि प्रियाणि च हितानि च |
मातृभ्यो मातृकार्याणि कृत्वा परमयंत्रितः || १-७७-२२
गुरूणां गुरुकार्याणि काले कालेऽन्ववैक्षत |_END


B_1_C_77_18
BEGIN_
एवं दशरथः प्रीतो ब्राह्मणा नैगमास्तथा || १-७७-२३
रामस्य शीलवृत्तेन सर्वं विषयवासिनः |
तेषामतियशा लोके रामः सत्यपराक्रमः || १-७७-२४
स्वयम्भूरिव भूतानां बभूव गुणवत्तरः |_END
BEGIN_
That way Dasharatha is pleased with the deportment and comportment of Rama, likewise the Brahman-s and urbanites, and even 
all of the indwellers in the entire kingdom are pleased, and he who has high distinction, his truthfulness alone is his 
vantage point, and whose hallmarks are of higher degree, that Rama has manifested himself to those subjects in the kingdom, 
and even to all of the living beings in the world, as the Self-Created Brahma. [1-77-23b, 24, 25a]_END

B_1_C_77_19
BEGIN_
रामश्च सीतया सार्धं विजहार बहूनृतून् || १-७७-२५
मनस्वी तद्गतमानस्य तस्या हृदि समर्पितः |_END
BEGIN_
Also, that hearty Rama who permeated into the heart of Seetha is ensconced in Seetha's heart alone, and he disported for 
many seasons along with Seetha. [1-77-25b, 26a]_END

B_1_C_77_20
BEGIN_
प्रिया तु सीता रामस्य दाराः पितृकृता इति || १-७७-२६
गुणाद्रूपगुणाच्चापि प्रीतिर्भूयोऽभिवर्धते |_END
BEGIN_
Seetha has become the beloved of Rama as she is wedded with the assent of his father Dasharatha, further Rama's love for 
Seetha burgeoned by virtue of Seetha's own virtues and loveliness. [1-77-26b, 27a]_END

B_1_C_77_21
BEGIN_
तस्याश्च भर्ता द्विगुणं हृदये परिवर्तते || १-७७-२७
अन्तर्गतमपि व्यक्तमाख्याति हृदयं हृदा |_END
BEGIN_
Even Rama as her husband made his mark in Seetha's heart twice as good, and they both used to clearly converse about their 
thoughts in their heart of hearts, just by their hearts. [1-77-27b, 28a]_END

B_1_C_77_22
BEGIN_
तस्य भूयो विशेषेण मैथिली जनकात्मजा |
देवताभिः समा रूपे सीता श्रीरिव रूपिणी || १-७७-२८_END
BEGIN_
In her mien Seetha is identical with goddesses, and she is like personified Goddess Lakshmi, thus she is the reshaped Divine 
Prosperity, and as she hails from Holy Mithila she shall be held Holy, and since she is the daughter of Janaka, a loftiest 
sagacious and invincible king, she is sagely and stately, besides being shapely, and she with all these heaps of natural 
traits and characteristics, Seetha is rejoicing the heart of Rama. [1-77-28b, c]_END

B_1_C_77_23
BEGIN_
तया स राजर्षिसुतोऽभिकामया
समेयिवानुत्तमराजकन्यया |
अतीव रामः शुशुभे मुदान्वितो
विभुः श्रिया विष्णुरिवामरेश्वरः || १-७७-२९_END
BEGIN_
When passionately conjugated with such a princess from the irreproachable king Janaka, Rama, the son of sagely king Dasharatha, 
has enthusiastically shone forth like the God of Gods and the Efficient Cause, namely Vishnu, when He is together with Goddess 
Lakshmi. [1-77-29]_END
